### [1] [Sensitivity of p_T Fluctuations to the QCD Equation of State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18211)
*Rutik Manikandhan,Rohit Gupta,Rene Bellwied*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个涵盖RHIC能量扫描能区（$\sqrt{s_{\text{NN}}} = 3.0$ 至 $200$ GeV）的横向动量关联 $C_{p{\rm T}}$ 的理论基准线，首次将基于格点QCD结果在有限重子化学势（baryochemical potential $\mu_{\rm B}$）下的状态方程（Equation of State, EOS）应用于该可观测量的统一框架描述，并指出高能区边缘碰撞中非热关联机制的涌现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为解释重离子碰撞中的横向动量涨落并寻找QCD临界点（QCD critical point），需要一个覆盖宽能量范围与中心度（centrality）依赖的理论基准线。此前缺乏从格点QCD状态方程出发、统一描述 $C_{p{\rm T}}$ 能量依赖的系统研究。

Method: 采用一个简化的流体动力学（fluid-dynamic）演化模型，核心创新在于将来自有限 $\mu_{\rm B}$ 下格点QCD计算的状态方程作为输入，统一描述从 $\sqrt{s_{\text{NN}}} = 3.0$ 到 $200$ GeV的横向动量关联 $C_{p{\rm T}}$ 的能量与中心度依赖性。

Result: 该简约动力学模型有效捕获了实验数据中 $C_{p{\rm T}}$ 的特征中心度标度行为。低能区的结果主要受状态方程和系统寿命（system lifetime）调控；但在最高能量下的边缘碰撞（peripheral collisions）中出现了显著偏离，表明非热关联机制开始起作用。

Conclusion: 该理论基线为横向动量涨落分析提供了一个必要的基准（benchmark），有助于在重离子碰撞中寻找QCD临界点。

Abstract: We construct a novel theoretical baseline for dynamical transverse momentum correlations, $C_{pT}$, across a wide range of collision energies spanning the RHIC Beam Energy Scan (BES) program. For the first time, a unified framework is developed to describe the energy and centrality dependence of $C_{p_{\rm T}}$ from $\sqrt{s_{\text{NN}}} = 3.0$ to $200$~GeV. A central feature of this study is the implementation of Equation of State (EOS) inputs derived from Lattice QCD results at finite baryochemical potential $μ_{\rm B}$, representing the first such application to the measured transverse momentum correlations. Despite the minimalist nature of the fluid-dynamic evolution employed, the model effectively captures the characteristic centrality scaling of the experimental data. Our results indicate that while the bulk evolution is largely governed by the EOS and system lifetime at lower energies, significant deviations in peripheral collisions at top energies highlight the onset of non-thermal correlation mechanisms. This baseline provides a necessary benchmark for interpreting transverse momentum fluctuations in heavy-ion collisions and can aid in the search for the QCD critical point.

</details>


### [2] [The equation of state for neutron stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17006)
*Veronica Dexheimer*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本章作为中子星及其并合过程中致密物质与状态方程（equation of state）的导论，回顾了从相对论框架到多自由度、模型、对称性与相变的理论发展，并总结了当前理论、实验与观测的认识，展望了未来十年的研究进展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为读者提供中子星内部致密物质及其状态方程的系统性导引，帮助理解该领域的历史演变、当前认知与未来发展方向。

Method: 采用综述性论述方式，依次介绍中子星内部结构、历史理论框架（侧重相对论形式论（relativistic formalism））、不同自由度（degrees of freedom）、模型（models）、对称性（symmetries）与相（phases），并结合理论、实验与观测三方面总结当前认识。

Result: 概述了当前对致密物质的理解现状，指出该领域涵盖理论、实验与观测三个维度的综合进展。

Conclusion: 预期未来十年内致密物质与中子星状态方程研究将取得显著进展。

Abstract: This chapter is intended as an introduction to dense matter and the equation of state of neutron stars and their mergers. It begins with a brief description of neutron star interiors, followed by a historical overview of the theoretical frameworks used to describe them focusing on relativistic formalisms, including different degrees of freedom, models, symmetries, and phases. It also provides an overview of our current understanding of dense matter (including theory, experiments, and observations) and discusses the advances we expect to see in the field over the next decade.

</details>


### [3] [Chemonuclear Transmutation and Noble Metal Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17238)
*Hidetsugu Ikegami,Masako Ikegami*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文研究类金属氢化物-电子供体混合物体系，发现吸附氢原子可转变为金属态并合金化，电子供体提供的密集巡游s-电子降低金属氢熔点，引发热力学液态活性。该体系在460K温度下使D2-D2聚变增强20–30个数量级、D3-D3化学核聚变增强30–46个数量级，产生23.8 MeV动能α粒子（α-particle/He离子），并级联诱导多种元素合成的化学核反应（chemonuclear reaction），类似于非均匀宇宙中的大爆炸核合成（Big Bang nucleosynthesis）。应用上可用于锶-90和铯-137的嬗变以实现放射性废物消除，并在氢-镍纳米粉-锂混合物中实现贵金属的规模化合成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索类金属氢化物-电子供体混合物体系在降低金属氢熔点、诱导热力学液态活性条件下的增强型核聚变与化学核反应机制，并评估其在放射性废物处理、元素合成及贵金属制备方面的潜在应用价值。

Method: 在类金属氢化物-电子供体混合物体系中，通过电子供体提供密集巡游s-电子（itinerant s-electrons）来降低金属氢的熔点，使体系在460 K温度下表现出热力学液态活性（thermodynamical liquid activity），从而增强D2-D2聚变与D3-D3化学核聚变反应速率，并触发α粒子诱导的级联化学核反应。

Result: D2-D2聚变增强20–30个数量级，D3-D3化学核聚变增强30–46个数量级，产生能量为23.8 MeV的α粒子；α粒子诱导的化学核反应可实现90Sr与137Cs的嬗变；在氢-镍纳米粉-锂混合物中，分散带电的跨金原子（trans-gold atoms）增强化学核α-簇发射（alpha-cluster emission），实现贵金属的规模化合成。

Conclusion: 类金属氢化物-电子供体混合物体系能够在相对低温（460 K）下大幅增强核聚变与化学核反应，具有类似于非均匀宇宙中大爆炸核合成的物理本质；该体系为放射性废物消除和贵金属合成提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: In the system of metallike hydride-electron donor mixtures, adsorbed hydrogen atoms are transformed into metallic states and alloyed. Dense itinerary s-electrons supplied by the electron donor cause a drop in the melting point of metallic hydrogen. As a result, this system reveals thermodynamical liquid activity. The coherent D2-D2 fusion and the D3-D3 chemonuclear fusion are enhanced with factors of 20 to 30 and 30 to 46 figures of magnitude respectively at T=460 K, hence the production of intense He ions of 23.8 MeV kinetic energy. The ions or alpha-particles induce enhanced cascade chemonuclear reactions towards diverse and useful element synthesis. This phenomenon is in the nature of the Big Bang nucleosynthesis that takes place in an inhomogeneous universe. An application of the alpha-induced chemonuclear reaction - i.e., the transmutation of 90Sr and 137Cs - is prescribed in this chapter. This system of metallike hydride-electron donor mixtures raises the possibility of radioactive waste vanishment. Stimulated by alpha-particle irradiation, trans-gold nuclei undergo exothermic alpha-cluster emissions, producing coherently line-up alpha-clusters. In the chemonuclear D-D fusion, the 4alpha-cluster reveals the thermodynamical activity of oxygen atoms. In the hydrogen-Ni nanopowder-Li mixtures, dispersively charged trans-gold atoms undergo enhanced chemonuclear alpha-cluster emissions, hence the mass synthesis of noble metals. The case of chemonuclear pion production is presented at the end of this chapter.

</details>

### [4] [Multibath Influence Matrices: Universal Scaling from Real-Time Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16411)
*Matan Lotem,Michael Sonner,Valentin Link,Alessio Lerose,Dmitry A. Abanin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过将时空张量网络压缩为半群影响矩阵（semigroup influence matrices）和矩阵乘积态（matrix-product states），有效解决了强关联多轨道系统中临界动力学（critical dynamics）的发散时间尺度问题。以双杂质安德森模型（two-impurity Anderson model）为基准，计算谱函数（spectral functions）描绘了从近藤共振（Kondo resonance）经非费米液体量子临界点到能隙单线态相的演化，并通过突然淬火（sudden quenches）和Kibble-Zurek斜坡（Kibble-Zurek ramps）得到普适的两通道近藤指数（two-channel-Kondo exponent），证实了多浴影响矩阵（multibath influence matrices）是处理实时动力学（real-time dynamics）的实用工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临界动力学中发散的时间尺度是经典和量子模拟的瓶颈，亟需一种能够压缩时空张量网络的方法来克服这一困难。

Method: 在时间维度上将时空张量网络压缩为半群影响矩阵，在空间维度上通过矩阵乘积态进行压缩，从而实现对强关联多轨道系统实时动力学的有效模拟。

Result: 以双杂质安德森模型为基准，成功计算了谱函数，描绘了从近藤共振经非费米液体量子临界点到能隙单线态相的完整演化。通过突然淬火和Kibble-Zurek斜坡解析了从瞬态到渐近动力学的过程，获得了普适的两通道近藤指数。

Conclusion: 多浴影响矩阵被确立为一种处理强关联多轨道系统中实时动力学的实用工具。

Abstract: Diverging timescales are the hallmark of critical dynamics and the bottleneck to their classical and quantum simulation. To tame this, we compress a spacetime tensor network: temporally into semigroup influence matrices and spatially via matrix-product states. Benchmarking on the two-impurity Anderson model with its four fermionic species, we compute spectral functions to map the evolution from a Kondo resonance, across a non-Fermi-liquid quantum critical point, and into a gapped singlet phase. Resolving transient through asymptotic dynamics in sudden quenches and Kibble-Zurek ramps, we obtain the universal two-channel-Kondo exponent. Together, these results establish multibath influence matrices as a practical tool for real-time dynamics in strongly correlated multi-orbital systems.

</details>


### [5] [$J_{1} - J_{2} - δ$ model on a square lattice: From Altermagnet to Columnar antiferromagnet via quantum disordered phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16415)
*Subharthi Paul,Darshan G. Joshi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究局域矩磁体中交变磁有序（altermagnetism）在磁阻挫（magnetic frustration）引发的量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）下的鲁棒性，通过方晶格上含棋盘格型次近邻相互作用的Heisenberg模型，利用线性自旋波理论（linear spin-wave theory）分析了Néel型交变磁体与柱状反铁磁体之间的相变，并发现两者之间存在一个量子无序（quantum disordered）中间相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnet）在无自旋各向异性相互作用或外场时具有零净磁化（zero net magnetization）和相反手性磁振子能带（magnon bands）分裂的特点，但其受磁阻挫引发的量子涨落的影响尚不清楚，本文旨在探究该鲁棒性。

Method: 在方晶格上考虑最近邻相互作用和两种棋盘格型次近邻相互作用的Heisenberg模型，该模型连续插值于$J_1-J_2$ Heisenberg模型与棋盘格晶格Heisenberg模型之间；采用线性自旋波理论计算磁振子色散（magnon dispersion）、序参量（order parameter）、静态与动态结构因子（static and dynamical structure factors）。

Result: 较弱次近邻相互作用时实现Néel型交变磁体相；较强次近邻相互作用时出现柱状反铁磁体（columnar antiferromagnet）相；两个磁有序相之间存在一个量子无序中间相，该相与$J_1-J_2$模型中的量子无序区域相关；向棋盘格晶格极限调谐时，量子无序区域进一步稳定。

Conclusion: 磁阻挫导致的量子涨落可以在交变磁体系统中诱导出量子无序相，从而破坏交变磁有序；该量子无序区域的稳定性随晶格趋向棋盘格极限而增强。

Abstract: Altermagnetism in the case of local-moment magnets is characterized by zero net magnetization and splitting of opposite chirality magnon bands in the absence of any spin-anisotropic interactions or external field. In this work we investigate the robustness of altermagnets against quantum fluctuations arising from magnetic frustration. We consider a Heisenberg model on a square lattice with two different types of second-neighbor interactions, as in a checkboard pattern, in addition to the nearest-neighbor interaction. This model continuously interpolates between the $J_{1}-J_{2}$ Heisenberg model on the square lattice and the Heisenberg model on the checkerboard lattice. For weaker second-neighbor interactions a Néel-type altermagnet phase is realized. On the other hand, for stronger second-neighbor interactions a columnar antiferromagnet emerges. Using linear spin-wave theory we calculate the magnon dispersion, order parameter, static and dynamical structure factors for the two magnetic phases. Further, we show that there is an intermediate quantum disordered phase separating the two magnetic phases, which is connected to the one realized in the $J_{1}-J_{2}$ model. The quantum disordered region is further stabilized as we tune towards the checkerboard lattice limit.

</details>


### [6] [Stroboscopic stability of a Floquet chiral spin liquid beyond the folding frequency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16515)
*Didier Poilblanc*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了4×4环面上手性J1-J2-K海森堡模型的双步Floquet动力学，发现拓扑简并态（chiral-spin-liquid topological doublet）在远低于共振频率的驱动下仍能存活，其稳定性由局域能量标度而非多体带宽控制，预示在热力学极限下存在预热Floquet手性自旋液体（prethermal Floquet CSL）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索周期驱动（periodic driving）下手性自旋液体（chiral spin liquid, CSL）拓扑态的稳定性，特别是在折叠能区（folded regime）中准能量（quasienergy）共振对拓扑简并态的影响，以及该稳定性能否推广到热力学极限。

Method: 在4×4环面上，对静态下具有准简并拓扑双重态（topological doublet）的手性J1-J2-K海森堡模型施加双步Floquet驱动，交替演化非手性海森堡部分H_AF和手性plaquette部分H_K。在所有动量/旋转对称性扇区中精确计算单周期传播子（one-period propagator），并分析Floquet本征态的时间平均能量和频闪时间演化（stroboscopic time evolution）。

Result: 拓扑双重态在频率远低于共振频率ω_res≃11.5J_1时仍存活；时间平均能量表明双重态在ω≳6J_1时仍是谱的隔离底部。频闪演化显示ω≳ω_res时无加热，更低频率下只有缓慢吸收。折叠区准能量共振在平均能量中不可见，表明其为参数弱避免交叉（parametrically weak avoided crossings）。最优手性PEPS（chiral PEPS）张量在折叠区深部仍可描述该驱动双重态。

Conclusion: 该拓扑态的稳定性由局域能量标度（local energy scales）而非多体带宽控制，这一机制预期在热力学极限下仍成立，从而支持预热Floquet手性自旋液体的存在——当频率ω高于局域标度阈值时，加热时间随ω/J_1呈指数增长。

Abstract: We study the two-step Floquet dynamics of the chiral $J_1$-$J_2$-$K$ Heisenberg model on the $4\times4$ torus, alternating its non-chiral Heisenberg part $H_{\rm AF}$ and its chiral plaquette part $H_K$, at the parameter point where the static model (recovered in the infinite frequency limit) hosts a quasi-degenerate, spectrally isolated chiral-spin-liquid (CSL) topological doublet. The one-period propagator is computed exactly in all momentum/rotation symmetry sectors. It is shown that, decreasing the frequency, the topological doublet survives the drive far beyond the frequency $ω_{\mathrm{res}}\simeq 11.5 J_1$ at which folded states first cross it in quasienergy: the time-averaged energy of the Floquet eigenstates, which orders the folded Floquet spectrum, shows that the doublet remains the isolated bottom of the spectrum down to $ω\simeq6J_1$, while stroboscopic time evolution over thousands of periods shows no heating for $ω\gtrsim ω_{\mathrm{res}}$ and only slow absorption below. The quasienergy resonances that occur in the folded regime are invisible in the average energy, identifying them as parametrically weak avoided crossings. We argue that this mechanism -- stability controlled by local energy scales rather than by the extensive many-body bandwidth -- is precisely the one expected to survive in the thermodynamic limit, where a prethermal Floquet CSL should persist for $ω$ above a threshold set by local scales, with heating times exponentially long in $ω/J_1$. Consistently, the optimal $D=3$ chiral PEPS of the static problem still describes the driven doublet deep in the folded regime, with an essentially unchanged local tensor.

</details>


### [7] [AIMS: An uncertainty-aware AI experimentalist for quantum matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16544)
*Siyuan Qiu,Philip D. Suh,Nhat Huy Tran,Xirui Wang,Heonjoon Park,Kutay Akin,Kevin K. S. Multani,Seungwon Jung,Wenkai Cai,Xinyu Liu,Ziyan Zhu,Chunjing Jia,Zhantao Chen,Zhixun Shen,Zhurun Ji*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为AIMS（AI Agent for Inference and Measurement in Science）的不确定性感知闭环AI实验智能体，用于低温微波阻抗显微镜实验。AIMS通过三个嵌套循环（导航、测量选择和机制归因）将实验不确定性转化为具体行动，并在扭曲双层MoSe₂材料中成功识别出异常的ν=1/2晶体态，归因于量子涨落重整化起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自主科学智能体大多运行在数字化或高度结构化的环境中，目标、对象和动作均预先定义。量子材料实验面临更困难的问题：仪器状态漂移、有用信号仅存在于非均匀样品的稀疏区域、物理机制通常不唯一确定。因此需要一种能够感知并处理不确定性的自主实验系统。

Method: AIMS是一个不确定性感知的闭环AI实验智能体，连接三个嵌套循环：（1）导航层（navigation under uncertain perception）：在低温位移后重新定位样品，标记不可靠的位置估计并启动恢复策略；（2）测量选择层（measurement selection under sample inhomogeneity）：在样品非均匀性下选择测量位置，映射扭转角分布和广义维格纳晶体分数；（3）机制归因层（scale-resolved mechanism attribution under ambiguous physics）：通过测试经典极限、改变跳跃项和库仑作用能标、保留样品形貌作为可检验变量，实现能标分辨的物理机制归因。

Result: 在导航层，AIMS显著缩短了样品定位时间。在测量层，成功识别出扭曲双层MoSe₂中具有最强关联响应的区域。在发现层，AIMS判定异常鲁棒的ν=1/2晶体态优先起源于量子涨落重整化（quantum-fluctuation-renormalized），而非单纯的经典或量子熔化机制。

Conclusion: AIMS展示了面向量子物质的不确定性感知实验智能体能力，将感知恢复、测量选择和能标分辨的机制归因集成于一个闭环系统中，为自主科学实验在复杂物理系统中的实际应用提供了可行框架。

Abstract: Autonomous scientific agents are beginning to accelerate discovery, but most demonstrations operate in digital or highly structured settings where the objects, actions, and objectives are largely predefined. Quantum materials experiments pose a harder problem where uncertainties involve: the instrument state can drift, the useful signal may occupy only rare regions of an inhomogeneous sample, and the physical mechanism is often under-determined. Here we introduce the AI agent for Inference and Measurement in Science (AIMS), an uncertainty-aware closed-loop AI experimentalist for cryogenic microwave impedance microscopy that converts uncertainty into experimental action. AIMS links three nested loops: navigation under uncertain perception, measurement selection under sample inhomogeneity, and scale-resolved mechanism attribution under ambiguous physics. In navigation, it relocates the sample after cryogenic displacement, flags unreliable position estimates, and invokes recovery strategies, significantly reducing sample-locating time. In measurement, it maps twist angle distribution and generalized Wigner crystal score of twisted bilayer MoSe$_2$ to identify regions with the strongest correlated response. In discovery, AIMS asks not whether melting is simply classical or quantum, but how the competition of Coulomb repulsion, hopping, and other energy scales shapes the observed hierarchy. By testing the classical limit, varying hopping and Coulomb scales, and preserving sample morphology as a secondary testable variable, AIMS prioritizes a quantum-fluctuation-renormalized origin of the anomalously robust $ν= 1/2$ crystal. AIMS demonstrates uncertainty-aware experimental agency for quantum matter with perception recovery, measurement choice, and energy-scale-resolved mechanism attribution in one closed loop.

</details>


### [8] [Tuning superconducting pairing symmetry via a staggered potential in the doped honeycomb Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16663)
*Yanmei Cai,Yicheng Xiong,Ying Liang,Tianxing Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过量子蒙特卡洛方法发现，在掺杂蜂窝哈伯德模型中，可调控的子晶格交错势（staggered potential）能够在不改变掺杂浓度的情况下，诱导主导超导配对对称性从 d+id 波转变为 f_n 波，为非常规超导体的设计提供了一种新的带工程（band-engineering）工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 化学掺杂之外的可调参数稀缺，是制约非常规超导体（unconventional superconductor）和拓扑超导体（topological superconductor）设计的主要瓶颈。本文旨在探索子晶格交错势（staggered potential）作为一种新型调控手段，对掺杂蜂窝哈伯德模型（honeycomb Hubbard model）中配对对称性（pairing symmetry）的影响。

Method: 采用有限温行列式量子蒙特卡洛方法（determinant quantum Monte Carlo, DQMC）和零温约束路径量子蒙特卡洛方法（constrained-path quantum Monte Carlo, CPQMC），分别计算不同通道下的自旋磁化率（spin susceptibility）和配对关联函数（pairing correlation）。

Result: 增大交错势会抑制反铁磁涨落（antiferromagnetic fluctuation）。在低掺杂下，交错势诱导主导配对倾向从 d+id 波转变为 f_n 波，两种 QMC 方法结果一致；在高掺杂下，即使增强交错势，系统仍以 d+id 波配对为主。此外，增强在位相互作用 U 会强化已有的主导配对通道。

Conclusion: 交错势可在不改变掺杂浓度的条件下，作为一种实用的带工程工具选择性调控非常规配对对称性。该发现为设计基于石墨烯的人造超导体（graphene-based artificial superconductor）以及 Li_x MNCl 等掺杂带绝缘体（doped band insulator）提供了理论启示。

Abstract: The ability to control superconducting pairing symmetry is crucial for designing unconventional and topological superconductors, yet practical tuning parameters beyond chemical doping remain limited. In this study, we investigate the effect of a tunable sublattice staggered potential on the pairing symmetry in the doped honeycomb Hubbard model. Determinant quantum Monte Carlo at finite temperature and constrained-path quantum Monte Carlo at zero temperature are employed to compute spin susceptibilities and pairing correlations in different channels. We find that increasing the staggered potential suppresses antiferromagnetic fluctuations and, at low doping, induces a transition in the dominant pairing tendency from $d+id$-wave to $f_n$-wave, with consistent results from both quantum Monte Carlo methods. In contrast, at higher doping levels, the system remains dominated by $d+id$-wave pairing even under an enhanced staggered potential. Moreover, strengthening the on-site interaction $U$ enhances the dominant pairing channel, underscoring the essential role of electronic correlations. Our results establish the staggered potential as a practical band-engineering tool for selecting unconventional pairing symmetries without varying the doping concentration, providing inspiration for designing graphene-based artificial superconductors and related doped band insulators such as Li${}_x$MNCl.

### [9] [Nematic Wigner crystals in rhombohedral multilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17027)
*Yang Ge,Ashwini Malviya,Ethan Angerhofer,Zhengguang Lu,Jiabin Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文利用投影哈特里-福克（projected Hartree-Fock, HF）和含时哈特里-福克（time-dependent Hartree-Fock, TDHF）计算，系统研究了菱方四层石墨烯（rhombohedral tetralayer graphene）中的维格纳晶体（Wigner crystals, WCs），发现了两类具有不同对称性和稳定性的向列相维格纳晶体（nWCs）与C₃不变的维格纳晶体，并预测了可通过扫描隧道显微镜（STM）和角度分辨输运实验加以识别的稳定向列相WC相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验报道了菱方石墨烯中存在维格纳晶体的证据，但关于菱方四层石墨烯体系中维格纳晶化的具体相结构、对称性破缺模式及其稳定性尚缺乏系统的理论研究，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用投影哈特里-福克（projected Hartree-Fock, HF）计算获得维格纳晶体的基态相图，再通过含时哈特里-福克（time-dependent Hartree-Fock, TDHF）计算检验各WC态的局域稳定性。

Result: 在每维格纳原胞一个电子的条件下得到了两种WC：向列相维格纳晶体（nWCs，自发破缺三重旋转对称性C₃）和C₃不变的维格纳晶体。相图中存在两个nWC区域：在大位移场低电子密度区域的一个较大区域，以及中间位移场高密度区域的一个较小区域。所有WC态均为谷极化（valley-polarized）且陈数（Chern number）为零，在HF能带中具有正间接带隙。TDHF稳定性测试表明，所有C₃不变WC和一半nWC局域稳定，另一半nWC向每个原胞两个电子的WC或金属态失稳。

Conclusion: 预测的稳定向列相WC相可通过扫描隧道显微镜（STM）观测其各向异性电荷分布，或通过角度分辨输运测量方向依赖的去钉扎电压（depinning voltage）进行实验识别。

Abstract: Recent experiments have reported evidence for Wigner crystals (WCs) in rhombohedral graphene. Here, we investigate Wigner crystallization in rhombohedral tetralayer graphene using projected Hartree-Fock (HF) calculations and time-dependent Hartree-Fock (TDHF) calculations. We first perform HF calculations with one electron per Wigner unit cell, and find nematic WCs (nWCs) that spontaneously break the threefold rotational symmetry $C_3$ and $C_3$-invariant WCs. In particular, there are two nWC regions in the phase diagram: one larger region at large displacement fields and low electron densities, and another smaller region at intermediate fields and high densities. Both the nWCs and the $C_3$-invariant WCs are valley-polarized states with zero Chern number, and have positive indirect gaps in the HF band structure. We then perform TDHF calculations to further test the local stability of the WC states. We find that all $C_3$-invariant WCs and half of the nWCs are locally stable, while the remaining nWCs are unstable towards WCs with two electrons per unit cell or metallic states. The predicted stable nWC phase can be identified experimentally by scanning tunneling microscopy through its anisotropic charge distribution or by angle-resolved transport measurements via a direction-dependent depinning voltage.

### [10] [GPU-accelerated finite-temperature Lanczos method for Heisenberg spin systems with non-Abelian permutation symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17429)
*Shadan Ghassemi Tabrizi,Thomas D. Kühne*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文将有限温度Lanczos方法（FTLM）的GPU实现从仅利用总磁化对称性扩展至完全置换对称性（包括非阿贝尔点群和空间群），提出免存储投影哈密顿量的矩阵自由形式体系，并在单个NVIDIA B200加速器上完成了十二面体s=3/2海森堡反铁磁体（希尔伯特空间维度~1.1×10¹²）和5×8方格子s=1/2体系（M=0维度1.4×10¹¹）的大规模数值计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有FTLM的GPU实现仅利用了总磁化对称性（total-magnetization symmetry），未充分利用完全置换对称性（full permutation symmetry），尤其是非阿贝尔点群和空间群，导致高度对称团簇（如二十面体多面体）的对称性约化潜力未被挖掘。

Method: 提出一种矩阵自由形式体系（matrix-free formalism），避免显式存储投影后的哈密顿量，从而支持非阿贝尔群的不可约表示（irreducible representations, irreps）对称性约化。该方法同样适用于阿贝尔群，且保留GPU加速优势；用户可通过提供位点置换生成元（site-permutation generators）和自动计算的irrep矩阵运行自定义团簇，无需修改代码。

Result: 在单个NVIDIA B200加速器上，完成十二面体s=3/2海森堡反铁磁体（最大迭代对称块维度3.6×10⁹）和5×8方格子s=1/2体系的计算；对于十二面体，使用每个对称块24个随机向量和60步Lanczos迭代，约需50 GPU小时。

Conclusion: 该方法通过完全置换对称性进一步压缩了对称块维度，显著降低了大规模量子多体系统计算的计算开销，代码已开源发布。

Abstract: We extend a recent GPU implementation of the finite-temperature Lanczos method (FTLM) for Heisenberg spin Hamiltonians, which uses only total-magnetization symmetry, to the full permutation symmetry, including non-Abelian point and space groups. For highly symmetric clusters such as icosahedral polyhedra, the multidimensional irreducible representations (irreps) of the permutation group reduce the block dimensions substantially further than any Abelian subgroup. Here, we provide a matrix-free formalism (avoiding explicit storage of the projected Hamiltonian) for using such symmetries. The implementation applies equally to Abelian groups, retaining the advantages of GPU acceleration. Several cluster topologies are built in; beyond these, symmetry groups can be supplied as site-permutation generators, with irrep matrices computed automatically, so that user-defined clusters run without any code changes. We demonstrate the approach in production runs on a single NVIDIA B200 accelerator for the s=3/2 Heisenberg antiferromagnet on the dodecahedron (Hilbert-space dimension 4^20 ~ 1.1x10^12) and for the s=1/2 square lattice of 5x8 sites (M=0 dimension 1.4x10^11). With R=24 random vectors per symmetry block and 60 Lanczos steps, the dodecahedron campaign (with the largest iterated symmetry block having a dimension of 3.6x10^9) requires about 50 GPU-hours. The code is openly available under the Apache-2.0 license at https://github.com/ghasdeke/ftlm-pg-gpu, archived at DOI: 10.5281/zenodo.21445872.

</details>


### [11] [Gate-tunable giant anomalous Hall effect in magnetic topological insulator bilayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17988)
*Basavaraja G,Mukul Kabir*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和经典海森堡蒙特卡洛模拟（classical Heisenberg Monte Carlo simulations），揭示了静电门控（electrostatic gating）和表面化学功能化（surface chemical functionalization）可在二维MnBi2Te4中驱动从拓扑（topological）到常规反常霍尔（conventional anomalous Hall）的交叉，并显著提升磁有序温度（magnetic ordering temperature），为可重构量子器件（reconfigurable quantum devices）提供设计框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维极限下的本征磁拓扑绝缘体（intrinsic magnetic topological insulator）MnBi2Te4为探索厚度依赖的量子态及其在外界扰动下的演化提供了重要平台，但尚缺乏系统调控其拓扑、磁性和输运性质的方法。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和经典海森堡蒙特卡洛模拟（classical Heisenberg Monte Carlo simulations），研究静电门控和表面化学功能化对体系电子结构和磁性的影响。

Result: 空穴掺杂（hole doping）将费米能级（Fermi level）推入价带，由贝里曲率热点（Berry curvature hot spots）诱导出高达1127 S/cm的反常霍尔电导率（anomalous Hall conductivity）。表面化学掺杂使本征σxy从e²/h降至约0.86 e²/h，源于手性边缘模式（chiral edge mode）与二维薄膜金属体态（metallic bulk states）的谱共存。两种调控路径均显著增强面内交换相互作用（in-plane exchange interactions），大幅提升磁有序温度。

Conclusion: 本文建立了在超薄MnBi2Te4中协同工程化拓扑、磁性和输运性质的通用框架，为可重构量子器件（reconfigurable quantum devices）的发展提供直接指导。

Abstract: In the two-dimensional limit, the intrinsic magnetic topological insulator MnBi2Te4 provides a compelling platform for exploring thickness-dependent quantum states and their evolution under external perturbations. Using first-principles calculations and classical Heisenberg Monte Carlo simulations, we demonstrate that electrostatic gating and surface chemical functionalization can drive a systematic crossover from the topological to the conventional anomalous Hall regime. This transition is governed by the simultaneous shift of the Fermi level away from the topological gap and a reversal of interlayer coupling from antiferromagnetic to ferromagnetic order. Results reveal that hole doping drives the Fermi level into the valence bands, inducing an exceptionally high anomalous Hall conductivity of 1127 S/cm arising from Berry curvature hot spots. In contrast, surface chemical doping drives a topological state where intrinsic $σ_{xy}$ is reduced from $e^2/h$ to $\sim 0.86\ e^2/h$ by the spectral coexistance of chiral edge mode with metallic bulk states of the two-dimensional film. Furthermore, we show that both tuning routes significantly enhance in-plane exchange interactions, leading to a substantial increase in the magnetic ordering temperature relative to the pristine bilayer. These results establish a versatile framework for the simultaneous engineering of topological, magnetic, and transport properties in ultrathin MnBi2Te4, offering direct implications for the development of reconfigurable quantum devices.

### [12] [Frustration induced dimensional reduction and coexistence of long and short-range magnetic order in NdCl$_{3}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17995)
*Eli Zoghlin,Matthew B. Stone,Vasile O. Garlea,Matthias D. Frontzek,Andrew D. Christianson,Andrew F. May*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文结合宏观物性测量与中子散射技术，研究了NdCl₃在挫败（frustration）效应下的磁学行为，发现了准一维短程反铁磁序与长程有序的共存，并指出各向异性交换相互作用挫败是造成准一维行为与有序共存的关键驱动机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挫败效应（frustration）能够极大丰富量子磁体的物理图景，本文旨在通过研究NdCl₃的磁性行为，深入理解挫败在低维量子磁体中的作用机制。

Method: 采用宏观物性测量（bulk properties measurements）与中子散射（neutron scattering）技术，包括弹性中子散射（elastic neutron scattering）对单晶样品进行表征，并结合热容（heat capacity）数据分析磁熵变。

Result: 热容显示两个磁相变温度T_N1=270 mK和T_N2=180 mK，磁熵主要在T_N1之上以T*≈450 mK为中心的宽峰释放；T_N2以上存在高度各向异性的磁扩散散射（magnetic diffuse scattering），证实准一维短程反铁磁序是热容宽峰的来源；T_N1以下出现以k=(0 0 1/2)为传播矢量的磁布拉格峰（magnetic Bragg peaks），且T_N2<T<T_N1区间内磁扩散散射持续存在，表明短程与长程有序共存；T_N2以下扩散散射消失，长程有序完全建立。观察到的磁散射以c轴磁矩为主，并伴有少量ab平面分量。

Conclusion: 尽管有序磁基态的确切性质尚不明确，但准一维行为以及短程与长程有序的共存很可能是由各向异性交换相互作用（anisotropic exchange interactions）的挫败效应所驱动。

Abstract: The phenomenon of frustration greatly enriches the accessible physics of quantum magnets. With this in mind we study the magnetism of NdCl$_{3}$ using a combination of bulk properties measurements and neutron scattering techniques. The low-temperature heat capacity reveals two magnetic transitions at $T_{N1}$ = 270 mK and $T_{N2}$ = 180 mK. However, much of the magnetic entropy is released above $T_{N1}$, manifesting as a broad peak centered at $T^{*} \approx$ 450 mK. Single crystal elastic neutron scattering reveals highly anisotropic magnetic diffuse scattering above $T_{N2}$, confirming that quasi-one-dimensional, short-range, antiferromagnetic order is the origin of the broad peak in the heat capacity. Magnetic Bragg peaks characterized by a $\vec{k}$ = ($0$ $0$ $\frac{1}{2}$) propagation vector emerge below $T_{N1}$. Interestingly, the magnetic diffuse scattering persists for $T_{N2} < T < T_{N1}$, indicating a regime of coexisting short and long-range order. The magnetic Bragg peaks exhibit an additional increase in intensity below $T_{N2}$ with no change in $\vec{k}$. Concomitantly, the diffuse scattering disappears indicating the attainment of full long-range order. While the precise nature of the ordered magnetic ground state remains unresolved, the observed magnetic scattering indicates predominate $c$-axis moments with a small $ab$-plane component. We propose that the quasi-one-dimensional behavior and the coexistence of short and long-range order are driven by frustration of anisotropic exchange interactions.

### [13] [Phonon dynamics in Chromium under pressure: absence of phonon criticality at the approach of the quantum critical point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18015)
*P. Rodière,J. E. Lorenzo,Q. N. Meier,L. Paolasini,A. Bosak*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过高压非弹性X射线散射实验和第一性原理计算，研究了铬（Chromium）中费米面嵌套（Fermi surface nesting）与反铁磁自旋密度波（antiferromagnetic spin density wave）量子临界点附近声子异常（Kohn anomalies）的关系。结果表明，即使在远高于临界压力的条件下，声子软化依然存在，因此这些声子异常并不在反铁磁有序中起主要作用；费米面嵌套在高压下的鲁棒性（robustness）才是Kohn异常持续存在的原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解铬中巡游反铁磁自旋密度波的起源，特别是费米面嵌套和声子异常（Kohn anomalies）在量子临界点（quantum critical point）附近的行为，是本研究的主要动机。实验旨在探究在远超临界压力$P_c$时，声子异常是否消失，以判断其对反铁磁有序的贡献。

Method: 采用高压非弹性X射线散射（inelastic X-ray scattering）实验，测量了从常压到15.6 GPa（远超临界压力$P_c\approx10$ GPa）的声子色散曲线（phonon dispersion curves）。同时结合基于第一性原理（ab-initio）的理论计算，分析费米面嵌套随压力的变化。

Result: 在高达15.6 GPa的压力下（远高于临界压力$P_c$），靠近布里渊区（Brillouin zone）$H$点的Kohn异常（声子软化）依然存在。该软化在50K以下保持不变，且在顺磁相（paramagnetic phase）和反铁磁相（antiferromagnetic phase）中均被观察到。

Conclusion: 声子异常（Kohn anomalies）在反铁磁有序中不起主要作用；费米面嵌套在高压下保持鲁棒性，这是Kohn异常能在临界压力以上持续存在的根本原因。

Abstract: Fermi surface nesting is key to understanding the origin of the itinerant antiferromagnetic spin density wave in Chromium. At very low temperature, this density wave is destroyed above the critical pressure $P_c\approx$10~GPa, defining a quantum critical point. Strong electron-phonon coupling induces a small phonon softening close to the $H-$point of the Brillouin zone as well as close to the $H$-point. These phonon anomalies are known as Kohn anomalies. They remain unchanged down to 50K and are known to be present in both the paramagnetic and the antiferromagnetic phases. This paper presents inelastic X-ray scattering experiments on the phonon dispersion curves under pressure, up to $P=$15.6~GPa far above the critical pressure $P_c$. The softening of the well-known phonon anomalies is still present which leads to conclude that they do not play a major role at the antiferromagnetic ordering. Based on ab-initio calculation, the robustness of the Fermi surface nesting under pressure, explain the presence of these Kohn anomalies above the critical pressure.

### [14] [Universal Dynamic Scaling of 2D Quantum Ising Transition on the Fuzzy Sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18028)
*Meng Zeng,Shuai Yin,Roderich Moessner*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用模糊球正则化方案（fuzzy sphere regularization scheme）研究二维横场伊辛模型（transverse-field Ising model）的实时量子动力学，通过线性扫描横场从顺磁相到临界点，分析了不同淬火速率下序参量平方、激发能量密度和两点关联函数的有限时间标度行为，发现中等淬火速率下序参量平方遵循基布尔-祖雷克标度（Kibble-Zurek scaling）预测，而激发能量密度由于有限尺寸能隙未达到同一标度区域，慢淬火下则恢复了准绝热标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解二维横场伊辛模型的实时量子动力学行为，并检验基布尔-祖雷克标度（Kibble-Zurek scaling）在中间淬火速率下的适用性，同时探索模糊球正则化方案作为研究强耦合共形场论（conformal field theory, CFT）实时临界动力学的可行途径。

Method: 采用模糊球正则化方案对二维横场伊辛模型进行数值模拟，通过线性扫描横场从顺磁相到临界点，测量序参量平方 $\langle m_z^2 \rangle$、激发能量密度 $Q$ 和两点关联函数，并分析其有限时间标度行为。

Result: 中等淬火速率下，$\langle m_z^2 \rangle$ 的标度行为符合 $3$D Ising 普适类的基布尔-祖雷克预测，关联函数呈现指数衰减且关联长度可估算非普适标度系数；但激发能量密度 $Q$ 由于对称性导致的能级稀疏产生大的有效有限尺寸能隙，未能在现有系统尺寸下达到相同标度区域。慢淬火速率下，$\langle m_z^2 \rangle$ 和 $Q$ 均恢复准绝热标度。

Conclusion: 模糊球正则化方案不仅能实现伊辛共形场论（Ising CFT），还可推广到更广泛的 $(2+1)$ 维共形场论，为研究强耦合 CFT 的实时临界动力学提供了一条新路径，弥补了现有计算方法在此类问题上的挑战。

Abstract: We revisit the problem of \textit{real-time} quantum dynamics of the paradigmatic two dimensional transverse-field Ising model using the recently developed fuzzy sphere regularization scheme. By linearly ramping the transverse field from the paramagnetic phase to criticality, we study the finite-time scaling behavior of the squared order parameter $\langle m_z^2 \rangle$, the excitation energy density $Q$, and the two-point correlation function of $m_z$. We establish numerically that, at intermediate quench rate, $\langle m_z^2 \rangle$ follows the conventional Kibble-Zurek prediction set by the critical exponents of the $3$D Ising universality class, and the correlation function exhibits the expected exponential decay whose correlation length can be used to estimate the non-universal scaling coefficient in the freeze-out time/length. In contrast, the excitation energy density $Q$ does not reach the same scaling regime at available system sizes due to large effective finite-size gap from symmetry-enforced level sparsity in the energy spectrum. At slow quench rates the universal quasi-adiabatic scaling for both $\langle m_z^2 \rangle$ and $Q$ is recovered. Since the fuzzy sphere construction can realize not only the Ising conformal field theory (CFT), but a broad family of $(2+1)d$ CFTs, our results establish a route to the real-time critical dynamics of strongly coupled CFTs that are otherwise computationally challenging to study.

</details>


### [15] [Color superconductors and holon metals from doping a Fractional Chern insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18238)
*Ya-Hui Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文为掺杂C=1/3分数量子陈绝缘体（FCI）的金属相和超导相建立了一个统一的理论框架，基于部分子构造和SU(3)规范×SU(3)谷对称性，将电荷-e/3的空穴子视为夸克，系统分析了色反对称配对、粒子-空穴希格斯场等不同序参量下的超导相与正交金属相，并讨论了从FCI到超导的化学势调控转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在建立一个统一的低能有效理论，描述由掺杂分数量子陈绝缘体（FCI）衍生出的金属态和超导态，并揭示其中电荷-e/3空穴子（holon）的配对行为与高温超导及高能物理中色超导（color superconductivity）之间的深层联系。

Method: 采用部分子构造（parton construction）将电子算符分解为三个部分子场：c(r)=f₁(r)f₂(r)f₃(r)，构建具有SU(3)规范×SU(3)谷对称性的低能理论；将电荷-e/3的空穴子类比为夸克，借助高能物理中的色超导理论；通过分析不同类型的配对序参量（色反对称配对、粒子-空穴色-谷希格斯场）和对称性破缺模式来分类各种物相。

Result: 识别出多种物相：色反对称配对产生角动量L=3n、手征中心电荷c₋=m/2（m为奇数）的电荷-2e超导体；粒子-空穴色-谷希格斯场产生两种Z₃正交金属（单态和三重态）；U(1)²空穴子金属可在保持三角晶格空间群的同时将谷对称性降至S₃，其配对不稳定性包括有能隙的电荷-2e f-if超导体和无能隙的电荷-2e正交超导体（具有Bogoliubov费米面）。

Conclusion: 电荷-e/3的任意子气体可以直接进入超导相而不需要预先形成束缚态；讨论了从FCI到超导的化学势调控转变，指出若转变保留完整的SU(3)谷对称性，则可能需要全部九个费米子参与。

Abstract: We develop a unified framework for metallic and superconducting phases obtained by doping a fractional Chern insulator (FCI) with $C=1/3$. Starting from the parton construction $c(\mathbf r)=f_1(\mathbf r)f_2(\mathbf r)f_3(\mathbf r)$, the low-energy theory has $SU(3)_{\mathrm{gauge}}\times SU(3)_{\mathrm{valley}}$ symmetry and nine Fermi pockets formed by charge-$-e/3$ holons $ψ_{ab}$, where $a$ and $b$ label color and valley. Viewing the holons as quarks connects this problem to color superconductivity in high-energy physics. Color-antisymmetric pairing produces a class of charge-$2e$ superconductors with angular momentum $L=3n$ and chiral central charge $c_-=m/2$, where $m$ is odd. Thus a gas of charge-$e/3$ anyons can enter a superconducting phase directly without binding. Particle--hole color--valley Higgs fields instead produce two $Z_3$ orthogonal metals with one or three pockets, transforming respectively as a singlet or triplet of $SU(3)_{\mathrm{valley}}$. A $U(1)^2$ holon metal with three identical pockets can preserve the triangular-lattice space group while reducing the emergent valley symmetry down to $S_3$. Its pairing instabilities include a gapped charge $2e$ $f-if$ superconductor and a gapless charge-$2e$ orthogonal superconductor with $\langle cc\rangle=0$ and a Bogoliubov Fermi surface at $Γ$. Finally, we discuss the possibility of a chemical-potential-tuned transition from the FCI to superconductivity and argue that all nine fermions may be required if the transition preserves the full emergent $SU(3)_v$ symmetry.

</details>

### [16] [Frame Representation of the First-Order Part of the Laplace-Beltrami Operator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16425)
*A. G. Nuramatov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了定向黎曼流形（oriented Riemannian manifold）上 Laplace--Beltrami 算子一阶部分的几何内容，指出该部分相对于局部正交标架定义了一个特殊向量场。对应的一次形式确定了一个协变导数（covariant derivative），其连接分解可移除一阶部分并将其替换为一个标量势（scalar potential）。该构造依赖于标架，而局部旋转下的变换补偿了平方和部分的变化，从而保持总算子不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阐明 Laplace--Beltrami 算子一阶部分的几何含义，探讨其与标架选取、协变导数及标量势之间的内在关系。

Method: 在任意局部正交标架下，利用 Levi--Civita 联络形式（connection forms）表达一阶部分的系数，从而定义出一个特殊的向量场及其对应的一次形式；通过该一次形式构造协变导数，实现连接分解以消除一阶项并引入标量势；分析标架局部旋转下该构造的变换行为。

Result: 揭示了 Laplace--Beltrami 算子一阶部分在标架旋转下的变换规律：其变化恰好补偿平方和部分的变化，使得全算子保持不变；同时指出该构造自然地产生一个标量势。

Conclusion: 这些结果揭示了 Laplace--Beltrami 算子一阶部分的几何角色，表明其并非冗余结构，而是与标架选取和联络几何密切相关的本质组成部分。

Abstract: We investigate the geometric content of the first-order part of the Laplace--Beltrami operator on an oriented Riemannian manifold. Relative to an arbitrary local orthonormal frame, the first-order part of the Laplace--Beltrami operator defines a distinguished vector field, whose coefficients are expressed through the Levi--Civita connection forms.
  The corresponding one-form determines a covariant derivative whose connection factorization removes the first-order part of the Laplace--Beltrami operator and replaces it by a natural scalar potential.
  The construction is frame dependent. We show that its transformation under local rotations of the orthonormal frame compensates the corresponding variation of the sum-of-squares part, leaving the full Laplace--Beltrami operator invariant.
  These results reveal the geometric role of the first-order part of the Laplace--Beltrami operator.

</details>


### [17] [Approximate thermodynamics of the two-dimensional Ising model in an external magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16735)
*Mathieu Gaudreault*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对存在外磁场（external magnetic field）的二维伊辛模型（two-dimensional Ising model），通过四元数表示（quaternion representation）和小角度近似（small angle approximation），推导了自由能、磁化强度、磁化率、内能和比热等热力学量的近似解析表达式，并与BKL算法的数值模拟结果进行了比较验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 外磁场破坏了二维伊辛模型的对称性，使得自由能的精确计算变得困难。为此，本文旨在提出一种近似方法，以得到该模型在外磁场下的热力学量解析表达式。

Method: 首先将模型写成四元数表示（quaternion representation），并相对于参考系（reference frame）施加小角度近似（small angle approximation）。该近似将转移矩阵（transfer matrix）简化为中心对称矩阵（centrosymmetric matrix），其最大特征值已知且依赖于外磁场强度。进而得到自由能的近似表达式，并推导出磁化强度（magnetization）、磁化率（susceptibility）、内能（internal energy）和比热（specific heat）。

Result: 将所得到的近似表达式与采用BKL算法的数值模拟结果进行对比，发现在近似有效的区域内，二者吻合良好。

Conclusion: 本文提出的近似方法能够合理描述外磁场下二维伊辛模型的热力学行为，且在适用范围内与数值模拟结果一致。

Abstract: We introduce approximate expressions for the thermodynamics of the two-dimensional Ising model in an external magnetic field. The external field breaks the system's symmetry, which complicates the exact calculation of the free energy. To address this, we write the model in its quaternion representation to apply a small angle approximation with respect to a reference frame. The approximation simplifies the transfer matrix to a centrosymmetric matrix for which the largest eigenvalue is known and depends on the external field strength. We therefore write an approximate expression for the system's free energy and derive the magnetization, susceptibility, internal energy, and specific heat. These results are compared with numerical simulations performed with the BKL algorithm. We find that the approximate expressions and numerical simulations agree in regions where the approximation is valid.

</details>


### [18] [Subextensive Random Boundary Perturbations in the Short-Range Edwards--Anderson Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16770)
*Hexiang Wang,Keheng Zhu,Mauris Chueng*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本论文证明了在立方体边界施加随机扰动时，只要扰动能量包络（energy envelope）相对于体积可忽略（期望与几乎必然意义下），则淬火比自由能（quenched specific free energy）的极限不变；对于高维独立有限方差体无序，还证明了几乎必然的自平均性（self-averaging），并验证了若干边界条件假设的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究边界随机扰动对近邻 Edwards–Anderson Ising 模型（nearest-neighbor Edwards–Anderson Ising model）淬火比自由能极限行为的影响，以及体无序（bulk disorder）条件下自平均性是否成立。

Method: 采用能量包络方法（energy envelope argument），结合期望与几乎必然（almost surely）两种收敛意义下的比较，并利用 Efron–Stein 估计（Efron–Stein estimate）证明高维独立有限方差无序下的自平均性。理论分析涵盖 i.i.d. 标量表面场、固定随机外自旋（fixed random exterior spins）以及周期缠绕键（periodic wrap-around bonds）等边界条件。

Result: 任意能量包络相对于体积可忽略的边界扰动不改变淬火比自由能的极限；在维度至少为 2 的独立有限方差体无序下，沿完整盒子序列的几乎必然自平均性成立；淬火期望的比较给出 $ O(L^{-1}) $ 的收敛阶。

Conclusion: 边界随机扰动对淬火比自由能极限无影响，且高维体无序满足自平均性。但该结论仅限于比自由能，不涉及有限体积 Gibbs 测度（finite-volume Gibbs measures）的收敛性。

Abstract: We consider the nearest-neighbor Edwards--Anderson Ising model on cubic boxes with random perturbations supported at the boundary. We prove that any perturbation admitting an energy envelope that is negligible compared with the volume, both in expectation and almost surely, leaves the limiting quenched specific free energy unchanged. For independent finite-variance bulk disorder in dimension at least two, an Efron--Stein estimate also yields almost-sure self-averaging along the full sequence of boxes. The hypotheses are verified for i.i.d. scalar surface fields, fixed random exterior spins, and periodic wrap-around bonds, with an $ O(L^{-1}) $ comparison of quenched means. The result concerns the specific free energy and does not assert convergence of finite-volume Gibbs measures.

</details>


### [19] [The Lee-Yang property of the Blume-Capel model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16958)
*Yuri Kozitsky,Yurij Holovatch*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了Blume-Capel模型中的Lee-Yang性质（Lee-Yang property），证明了即使单自旋配分函数（single-spin partition function）不满足该性质，铁磁相互作用（ferromagnetic interaction）仍可诱导该性质的出现，这是首次报道此类结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lee-Yang理论为理解铁磁Ising模型中的相变（phase transitions）和临界现象（critical phenomena）提供了有力工具，但其应用常被扩展到该定理有效性尚未被证明的模型中。Blume-Capel模型因各向异性项（anisotropy term）的存在，在参数βΔ > ln 2时单自旋配分函数不满足Lee-Yang性质，需要检验铁磁相互作用能否弥补这一缺失。

Method: 基于E. H. Lieb与A. D. Sokal（1981）提出的定理，即铁磁模型中Lee-Yang定理的成立可由单自旋配分函数是否具有该性质来保证。本文通过分析Blume-Capel模型中铁磁相互作用对整体配分函数的影响，考察在单自旋性质失效的参数区域（βΔ > ln 2）中，相互作用能否诱导出Lee-Yang性质。

Result: 研究结果表明，对于Blume-Capel模型，即使单自旋配分函数在βΔ > ln 2时失去Lee-Yang性质，铁磁相互作用本身仍可诱导该性质的成立。据作者所知，这是首次获得此类结果。

Conclusion: 铁磁相互作用可以弥补单自旋配分函数中Lee-Yang性质的缺失，使得Blume-Capel模型在更大参数范围内仍具有Lee-Yang性质，这一发现拓展了Lee-Yang理论的适用范围。

Abstract: The Lee-Yang theory is based on the theorem concerning a property of the ferromagnetic Ising model partition function proved by T. D. Lee and C. N. Yang in 1952. It provides powerful tools for understanding the very nature of phase transitions and critical phenomena in various spin and similar models. Sometimes, this theory is applied to models for which the theorem's validity has not been proved. By the main result of E. H. Lieb and A. D. Sokal, Commun. Math. Phys. 80, 153 (1981), for a given ferromagnetic model, this validity is guaranteed by the same property of the single-spin partition function. Due to the anisotropy term $\sum_i ΔS_i^2$, the single-spin partition function of the Blume-Capel model fails to have the Lee-Yang property for $βΔ> \ln 2$. In this article, we show that the ferromagnetic interaction in such a model can induce the Lee-Yang property, even for these values of $βΔ$. To the best of our knowledge, it is the first result of this kind.

</details>


### [20] [Stochastic stability of master-slave synchronization for dissipative PDEs with Burgers-type nonlinearity and application to data assimilation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17002)
*Joaquín Miguez,Inés P. Mariño*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类包含 Burgers、Kuramoto–Sivashinsky 等非线性耗散发展方程（nonlinear dissipative evolution equations）在 master–slave 同步框架下的随机稳定性（stochastic stability），在观测噪声下推导了同步误差的有限时间与时间一致均方界及尾概率估计，并将其解释为基于同步的数据同化方案（data-assimilation scheme），与集合卡尔曼–布西滤波器（ensemble Kalman–Bucy filter）进行了对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解带对流非线性和多项式线性微分算子的一类非线性耗散系统在观测噪声下的同步行为，并建立严格的随机稳定性理论，为同步（synchronization）在数据同化中的应用提供理论基础。

Method: 在周期性边界条件下对系统进行有限维傅里叶截断（finite-dimensional Fourier truncation），建立 master–slave 耦合模型；在确定性情形下通过耦合强度条件证明局部指数稳定性（local exponential stability）；引入观测噪声（observational noise）将 slave 系统转化为伊藤扩散（Itô diffusion），在傅里叶空间中推导偏差量的均方界和尾概率估计，并利用帕塞瓦尔关系（Parseval's relation）转换回物理空间。

Result: 在对耦合强度施加简单条件时，确定性同步流形（synchronization manifold）具有局部指数稳定性；在噪声干扰下，随机同步误差与确定性参考误差之间的偏差满足有限时间 $\mathcal{O}(\sigma^2)$ 均方界及相应的尾概率估计；在全局单边耗散性（one-sided dissipativity）假设下，进一步得到时间一致的 $\mathcal{O}(\sigma^2)$ 界。

Conclusion: 本文为带有 Burgers 型对流非线性的一类耗散发展方程建立了随机同步的定量稳定性理论，揭示了预设稳定性增益与基于协方差自适应增益（如集合卡尔曼–布西滤波器）之间的结构差异，为该类系统在噪声环境下基于同步的数据同化提供了理论保证。

Abstract: We investigate the stochastic stability of master--slave synchronization for a class of nonlinear dissipative evolution equations with a Burgers-type convective nonlinearity and a polynomial linear differential operator. The family includes the Burgers, Kuramoto--Sivashinsky, Kawahara, Benney--Lin, and Nikolaevskiy equations. Under periodic boundary conditions, each equation is represented through a finite-dimensional Fourier truncation, yielding a complex state vector coupled to a slave system driven by observations of the master. We first establish local exponential stability of the deterministic synchronization manifold under a simple condition on the coupling strength. We then introduce observational noise in the coupling signals, which transforms the slave system into an Itô diffusion and prevents exact synchronization. Our analysis focuses on the deviation $Δ(t)$ between the stochastic synchronization error and the exponentially stable deterministic reference error. We prove an $\mathcal{O}(σ^2)$ finite-time mean-square bound on $\|Δ(t)\|^2$, together with a corresponding tail-probability estimate. Under a global one-sided dissipativity assumption, the localization is removed and an $\mathcal{O}(σ^2)$ time-uniform bound is obtained. These estimates are derived in Fourier space and translated to physical space via Parseval's relation. Finally, we interpret the stochastic slave dynamics as a continuous-time synchronization-based data-assimilation scheme and compare its structure with the ensemble Kalman--Bucy filter, emphasizing the difference between prescribed stability-oriented and adaptive covariance-based gains.

</details>


### [21] [The de Sitter Scalar Discrete Series: Gupta-Bleuler Structure and Holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17124)
*Maryam Bajalan,Jean-Pierre Gazeau,Hamed Pejhan*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了de Sitter群SO₀(1,4)的标量离散序列幺正不可约表示Π_{p,0} (p=1,2,…)在dS双曲面上具有dS协变的Krein实现，该实现组织为Gupta-Bleuler三重态结构，并通过Fourier型体-边变换建立了体区域与共形边界上的物理扇区之间的一一对应关系，同时保持了反射正定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: de Sitter(dS)时空上的量子场论中存在规范冗余和不定范数结构，这些结构如何与dS群的离散序列幺正不可约表示(UIRs)兼容，以及体-边对应的具体实现机制尚不清楚。本文旨在揭示这些表示在体区域和共形边界上的具体实现方式及其联系。

Method: 采用Krein空间方法，在dS超曲面上构造dS协变的Klein-Gordon(KG)半双线性型，分析其退化性和零化子(radical)，从而得到Gupta-Bleuler三重态。进一步引入Fourier型体-边变换(bulk-boundary transform)，建立体区域与未来/过去共形边界(ℐ^±)上的实现之间的dS协变对应。

Result: 离散序列UIR Π_{p,0}在体区域中自然组织为Gupta-Bleuler三重态，其正范数扇区和负范数扇区存在于Krein空间中，零范数扇区仅出现在中间阶段。体区域的负范数扇区无法独立存在于边界上，但边界实现保留了来自体区域的物理和规范结构。边界模仍然是不可分解的(indecomposable)，其物理商空间承载离散序列表示Π_{p,0}。对径对称性(antipodal symmetry)保证了ℐ^+和ℐ^-上实现的一致性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了dS体区域与共形边界上离散序列表示Π_{p,0}之间的精确一一对应，这种对应通过Fourier型体-边变换实现并保持反射正定性(reflection positivity)，为dS时空中的体-边对应(Bulk-boundary correspondence)提供了严格数学框架。

Abstract: We show that scalar discrete-series unitary irreducible representations (UIRs) $Π_{p,0}$ ($p=1,2,\cdots$) of the de Sitter (dS) group $\mathrm{SO}_0(1,4)$ admit a dS-covariant Krein realization on the dS hyperboloid, endowed with a dS-invariant non-degenerate Klein-Gordon (KG) sesquilinear form, in which the group action is indecomposable and organizes naturally into a Gupta-Bleuler triplet. The positive- and negative-norm sectors are already present in the underlying Krein space, whereas a null sector emerges only at an intermediate stage, where the induced KG form becomes degenerate and its radical leads canonically to the physical quotient carrying the UIR $Π_{p,0}$. We further show that suitable limits of the bulk theory at the ``future'' and ``past'' conformal boundaries ${\mathcal{I}}^\pm$ give rise to dS-invariant boundary realizations endowed with induced kernel inner products. While the bulk negative-norm sector admits no independent boundary counterpart, the boundary realization retains the physical and gauge structures inherited from the bulk. The resulting boundary module nevertheless remains indecomposable, with its physical quotient carrying the discrete-series representation $Π_{p,0}$. The antipodal symmetry provides a natural relation between the realizations on ${\mathcal{I}}^+$ and ${\mathcal{I}}^-$, ensuring the consistency of the boundary construction and its geometric interpretation. At the heart of the analysis lies a Fourier-type bulk-boundary transform that provides a dS-covariant identification of the bulk and boundary physical sectors, establishing a one-to-one intertwining correspondence between the bulk and boundary realizations of $Π_{p,0}$ while preserving reflection positivity.

</details>


### [22] [Moving Collinear Cracks in a Prestressed Dry Sandy Medium Fracture Response under Traveling Punch Loads](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17155)
*Diksha,Soniya Chaudhary,Pawan Kumar Sharma*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了受初始应力作用的干砂介质中两个移动共线Griffith裂纹在集中裂纹面载荷与移动冲头压力下的动态断裂行为。通过移动坐标系、Fourier积分变换和Hilbert变换，解析求解了耦合Cauchy型奇异积分方程，获得了裂纹密度函数、I型应力强度因子和裂纹张开位移的闭式表达式，揭示了裂纹速度、几何形状、初始应力、砂质含量和移动冲头载荷对裂纹尖端强化的联合影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的断裂力学研究较少同时考虑初始应力（initial stress）、砂质介质（sandy medium）特性和移动载荷（moving load）对动态裂纹扩展行为的耦合影响。本研究旨在建立解析框架，系统分析这些因素对共线Griffith裂纹动态断裂的作用机制。

Method: 采用移动坐标系将瞬态问题转化为稳态问题；将初始应力和砂质影响纳入控制方程；利用Fourier积分变换得到特征方程和变换后的牵引-位移关系；借助裂纹面、对称性和外表面条件将问题简化为耦合Cauchy型奇异积分方程；对于足够厚的条带，发展渐近核简化方法，并利用有限Hilbert变换（finite Hilbert transform）解析求解。

Result: 推导了裂纹密度函数（crack density function）、内尖端和外尖端处的I型应力强度因子（Mode I stress intensity factor）以及裂纹张开位移（crack opening displacement）的闭式表达式。从一般公式中恢复出多个极限情况，提供了分析一致性检验。结果展示了裂纹速度、裂纹几何、初始应力、砂质含量和移动冲头载荷对裂纹尖端强化和裂纹张开的联合影响。

Conclusion: 本文提出的解析框架为涉及干砂介质中移动载荷的断裂评估和工程设计提供了有用见解，适用于交通基础设施、岩土系统、地下开挖及其他工程结构的设计与分析。

Abstract: The dynamic fracture behaviour of two moving collinear Griffith cracks in an initially stressed dry sandy medium subjected to concentrated crack-face loading and moving punch pressure is investigated. A moving coordinate system transforms the transient problem into a steady state formulation, while the effects of initial stress and sandiness are incorporated into the governing equations. Fourier integral transforms are employed to obtain the characteristic equation and the transformed traction displacement relations. The crack face, symmetry, and outer surface conditions reduce the problem to coupled Cauchy type singular integral equations. For a sufficiently thick strip, an asymptotic kernel reduction is developed, and the resulting equations are solved analytically using the finite Hilbert transform. Closed form expressions are derived for the crack density functions, Mode I stress intensity factors at the inner and outer crack tips, and the crack opening displacement. Several limiting cases are recovered from the general formulation, providing analytical consistency checks. The results demonstrate the combined influence of crack speed, crack geometry, initial stress, sandiness, and moving punch loading on crack tip intensification and crack opening. The proposed analytical framework provides useful insights for fracture assessment and the design of transportation infrastructure, geotechnical systems, underground excavations, and other engineering structures involving dry sandy media subjected to moving loads.

### [23] [Fouling maps and polynomial first integrals from symmetric tensor fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17407)
*Rafael Azuaje,Juan Carlos Marrero,Edith Padrón*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在余切丛上时间无关哈密顿力学的框架下，提出了“fouling映射”作为非可逆变体的概念，发展了一种构造多项式fouling映射的张量方法，并证明该类映射可生成在哈密顿流下不变的(1,1)-张量场，其幂次迹为多项式运动常数。针对半黎曼位形空间上的机械哈密顿函数，完整刻画了由对称张量场诱导的多项式丛映射及其成为fouling映射的条件，并以欧氏平面和二维球面为例进行了展示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在经典力学中，fouling变换（保持位形坐标的准正则变换）是可逆的；将其推广到非可逆情形（fouling映射），以拓展运动常数（constants of motion）的生成机制和对称性分析的工具。

Method: 在余切丛（cotangent bundle）$T^*Q$上，基于时间无关哈密顿力学（time-independent Hamiltonian mechanics）框架，引入非可逆的fouling映射。采用张量方法（tensorial method）构造多项式fouling映射，并利用其诱导的(1,1)-张量场的幂次迹来生成多项式运动常数。对机械哈密顿函数（mechanical Hamiltonian function）情形，使用对称$(k+1,0)$-张量场完整刻画多项式丛映射（polynomial bundle maps）及其fouling性质。

Result: 每个多项式fouling映射诱导一个在哈密顿流（Hamiltonian flow）下不变的(1,1)-张量场，其各幂次迹给出多项式运动常数。在半黎曼位形空间（semi-Riemannian configuration space）上，完全表征了由对称$(k+1,0)$-张量场诱导的多项式丛映射成为fouling映射的条件，并在欧氏平面和二维球面上给出了具体构造实例。

Conclusion: fouling映射作为非可逆变换，为在哈密顿力学中构造多项式运动常数提供了新途径，且可借助对称张量场进行系统刻画。该方法在欧氏平面和二维球面上的实例验证了其有效性。

Abstract: Under the framework of time-independent Hamiltonian mechanics on the cotangent bundles $T^*Q$ of the configuration spaces $Q$ of mechanical systems, we introduce the concept of fouling map as a non-invertible generalization of the so-called fouling transformations --canonoid transformations preserving configuration coordinates--. We develop a tensorial method for constructing polynomial fouling maps. We show that each such map induces a $(1,1)$-tensor field invariant under the Hamiltonian flow, whose traces of its powers are polynomial constants of motion. For mechanical Hamiltonian functions --the kinetic energy plus the potential energy on a semi-Riemannian configuration space $(Q,g)$--, we completely characterize polynomial bundle maps arising from symmetric $(k+1,0)$-tensor fields and derive the conditions ensuring their fouling nature. Several explicit examples on the Euclidean plane and on the 2-sphere illustrate the method.

### [24] [Baxter Q-operators from a Schwinger-Boson construction of the master T-operator and the mKP hierarchy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17642)
*Zengo Tsuboi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对有理非齐次 gl(M) 自旋链，通过在辅助福克空间（Fock space）上定义主 T-算子（master T-operator），将其与修正 KP 方程族的 tau 函数联系起来，并利用 Howe 对偶（Howe duality）复现了 Schur 函数展开。该实现将两种不同构造的 Baxter Q-算子统一起来：一种通过 Miwa 变量留数得到，另一种通过退化 Yangian L-算子得到。文章还展示了通过归一化极限和 Holstein–Primakoff 型收缩，从主 T-算子导出了退化 Yangian L-算子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主 T-算子（master T-operator）是转移矩阵的生成函数，也是修正 KP 方程族（modified KP hierarchy）的 tau 函数。传统上它通过 Schur 函数展开引入，其系数满足 Cherednik–Bazhanov–Reshetikhin 行列式公式。本文旨在为有理非齐次 gl(M) 自旋链（rational inhomogeneous gl(M) spin chains）提供一种替代定义，并通过该定义统一已有的两种 Baxter Q-算子构造方法。

Method: 在辅助福克空间（Fock space）上实现 gl(M)，该空间由有限族 Schwinger 玻色子（Schwinger bosons）生成；从所得 L-算子构造单值矩阵（monodromy matrix），并将其在该福克空间上的迹定义为主 T-算子（master T-operator）。利用 Howe 对偶（Howe duality）复现 Schur 函数展开。通过两种极限过程从主 T-算子导出退化 Yangian L-算子：一是在 Miwa 变量趋近边界扭特征值倒数时进行归一化极限以保留最高阶极点项；二是对具有固定总占据数的子空间进行 Holstein–Primakoff 型大占据数收缩。

Result: 该实现将两种 Baxter Q-算子的构造联系起来：一种来自主 T-算子关于选定 Miwa 变量（Miwa variables）的留数；另一种使用退化 Yangian L-算子（degenerate Yangian L-operator）的振子形式。在归一化极限下，主 T-算子的迹给出对应的 Q-算子的显式留数公式。同时，Holstein–Primakoff 型大占据数收缩也得到相同的退化 Yangian L-算子。

Conclusion: 本文提供的主 T-算子新定义不仅统一了两种 Baxter Q-算子的构造路径，还通过两种不同极限过程（留数极限与大占据数收缩）得到了同一退化 Yangian L-算子，揭示了其中内在的结构一致性。

Abstract: The master T-operator is a generating function for transfer matrices and a tau-function of the modified KP (mKP) hierarchy. It is conventionally introduced through a Schur-function expansion whose coefficients are fused transfer matrices satisfying the Cherednik--Bazhanov--Reshetikhin determinant formula. For rational inhomogeneous gl(M) spin chains, we give an alternative definition: we realize gl(M) on an auxiliary Fock space generated by finitely many families of Schwinger bosons, form a monodromy matrix from the resulting L-operator, and define the master T-operator as its trace over the Fock space. Howe duality then reproduces the Schur-function expansion. This realization relates two constructions of Baxter Q-operators. In the construction of [arXiv:1112.3310] (see also [arXiv:1010.4022]), the Q-operators are obtained from residues of the master T-operator with respect to selected Miwa variables. In the construction of [arXiv:1010.3699], they are defined using degenerate Yangian L-operators in oscillator form. When selected Miwa variables approach the inverses of boundary-twist eigenvalues, the defining trace develops poles. After a suitable rescaling of this L-operator, only the terms contributing to the highest-order pole survive in the normalized limit; before the trace is taken, they form the degenerate Yangian L-operator of the second construction. The trace then gives an explicit residue formula for the corresponding Q-operator. Independently, a Holstein--Primakoff-type large-occupation-number contraction of this L-operator on subspaces with fixed total occupation numbers yields the same degenerate Yangian L-operator.

### [25] [Universal Correlators on Exponentially Ramified Spectral Curves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17711)
*Mohamad Alameddine,Alexander Hock*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究在带有指数奇点（exponential singularities）或更一般本性奇点（essential singularities）的紧致谱曲线（compact spectral curves）上的广义拓扑递归（generalized topological recursion），通过围道变形将本性奇点的贡献转化为亚纯点（meromorphic points）上的留数，从而建立统一的递归框架，并展示其作为Bouchard-Eynard高阶拓扑递归极限情形的视图及若干实例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有广义拓扑递归主要适用于具有多项式型或亚纯型奇点的谱曲线，而带有指数型或本性奇点的谱曲线（如指数奇异曲线）缺乏自然的递归框架。作者旨在填补这一空白，将广义拓扑递归推广到此类更一般的奇点情形。

Method: 利用广义拓扑递归的全局表述（global formulation），对递归留数公式（recursive residue formula）进行围道变形（contour deformation），将本性奇点处的贡献替换为亚纯点上的留数。该方法也可视为Bouchard-Eynard高阶拓扑递归（higher-order topological recursion）在分歧点（ramification point）阶数趋于无穷时的收敛极限。

Result: 建立了适用于指数分支谱曲线的自然递归框架，完全在广义拓扑递归形式体系内运作。通过多个实例进行了验证，包括超越函数（transcendental functions）和Mirzakhani曲线的$x$-$y$对偶（dual）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的框架成功将广义拓扑递归扩展到具有指数型和本性奇点的谱曲线，并展示了与已有高阶拓扑递归的极限联系，为处理此类奇异曲线提供了统一的递归工具。

Abstract: We investigate generalized topological recursion on compact spectral curves admitting exponential, and more generally essential, singularities as ramification points. Exploiting the global formulation of generalized topological recursion, we establish a contour deformation of the recursive residue formula that replaces contributions from these essential singularities by residues at meromorphic points. This provides a natural recursive framework for exponentially ramified spectral curves while remaining entirely within the generalized topological recursion formalism. Our formalism can also be viewed as a limiting case of the Bouchard-Eynard higher-order topological recursion, obtained when the order of a ramification point tends to infinity in a convergent manner, as occurs, for example, for exponential singularities while $dy$ remains regular and non-vanishing. We further illustrate the resulting formalism through several examples, including transcendental functions and the $x$-$y$ dual of the Mirzakhani curve.

Method: 建立了一个耦合PFO动力学与Sips等温线的柱吸附模型，并采用行波近似（traveling wave approximation）推导出特定操作条件下的解析解。随后，利用来自文献的多样化实验数据集对解析解进行验证。

Abstract: We present a column adsorption model that couples a Pseudo-First-Order (PFO) kinetic formulation with the Sips isotherm framework. Using a traveling wave approximation, we derive analytical solutions for specific operating conditions. Qualitatively, these solutions deviate significantly from their pure Sips counterparts: instead of a smooth, continuous increase in concentration at the column outlet, the PFO-Sips model predicts an abrupt, sudden breakthrough. We validate these analytical solutions against diverse experimental datasets from the literature. The results reveal that the PFO-based model consistently underperforms compared to the original Sips formulation. Furthermore, this validation exposes fundamental inconsistencies within the PFO framework. We demonstrate that despite its widespread use in the literature for almost a century, the PFO model is inherently flawed and structurally unfit for describing column adsorption dynamics.

Method: 沿用Iorgov--Lisovyy--Teschner的方法框架，利用(1,k) Virasoro 模型的共形块构造（修正）Riemann--Hilbert问题的解。针对k=2情形，在三点情况下显式构造解，并通过合适的初始数据条件（initial data conditions）证明其唯一性。

Conclusion: 本文扩展了Iorgov--Lisovyy--Teschner方法至k>1情形，以k=2为例解决了Riemann--Hilbert问题解的非唯一性问题，并揭示了与c=-2中心荷及辛费米子相关的新的数学结构（双线性关系）。

We specifically study the $k=2$ case, which corresponds to the central charge $c=-2$ and symplectic fermions. We explicitly construct a corresponding solution of the modified Riemann--Hilbert problem in the case of 3 punctures and prove its uniqueness under suitable initial data conditions. We also obtain new bilinear relations for $c=-2$ tau functions.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将信息论定义的熵产生率（相对熵）与经典热力学公式（Clausius关系）在非平衡统计力学框架下建立严格联系，并发展一种适用于腔室化系统的模组化分析方法，以实现对复杂非平衡系统的解析求解。

Method: 首先将平稳熵产生率定义为前向与时间反演路径测度之间的相对熵；在互易性（reciprocity）假设下引入温度，证明该信息论定义约化为经典热力学公式（随机Clausius关系）。进而对腔室化系统进行模组化分析，每个开放腔室由其散射算子（scattering operator）和驻留统计量表征；腔室入口状态序列构成马尔可夫链（Markov chain），利用更新-报酬定理（renewal-reward theorem）将各腔室贡献组装为全局熵产生率。

Result: 通过广义Maxwell-Smoluchowski散射算子（由温度、部分热适应系数、势垒高度和孔隙率系数定义）的系列示例验证了框架。对于全热适应下的三腔循环系统（两个不同温度的腔壁加一个势垒），推导出熵产生率和净概率环流的闭式表达式，揭示了类似于热蒸腾（thermal transpiration）的热棘轮效应（thermal ratchet effect）。

Conclusion: 该模组化框架成功将信息论的熵产生定义与经典热力学联系起来，并为腔室化非平衡系统提供了可解析求解的分析工具；热棘轮效应的发现表明该框架可用于研究非平衡输运中的定向流现象。

Abstract: We investigate entropy production and nonequilibrium transport in a class of random dynamical systems modeling a Knudsen gas confined to a compartmented container. The system consists of a single particle undergoing random billiard motion, with collisions leading to random reflection or transmission through semi-reflecting, compartment-separating walls.
  The stationary entropy production rate is first expressed as the relative entropy between forward and time-reversed path measures. Under a reciprocity assumption, used to introduce temperature into the general random billiard system, it is shown how this information-theoretic definition reduces to the classical thermodynamic formula: the mean energy transferred to the walls divided by their local temperatures, a stochastic Clausius relation. We then develop a modular analysis of compartmented systems. Each open compartment is characterized by a compartment scattering operator and its sojourn statistics. The sequence of compartment entrance states defines a Markov chain whose stationary distribution is used in a renewal-reward theorem to assemble the compartment contributions into the global entropy production rate.
  The framework is illustrated with a series of examples of increasing complexity governed by a generalized Maxwell-Smoluchowski scattering operator and amenable to detailed and explicit analysis. Such operators are defined by a few parameters: temperature, a partial thermal accommodation, the height of potential barriers, and a porosity coefficient. The central example is a cyclic three-compartment system consisting of two thermal walls at different temperatures and a potential barrier. For full thermal accommodation we obtain closed-form expressions for the entropy production rate and net probability circulation around the cycle, revealing a thermal ratchet effect analogous to thermal transpiration.

</details>

### [29] [Observability of Finite-Depth Double-Diffusive Exchange from Sparse Temperature-Salinity Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16272)
*Sriram P. Kalathoor*

Main category: physics.geo-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过将四个有限深度双扩散交换历史作为已知真实场，模拟垂直剖面、剖面束、垂直粗化、Argo式和断面式等多种观测格式的采样过程，并与实际观测产品对比，发现孤立剖面难以识别双扩散交换路径（路径族准确率约0.53–0.56），而多剖面束能显著提升识别能力（四剖面束路径族准确率达0.994），表明有效观测单位应为剖面束或断面而非孤立剖面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双扩散界面（double-diffusive interfaces）支持的交换历史具有空间组织性但观测稀疏。实际观测产品通常提供剖面、重复观测、自动浮标记录或水文断面，而高分辨率三维数值计算揭示了标量梯度展宽、保持紧凑、与有限深度层远程连接或水平组织化等路径特征。本研究旨在回答：在测量降采样后，有限深度双扩散交换中哪些与路径相关的特征仍然可被观测到。

Method: 将四个受控的有限深度交换历史作为已知真实场（known truth fields），分别采用垂直剖面、剖面束、垂直粗化、Argo式和断面式五种观测格式进行采样。将得到的模拟观测数据与冰基剖面仪（Ice-Tethered Profiler）、Argo以及CCHDO/GO-SHIP的实际观测产品进行对比，将模拟测量置于现实的观测背景中。

Result: 孤立剖面识别能力较弱：严格案例准确率低于0.48，留一法剖面分类中路径族准确率约0.53–0.56，36个剖面中有22个更接近不同路径的剖面而非同路径剖面。剖面束则包含更多信息：在剖面束枚举框架下，单剖面的晚期路径族基线为0.694，而二、三、四剖面束的路径族准确率分别达到0.917、0.961和0.994。垂直粗化采样可保留宽尺度路径分离但扭曲局部界面宽度估计，断面采样仅在测站间距能解析相关模态时提供水平尺度信息。

Conclusion: 对于隐藏的有限深度双扩散交换，有用的观测单位（observing unit）是剖面束或断面，而非孤立剖面。

Abstract: Double-diffusive interfaces can support exchange histories that are spatially organized but only sparsely observed. A resolved three-dimensional calculation contains the route by which scalar gradients broaden, remain compact, connect with remote parts of a finite-depth layer, or organize horizontally, whereas field products usually provide profiles, repeated casts, autonomous-float records, or hydrographic sections. We ask which route-relevant features of finite-depth double-diffusive exchange remain observable after that measurement reduction. Four controlled finite-depth exchange histories are treated as known truth fields and sampled with vertical-profile, profile-bundle, vertical-coarsening, Argo-style, and section-like observing formats. The resulting observables are compared with selected Ice-Tethered Profiler, Argo, and CCHDO/GO-SHIP products to place the synthetic measurements in realistic observing contexts. Isolated profiles are weak route identifiers: at the final comparison time, strict case accuracy remains below 0.48, route-family accuracy is about 0.53--0.56 in leave-one-out profile classification, and 22 of 36 profiles are closer to a different-route profile than to a same-route profile under the current feature set. Profile bundles are substantially more informative. In the bundle-enumeration framework, the one-profile late-time route-family baseline is 0.694, while two-, three-, and four-profile bundles reach route-family accuracies of 0.917, 0.961, and 0.994. Coarse vertical sampling can preserve broad route separation while distorting local interface-width estimates, and section-like sampling adds horizontal-scale information only when station spacing resolves the relevant mode. The useful observing unit for hidden finite-depth double-diffusive exchange is therefore an ensemble or section, not an isolated cast.

### [30] [Simulating neural network criticality and resource dynamics with Rydberg gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16368)
*Patrick Mischke,Herwig Ott,Michael Fleischhauer,Thomas Niederprüm*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用超冷里德伯气体（ultracold Rydberg gas）作为高度可控的模拟平台，实验探索了神经网络临界性（neural network criticality），验证了激发雪崩（excitation avalanches）的幂律标度、普适雪崩形状坍塌（universal avalanche shape collapse）等临界判据，并通过受控增益机制实现非平衡稳态，观察到临界点处的时间关联峰值及活跃相中的随机振荡与“龙王雪崩”（dragon king avalanches）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经网络的高效运行被认为与其非平衡激发动力学中的临界性（criticality）有关，但由于生物系统中控制手段有限且采样不足，实验验证这一猜想面临困难。因此，作者希望利用一个高度可控的物理模拟平台来实验检验神经网络临界性的关键特征。

Method: 作者采用超冷里德伯气体作为可调控模拟器，利用里德伯 facilitation 实现的激发扩散来类比神经元放电活动的突触连接，从而构建表现出吸收相（absorbing phase）与活跃相（active phase）的非平衡系统。同时，引入受控增益机制补偿原子损失，模拟代谢资源补充，使系统维持在可控的非平衡稳态。

Result: 实验系统地解析了临界性判据，观察到激发雪崩的幂律标度以及普适雪崩形状坍塌。在临界点处检测到峰值时间关联，并在活跃相中发现随机振荡与“龙王雪崩”现象。这些结果与关于系统绕行临界性（orbiting criticality）的理论预测一致。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了 facilitated 里德伯气体作为研究神经网络临界性、资源动力学（resource dynamics）以及涌现振荡（emergent oscillations）的实验平台，为理解神经网络中的临界行为提供了新的可操控的物理模拟途径。

Abstract: Efficient operation of neural networks has been linked to criticality in their underlying non-equilibrium excitation dynamics. However, obtaining experimental evidence of this conjecture remains challenging due to limited control and undersampling in biological systems. Here, we experimentally explore neural network criticality using an ultracold Rydberg gas as a highly controllable simulator. We highlight the similarity of the excitation spreading via Rydberg facilitation and the synaptic connection of spiking activity of neurons, giving rise to distinct absorbing and active phases. We systematically explore and resolve criticality criteria, including power-law scaling of excitation avalanches and the emergence of universal avalanche shape collapse. Crucially, we implement a controlled gain mechanism to compensate for atom loss, mimicking metabolic resource replenishment and stabilizing the system in a controlled non-equilibrium steady state. We find peak temporal correlations at the critical point and stochastic oscillations with dragon king avalanches in the active phase, consistent with predictions for systems orbiting criticality. Our work establishes facilitated Rydberg gases as a platform for investigating criticality, resource dynamics, and emergent oscillations in neural networks.

### [31] [Repeated differentiation of deterministic polynomials with asymptotically radial root distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16954)
*Brian C. Hall,Daniel Perales*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文简化并推广了 Galligo、Najnudel 和 Vu 等人关于多项式重复微分后根分布收敛性的证明，将结果从重复微分推广至微分算子 $z^a(d/dz)^b$ 的重复作用，并补充了当 $m$ 固定、$n$ 趋于无穷时极限根分布的计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Galligo、Najnudel 和 Vu 等人（2025–2026）证明了当 $m\gg \log(n)$ 且 $P(z)=p(z^m)$ 的根分布收敛于径向概率测度时，其 $\lfloor nmt\rfloor$ 阶导数的根分布也收敛到由径向分位数函数（radial quantile function）显式给出的 $μ_t$。本文旨在给出该结果的简化证明，并将其推广至更一般的微分算子 $z^a(d/dz)^b$。

Method: 作者通过显著简化的论证重新证明已有结果，并利用算子 $z^a(d/dz)^b$ 的代数结构，将重复微分情形推广为该算子的重复作用。此外，作者还独立处理了 $m$ 固定、$n$ 趋于无穷的极限情形，给出了相应的极限根分布。

Result: 本文得到了原定理的简化证明，并将结论从重复微分算子 $d/dz$ 推广至更一般的微分算子 $z^a(d/dz)^b$。同时，在 $m$ 固定、$n$ 趋于无穷的设定下，计算了极限根分布的显式形式。

Conclusion: 本文的工作一方面降低了原证明的复杂度，另一方面拓展了结果的适用范围，为理解一般微分算子作用下多项式的根分布演化提供了更简洁且更通用的分析框架。

Abstract: Recent works of Galligo, Najnudel, and Vu (2025) and Najnudel and Vu (2026) study repeated differentiation for polynomials of the form $P(z)=p(z^m)$, where $p$ is a deterministic polynomial of degree $n$ with real, non-negative roots, in the regime where $m$ and $n$ are large. If $m\gg \log(n)$ and the root distribution of $P$ converges to a compactly supported, radial probability measure $μ_0$, these works show that for $0\le t<1$, the root distribution of the $\lfloor nmt\rfloor$-th derivative of $P$ converges to a compactly supported probability measure $μ_t$ given by an explicit formula for its radial quantile function.
  We give a substantially simplified proof of this result and also extend the result from repeated differentiation to repeated applications of the differential operator $z^a(d/dz)^b$. We also compute the limiting root distribution in the case when $m$ is fixed and $n$ tends to infinity.

### [32] [Optimal Covariance Estimates for Schrödinger Semigroups with White Noise in $d=1,2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17393)
*Youssef Djellouli,Pierre Yves Gaudreau Lamarre*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文针对 d=1,2 维空间中带有高斯白噪声（Gaussian white noise）和幂律增长确定性势能（deterministic potential）的随机薛定谔算子（random Schrödinger operator），利用费曼-卡茨公式（Feynman-Kac formula）给出了薛定谔半群迹的协方差在短时极限下的最优渐近上下界，并据此证明了迹的定量超均匀性（hyperuniformity）性质与去相关速率（decorrelation rate）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前在 d=1 情形下对随机薛定谔算子半群迹的协方差估计不够精确，且在 d=2 情形下尚无同类结果。本文旨在填补这一空白，给出最优的渐近上下界，并进一步揭示迹的短时关联衰减行为。

Method: 采用费曼-卡茨公式（Feynman-Kac formula）将薛定谔半群迹 $\mathrm{Tr}[e^{-sH}]$ 的协方差表达为布朗桥局部时（Brownian bridge local times）的泛函，通过对该局部时的精细估计导出协方差的渐近上下界。

Result: 在 d=1 情形下显著改进了已知的协方差上界；在 d=2 情形下首次获得了同类最优渐近估计。作为应用，推导了迹在 $s,t\to0$ 时的定量超均匀性性质与去相关速率。

Conclusion: 本文建立的协方差渐近估计为 d=1,2 维随机薛定谔算子提供了短时关联结构的精确刻画，并展示了其在超均匀性和去相关性分析中的应用价值。

Abstract: For $d\in\{1,2\}$, let $H=-\frac{1}{2}Δ+ V +ξ$ be the random Schrödinger operator on $L^2(\mathbb{R}^d)$ where $ξ$ is a standard Gaussian white noise and $V$ is a deterministic potential with power-law growth at infinity. Using a Feynman-Kac formula for the trace of the Schrödinger semigroup, we give optimal asymptotic upper and lower bounds on the covariance of $\mathrm{Tr}[e^{-sH}]$ and $\mathrm{Tr}[e^{-tH}]$ as $s,t\to0$ through estimates on Brownian bridge local times. These estimates are a significant improvement on previous bounds in the case $d=1$ and are the first of their kind for $d=2$. As an application of these new estimates, we prove a quantitative hyperuniformity-type property and decorrelation rate for the trace as $s,t\to0$.

### [33] [FRSB in the SK spin glass: convergence to full-interval support at zero temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18032)
*Hong-Bin Chen*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了零场谢林顿-柯克帕特里克（Sherrington-Kirkpatrick）模型在零温下的完全复制对称性破缺（full replica symmetry breaking）：巴黎（Parisi）最小化子是绝对连续的，具有光滑密度，支撑集为 [0,1)。同时，对于逆温度β>1，巴黎测度的支撑集为 [0,q_β]，且证明了 q_β 在 β→∞ 时收敛到 1。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数学分析的方法，结合已有文献中关于巴黎测度（Parisi measure）支撑集为 [0,q_β] 的结果，进一步证明零温下巴黎极小化子的绝对连续性、密度光滑性及支撑集性质，并分析 q_β 在 β→∞ 时的渐近行为。

Result: 零温下巴黎极小化子是绝对连续的（absolutely continuous），具有光滑密度（smooth density），且支撑集为 [0,1)；对于逆温度 β>1，巴黎测度的支撑集为 [0,q_β]，且 q_β 在 β→∞ 时收敛到 1。

Conclusion: 该结果严格验证了零场SK模型在零温下的完全复制对称性破缺，补充并推广了已有文献中关于有限温度下巴黎测度支撑集的结果。

Abstract: We prove full replica symmetry breaking for the zero-field Sherrington-Kirkpatrick model at zero temperature: the Parisi minimizer is absolutely continuous, has a smooth density, and has support $[0,1)$. At inverse temperature $β>1$, [arxiv.org/abs/2607.11756v3] recently proved that the Parisi measure has support $[0,q_β]$. Here, we show $q_β$ converges to $1$ as $β\to\infty$.
