### [34] [The Brownian loop-catcher](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18070)
*Gefei Cai*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文引入一族平面布朗运动（Brownian motion）的随机连通闭子集——布朗环捕手（Brownian loop-catchers），用于插值连续环擦除随机游走（LERW）与布朗轨迹（Brownian trace），从而将布朗环汤簇（Brownian loop soup clusters）的中心荷（central charge）$c$ 规范延拓至 $-2 \le c < 0$。该构造始于有限图上的随机游走环捕手，通过纠缠多路径 LERW 和格林函数检验（Green function test）证明其收敛性及恢复性质（recovery property），并推导出外边界为局部 SLE$_κ$ 曲线（$κ \in [2, 8/3)$）以及交点概率渐近行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 布朗环汤簇此前仅对中心荷 $c \ge 0$ 有严格构造；本文旨在将其规范延拓到负中心荷区域 $-2 \le c < 0$，从而填补布朗运动与环擦除随机游走之间的缺失插值，并揭示布朗轨迹内部包含 SLE$_κ$ 型曲线的完整谱系（$κ \in [2, 8/3]$）。

Method: 首先在任意有限图上定义随机游走环捕手，其分布由有限线性系统决定，并证明该系统在 $-2 \le c < 0$ 时解非负，在 $c < -2$ 时可能非负性破缺。关键工具是纠缠多路径环擦除随机游走（entangled multipath LERW）。为证明收敛到布朗环捕手，提出格林函数检验：将布朗环捕手的恢复性质转化为剩余区域中格林函数的所有混合矩（mixed moments）。

Result: 每个布朗环捕手满足恢复性质：用强度为 $-c/2$ 的独立布朗环汤中所有与之相交的环进行装饰，可恢复完整的布朗轨迹；对于 $c < -2$，不存在这样的分布。其外边界是局部 SLE$_κ$，其中 $κ = \frac{1}{3}\left(13 - c - \sqrt{(1-c)(25-c)}\right) \in [2, 8/3)$。当 $-2 < c < 0$ 时，它与半径 $\varepsilon$ 的内球相交的概率渐近正比于 $|\log\varepsilon|^{-1 + c/2}$。因此，平面布朗轨迹对每个 $κ \in [2, 8/3]$ 都包含一条 SLE$_κ$ 型曲线。

Conclusion: 布朗环捕手家族实现了布朗环汤簇从 $c \ge 0$ 到 $-2 \le c < 0$ 的规范延拓，并揭示了布朗轨迹内部 SLE 曲线的完整谱系。恢复性质不仅刻画了布朗环捕手的填充（filling），还完全决定了其分布律。格林函数检验方法还可推广至三维情形。

Abstract: We introduce a family of random connected closed subsets of planar Brownian motion, called Brownian loop-catchers, which interpolate between the continuum loop-erased random-walk (LERW) and the Brownian trace. This provides the canonical continuation of Brownian loop soup clusters to central charges $-2\le c<0$. For each such $c$, the corresponding loop-catcher satisfies the following recovery property: adding all loops from an independent Brownian loop soup of intensity $-c/2$ that intersect it recovers the Brownian trace. Furthermore, no such law exists for $c<-2$. We also show that its outer boundary is locally SLE$_κ$ with $κ= \frac{1}{3}\left(13 - c - \sqrt{(1-c)(25-c)}\right)\in[2,\frac83)$, and the probability that it intersects an interior ball of radius $\varepsilon$ is asymptotically proportional to $|\log\varepsilon|^{-1+\frac{c}{2}}$ when $-2<c<0$. Therefore, a planar Brownian trace contains an SLE$_κ$-type curve for every $κ\in[2,\frac83]$.
  Our construction begins with a random-walk loop-catcher on any finite graph, whose law is determined by a finite linear system. We prove that its solution is nonnegative for $-2\leq c<0$, while nonnegativity can fail for $c<-2$. The key ingredient is a new entangled multipath LERW, which recovers a union of independent random-walk paths when decorated with a single common random-walk loop soup. We then prove that the random-walk loop-catcher converges to the Brownian loop-catcher under lattice approximations. To this end, we propose a novel Green function test which converts the recovery property of the Brownian loop-catcher into all mixed moments of Green functions in the remaining domain, based on the entangled multipath LERW. Consequently, the recovery property characterizes the full law of the Brownian loop-catcher, not only its filling. The Green function test also extends to the three-dimensional case.

</details>


### [35] [Periodic directed landscape](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18104)
*Amol Aggarwal,Ivan Corwin,Dominik Schmid*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文构造了周期性有向景观（periodic directed landscape），证明其是 Kardar-Parisi-Zhang（KPZ）普适类中周期模型的标度极限（scaling limit），并建立了周期性指数末次渗流（periodic exponential last passage percolation）到该极限的收敛性，同时确认了关于周期 KPZ 不动点（periodic KPZ fixed point）局部结构的猜想，以及周期 ASEP 到周期 KPZ 不动点的收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为 KPZ 普适类中的周期模型建立统一的标度极限理论，并验证已有的结构和收敛性猜想。

Method: 关键技术是提出一种“粘合”（gluing）全空间有向景观（full-space directed landscapes）及其前极限（prelimits）的方法，该方法本身具有独立的理论价值。

Result: 构造了周期有向景观；证明了周期指数末次渗流收敛到该极限；确认了 Baik、Liao 和 Liu 关于周期 KPZ 不动点局部结构的猜想；建立了周期 ASEP（periodic ASEP）到周期 KPZ 不动点的耦合收敛。

Conclusion: 周期有向景观是周期 KPZ 模型标度极限的候选对象；粘合技术为处理有向景观的周期性问题提供了有效工具。

Abstract: We construct the periodic directed landscape, which is the conjectured scaling limit for periodic models in the Kardar-Parisi-Zhang universality class. We establish the convergence of periodic exponential last passage percolation to the periodic directed landscape. Moreover, we confirm conjectures by Baik, Liao and Liu on the local structure of the periodic KPZ fixed point, and establish the convergence of periodic ASEPs to periodic KPZ fixed points, coupled according to the same periodic directed landscape. Our main tool to construct the periodic directed landscape (and prove convergence to it) is a technique for gluing full-space directed landscapes (and their prelimits), which is of independent interest.

</details>


### [36] [Temperature chaos in directed polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18194)
*Shirshendu Ganguly,Victor Ginsburg,Zoe Himwich*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文首次严格证明连续定向随机聚合物（CDRP）在高温差极限下解耦为两个独立的定向景观（directed landscape），即“跨温度能量退耦”现象，并作为副产品证明了定向景观是二维黑噪声（black noise）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无序系统（如自旋玻璃和聚合物）对温度扰动极其敏感，表现出“混沌”（chaos）现象。本文旨在从严格数学角度研究KPZ普适类（KPZ universality class）中典范模型——连续定向随机聚合物（CDRP）的温度混沌性质。

Method: 通过耦合同一白噪声下两个不同逆温度(β₁, β₂)的CDRP自由能，测量“枢轴性”（pivotality）或“影响力”（influence）在空间薄条带中的行为，建立关键估计。该策略利用了最后通道渗流（last passage percolation）模型中的技术。

Result: 证明当β₂ ≫ β₁ ≫ 1时，耦合的CDRP自由能在极限下退耦，收敛为一对独立的定向景观。这是首个“跨温度能量退耦”（energetic de-correlation across temperatures）结果。同时，证明了定向景观是二维黑噪声（black noise），这是继临界平面逾渗（critical planar percolation）和布朗虫网（Brownian web）后的第三个已知二维黑噪声例子。

Conclusion: 本文为KPZ普适类模型的温度混沌行为提供了严格的数学基础，并确认了定向景观的二维黑噪声性质，验证了Virág此前的猜想。

Abstract: Disordered systems such as spin glasses and polymers characteristically exhibit random energy landscapes with many macroscopically separated energetic valleys corresponding to near-ground states. This high complexity renders these systems extremely sensitive to perturbations of external parameters. For instance, the support of associated Gibbs measures may change macroscopically under such perturbations, a phenomenon known as chaos in the literature. In experiments, chaotic phenomena are typically studied via temperature perturbations.
  In this article, we initiate the rigorous study of temperature-chaotic properties of the continuum directed random polymer (CDRP), a canonical model in the KPZ universality class. The CDRP is driven by white noise and is parametrized by inverse temperature $β$, and is known [Wu '26, Das-Zhu '24] to converge in the zero-temperature limit $β\to \infty$ to the directed landscape constructed in [Dauvergne-Ortmann-Virág '22], the putative universal scaling limit of models in the KPZ universality class. The main result of this article considers the CDRP free energies coupled through the same white noise at a pair of inverse temperatures $(β_1, β_2)$, and shows that they decouple in the limit $β_2 \gg β_1 \gg 1$, converging to a pair of independent directed landscapes. This is the first such "energetic de-correlation across temperatures" result. Our key estimate measures the "pivotality" or "influence" of spatially thin strips in models of last passage percolation. As a byproduct, the proof strategy also allows to show that the directed landscape is a two-dimensional black noise (in the sense of [Tsirelson-Vershik '98]), previously conjectured by Virág. This provides the third known example of a two-dimensional black noise after critical planar percolation [Schramm-Smirnov '11] and the Brownian web [Ellis-Feldheim '16].

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了实现反应堆中微子物理学的物理目标，JUNO探测器使用的材料必须具有低放射性污染水平，以避免意外符合本底干扰反应堆中微子分析。

Method: 自建造阶段起，对数千种材料的天然放射性含量进行筛选，选择符合设计本底预算（background budget）的材料；探测器 fiducial 体积（半径R < 17.2 m）内液体闪烁体的单事件率要求约为7 Hz（能量>0.7 MeV），对应意外符合本底约每天1个事件。

Result: 总结了最终用于JUNO探测器的材料放射性杂质浓度数据。整个探测器建造及液体闪烁体灌注于2025年8月完成，初始数据显示 fiducial 体积内天然放射性总计数率已达到设计要求。

Conclusion: JUNO探测器的天然放射性本底水平能够支持反应堆反中微子分析工作。

Abstract: The Jiangmen Underground Neutrino Observatory (JUNO) collaboration has completed the construction of the 20,000-ton liquid scintillator detector and the associated muon veto detector system. To meet the physics objectives, the materials used in the detector must exhibit low radioactive contamination. The single-event rate in the fiducial volume (R $<$ 17.2 m) of the scintillator is required to be approximately 7 Hz for energies above 0.7 MeV, resulting in an accidental coincidence background of about 1 event per day for reactor neutrino physics analyses. Since the beginning of the construction phase, we have screened the natural radioactivity content of thousands of materials, to select those that meet the design background budget. The radioactive impurity concentrations of the materials ultimately used in the JUNO detector are summarized in this paper. The construction of the entire detector and the subsequent filling of the liquid scintillator were completed in August 2025. From the initial data, the total count rate of natural radioactivity within the detector's fiducial volume has met the requirements and is sufficient to support the reactor antineutrino analysis.

### [38] [Rolling Galileons: Evolving Braiding Strength for Viable Dark Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16395)
*James Hallam,Krishna Naidoo,Sergi Sirera,Tessa Baker*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出“滚动伽利略引力（Rolling Galileon gravity）”——一种破缺平移对称性的三次伽利略理论（cubic Galileon）扩展，允许耦合系数变化从而产生演化的缠绕强度（evolving braiding strength）。通过解析条件与贝叶斯分析，证明该系统能够同时满足穿越幻象（phantom-crossing）状态方程、正的积分萨克斯-沃尔夫（integrated Sachs-Wolfe）信号、以及宇宙空洞中无屏蔽标量力病理三项要求，并与膨胀历史数据兼容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 日益增多的观测迹象表明暗能量（dark energy）可能是动力学的（dynamical），因此需要构建能够描述这一特征的理论框架。

Method: 研究者在平移对称性破缺的框架下扩展三次伽利略理论，允许耦合系数变化从而引入演化的缠绕强度。通过分析场重新定义下的封闭性，将理论空间简化为两个函数；进而推导出满足三项观测现象学要求的解析条件，并对最小滚动伽利略模型进行贝叶斯分析（Bayesian analysis）。

Result: 满足三项要求（穿越幻象状态方程、正的积分萨克斯-沃尔夫信号、无病理的屏蔽标量力）的共同条件为：缠绕强度相对于动力学部分（kinetic sector）递增。最小滚动伽利略模型在贝叶斯分析中既能满足上述三项可行性要求，也与膨胀历史数据（expansion-history data）拟合良好。

Conclusion: 滚动伽利略引力提供了一个理论自洽且与数据兼容的动力学子暗能量框架，其中递增的缠绕强度是实现关键观测现象的关键机制。

Abstract: Motivated by growing observational indications that dark energy may be dynamical, we introduce Rolling Galileon gravity: a minimal shift-symmetry-breaking extension of the cubic Galileon in which the coupling coefficients are allowed to vary, giving rise to an evolving braiding strength. The full theory space, shown to be closed under field redefinitions, is characterised by two functions. We derive analytical conditions to satisfy three phenomenological requirements: i) a phantom-crossing equation of state at late times, ii) a positive integrated Sachs-Wolfe signature, and iii) absence of pathologies in the screened scalar force in cosmic voids. We show that these conditions are collectively satisfied by an increasing braiding strength relative to the kinetic sector. A Bayesian analysis of minimal Rolling Galileon models finds that they can satisfy the viability requirements i)-iii) whilst providing an acceptable fit to expansion-history data.

</details>


### [39] [The Goldstone Awakens: Unimodular dark energy in scale-invariant $R^2$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16405)
*Mariaveronica De Angelis,Javier Rubio*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文基于标度不变性（scale invariance）和幺模引力（unimodular gravity）构建了一个 R² 宇宙学模型，其中膨胀子（dilaton）的戈德斯通玻色子（Goldstone boson）在暴胀（inflation）与暗能量（dark energy）之间建立了可预测的联系。幺模积分常数在暴胀后可忽略的戈德斯通方向上产生指数势，其斜率由场空间几何而非自由参数决定，从而将早期宇宙的谱指数（spectral tilt）与晚期暗能量状态方程参数紧密关联起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有宇宙学模型中，暴胀和暗能量通常被视为两个独立的问题，缺乏统一的理论基础。本文旨在利用标度不变性与幺模引力，通过膨胀子的戈德斯通玻色子将暴胀与暗能量统一到一个预测性框架中，从而建立早期宇宙与晚期宇宙可观测量之间的内在联系。

Method: 作者构建了一个基于标度不变性和幺模引力的 R² 宇宙学模型。利用膨胀子对应的诺特流（Noether current）守恒将暴胀轨迹约束到场空间的一维轨道上，从而冻结戈德斯通方向，使暴胀动力学有效成为单场（single-field）模型。暴胀后系统弛豫至闵可夫斯基真空流形（Minkowski vacuum manifold），此时在暴胀阶段可忽略的幺模积分常数抬起平坦的戈德斯通方向，生成一个指数势（exponential potential）。

Result: 该模型的暗能量势能斜率由暴胀吸引子（inflationary attractor）的场空间几何决定，因此并非自由参数。该几何排除了物质时代的跟踪行为（tracking），在暴胀可行性区域内将场置于与加速膨胀兼容的解冻区（thawing regime）。对于一个具有代表性的暴胀基准点，该赝戈德斯通场（pseudo-Goldstone field）直至接近当前纪元才解冻，给出 CPL 参数化下的暗能量状态方程参数 (w₀, wₐ) ≈ (-0.992, -0.011)。控制暴胀谱倾斜（spectral tilt）的同一参数也固定了暗能量势的斜率，导致 nₛ 较低时解冻信号增强，而 nₛ 接近 1 时模型趋近于 ΛCDM。

Conclusion: 标度不变性与幺模引力的结合为暴胀与暗能量提供了统一的理论框架。该模型在暴胀与暗能量之间建立了可预测的关联，其中暴胀谱指数 nₛ 与暗能量状态方程参数之间存在紧密的对应关系，使得早期宇宙和晚期宇宙的可观测量相互约束，从而为检验该模型提供了可观测的预测。

Abstract: We construct an $R^2$ cosmology based on scale invariance and unimodular gravity in which the Goldstone boson of dilatations establishes a predictive connection between inflation and dark energy. The conservation of the corresponding Noether current confines the inflationary trajectory to a one-dimensional orbit in field space, freezing the Goldstone direction and rendering the inflationary dynamics effectively single field. After inflation, the system settles on a Minkowski vacuum manifold. The unimodular integration constant, already present in the full theory but negligible during inflation, lifts the flat Goldstone direction, generating an exponential potential for the canonically normalised field. Unlike in phenomenological quintessence models, its slope is not a free DE parameter, but is instead fixed by the field-space geometry inherited from the inflationary attractor. This geometry excludes matter-era tracking and, throughout the inflationary viability region, places the field in the thawing regime compatible with accelerated expansion. For a representative inflationary benchmark, the now pseudo-Goldstone field remains frozen until close to the present epoch, yielding DE equation-of-state parameters $(w_0,w_a)\simeq(-0.992,-0.011)$ in the CPL parametrisation $w(a)=w_0+w_a(1-a)$. More generally, the same parameter controlling the inflationary spectral tilt also fixes the slope of the DE potential, leading to a tight correlation between early- and late-Universe observables: increasing the thawing signal lowers $n_s$, while values of $n_s$ closer to unity drive the model towards $Λ$CDM.

</details>


### [40] [One Year and One Night to 1% in $\mathbf{H_0}$: Efficient Spectroscopic Strategy for Dark Siren Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17284)
*Yixuan Dang,Ariel J. Amsellem,Ignacio Magaña Hernandez,Antonella Palmese,B. S. Sathyaprakash*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了通过暗 sirens（dark sirens）方法，利用体积限制星系目录（volume-limited galaxy catalog）的深度推断哈勃常数（$H_0$），并提出了一种高效的光谱观测策略，可在一年内以最少一至五个观测夜实现0.98%的中位精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波事件（gravitational-wave events）来自致密双星并合（compact binary coalescences, CBCs），可作为标准 sirens（standard sirens）测量哈勃常数，但缺乏电磁对应体时需依赖暗 siren 方法。本文旨在探究星系目录深度对该推断的影响，并识别出实现无偏测量 $H_0$ 的最优光谱观测策略。

Method: 采用暗 siren（dark siren）或称星系目录法（galaxy catalog method），通过统计事件定位体积内的编录星系，在无电磁对应体情况下推断哈勃常数。研究评估了体积限制星系目录（volume-limited galaxy catalog）的深度对推断的影响，并设计了最佳光谱巡天（spectroscopic survey）策略。

Result: 针对LIGO Hanford、LIGO Livingston 和 LIGO-India 网络在 A$^\#$ 灵敏度下一年内十个最佳定位事件，光谱巡天深度达到 $r \sim 19$ 时，可实现 $H_0$ 的0.98%中位精度。该观测策略最少仅需一个电磁后随观测夜，最保守假设下为五个观测夜。对于 Hanford、Livingston 和 Virgo 网络在 A$+$ 灵敏度下，相同十事件策略的中位精度为2.63%。

Conclusion: 通过合理选择星系目录深度和观测策略，暗 siren 方法可以在极少电磁后随观测资源下，实现对哈勃常数的高精度无偏测量。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave events from compact binary coalescences (CBCs) can be used as standard sirens: they encode the luminosity distance to their sources, which yields a measurement of the Hubble constant ($H_0$) if the source's redshift is known. In the absence of an electromagnetic counterpart, $H_0$ can still be inferred statistically from the cataloged galaxies within the event's sky localization volume via the dark siren, or galaxy catalog method. In this work we examine how the depth of a volume-limited galaxy catalog affects this inference and identify the most efficient spectroscopic strategy for an unbiased measurement of $H_0$ at a median precision of $0.98\%$. The strategy is to carry out spectroscopic surveys to a depth of $r \sim 19$ for the ten best-localized events observed in one year by the LIGO Hanford, LIGO Livingston, and LIGO-India network at A$^\#$ sensitivity. Such a campaign requires a minimum of one night of electromagnetic follow-up observations, or five nights under the most conservative assumptions. For the Hanford, Livingston, and Virgo network at A$+$ sensitivity, the same ten-event strategy yields a median precision of $2.63\%$.

</details>


### [41] [Magnetically assisted primordial scalar perturbations: Scalar-Induced Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17875)
*Arko Bhaumik,Theodoros Papanikolaou,Anish Ghoshal*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了原初磁场（PMF）在恒定状态方程（EoS）参数$w$的后暴胀时期中如何通过各向异性应力激发标量度规扰动，并进一步在二阶诱导出标量诱导引力波（SIGW）。分析表明，对于$w>1/3$（更硬）的背景，超视界尺度上PMF源标量扰动的增长更快；在特定参数区间（类似于kination的后暴胀时代与近尺度不变的PMF），PMF源SIGW信号可超越直接PMF生成的张量背景，且可能被下一代引力波探测器在mHz–kHz频段探测到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原初磁场（PMF）通过其各向异性应力（anisotropic stress）构成宇宙学扰动的重要来源，可能同时在标量（scalar）和张量（tensor）扇区留下可观测印记。本研究旨在理解PMF源标量扰动在后暴胀时期（post-inflationary epoch）的演化行为及其二阶诱导引力波信号，以探索其可观测性。

Method: 在规范不变（gauge-invariant）框架下，推导了Bardeen引力势（Bardeen gravitational potential）在恒定状态方程（equation-of-state, EoS）参数$w$背景下的源演化方程。通过分析超视界尺度上不同$w$值对应的扰动增长行为，并进一步从磁生标量扰动出发，计算二阶标量诱导引力波（scalar-induced gravitational wave, SIGW）背景。

Result: 对于更硬的背景（$w>1/3$），PMF源标量扰动在超视界尺度上增长更快；对于更软的背景（$w<1/3$），增长更慢，以辐射主导（$w=1/3$）为边界。在kination-like后暴胀时期与近尺度不变PMF的参数区间内，PMF源SIGW信号可能主导直接PMF生成的张量背景；同时诱导张量模对背景的反作用（backreaction）可忽略。当暴胀能标$H_{\rm inf}\sim10^3-10^9$ GeV且再加热持续时间$N_{\rm reh}\sim8-10$时，该SIGW信号有望被下一代地基与空间干涉引力波探测器在mHz–kHz频段探测到。

Conclusion: PMF源标量扰动的演化显著依赖于后暴胀时期的状态方程参数$w$；在特定参数条件下，PMF源SIGW信号可作为主导的引力波背景并被未来实验探测，这为约束原初磁场与后暴胀宇宙学提供了新窗口。

Abstract: Primordial magnetic fields (PMFs) provide a well-motivated source of cosmological perturbations through their anisotropic stress and may leave observable imprints in both the scalar and tensor sectors. In this work, we study scalar metric perturbations sourced by a PMF evolving through a finite post-inflationary epoch characterized by a constant equation-of-state (EoS) parameter $w$. Working in a gauge-invariant framework, we derive the sourced evolution equation for the Bardeen gravitational potential in a general constant-$w$ background. Our analysis indicates faster (slower) growth of PMF-sourced scalar perturbations on superhorizon scales for a stiffer $w>1/3$ (softer $w<1/3$) background compared to the marginal radiation-dominated scenario with $w=1/3$. We then derive the scalar-induced gravitational wave (SIGW) background induced at second order by the magnetically generated scalar perturbations. Our analysis indicates a narrow viable parametric region for a kination-like post-inflationary era and a nearly scale-invariant PMF that may give rise to a PMF-sourced SIGW signal dominating over the direct PMF-generated tensor background. Simultaneously, the induced tensor modes are found to be perturbatively small compared to the magnetic sector, which, in turn, exerts negligible backreaction on the background. Interestingly enough, for an inflationary scale $H_{\rm inf}\sim10^3-10^9$ GeV and duration of reheating in $e$-folds $N_{\rm reh}\sim8-10$, the dominant PMF-sourced SIGW signal may be detectable by next-generation terrestrial and space-based interferometric GW detectors spanning the mHz$-$kHz frequency range.

</details>


### [42] [Repulsive dark matter from Hosotani mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17727)
*Philippe Brax,Patrick Valageas*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个具有排斥性自相互作用的超轻暗物质（ultralight dark matter）模型，起源于五维（5D）作用量，仅包含 U(1) 规范场和若干有质量带电费米子。通过紧致化（compactification）到四维，暗物质标量场对应规范场的第五分量；借助 Scherk-Schwarz twist，两个费米子即可产生排斥性自相互作用。模型在从暴胀（inflation）到当前的演化阶段均保持自洽，参数空间广泛允许：标量质量低于 10⁻¹² eV 时表现为模糊暗物质（fuzzy dark matter），更高质量时排斥性自相互作用主导天体尺度孤子（soliton）的形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有超轻暗物质模型通常只考虑吸引性自相互作用，而排斥性自相互作用对解释暗物质晕中的孤子结构等天体物理现象至关重要。本文旨在从高维规范理论出发，构建一个自然产生排斥性自相互作用的暗物质模型，并检验其观测与理论自洽性。

Method: 从包含 U(1) 规范场和多个有质量带电费米子的五维作用量出发，通过紧致化到四维，使暗物质标量场对应于规范场的第五分量。利用围绕第五维的 Scherk-Schwarz twist，使两个费米子共同作用产生排斥性自相互作用。随后检验模型从暴胀时期至今的观测与理论自洽性。

Result: 模型参数空间在大范围内允许。当标量质量低于 10⁻¹² eV 时，自相互作用可忽略，模型行为类似于模糊暗物质（fuzzy dark matter）。当质量更高时，排斥性自相互作用主导天体尺度孤子（soliton）的形成；更大的孤子尺寸需要较大的初始 misalignment 或处于模糊暗物质区域的较小质量。

Conclusion: 该五维超轻暗物质模型能够在不同质量区间分别呈现模糊暗物质或排斥性自相互作用主导的孤子行为，且具有广泛的允许参数空间，为暗物质的天体物理观测提供了可检验的理论框架。

Abstract: We build an ultralight dark matter model with repulsive self-interactions, starting from a 5D action that only includes a $U(1)$ gauge field and several massive and charged free fermions. The dark matter scalar field corresponds to the fifth component of the gauge field, after compactification to 4D. Although the single-fermion case only leads to attractive self-interactions, two fermions can already give rise to repulsive self-interactions, thanks to a Scherk-Schwarz twist around the fifth dimension. We check the observational and theoretical self-consistency of this scenario, from the inflation stage to the current time. We find that large ranges of model parameters are allowed. For scalar masses below $10^{-12}$ eV the self-interactions are negligible and the model behaves as fuzzy dark matter. For higher masses the repulsive self-interactions govern the formation of solitons of astrophysical size. Larger sizes require a large initial misalignment or small masses in the fuzzy dark matter regime.

</details>


### [43] [Cosmological consequences of a dynamical dark matter in the light of DESI DR2 measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18234)
*Abhijith Ajith,Utkarsh Kumar*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文针对DESI最近观测中倾向于破坏零能量条件（Null Energy Condition）的动态暗能量（dynamical dark energy）现象，提出了一种替代解释：该信号可能源于非传统暗物质动力学，而非暗能量。通过构建一个状态方程（EoS）随尺度因子平滑演化的动态暗物质（DDM）模型，并利用CMB、DESI DR2 BAO、多个超新星数据集和增长速率数据进行联合分析，发现当前暗物质状态方程在一定数据集组合下显著为负，模型在部分数据组合中优于ΛCDM，但不如CPL暗能量参数化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DESI的最新数据倾向于支持违反零能量条件的动态暗能量，表现为早期鬼魅行为（phantom behaviour）。本文旨在探索一种替代解释，即这种偏好并非来自暗能量，而是由非常规的暗物质动力学所导致。

Method: 提出一个动态暗物质（dynamical dark matter, DDM）模型，其状态方程（equation of state, EoS）非零，并在一个过渡尺度因子（transition scale factor）$a_t$ 处平滑插值（interpolates）早期与晚期渐近值。利用宇宙微波背景（CMB）、DESI DR2 BAO、三种超新星数据集（PantheonPlus、Union3、DESY5）以及增长速率（growth rate）数据对模型进行联合约束。

Result: 早期暗物质状态方程与零一致，但当前值在部分数据组合下显著为负（最高达$3.02σ$）。CMB+DESI+DESY5组合给出当前状态方程$-0.060^{+0.013}_{-0.028}$和$a_t=0.41^{+0.088}_{-0.13}$（68%置信水平）。模型预测的$σ_8$和$S_8$低于ΛCDM，与弱引力透镜数据更一致；$H_0$不变，仍与局域距离阶梯测量存在冲突。DDM模型在部分组合中优于ΛCDM（$Δχ^2_{\rm MAP} = -14.093$, $Δ{\rm DIC} = -7.838$），但逊于CPL暗能量参数化。

Conclusion: 非零晚期暗物质状态方程的偏好是稳健的，在不同超新星编译和加入增长速率数据后仍成立。然而，DDM模型在统计上不如CPL参数化对暗能量的描述，说明DESI观测中的动态行为可能仍需暗能量作为主要驱动机制。

Abstract: Recent DESI results exhibit preference for a Null Energy Condition violating dynamical dark energy, with early phantom behaviour. We explore an alternative interpretation in which this preference arises from unconventional dark matter dynamics rather than from dynamical dark energy. We propose a dynamical dark matter (DDM) model, with a non-zero equation of state (EoS) that smoothly interpolates between early time and late time asymptotes across a transition scale factor $a_t$, and study its consequences against cosmological datasets including CMB, DESI DR2 BAO, SNeIa (PantheonPlus, Union3, and DESY5) and growth rate data. We find the early time EoS to be consistent with zero, while the present day value is negative at a significance ranging from $0.42σ$ to $3.02σ$ depending on the dataset combination. The strongest preference occurs from the combination of CMB, DESI, and DESY5 giving the present day EoS to be $-0.060^{+0.013}_{-0.028}$ and $a_t = 0.41^{+0.088}_{-0.13}$ at 68\% CL. This preference for a non-zero, late time DM EoS persists when growth rate data are included and across all three SNeIa compilations considered, while the matter density $Ω_m$ mildly shifts to higher values relative to $Λ$CDM. The model also predicts a lower $σ_8$ and $S_8$ than $Λ$CDM, in better agreement with weak-lensing data, while $H_0$ remains unchanged and in tension with local distance-ladder measurements. The DDM model is preferred over $Λ$CDM ($Δχ^2_{\rm MAP} = -14.093$, $Δ{\rm DIC} = -7.838$ for Planck+DESI+DESY5) but disfavored relative to the CPL parameterization of DE ($Δχ^2_{\rm MAP} = 6.755$, $Δ{\rm DIC} = 7.966$). This preference is consistent among other combination of datasets as well.

</details>

### [44] [A Four-Dimensional Gaussian Random Field Generator for Modeling Spatiotemporal Variability in Astrophysical Sources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16576)
*Alejandro Cárdenas-Avendaño,Diego Rubiera-Garcia,Frederic H. Vincent*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一模型，将非赤道面、非测地线的Kerr流体转动律与四维非齐次各向异性高斯随机场相结合，为相对论性黑洞电影（black-hole movies）提供可直接实现的时变厚盘及盘-喷流发射模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞电影的半解析模型要么局限于赤道面（equatorial）发射，要么依赖时间无关（time-independent）的源，缺乏兼具非赤道面流动与时间变化性的统一方案。

Method: 首先，通过提升赤道面比角动量（specific-angular-momentum）分布至柱面、将四速度极向分量设为零、利用完整Kerr度规在时空点归一化流动，构建非赤道面、非测地线（nongeodesic）的Kerr流体转动律，并可选择恢复测地线（geodesic-like）坠入行为。其次，将该速度场作为盘面上的平流场（advection field），嵌入四维非齐次各向异性Matérn型高斯随机场（Gaussian random field）。最后，通过单一复合关联张量（composite correlation tensor）为环状盘与中心喷流（jet）提供参数化模型。

Result: 得到一个可用于相对论研究的、可直接实现的时变厚盘及盘-喷流发射的有效模型（effective model）。

Conclusion: 该模型统一了非赤道面流动描述与时变源建模，为后续黑洞成像与电影模拟提供了更灵活、直接可用的半解析框架。

Abstract: Semi-analytic models of black-hole movies require both an emitting flow prescription and a time-dependent source variability. Existing prescriptions are often limited to either equatorial emission or time-independent sources. In this work we present a unified model for these two ingredients. First, we prescribe an off-equatorial, nongeodesic Kerr fluid rotation law by lifting an equatorial specific-angular-momentum profile to cylindrical surfaces, setting the polar component of the four-velocity to zero, normalizing the flow with the full Kerr metric at the spacetime point, and retaining the option to recover a geodesic-like plunging prescription when needed. Second, we use this velocity as the disk advection field in a four-dimensional inhomogeneous, anisotropic Matérn-like Gaussian random field. We provide a parametrized model for a torus-like disk and a central jet through a single composite correlation tensor. The resulting effective model is an implementation-ready prescription for time-dependent thick-disk and disk-jet emission for relativistic studies.

</details>


### [45] [Electromagnetic Emission from a Black Hole Evaporating in External Magnetic Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16880)
*Soumya Samrat Mandal,Maxim Lyutikov*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该论文描述了一种黑洞在真空中外部磁场里蒸发时产生的经典（非量子）电磁辐射过程，该过程不涉及任何电荷，机制类似于Gertsenshtein-Zel'dovich效应，辐射能谱以低频（红色）为主，且不存在蒸发末期的明亮爆发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在经典黑洞辐射研究中，除Hawking辐射外是否存在其他由黑洞蒸发诱发的电磁发射过程尚待探索；本文旨在揭示时变时空对外部静态磁场的扰动如何产生无电荷的经典辐射。

Method: 将Hawking辐射近似为中心质量M(t)随时间变化的球对称零流体（null fluid）出流，采用Laplace变换选取电磁响应的延迟出射支（retarded outgoing branch），从而固定因果辐射方向；通过解析求解得到辐射场和能量谱表达式。

Result: 发射的电磁辐射为纯横电（Transverse Electric, TE）模，光谱能量密度满足dℰ_B/dω ∝ B₀² m₀² τ_H^{-2/3} ω^{-8/3}，表现出低频主导（红色主导）特征；蒸发过程结束时无明亮爆发。

Conclusion: 在外部磁场中蒸发的黑洞会额外产生一种无电荷的经典电磁辐射，该过程可通过传输线发射（transmission-line emission）或时变介电常数介质中的位移电流发射（displacement current emission）提供经典类比。

Abstract: We describe a classical (non-quantum) radiation process: additional (to Hawking) emission by a black hole evaporating in an external magnetic field in vacuum. The electromagnetic radiation process is completely electric charge-free and bears some resemblance to the Gertsenshtein-Zel'dovich effect. The time evolution of the spacetime metric perturbs a static background magnetic field, inducing a radiative field that acts as an effective electromagnetic source even in the absence of physical charges or currents. To isolate the dynamic effects of the time-dependent spacetime on the external magnetic field, we approximate Hawking radiation as a spherically symmetric outflow of null fluid governed by the prescribed time-dependence of the central mass $M(t)$.
  We employ Laplace transform, which selects the retarded outgoing branch of the electromagnetic response, producing fields proportional to $Θ(t-r)$ and thereby fixing a causal radiative arrow of emission. The emitted spectral energy is red-dominated, scaling as $d\mathcal{E}_B/dω\propto B_0^2 m_0^2 τ_H^{-2/3} ω^{-8/3}$, where $τ_H$ is the Hawking evaporation timescale, and corresponds to a pure Transverse Electric (TE) mode. There is no final bright burst at the end of the evaporation. We offer classical analogues for this mechanism as transmission-line emission and, separately, as the displacement current emission from a medium with time-varying dielectric permittivity.

</details>

### [46] [Nanowire networks' interconnection graphs from their photomicrographs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16445)
*Javier Tau Anzoátegui,Juan Ignacio Diaz Schneider,Eduardo D. Martínez,Pablo Levy,Oscar Filevich,Cynthia P. Quinteros*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出一套图像后处理流水线（pipeline），从银纳米线网络（AgNWN）的光学显微照片中提取互连图（interconnection graph），分析其图论指标（如度分布、聚类系数、路径长度），并与小世界（small-world）、模块化（modular）和无标度（scale-free）拓扑模型进行对比。实验网络展现出类似小世界与模块化拓扑的特征，同时本文还探讨了由于光学图像无法区分真实连接与伪交叉点而导致的互连高估问题，并研究了人为移除结点对聚类系数和路径长度的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可调单元的自组装体系在信号处理领域受到广泛关注，银纳米线网络（silver nanowire networks, AgNWNs）已被证明具备累积、非线性和多时间尺度记忆保持能力，适合用于神经形态计算。本研究旨在从实验获取的网络结构中提取互连方案，以分析其拓扑特性，并为数值仿真平台提供输入。

Method: 通过对AgNWN的光学显微照片进行后处理，构建了一套优化的流水线（pipeline），用于提取纳米线之间的交点和互连图。基于图（graph）表示，计算度分布、社区规模（community size）、聚类系数（clustering coefficient）和路径长度（path-length）等图论指标，并与参考拓扑模型进行对比。此外，通过人为移除图中的连接结点，研究光学图像高估互连数对聚类系数和路径长度的影响。

Result: 实验组装网络的度分布、邻接矩阵等分析结果表明，其拓扑特征与small-world和modular拓扑结构具有相似性。基于天顶视角光学图像提取的互连方案因无法区分真实结点与纳米线垂直位移造成的伪交叉点，导致互连数量被高估。

Conclusion: 所提出流水线能够有效提取AgNWN的实验网络结构并进行拓扑分析。光学图像对互连的高估问题会影响聚类系数和路径长度等指标，研究中通过人为移除结点的方法量化了该偏差的影响。

Abstract: Self-assemblies of tunable units are being intensively studied as physical systems with signal-processing capabilities. Specifically, silver nanowire networks (AgNWNs) have demonstrated accumulation, non-linearity, and memory retention with multiple timescales, features that enable a wide variety of neuromorphic implementations. In this study, we aim to extract the interconnection scheme to analyze the experimentally obtained network architecture and, eventually, use it as input to a previously developed simulation platform. By post-processing photomicrographs of AgNWN, we present a pipeline optimized to extract the interconnection diagram, recognizing the intersections formed among the nanowires, to determine the associated graph for each physical sample. A graph is a collection of nodes and edges whose properties can be associated with different electrical responses. It is thus possible to study graphs' metrics, such as the degree distribution, community size, clustering coefficient, and path-length, to compare the experimental assemblies' attributes to those of topological models of reference. Small-world, modular, and scale-free are well-known structures in the field of mathematical graphs. By analyzing the degree distribution, the adjacency matrices, among other useful representation means, the experimental assemblies reveal similarities to both small-world and modular topologies. All the mentioned analyses were conducted considering the interconnection scheme obtained from zenithal-view optical images, which overestimates the number of NWs' interconnections (due to the impossibility of distinguishing real junctions from spurious cross-points between vertically displaced NWs). For that reason, this communication also studies the impact of artificially removing junctions from the resulting graphs on the previously calculated clustering coefficient and path length.

</details>


### [47] [Point Group Equivariant Graph Neural Networks for Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16871)
*Alexander J. Heilman,Qimin Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 提出点群对称感知的等变图神经网络（PGEqNN），通过将滤波器函数与对称感知索引对齐，在弹性与介电张量预测任务中，利用A1限制变体在减少训练参数的同时达到与完整点群及SO(3)分区模型相当或更优的精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统等变图神经网络仅满足完整的O(3)等变性（equivariance），未能充分利用原子系统的额外点群对称性（point-group symmetry），且滤波器函数的对称性需从数据中隐式学习而非严格施加。

Method: 提出点群对称感知的等变图神经网络（point-group symmetry aware equivariant graph neural networks, PGEqNN），将滤波器函数与对称感知索引（symmetry-aware indices）对齐，以实现更高粒度的预测。

Result: 在弹性与介电张量数据集上，等变网络的大部分预测能力集中于点群适应基的平凡子空间（trivial subspaces）；基于此发现的A1限制变体（A1-restricted variant）在训练更少有效参数的条件下，性能匹配或超越完整点群与SO(3)分区版本。

Conclusion: 通过主动施加点群对称性，可在保持预测精度的同时显著降低模型复杂度，得到更精简且精度不变的模型。

Abstract: Equivariant graph neural networks have proven effective tools for inference of material's properties directly from their structure. Traditionally, these have been applied such that they respect full $O(3)$ equivariance, so that any rotation or reflection of the input structure is respected in the model's output. While this works for general arrangements of atoms, additional symmetries of atomistic systems are left unleveraged. Furthermore, any symmetries of the filter functions are implicitly learned from the full dataset and not strictly enforced. In this work, we introduce point-group symmetry aware equivariant graph neural networks (PGEqNN) for materials science, with filter functions aligned with symmetry-aware indices for greater granularity in predictive tasks. With this architecture, we show that most of the predictive power of equivariant networks for tensorial elastic and dielectric datasets lies in the trivial subspaces of the point-group adapted bases. Exploiting this, an $A_1$-restricted variant matches or improves on its full point-group and $SO(3)$-partitioned counterparts while training fewer active parameters, yielding leaner models of equal accuracy.

</details>


### [48] [Transport-Weighted Coercivity in Granular CrO2: Why Magnetoresistance and Magnetization Can Disagree](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16984)
*E. Yu. Beliayev,I. G. Mirzoiev,V. A. Horielyi,I. A. Chichibaba*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过重新分析半金属铁磁体CrO₂粉末压块的数据，证明在颗粒导体中，电阻最大值对应的磁场Hp不能简单等同于体矫顽场Hc；其差值Hp-Hc可表征电流路径局域化、势垒演变及器件差异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁电阻磁滞回线常被用于估算磁性材料的矫顽场（coercive field）。本文旨在验证这种识别方法在颗粒导体（granular conductor）中是否仍然成立。

Method: 重新分析了已发表的关于半金属铁磁体（half-metallic ferromagnet）CrO₂粉末压块的磁输运（magnetotransport）和磁强（magnetometry）数据，比较了电阻最大值对应的磁场Hp和体矫顽场Hc在不同温度与测量电流下的关系。

Result: 电阻最大值对应的磁场Hp可能接近、高于或低于体矫顽场Hc，具体取决于温度和测量电流。在不同颗粒形状和绝缘壳层厚度的三个样品中，比值Hp/Hc遵循相同的定性序列，并在约15K附近表现出共同交叉。该行为被解释为控制电响应的颗粒间结（interparticle junction）发生了变化。

Conclusion: 体磁强计测量平均了整个磁体积，而隧穿电阻（tunnelling resistance）最大权重地贡献给了承载电流的小部分连接。Cohn精确的网络灵敏度定理（network-sensitivity theorem）给出了这些输运权重的严格线性响应定义。结合磁对关联效应（magnetic pair-correlation effects），引出了输运加权矫顽力（transport-weighted coercivity）的概念。在颗粒传感器和自旋相关复合材料中，电阻峰不能自动视为体矫顽场；反之，差值Hp-Hc可作为电流路径局域化、势垒演变和器件变异性的诊断工具。

Abstract: Magnetoresistance hysteresis is often used to estimate the coercive field of a magnetic material. We reanalyse our published magnetotransport and magnetometry data on compacted powders of the half-metallic ferromagnet CrO2 and show that this identification can fail in a granular conductor. The field Hp at the resistance maximum may be close to, above, or below the bulk coercive field Hc, depending on temperature and measuring current. For three samples with different particle shapes and insulating-shell thicknesses, the digitized ratio Hp/Hc follows the same qualitative sequence and suggests a common crossover near 15 K. We interpret this behaviour as a change in which interparticle junctions control the electrical response. Bulk magnetometry averages over the entire magnetic volume, whereas tunnelling resistance gives the largest weight to the small set of links that carries the current. Cohn's exact network-sensitivity theorem provides a rigorous linear-response definition of these transport weights. In simple terms, Cohn showed that the influence of a given contact on the total resistance is proportional to the square of the current flowing through that contact. Combined with known magnetic pair-correlation effects, this leads to the concept of transport-weighted coercivity. In granular sensors and spin-dependent composites, the resistance peak cannot automatically be treated as the bulk coercive field. Conversely, the difference Hp - Hc may serve as a diagnostic of current-path localization, barrier evolution, and device-to-device variability.

</details>


### [49] [Distinct reentrant transitions in a quasi-periodic Raman lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17104)
*Xingbo Wei,Zhentian Xie,Tong Liu,Gao Xianlong,Yunbo Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文研究了一维自旋-轨道耦合晶格中由塞曼势（Zeeman potential）驱动的异常迁移率边（mobility edges）与回返临界性转变（reentrant criticality transition），揭示了扩展态、局域态与临界态之间回返现象的基本框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）与含均匀及准周期分量的塞曼势（Zeeman potential）共同作用下，一维晶格中异常迁移率边（anomalous mobility edges）的出现及其诱导的回返转变（reentrant transition）机制。

Method: 在一维晶格模型中引入自旋-轨道耦合与均匀/准周期塞曼势，通过调节SOC强度分析迁移率边的演化及临界态（critical states）与非临界态（non-critical states）之间的转变。

Result: SOC可产生将临界态与非临界态分离的异常迁移率边，导致两种混合相之间的回返转变M₁→M₂→M₁；均匀塞曼势通过迁移率边移动分裂局域区，驱动回返退局域化转变（reentrant delocalization transition）。

Conclusion: 识别了一种新的“回返临界性转变”（reentrant criticality transition），即多次进入临界相；该发现作为回返退局域化/局域化转变的对应，完善了扩展态、局域态与临界态之间回返现象的基本框架，并揭示了不同于杂化机制（hybridization mechanisms）的回返现象新路径。

Abstract: We investigate a one-dimensional lattice with spin-orbit coupling (SOC) and a Zeeman potential containing uniform and quasiperiodic components. By tuning SOC, anomalous mobility edges emerge that separate critical from non-critical states, yielding a reentrant transition between two mixed phases, M$_1$$\to$M$_2$$\to$M$_1$, where M$_1$ (M$_2$) lacks (hosts) anomalous mobility edges. A new \emph{reentrant criticality transition}, defined as multiple entries into the critical phase, is identified. As a counterpart to reentrant delocalization/localization transitions, it completes the basic framework of reentrant phenomena across extended, localized, and critical states. The uniform Zeeman potential drives a reentrant delocalization transition, arising from the splitting of the localized region induced by the shift of mobility edges. This reveals a distinct pathway for reentrant phenomena beyond hybridization mechanisms.

</details>


### [50] [The Geometry of Semantic Space: A Continuous Geometric Framework for the Transformer Architecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17146)
*Zhihua Liang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出一个连续的几何框架，将Transformer架构的离散代数操作建模为语义纤维丛上的积分-微分方程，并通过跨越五个架构、参数规模达8B的六部分实验验证了该框架的定量预测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Transformer分析多停留在离散代数层面，缺乏一个统一的连续几何理论来理解其稳定性、上下文界限和优化动力学等深层机制。

Method: 基于单一几何公理——令牌序列构成带规范测度格的离散1-流形——将Transformer核心组件（RMSNorm、RoPE、Softmax注意力、前馈网络、残差流、SGD、权重衰减）翻译为微分几何、测度论和随机微积分的连贯词汇，并构建语义纤维丛上的积分-微分方程。

Result: 六部分实验在五个架构（Qwen3、LLaMA-3.1、Gemma-3、GPT-2、Mistral）上验证了：ε^{-1/2} Lipschitz缩放校准达到机器精度（R²=1.000）、Lie-Trotter算子分裂扭转、对称消融不稳定性、RoPE环面上庞加莱回归的O(1/√k)热力学抑制、热力学上下文极限相变，以及非平衡稳态参数涡旋。

Conclusion: 通过连续随机微分几何的视角分析Transformer，为大语言模型（Large Language Models）的稳定性极限、上下文界限和优化动力学提供了具有预测性和描述性的词汇体系。

Abstract: We present a continuous geometric framework that models the discrete algebraic operations of the Transformer architecture as an integro-differential equation (IDE) on a semantic fiber bundle $\calE = \calM \times \R^d$. Beginning from a single geometric axiom -- that the token sequence forms a discrete $1$-manifold equipped with a canonical measure lattice -- we translate every core component of the modern Transformer (RMSNorm, RoPE, Softmax Attention, FFN, Residual Stream, SGD, Weight Decay) into a cohesive vocabulary of differential geometry, measure theory, and stochastic calculus. The resulting framework yields quantitative predictions spanning entropic optimal transport (Attention as a Schrödinger bridge) and non-equilibrium thermodynamics (SGD as Itô diffusion violating detailed balance). We conduct a six-part experimental campaign across five architectures (Qwen3, LLaMA\nobreakdash-3.1, Gemma\nobreakdash-3, GPT-2, Mistral) spanning $124$M to $8$B parameters. The empirical observables are quantitatively consistent with the geometric predictions: the $ε^{-1/2}$ Lipschitz scaling calibration at machine precision ($R^2 = 1.000$), the Lie--Trotter operator-splitting torsion, the symmetric ablation instability confirming the Dual-Law of Topological Stability, the $\calO(1/\sqrt{k})$ thermodynamic suppression of Poincaré recurrence on the RoPE torus, the thermodynamic context-limit phase transition, and the Non-Equilibrium Steady State parameter vortex -- verified across two optimizers (AdamW and Pure SGD) to exclude momentum artifacts. The results demonstrate that analyzing Transformers through the lens of continuous stochastic differential geometry provides a predictive descriptive vocabulary for the stability limits, context bounds, and optimization dynamics of Large Language Models.

</details>


### [51] [Statistical-mechanics of a three-body Hopfield model with finite connectivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17234)
*Yushi Sugawara,Koji Hukushima*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本研究通过复制对称（replica-symmetric, RS）分析研究了定义在稀疏随机图（sparse random graph）上的三体Hopfield模型，发现三体相互作用导致不连续的记忆检索相变、顺磁与检索解的共存以及独特的旋节线结构。研究表明，稀疏连接与三体相互作用的结合会在单模式嵌入时产生自旋玻璃陷阱，并明确了存储容量与平均连接度的线性关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有两体稀疏Hopfield模型已被广泛研究，但三体相互作用（three-body interaction）在图结构稀疏连接条件下的动力学与热力学行为尚不清楚，特别是其对联想记忆（associative memory）的可访问性与存储容量的影响需要理论阐明。

Method: 采用复制对称（replica-symmetric）分析方法，将传统的有限连接两体Hopfield模型的泛函复制框架（functional replica framework）推广到三体情形；推导局部场分布（local-field distribution）的自洽方程，并通过种群动力学（population dynamics）进行数值求解；辅以有限规模蒙特卡罗模拟（finite-size Monte Carlo simulation）和种群退火（population annealing）进行验证。

Result: 三体Hopfield模型表现出不连续的检索转变、顺磁与检索解的共存以及独特的旋节线结构。从无先验信息的有限振幅场分布出发的RS种群动力学在低温下收敛到自旋玻璃类不动点而非检索态，该陷阱在单模式嵌入时即存在。增大嵌入模式数量会导致检索分支与玻璃态自由能分支交叉，使玻璃态在高负载时热力学稳定。存储负载特征性地与平均连接度呈线性关系。有限规模蒙特卡罗模拟支持RS对检索分支的描述并再现冷却陷阱行为，但玻璃态分支的偏差暗示低温玻璃态区域的复制对称破缺。

Conclusion: 该研究阐明了多体不连续性（many-body discontinuity）与稀疏图无序（sparse graph disorder）如何同时影响联想记忆的可访问性与容量，为理解稀疏连接网络中高阶相互作用对记忆检索行为的深层机制提供了理论依据。

Abstract: A three-body Hopfield model defined on sparse random graphs with finite mean connectivity is studied using a replica-symmetric (RS) analysis. By extending the functional replica framework for conventional two-body finite-connectivity Hopfield models, self-consistent equations for the local-field distribution are derived and solved numerically by population dynamics. In contrast to two-body sparse Hopfield models, three-body interactions induce a discontinuous retrieval transition, coexistence of paramagnetic and retrieval solutions, and a distinct spinodal structure. Starting the RS population dynamics from an uninformative finite-amplitude field distribution leads to a spin-glass-like fixed point at low temperatures rather than to the retrieval state. This trapping already occurs for a single embedded pattern, where conventional cross-talk noise among stored patterns is absent, indicating that it originates from the combination of sparse connectivity and three-body interactions. Within the RS description, increasing the number of embedded patterns drives a crossing between the retrieval and glassy free-energy branches, making the glassy branch thermodynamically stable at high load. Finite-size Monte Carlo simulations using population annealing support the RS description of the retrieval branch and reproduce the trapping behavior under cooling, while deviations from the RS spin-glass branch point to replica-symmetry breaking in the low-temperature glassy regime. The characteristic storage load scales linearly with the mean connectivity, reflecting the sparse number of couplings. These results clarify how many-body discontinuity and sparse graph disorder simultaneously influence the accessibility and capacity of associative memory.

</details>


### [52] [Semi-fractality and localization on a chiral Cayley tree](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18179)
*Carlo Vanoni,Vladimir E. Kravtsov,Boris L. Altshuler*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究无位无序（on-site disorder）的量子粒子在无限Cayley树上的跳跃，跳跃振幅服从奇异幂律分布，发现系统因手征对称性（chiral symmetry）产生半分形（semi-fractality）的波函数统计行为，并随跳跃分布指数变化经历从半分形到局域化的相变，在过渡区出现半局域化（semi-localized）态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在手征对称性下、仅含近邻跳跃振幅幂律奇异分布（无位无序）的量子系统，其能谱中心处的本征态统计行为是否会出现非传统的新奇形式。

Method: 采用群体动力学（population dynamics）数值求解传播子（propagator）的腔方程（cavity equations），分析局域态密度（local density of states）的分布函数。

Result: 局域态密度分布展现出宽幂律尾（broad power-law tails），导致波函数统计呈半分形：本征态占据系统的广泛部分（extensive fraction），但高阶矩（higher moments）行为类似多分形（multifractal）。局域态密度分布的对称性随跳跃分布指数连续变化，而非仅由对称类决定。系统随指数改变从半分形跨越到局域化相；在相变点，波函数呈现半局化态，支撑集（support）同时延展但高阶矩显示局域化。

Conclusion: 手征对称性与跳跃振幅的奇异幂律分布耦合，可产生半分形等新型波函数统计行为，且其临界性质受幂律指数连续调控，拓展了对无序系统中对称性与局域化相互作用的理解。

Abstract: We study a quantum particle hopping on an infinite Cayley tree with nearest-neighbor hopping amplitudes drawn from a distribution singular as $|t|^{-a}$ near weak links and no on-site disorder. Because the graph is bipartite, the model has chiral symmetry, which strongly affects the statistics of eigenstates at the center of the spectrum. Using population dynamics to solve the cavity equations for the propagator, we analyze the distribution of the local density of states and show that it develops broad power-law tails. These tails imply an unusual form of wave-function statistics, which we call semi-fractality: the eigenstates occupy an extensive fraction of the system, but their higher moments behave as in a multifractal state. We find that the symmetry properties of the local-density-of-states distribution are not fixed only by the symmetry class, but vary continuously with the exponent controlling the power-law hopping distribution. As this exponent is changed, the system crosses from a semi-fractal regime to a localized one. At the transition, the wave functions realize an extreme intermediate form that we call semi-localized, simultaneously extended in their support but localized according to higher moments.

</details>

### [53] [Asymptotic Equivalence Between Quasi-Grammian and Quasi-Wronskian $N$-Soliton Solutions of the Anti-Self-Dual Yang-Mills Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17749)
*Shan-Chi Huang*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文证明了反自对偶杨-米尔斯（ASDYM）方程在J-矩阵表述（Yang方程）中，N-孤子解的拟格拉姆型（quasi-Grammian）与拟朗斯基型（quasi-Wronskian）表示之间在相差一个常数矩阵因子的意义下具有渐近等价性。通过计算U(2)群下四维Wess-Zumino-Witten（WZW₄）模型的作用密度，验证了两种表示展示相同的渐近孤子轮廓，并显式获得了N-孤子碰撞的相移因子。孤子可视为流体动力学中KP/KdV型多孤子的四维类比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立ASDYM方程（Yang方程）的拟格拉姆型与拟朗斯基型N-孤子解表示之间的渐近等价关系，从而统一这两种表述方式，并揭示其与高维Sato理论的可能联系。

Method: 基于J-矩阵表述下的Yang方程（等价于四维WZW₄模型的运动方程），对G=U(2)情形计算WZW₄模型的作用密度，对比两种表示下的渐近孤子轮廓与相移因子，并给出N≤4的精确拟格拉姆型N-孤子解。

Result: 在相差一个常数矩阵因子的意义下，拟格拉姆型与拟朗斯基型表示渐近等价；两种表示在U(2)情形下呈现相同的渐近孤子轮廓，并能显式导出N-孤子碰撞的相移因子。此外，给出了N≤4的精确拟格拉姆型N-孤子解。

Conclusion: 由于孤子的类粒子性质，两种表示描述同一类ASDYM N-孤子解；这些孤子可视为KP/KdV型多孤子的四维类比，暗示ASDYM方程与高维Sato理论之间可能存在联系。

Abstract: Asymptotic equivalence between the quasi-Grammian and quasi-Wronskian representations of $N$-soliton solutions in the $J$-matrix formulation of the anti-self-dual Yang-Mills (ASDYM) equation is established up to a constant matrix factor. This formulation, known as the Yang equation, serves as the equation of motion of the four-dimensional Wess-Zumino-Witten (WZW$_4$) model and is equivalent to the ASDYM equation. To visualize the solitonic behavior, the action density of the WZW$_4$ model is evaluated for $\mathrm{G}=\mathrm{U}(2)$, demonstrating that the quasi-Grammian and quasi-Wronskian representations exhibit the same asymptotic soliton profiles, while the phase shift factors associated with $N$-soliton collisions are obtained explicitly. Hence, by virtue of the particle-like nature of solitons, the two representations describe the same class of ASDYM $N$-soliton solutions. These solitons can be regarded as a four-dimensional analogue of KP/KdV-type multi-solitons in fluid dynamics, suggesting a possible connection between the ASDYM equation and higher-dimensional Sato theory. Exact quasi-Grammian $N$-soliton solutions are also presented for $N\leq4$.

</details>


### [54] [Integrable Volterra hierarchies over nonabelian algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17868)
*J. P. Wang,S. Carpentier,A. V. Mikhailov*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文识别了一类介于量子代数（quantum algebras）与自由代数（free algebras）之间的新型非交换代数（noncommutative algebras），该代数与微分-差分可积方程的动力学相容，并通过非阿贝尔Volterra层级（nonabelian Volterra hierarchy）的约化将其推广至Toda晶格、Ablowitz-Ladik系统等广泛可积系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有的含非交换依赖变量的可积系统（integrable systems）通常构建于自由结合代数、量子代数或Grassmann代数之上。本文旨在为微分-差分可积方程寻找一类新的非交换代数，使其既与动力学相容，又能在代数结构上介于量子代数与自由代数之间。

Method: 通过分析非阿贝尔Volterra层级在新代数上的约化（reductions），展示该代数结构与微分-差分可积方程的相容性。该方法进一步扩展至Toda晶格、Ablowitz-Ladik系统等其他可积系统。

Result: 识别出一类新型非交换代数，其代数结构位于量子代数与自由代数之间，并与微分-差分可积方程的动力学相容。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法不仅适用于非阿贝尔Volterra层级，还可推广至包括Toda晶格、Ablowitz-Ladik系统在内的广泛可积系统家族。

Abstract: Known integrable systems with noncommutative dependent variables are typically formulated over free associative algebras, quantum algebras, or Grassmann algebras. For differential-difference integrable equations, we identify a new class of noncommutative algebras that is compatible with the dynamics and can be positioned between quantum and free algebras. In this brief communication, we consider reductions of the nonabelian Volterra hierarchy to new algebras. This approach extends to a broad class of integrable systems, including the Toda lattice, the Ablowitz-Ladik system, and many others.

</details>

### [55] [Measurement of the branching ratio of the $K^{+}\rightarrowπ^{+}ν\barν$ decay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16413)
*NA62 Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: NA62实验基于2023-2024年数据测得$K^+\toπ^+ν\barν$稀有衰变的分支比为$(7.2^{+2.3}_{-2.1})\times10^{-11}$，结合2016-2022年数据得到综合分支比$(9.6^{+1.9}_{-1.8})\times10^{-11}$，相对精度达20%，与标准模型（Standard Model）预言一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量稀有衰变$K^+\toπ^+ν\barν$的分支比，该衰变过程在标准模型（Standard Model）中受到高度压低（highly suppressed），对超出标准模型的新物理（new physics）信号敏感。

Method: 利用NA62实验在2023-2024年期间于CERN SPS收集的数据进行分支比测量，并将结果与2016-2022年数据联合分析，得到2016-2024年的综合测量值。

Result: 2023-2024年数据测得分支比${\rm B}_{\rm 2023-2024}=(7.2^{+2.3}_{-2.1})\times10^{-11}$；2016-2024年联合分析得到分支比${\rm B}_{\rm 2016-2024}=(9.6^{+1.9}_{-1.8})\times10^{-11}$，相对精度达到20%。

Conclusion: 测量结果与标准模型（Standard Model）预言一致，未发现显著的新物理（new physics）信号。

Abstract: The NA62 experiment has measured the branching ratio of the rare decay $K^+\toπ^+ν\barν$ using data collected in 2023 and 2024 at the CERN SPS, obtaining ${\rm B}_{\rm 2023-2024}(K^+\toπ^+ν\barν) = \left(7.2^{+2.3}_{-2.1}\right)\times10^{-11}$. With results from data collected between 2016 and 2022, the analysis gives ${\rm B}_{\rm 2016-2024}(K^+\toπ^+ν\barν) = \left(9.6^{+1.9}_{-1.8}\right)\times10^{-11}$, corresponding to a relative precision of $20\%$. This value is consistent with Standard Model predictions.

</details>


### [56] [Measuring the Acceleration-Dependent Temperature of the Minkowski Vacuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17744)
*Daine L. Danielson,Netta Engelhardt,Lindley A. Winslow*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出利用尾波加速器（wakefield accelerator）产生的高加速度梯度，结合前向实验室频率~太赫兹（THz）探测器阵列，测量加速观测者所经历的热辐射（Unruh效应），并利用量子细致平衡（quantum detailed balance）作为信号提取的独特手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Unruh效应是相对论性量子场论（relativistic quantum field theory）的重要预言，但至今未被直接观测到；现有技术条件下缺乏可行的实验方案。

Method: 利用尾波加速器提供的高加速度梯度来模拟非惯性系，配合前向实验室频率约太赫兹的探测器阵列，捕获由此产生的前向辐射信号，并通过量子细致平衡原理将信号与背景噪声分离。

Result: 文中未给出具体实验数据或结果，仅指出这一测量方案虽具有挑战性，但基于当前加速器与探测器技术已具备实现的可能性。

Conclusion: 所提出的实验方案为直接观测Unruh效应提供了现实可行的技术路径，有望在现有技术条件下实现验证。

Abstract: Relativistic quantum field theory is the structure on which the Standard Model and beyond-Standard Model physics are built. One of its most striking predictions is the Unruh effect: an accelerating observer measures the Minkowski vacuum as a thermal bath at a fixed temperature. Despite decades of theoretical interest, this effect has never been directly observed. We propose to use the high acceleration gradients provided by wakefield accelerators, coupled with a forward laboratory-frequency ~THz detector array, to measure the resulting forward-beamed radiation, and outline the unique signature provided by quantum detailed balance to extract the signal from backgrounds. While challenging, such a measurement appears within reach of present-day accelerator and detector technologies.

</details>


### [57] [Performance Enhancement of Gas Electron Multipliers Using an Optimized Single-Conical Hole Geometry for Different Charged Particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17756)
*Poojan Angiras,Sachin Rana,Md. Kaosor Ali Mondal,Shakir Eqbal,Amal Sarkar*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于Garfield$^{++}$和ANSYS模拟，系统比较了传统双锥形（bi-conical）与优化的单锥形（single-conical）GEM探测器对μ子、π介子、K介子和质子的响应性能，发现优化几何结构能有效改善有效增益与离子反流（ion backflow）之间的平衡，适用于未来高计数率微图案气体探测器（MPGD）应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 气体电子倍增器（Gas Electron Multiplier, GEM）是高能物理实验中探测带电粒子的关键组件，但传统双锥形GEM设计在高计数率环境下因离子反流（ion backflow）导致空间电荷积累和电场畸变，限制了性能。因此，需要对其几何结构进行优化，以提升对不同类型轻子和强子（如μ子、π介子、K介子、质子）的探测效率。

Method: 采用Garfield$^{++}$和ANSYS软件对传统双锥形（bi-conical）与优化的单锥形（single-conical）GEM探测器进行系统模拟，考察不同带电粒子（μ子、π介子、K介子、质子）在不同入射能量下的电离特性对电荷放大和离子反流的影响。

Result: 两种几何构型的探测器性能均表现出随粒子类型和入射能量变化的系统性差异。与双锥形设计相比，优化的单锥形几何结构在有效增益与离子反流之间取得了更好的平衡，显示出明显性能提升。

Conclusion: 几何优化是解决传统GEM在高计数率环境下性能限制的有效途径，单锥形GEM设计在改善增益与离子反流权衡方面具有优势，展现出应用于未来高计数率微图案气体探测器（MPGD）的潜力。

Abstract: Gas Electron Multipliers (GEMs) are essential detector components in modern high-energy physics experiments, where precise and stable detection of charged particles over a broad energy range is required. We present a comprehensive Garfield$^{++}$ and ANSYS-based study of conventional bi-conical and optimized single-conical GEM detectors to investigate the performance of the GEM detector for muons ($μ$), pions ($π$), kaons ($K$), and protons ($P$), which constitute the dominant charged particles measured directly in collider-based experiments. The aim is to examine the impact of particle-dependent ionization characteristics on charge amplification and ion backflow, and to evaluate the potential of an optimized GEM configuration for different leptons and hadrons. The conventional bi-conical GEM design does not always operate at optimal efficiency, as ion backflow can lead to space-charge accumulation and electric field distortions, ultimately limiting performance in high-rate environments. Thus, geometrical optimization is essential to address these limitations and enhance detector performance. A single-conical hole geometry is introduced and systematically compared with the conventional bi-conical design. For both of these configurations, the results exhibit clear and systematic variations in the detector performance with the particle type and the incident energy. The optimized geometry improves the balance between effective gain and ion backflow, demonstrating its potential for future high-rate MPGD applications.

</details>

Riedl,D. I. Ryabchikov,A. Rychter,A. Rymbekova,V. D. Samoylenko,A. Sandacz,S. Sarkar,I. A. Savin,G. Sbrizzai,H. Schmieden,A. Selyunin,S. Seriubin,L. Sinha,D. Spulbeck,A. Srnka,M. Stolarski,M. Sulc,H. Suzuki,S. Tessaro,F. Tessarotto,A. Thiel,F. Tosello,A. Townsend,V. Tskhay,B. Valinoti,B. M. Veit,J. F. C. A. Veloso,A. Vijayakumar,M. Virius,M. Wagner,S. Wallner,K. Zaremba,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zemko,E. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用COMPASS（Common Muon and Proton Apparatus for Structure and Spectroscopy）探测器的高统计量数据，测量了π⁻p → η⁽ᐟ⁾π⁻ p反应的周边产生（peripheral production），并首次对ηπ⁻和η′π⁻系统的高质量区进行无分箱分析（unbinned analysis），以解耦其交换机制。

Result: 在两个反应道中均以超过5σ的显著性（high significance）首次观测到高能散射中的奇异雷吉子，该信号很可能对应于奇异介子π₁(1600)。

Conclusion: 实验首次在高能散射中观测到与π₁(1600)相关的奇异雷吉子，为理解奇异介子的产生机制提供了直接证据。

Abstract: We present new \compass high-statistics measurements of the peripheral production of $ηπ^-$ and $η^\prime π^-$ pairs in the reactions $π^- p \to η^{(\prime)}π^- p$. For the first time, we perform an unbinned analysis of the high-mass region of the $ηπ^-$ and $η^\primeπ^-$ systems, which allows us to disentangle the exchange mechanisms governing their production. We report the first observation in high-energy scattering of an exotic Reggeon with high significance exceeding $5\,σ$ for both channels, which is, most likely, related to the exotic $π_1(1600)$.8

### [59] [The Dimension of Nonterminating Resampling Computations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17469)
*Yunbei Xu*

Main category: cs.CC

TL;DR: 本文研究随机算法几乎必然终止（almost sure termination）的边界条件，通过生存后缀（survival tail）、柯尔莫哥洛夫复杂度（Kolmogorov complexity）和豪斯多夫维数（Hausdorff dimension）刻画算法永不终止的例外随机纸带集合；主要定理在修复矩阵（repair matrices）可交换的条件下，对任意确定性非预见选择器（nonanticipating selector）给出了生存前缀权重和的上界，并应用于有界依赖k-SAT（bounded-dependence k-SAT）的指数终止性与有效维数分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机算法即使几乎必然终止，仍存在使算法永不终止的例外随机纸带（exceptional random tapes）；已有理论无法充分刻画这类例外集合的结构和大小，亟需建立统一的度量框架以描述非终止集合的复杂性与维数特征。

Method: 利用生存后缀的权重和上界（对生存前缀w求和ΣP[w]^s）、柯尔莫哥洛夫复杂度以及豪斯多夫维数（Hausdorff dimension）作为分析工具；通过修复矩阵（repair matrices）在幂次s上可交换的条件建立主定理；引入有效维数（effective dimension）和迹增长（trace growth）概念用于有界依赖k-SAT分析；采用精确后验似然恒等式（exact backward likelihood identity）补充尾部与编码界。

Result: 对于同一有限纸带源（finite tape source）上的两条重叠分歧修复规则（disagreement-repair rules），尽管具有相同的普通核（ordinary kernel）和停时律，非终止维数（nontermination dimension）可分别趋近于0和1；在相同源功率（source-power）水平下，同一条支配纸带源（dominated tape source）使一条规则永不终止而另一条具有指数终止尾部；对于有界依赖k-SAT，条件块最小熵（conditional block min-entropy）高于迹增长阈值（trace-growth threshold）时给出指数终止；树公式（tree formulas）渐近达到最大度维数（maximum-degree dimension）和全局源界，团公式（clique formulas）在指定体制中达到图特定单步阈值。

Conclusion: 动作标签（action labels）若产生相同状态转移则在幂次一（power one）处不可见，却足以导致终止行为的根本性分离，说明传统停时律和普通核的刻画能力存在本质局限；所建立的维数框架为随机算法的终止性分析提供了比经典停时理论更精细的区分工具。

Abstract: A randomized algorithm may terminate almost surely even though exceptional random tapes make it run forever. This paper studies the survival tail, the Kolmogorov complexity of one such tape, and the Hausdorff dimension of all of them. For each $s>0$ at which the powered repair matrices commute, the main theorem bounds $\sum_wP[w]^s$ over surviving prefixes $w$, uniformly over deterministic nonanticipating selectors. The case $s=1$ controls termination; the full family gives weak-source and dimension bounds.
  The source powers contain information absent even from the ordinary repair kernel and the complete stopping-time law. Under one common finite tape source, two overlapping disagreement-repair rules on a four-vertex path have the same ordinary kernels and the same stopping-time law for every selector, yet their nontermination dimensions can be arbitrarily close to zero and one. At one common source-power level, the same dominated tape source makes one rule run forever but gives the other an exponential stopping tail. The separation is caused by action labels that produce the same state transition and are therefore invisible at power one. For bounded-dependence $k$-SAT, conditional block min-entropy above the trace-growth threshold gives exponential termination, and the effective dimension of an individual infinite run is bounded by the trace growth induced by the clauses repaired infinitely often. Tree formulas asymptotically attain the maximum-degree dimension and global source bounds, while clique formulas attain the graph-specific one-step threshold in the stated regime. An exact backward likelihood identity complements these setwise results with tail and coding bounds for each run.

</details>

### [60] [A principled closure framework for higher-order SIS epidemic models on networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18003)
*Kevin Teo,Peter L Simon,István Zoltán Kiss*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种自下而上的高阶SIS流行病模型推导框架，通过网络相关的闭包算子在节点、边、三元组和四体相互作用层面系统构建矩闭包近似，并揭示已有启发式模型背后隐含的结构与动力学假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高阶网络（higher-order networks）中SIS流行病模型的矩闭包近似存在组合爆炸问题，现有模型均采用启发式推导，其背后的结构与动力学假设不透明，缺乏系统性的推导方法。

Method: 从节点层面方程出发，逐步构建对、三元组及三体相互作用的矩方程，引入网络依赖的闭包算子（closure operator），利用局部成对和三元结构生成拓扑适当的近似，并以此框架统一和还原已有模型。

Result: 本框架将Burgio等人的最大团（maximal clique）模型、Malizia等人的成对基（pair-based）模型和跨阶（inter-order）模型作为特例恢复，并揭示了Malizia等人的跨阶重叠参数（inter-order overlap parameter）单独不足以表达该模型，其原始推导隐含了额外的结构假设。

Conclusion: 该框架为高阶流行病建模提供了系统性基础，揭示了启发式平均场闭包中隐含的假设，并为生成新型模型提供了原则性路径。

Abstract: Susceptible-infected-susceptible (SIS) epidemic models on networks are governed by hierarchical moment equations where the dynamics of smaller subsystems depend on the state of larger ones. Moment closure approximations, which truncate this hierarchy by expressing higher-order state probabilities in terms of lower-order ones, are essential for obtaining tractable reduced systems. Higher-order networks, which extend the pairwise structure to include group interactions, introduce a combinatorial explosion of closure configurations, making systematic derivation harder. Consequently, existing higher-order SIS models are derived heuristically, where structural and dynamical assumptions underpinning their closures are not always apparent from the formulation alone. We develop a bottom-up derivation of higher-order SIS dynamics, building systematically from node-level equations to pairs, triplets, and three-body interactions. Central to our approach is a network-dependent closure operator that generates topologically appropriate approximations from local pairwise and triadic structure. Using this framework, we recover three existing higher-order SIS models--Burgio et al.'s maximal clique, Malizia et al.'s pair-based and inter-order models--as special cases, each arising under specific topological and dynamical assumptions. Our derivation reveals assumptions that are invisible from heuristic approaches: for instance, Malizia et al.'s inter-order overlap parameter is insufficient alone to express the model within our framework despite performing well against simulations, with the original derivation implicitly invoking additional structural assumptions. Our framework offers both a foundation for higher-order epidemic modeling and a constructive pathway for understanding the assumptions implicit in heuristically derived mean-field closures and provides a principled method of generating new models.

</details>

### [61] [Non-symmetric vector dyson equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16333)
*Jiaoyang Huang,Zhonggen Su,Ruizhe Xu*

Main category: math.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究向量戴森方程（vector Dyson equation），建立了解的完全测度分解与正则性，并发展了一种图论方法来分析非对称矩阵的奇异性和稳定性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究向量戴森方程的解的结构性质，特别是针对非对称矩阵（non-symmetric matrices）的奇异性（singularity）与稳定性（stability）问题，此前缺乏系统的图论分析框架。

Method: 首先证明向量戴森方程在复上半平面（complex upper half-plane）上存在唯一解，并建立其测度分解与正则性。随后引入基于图论（graph-theoretic）的方法，利用矩阵S的图结构识别稳定性算子（stability operator）在z趋近实轴时的退化模式。

Result: 对于非回溯矩阵（non-backtracking matrices），证明在正则边（regular edges）处成立平方根增长（square-root growth），在正则尖点（regular cusps）处成立立方根增长（cubic-root growth），并给出完整的稳定性估计。此外，还获得了周期设定下对称矩阵的相应估计。

Conclusion: 图结构有效刻画了非对称矩阵戴森方程解的奇异性类型，为随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）和谱分析提供新的分析工具。

Abstract: We study the vector Dyson equation $$-\frac{1}{m(z)}=z\mathbf{1}+\mathbf{a}+Sm(z),$$ with parameter $z$ in the complex upper half-plane $\mathbb{C}_+$, where $\mathbf{a}\in\mathbb R^d$ and $S$ is a nonnegative matrix, not necessarily symmetric. This equation has a unique vector solution $m(z)\in\mathbb{C}_+^d$, for which we establish a complete measure decomposition and prove regularity. We then develop a graph-theoretic approach to the singularity and stability problem for non-symmetric matrices $S$. The graph structure of $S$ identifies the possible degeneracies of the stability operator as $z$ approaches the real axis. In particular, for non-backtracking matrices, we prove square-root growth at regular edges, cubic-root growth at regular cusps, and complete stability estimates. We also obtain the corresponding estimates for symmetric matrices in the periodic setting.

</details>

### [62] [Nonlocal Electrostatic Field Theory from Microscopic Description](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16429)
*Varazdat Stepanyan,Yevgeni Sh. Mamasakhlisov,Armen E. Allahverdyan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究从微观运动方程出发，构建了一个统一的平均场福克-普朗克方程（mean field Fokker-Planck equation），用以描述非局域非线性系统的非平衡静电学，并得到了广义泊松-玻尔兹曼方程（generalized Poisson-Boltzmann equation）及静电自由能表达式。在线性近似下，论文发现各向同性流体中存在各向异性磁化率（anisotropic susceptibility），从而实现了静电学中的局域线性响应反演。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软材料中电场的研究通常分裂为两条路径：非线性理论中的点状粒子（point-like particles, 局域）研究，或非局域线性理论中有限大小粒子（particles with finite sizes）的使用。本工作旨在弥合这一分裂，构建一个统一框架。

Method: 从微观运动方程出发，构建了一个统一的平均场福克-普朗克方程，该方程适用于非局域非线性系统。通过该方程，推导出广义泊松-玻尔兹曼方程及静电自由能表达式，并在线性近似下进行解析处理。

Result: 在线性近似下，在各向同性流体（isotropic fluid）中获得了各向异性磁化率，使得静电学中的局域线性响应反演（local linear response inversion）成为可能。

Conclusion: 本工作为软材料中非局域非线性系统的非平衡静电学提供了一个统一的平均场理论框架，并在线性近似下揭示了各向同性流体中磁化率的各向异性特性。

Abstract: The study of electric fields in soft materials converges either to the study of point-like particles (local) in nonlinear theories or to the use of particles with finite sizes in nonlocal linear theories. In this work we start from the microscopic equations of motion and construct a unified mean field Fokker-Planck equation that describes the non-equilibrium electrostatics of nonlocal nonlinear systems. We obtain a generalized Poisson-Boltzmann equation for such systems as well as their electrostatic free energy expression. In the linear approximation we obtain an anisotropic susceptibility in an isotropic fluid which allows for local linear response inversion in electrostatics.

</details>


### [63] [Unified Theory of Relaxation in Equilibrium and Nonequilibrium Glass-Forming Liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16460)
*Zi-Long Wang,Qi-Lu Yuan,Yun-Jiang Wang,Jack F. Douglas,Matteo Baggioli,Zhao-Yan Sun,Wen-Sheng Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过模拟研究，揭示了稳态剪切驱动下玻璃形成液体的结构弛豫机制：外部驱动抑制了平衡态中控制弛豫的弦状协同运动，导致动力学显著加快；基于集体运动与涨落-耗散关系独立确定的剪切依赖有效温度的理论，无需额外非平衡拟合参数即可定量预测全温度与剪切率范围内的结构弛豫时间，表明平衡与非平衡弛豫受相同协同机制支配，但处于不同的有效热力学条件下。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解结构弛豫（structural relaxation）如何从平衡条件演化到非平衡条件是玻璃物理学（glass physics）中的一个核心问题。

Method: 采用模型玻璃形成体在稳态剪切（steady shear）下的模拟方法，并基于集体运动（collective motion）与由涨落-耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relations）独立确定的剪切依赖有效温度（shear-dependent effective temperature）构建理论框架。

Result: 外部驱动逐步抑制了平衡态中控制弛豫的弦状协同重排（stringlike cooperative rearrangements），导致动力学显著加快；所提出的理论无需额外非平衡拟合参数，即可定量预测全温度与剪切率范围内的结构弛豫时间（structural relaxation time）。

Conclusion: 平衡与非平衡弛豫受相同的潜在协同机制支配，但在稳态剪切下发生于不同的有效热力学条件；该研究为玻璃形成液体中热驱动与机械驱动动力学提供了统一的微观描述。

Abstract: Understanding how structural relaxation evolves from equilibrium to nonequilibrium conditions remains a central problem in glass physics. Using simulations of model glass formers under steady shear, we show that external driving progressively suppresses the stringlike cooperative rearrangements that control relaxation in equilibrium, leading to dramatically faster dynamics. A theory based on collective motion and a shear-dependent effective temperature independently determined from fluctuation-dissipation relations quantitatively predicts the structural relaxation time across the full range of temperatures and shear rates investigated without additional nonequilibrium fitting parameters. These results show that equilibrium and nonequilibrium relaxation are governed by the same underlying cooperative mechanism, but they occur under different effective thermodynamic conditions under steady shear. More broadly, our study provides a unified microscopic description of thermal and mechanically driven dynamics in glass-forming liquids.

</details>


### [64] [The hydrodynamic Euler-elastica: shape transitions in the dynamical buckling of elastic filaments in Stokes flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16468)
*Clément Moreau,Laetitia Giraldi,Hermes Bloomfield-Gadêlha*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过粗粒化数值模型研究粘性流体中弹性细丝（filament）的屈曲动力学，发现三种长时标形态模式（翻转、环结、打结），其主导由无量纲屈曲数（buckling number Bu）控制，形态转变源于前三个曲率模态（curvature mode）的竞争，且存在对小扰动的确定性敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弹性细丝在粘性流体中的屈曲（buckling）广泛存在于鞭毛（flagella）、微管（microtubules）和DNA等生物体系中，但传统静态Euler-弹性杆（Euler-elastica）理论无法解释动态屈曲时出现的复杂不可预测形态，因此需要探索其长时标动力学行为。

Method: 采用粗粒化数值模型（coarse-grained numerical model）模拟Stokes流中细丝屈曲的长时标动力学，并通过傅里叶分析（Fourier analysis）研究形状模态的竞争机制与衰减规律。

Result: 识别出三种不同形态学区域（morphological regimes）：翻转（flip）、环结（loop）和打结（knot），其主导性由无量纲屈曲数Bu决定；形态转变源于前三个曲率模态的竞争，高阶模态衰减服从指数律；在某些参数区间，相近初始条件对应共存的不同形态，表明存在对小扰动的确定性敏感性（deterministic sensitivity）。

Conclusion: 本研究连接了静态与动态屈曲理论，对理解生物推进机制以及微观细长游泳体（microscale slender swimmers）的设计具有启示意义。

Abstract: The buckling of elastic filaments in viscous fluids, ubiquitous in biological systems like flagella, microtubules, and DNA, has long been described by the static Euler-elastica. Yet, when such filaments buckle dynamically, their shapes defy static predictions, exhibiting complex, unpredictable behaviours. Here, we use a coarse-grained numerical model to explore the long-timescale dynamics of filament buckling in Stokes flow, revealing three distinct morphological regimes, termed flip, loop, and knot. The dominance of each regime is primarily governed by the dimensionless buckling number $\mathrm{Bu}$. Fourier analysis shows that these transitions between shape regimes arise from competition between the first three curvature modes, with high-order modes decay fitting an exponential law. In some parameter ranges, distinct shapes coexist for close initial conditions, indicating deterministic sensitivity to small perturbations. These findings bridge static and dynamic buckling theories, with implications for biological propulsion and the design of microscale slender swimmers.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文在三维（3D）结构中实现了全向拓扑弹性（omnidirectional topological elasticity），通过引入弯曲刚度（bending stiffness）将零频拓扑力学态提升为有限频声子模式，实验与数值结果验证了由体拓扑极化（bulk topological polarization）与边界局域表面模式共同驱动的稳健非对称能量隔离，为三维超材料（metamaterials）在振动屏蔽与定向波操控方面提供了新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑极化弹性（topologically polarized elasticity）在低维体系中已得到广泛研究，但其三维对应物仍基本未被探索。

Method: 在三维结构中引入弯曲刚度，将原本存在于零频率的拓扑力学态（topological mechanical states）提升为有限频率声子模式（phononic modes）；通过体拓扑极化与边界局域表面模式的相互作用实现力学行为的高度极化。

Result: 该三维结构在所有空间维度上均表现出高度极化的力学行为，建立了全向非对称拓扑弹性（omnidirectional asymmetric topological elasticity）。实验与数值结果证实了稳健的非对称能量隔离效果。

Conclusion: 研究成果为三维超材料建立了新范式，在振动屏蔽（vibration shielding）与定向波操控（directional wave manipulation）等领域具有应用前景。

Abstract: Topologically polarized elasticity has been extensively studied in lower-dimensions, yet its three-dimensional (3D) counterpart remains largely unexplored. Here, we demonstrate omnidirectional topological elasticity in 3D structures that incorporate bending stiffness, which elevates zero-frequency topological mechanical states into finite-frequency phononic modes. These modes are localized at a single boundary, creating a pronounced stiffness contrast in both static and finite-frequency dynamic regimes. This three-dimensional structure exhibits highly polarized mechanical behavior across all spatial dimensions, establishing omnidirectional asymmetric topological elasticity. Experimental and numerical results confirm robust, asymmetric energy isolation, arising from the interplay between bulk topological polarization and boundary-localized surface modes. Our findings establish a paradigm for 3D metamaterials, with promising applications in vibration shielding and directional wave manipulation.

### [66] [Rolling pepper shaker on a slope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16711)
*Mizuki Ono,Hirofumi Wada*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验与理论相结合的方式，分析了部分填充颗粒介质的刚性圆柱体在斜面上的滚动行为，发现了包括阻尼振荡停止、蜿蜒崩塌停止等多种滚动模式，建立了相图，并基于刚体力学和颗粒介质静力学解释了停止与滚动之间的转变及相边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 日常生活中固体物体的滚动行为看似平凡，但当固体具有内部自由度（如半充水瓶）时，其运动可能极为复杂且物理丰富。现有研究常假设滚动过程中无滑移，但对实际存在显著滑移的现象理解不足，缺乏对不同滚动行为的系统分类与物理机制解释。

Method: 采用实验与理论相结合的方法。实验上观察部分填充颗粒介质的刚性圆柱体在斜面上的滚动行为；理论上基于刚体力学（rigid-body mechanics）结合颗粒介质静力学（statics of granular media）解释行为转变与相边界。

Result: 实验发现多种滚动行为：阻尼振荡后停止、蜿蜒崩塌后停止、平稳滚动以及恒定加速度滚动。发现了滚动过程中存在显著的滑移（slip）。将滚动行为划分为三个不同阶段并建立了相图。

Conclusion: 从理论上解释了停止与滚动之间的转变，并基于刚体力学和颗粒介质静力学合理化了相边界。该研究不仅满足对日常现象的好奇心，还对粉末制造技术（powder manufacturing technologies）到机器人学（robotics）等广泛物理应用具有重要启示。

Abstract: Although the rolling of a solid object is a mundane phenomenon in our daily life, its movement can be surprisingly complex and physically rich, particularly when the solid object has certain internal degrees of freedom, such as a half-filled plastic bottle of water. The translational and rotational motion of such an object couple in a highly nontrivial manner, often leading to seemingly unpredictable trajectories. We use a combination of experimental and theoretical approaches to analyze the rolling behaviors of a rigid cylinder that is partially filled with granular media, rolling on an inclined plane. We experimentally find a wide variety of rolling behaviors, including damped oscillation leading to a stop, meandering with avalanches coming to a stop, in addition to the stationary rolling and rolling with a constant acceleration. We address the occurrence of substantial slip during rolling, in contrast to what is often assumed. We classify the rolling behavior into three distinct phases and establish a phase diagram. We theoretically explain the transition between stopping and rolling and rationalize the phase boundary based on the rigid-body mechanics combined with the statics of granular media. Our study addresses the curiosity to understand the everyday phenomena and has significant implications for a wide range of physical applications from powder manufacturing technologies to robotics.
