### [67] [Theory of associating polymers with annealed and quenched sticker disorder: Mean-field solution and phase behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16807)
*Sofia Moschin,Achille Giacometti,Amos Maritan,Angelo Rosa*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种针对缔合高分子溶液的密度泛函理论（density-functional theory），通过局域二元自由度描述带电单体（stickers）之间的吸引作用，并在平均场水平上分别求解了退火（annealed）和淬火（quenched）电荷分布情形，得到了定性不同的自由能泛函。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论在处理缔合高分子中带电单体间的吸引相互作用时缺乏统一的场论框架，特别是在退火与淬火两种电荷分布情形下的系统比较尚未明确建立。

Method: 将Garel与Orland针对单链系统的场论方案扩展到相互作用的链系综，精确构建了退火与淬火两种电荷分布下的模型，并在平均场（mean-field）水平求解。

Result: 退火情形下，理论自然产生了一个非平凡的标量序参量（order parameter）用于描述键合粘附单体（sticker monomers）的比例，并在鞍点（saddle point）处得到自洽的质量作用定律（mass-action law）。淬火情形下则不出现独立的键合序参量，主要效应是有效两体和三体相互作用参数的重整化（renormalization）。

Conclusion: 该理论在哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）层面是微观的，并在同一场论框架内为超越平均场近似的涨落修正提供了系统的出发点。

Abstract: We develop a density-functional theory for solutions of associating polymers where attractions among charged monomers (stickers) are represented by local binary degrees of freedom, which are randomly placed along the chains. Extending the original Garel and Orland's field-theoretic scheme for single-chain systems to an ensemble of interacting chains, we give the exact formulations of the model in both cases of annealed and quenched distributions of charges which we solve at the mean-field level. The solution produces qualitatively different free energy functionals. In the annealed case, the theory naturally yields a nontrivial scalar order parameter for the fraction of bonded sticker monomers and a self-consistent mass-action law at the saddle point. By contrast, in the quenched case no independent bonding order parameter emerges and the main effect is a renormalization of the effective two-body and three-body interaction parameters. The formulation is microscopic at the Hamiltonian level and, within the same field-theoretic framework, provides a systematic starting point for fluctuation corrections beyond the mean-field approximation.

</details>


### [68] [Collective Ring Formation in Active Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16905)
*Debraj Dutta,Urna Basu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了二维相互作用活性粒子系统中环状结构的形成，推导了活性布朗粒子（active Brownian particles）和跑动-翻滚粒子（run-and-tumble particles）的径向分布与极化分布的精确解析表达式，揭示了两类活性模型在强活性区域中空间与取向组织的定性差异，并建立了统一分析框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解活性物质（active matter）中自组织环状结构的形成机制，以及不同推进机制（propulsion mechanism）如何影响其空间与取向组织。

Method: 通过解析推导，分别对活性布朗粒子（active Brownian particles）和跑动-翻滚粒子（run-and-tumble particles）两种模型，得到径向分布（radial distribution）和极化分布（polarization distribution）的精确解析表达式。

Result: 两种模型均呈现环形稳态（annular steady states），但在强活性区域（strongly active regime）中，其空间组织和取向组织存在定性差异；推进机制的本质决定了环状结构与粒子取向统计的不同。

Conclusion: 研究提供了一个统一的解析框架，用于表征活性物质中的环形态，并识别出区分连续与离散重新定向（continuous and discrete reorientation）的持久活性动力学（persistent active dynamics）的鲁棒特征（robust signatures）。

Abstract: We study the formation of ring-like structures in interacting active particle systems in two dimensions. The emergent structure shows signatures of both spatial and orientational organization. The spatial organization is characterized by the radial distance of a tagged particle from the centroid of the assembly, while orientational organization is characterized by the radial alignment of its self-propulsion direction. We derive exact analytical expressions for the radial and polarization distributions for systems of active Brownian particles and run-and-tumble particles. While both models exhibit annular steady states, we show that their spatial and orientational organization differ qualitatively in the strongly active regime. A direct comparison of the two models reveals how the nature of the propulsion mechanism leads to the distinction in both the structure of the annulus and the statistics of particle orientations. Our results provide a unified analytical framework for characterizing emergent annular states in active matter and identify robust signatures that distinguish persistent active dynamics with continuous and discrete reorientation.

</details>


### [69] [To win, a model must thin: Capillary thinning as a benchmark complex flow for constitutive models of viscoelastic polymer solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17197)
*Ranganathan Prabhakar,Joseph P. Connell*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出应将毛细断裂流变学（CBR）中的液桥拉伸过程视为检验本构模型的基准复杂流动，而非仅用于测量单一松弛时间；通过引入弹性魏森贝格数（Wi_e）和弹性毛细Pipkin图（elastocapillary Pipkin diagram）重新组织实验数据，并利用C2D2模型解释表观松弛时间的系统变化性，揭示其源于构象-浓度依赖拖拽与线圈-拉伸滞后效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 毛细断裂流变学（CBR）传统上被视为测量单一松弛时间的工具，但实验发现表观松弛时间随聚合物浓度、设备几何和制备方案系统变化。现有模型（如FENE-P）无法解释这种变异性，表明需要新的框架来理解拉伸主导流动中的普遍规律。

Method: 将CBR实验的输出重新解释为自选弹性应变率，通过弹性魏森贝格数（Wi_e）表示，并构建弹性毛细Pipkin图——以弹性魏森贝格数（Wi_e）为纵轴、几何控制的德博拉数（Deborah number）为横轴。采用单模中细丝应力平衡导出具有普适特征的Pipkin曲线族，并通过缩放分析将其坍缩为一条主曲线，其中弹性起始参考德博拉数吸收了未测量的初始预拉伸。

Result: 单模应力平衡导出的Pipkin曲线展现两个普适特征：低De_0平台和有限延伸性约束的上升。缩放分析将曲线坍缩为一条主曲线。构象与浓度依赖拖拽（C2D2）模型通过线圈-拉伸滞后效应将平台值降低至Entov-Hinch值以下，并成功组织跨越多个数量级的分子量和浓度数据，而经典FENE-P模型无法做到。

Conclusion: Pipkin图框架为不同类聚合物溶液绘制主曲线提供了路径，阐明了拉伸主导流动中的普遍性特征，并将表观松弛时间的变异性从缺陷重新定义为复杂流动的固有属性。

Abstract: Capillary thinning of a liquid bridge is an exemplar of complex flow, where the macroscopic geometry couples tightly to the microscopic evolution of polymer conformations. Since its inception, capillary-breakup rheometry (CBR) has been viewed as a tool for measuring a single relaxation time. Yet experiments show that the apparent relaxation time depends systematically on polymer concentration, device geometry, and the preparation protocol. We argue that this variability is not a flaw, but evidence that thinning should be treated as a benchmark complex flow for testing constitutive models. We recast the output of a CBR experiment as the self-selected elastic strain rate, expressed through the elastic Weissenberg number Wi_e, rather than an apparent relaxation time, and organize it in an elastocapillary Pipkin diagram -- Wi_e against a geometry-controlled Deborah number. A single-mode, mid-filament stress balance yields a family of Pipkin curves with universal features -- a low-De_0 plateau and a finite-extensibility-constrained rise -- that a scaling analysis collapses onto a master curve, with an elastic-onset-referenced Deborah number absorbing the unmeasured initial prestretch. The Conformation- and Concentration-Dependent Drag (C2D2) model, acting through coil-stretch hysteresis, lowers the plateau below the Entov-Hinch value and organizes data spanning decades in molecular weight and concentration, across a range of devices, where the classical FENE-P model cannot. The Pipkin diagram framework offers a path toward master plots for classes of polymer solutions, clarifying what is universal in extension-dominated flows.

</details>


### [70] [Universal Jamming Criticality and Self-Organizing Principles from Disorder to the Limit of Perfect Crystalline Order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17549)
*Jianhua Zhang,Jiaqi Si,Ning Xu,Hua Tong*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过系统调控从晶体到完全无序的弹性堆积结构，揭示无序固体的力学性质普遍受堆积临界性（jamming criticality）支配，并发现堆积密度可趋近密堆积，表明堆积临界性与玻璃转变物理之间存在根本性解耦；此外，边缘堆积态中普遍存在接触超均匀性（contact hyperuniformity），与粒子级结构无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶体由周期性有序定义，而非晶固体的本质因其无序、多样且非平衡的结构特征而难以捉摸；本文旨在通过系统调控无序程度，揭示无序固体中涌现刚性的普适底层机制。

Method: 以弹性堆积（jammed elastic packings）为研究对象，系统调控结构从晶态到完全无序，通过分析堆积转变（jamming transition）附近的标度行为（scaling behaviors），并引入接触级无序（contact-level disorder）导致的随机非仿射弹性（random nonaffine elasticity）进行机制解释。

Result: 力学性质普遍受堆积临界性支配，在堆积转变附近呈现特征标度行为，唯密堆积奇异点除外；堆积密度可趋近密堆积，表明堆积临界性与玻璃转变物理（glass transition physics）解耦；边缘堆积态（marginally jammed states）中配位数分布与接触超均匀性具有普适性，与粒子级结构无关。

Conclusion: 研究结果为无序固体中涌现刚性提出了一种普适的组织机制（general organizing mechanism），强调了堆积物理学（jamming physics）的广泛适用性，并补充了力学自组织（mechanical self-organization）原理。

Abstract: While crystals are defined by periodic order, the nature of amorphous solids remains elusive due to their disordered, diverse, and nonequilibrium structures. Here, we focus on jammed elastic packings and systematically tune structure from crystalline to fully disordered to unveil the universal underlying characteristics. We demonstrate that their mechanical properties are universally governed by jamming criticality, featuring characteristic scaling behaviors near the jamming transition, excepting the singular close-packed point. This is facilitated by random nonaffine elasticity arising from contact-level disorder. Consequently, the jamming density can approach close packing, suggesting a fundamental decoupling between jamming criticality and the glass transition physics. Moreover, we uncover a universal coordination-number distribution and contact hyperuniformity in marginally jammed states, independent of particle-level structure. These findings suggest a general organizing mechanism for emergent rigidity in disordered solids, underscore the broad relevance of jamming physics, and complement principles of mechanical self-organization.

### [71] [History-dependent discharge of compressed particle rafts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17683)
*Mario Nabernik,Gregor Plohl,Kathrin Schulte,Carole Planchette*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过颗粒筏（particle rafts）的单轴压缩后通过局部收缩（constriction）的松弛实验，发现了一种可重复且持续的“老化（aging）”过程。该过程表现为颗粒迁移率与筏的可变形性逐渐增加，宏观松弛程度与介观流动特征（如颗粒通量、剪切带宽度及颗粒重排）相关。老化源于颗粒受约束地通过收缩口，其微观机制可能与颗粒周围接触线的演化有关，该实验提供了一种控制与比较不同颗粒组装体中老化的简单方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 颗粒-液体界面（particle-laden interfaces）在自然与工业过程中至关重要，但其力学性质预测仍是一大挑战。这类系统兼具颗粒接触引发的颗粒材料特性与毛细相互作用（capillary interactions）赋予的弹性行为，对历史过程高度敏感。因此，理解其时间演化（老化）机制是当前研究的核心动机。

Method: 采用单轴压缩颗粒筏通过局部收缩的松弛实验作为模型体系（model experiment），分别对前端压缩（front-compressed）与后端压缩（back-compressed）的颗粒筏进行观测。通过分析宏观松弛程度、介观流动特征（颗粒通量、剪切带宽度、颗粒重排）以及微观机制推测来表征老化过程。

Result: 观察到可重复且持续的老化过程，表现为颗粒迁移率（particle mobility）与筏的可变形性（raft deformability）逐步增加。老化同时存在于前端压缩与后端压缩的颗粒筏中。宏观松弛程度与介观层面的颗粒通量增大、剪切带（shear zone）变宽及颗粒重排（particle rearrangements）增强相关。

Conclusion: 老化明确归因于颗粒受约束地通过收缩口，其微观起源可能与颗粒周围接触线（contact line）的演化有关。该收缩流实验提出了一个简单方法来控制和比较不同颗粒组装体中的老化行为，为理解颗粒筏的历史效应提供了新视角。

Abstract: While particle-laden interfaces play a central role in many natural and industrial processes, predicting their mechanical properties remains a major challenge. These systems combine granular characteristics conferred by particle-particle contacts with elastic behavior originating from capillary interactions, making them very sensitive to their history. Using the relaxation of uniaxially compressed particle rafts through a local constriction as a model experiment, we demonstrate the existence of a reproducible and continuous aging process. Aging is observed for both front- and back-compressed rafts and is characterized by a progressive increase in particle mobility and raft deformability. Macroscopic changes are seen, for example, in the extent of relaxation and are correlated with flow modifications observed at the mesoscopic level among which are increased particle fluxes, broader shear zones and enhanced particle rearrangements. While aging can be attributed unambiguously to the constrained passage of the particles through a constriction, its microscopic origin remains hypothetical, the results suggesting that contact lines around the particles may evolve. Beyond providing new insight into the effects of raft history, the proposed constriction flow experiment offers a simple method to control and compare aging in different particulate assemblies.

### [72] [Emergent odd response in active chiral films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17717)
*Seema Chahal,Naveen Kumar D,Brato Chakrabarti*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主动手性流体中的奇黏度（或霍尔黏度）作为一种无耗散输运系数已被广泛认可，但其如何从具体的微观相互作用中涌现仍未完全理解。本文旨在弥补这一空白。

Method: 基于经典剪切流变学，针对锚定在无滑移表面上的主动手性薄膜（如细菌地毯（bacterial carpet）），构建锚定粒子取向动力学的动理学理论（kinetic theory），推导其对剪切流的应力响应，并以非线性动理学理论数值解分析强剪切下的行为。

Result: 剪切诱导的重新取向导致流动对齐的极化（flow-aligned polarization）和横向表面牵引力（transverse surface traction），由此得到奇黏度张量的闭合解析形式。强剪切下，横向牵引力因剪切诱导取向动力学而出现饱和，表明偏离线性响应。

Conclusion: 奇黏度可自洽地作为主动流体-结构相互作用的粗粒化流变学特征而涌现；主动手性薄膜为奇流体动力学（odd hydrodynamics）提供了可控的新实验体系。

Abstract: Active chiral fluids can support a nondissipative transport coefficient known as odd (or Hall) viscosity. Hydrodynamic descriptions of such fluids typically introduce odd viscosity phenomenologically. How such a response emerges from specific microscopic interactions remains incompletely understood. Here, building on classical shear rheology, we microscopically derive an odd rheological response in active chiral films: thin layers of torque-exerting, elongated particles anchored to a no-slip surface. A canonical realization of such a film is the bacterial carpet, in which flagellated bacteria are tethered head-down to a solid surface while their flagella remain free to spin and inject angular momentum into the surrounding fluid. Using a kinetic theory for the orientational dynamics of these anchored particles, we derive their stress response to an imposed shear flow. We reveal that shear-induced reorientation leads to a flow-aligned polarization and a transverse surface traction from which the odd-viscosity tensor follows in closed form. Numerical solutions of the nonlinear kinetic theory further highlight saturation of the transverse traction at strong shear, driven by shear-induced orientation dynamics -- signaling departure from linear response. Our results demonstrate how odd viscosity can emerge self-consistently as a coarse-grained rheological signature of active fluid-structure interaction and establish active chiral films as a new controllable setting for odd hydrodynamics.

### [73] [Molecular chirality controls droplet division and helical fiber formation in liquid crystal emulsions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17856)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 向由可变形双表面活性剂界面（deformable two-surfactant interface）约束的向列相液晶液滴中加入手性掺杂剂，通过改变冷却条件实现形态控制；结合数值模拟分析手性驱动的界面弹性应力。

Conclusion: 胆甾相螺距可作为设计变量（design variable）精确控制液滴分裂，并使自发形成的介观结构的尺寸与温度依赖性解耦（decouple）。

Abstract: Molecular chirality is a source of broken mirror symmetry, but using it to control mesoscale structures with a tunable length scale remains challenging. Here, we demonstrate that adding a chiral dopant to nematic liquid crystal droplets bounded by a deformable two-surfactant interface controls their morphogenesis: the ratio of droplet diameter to cholesteric pitch determines whether droplets divide asymmetrically or symmetrically upon cooling, and whether they transform into single- or double-strand helical fibers. The fiber periodicity and thickness both scale linearly with the cholesteric pitch, which varies by less than 2% with temperature across the self-shaping window. Numerical simulations reveal that chirality-driven elastic stresses at the interface destabilize the droplets and trigger cusp-mediated shape transformations. These results establish cholesteric pitch as a design variable to precisely control droplet division and decouple the dimensions of spontaneously formed mesoscale structures from temperature dependence.

### [75] [Particle-scale structure of granular suspensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18090)
*Santos Bravo Yuste y Antonio M. Puertas*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过朗之万动力学（Langevin dynamics）模拟研究非平衡态颗粒悬浮液的微观结构，并检验了基于平衡态思想的有理函数近似（RFA）方法。研究发现，除最小波数区域外，RFA能准确描述径向分布函数和静态结构因子，优于Percus-Yevick近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 颗粒悬浮液具有内在的非平衡特性，耗散性颗粒碰撞与溶剂驱动力共存。目前对其微观结构的理论描述尚不完善，需要探索能否借鉴平衡态硬球体系的解析方法，构建适用于非平衡体系的近似理论框架。

Method: 采用由浸没在热浴中的非弹性硬球（inelastic hard spheres）构成的颗粒悬浮液模型，通过朗之万动力学模拟计算径向分布函数 $g(r)$ 和静态结构因子 $S(q)$。将平衡态硬球有理函数近似（RFA）中的接触值和类等温压缩率量替换为非平衡输入，从而在拉普拉斯空间和q空间得到解析表达式。

Result: RFA在较宽的密度、拖曳系数和非弹性系数范围内，都能很好地描述颗粒悬浮液的短程和中程结构。在非弹性状态下，RFA对 $g(r)$ 的复现显著优于Percus-Yevick近似，尤其在接触区域。对于 $S(q)$，除最小波数区域外RFA描述良好；最小波数处模拟结果显示存在依赖拖曳的增强，表明存在超出平衡类描述的额外长波非平衡关联。

Conclusion: 基于平衡态的硬球方法能够准确描述当前非弹性硬球朗之万模型的颗粒尺度结构（最小q区域除外）。类似平衡态启示的方法可能同样适用于相关的非平衡硬球悬浮液模型，包括多组分系统。

Abstract: Granular suspensions are intrinsically nonequilibrium systems in which dissipative grain-grain collisions coexist with solvent-induced forcing. We study the particle-scale structure of a granular suspension modeled by inelastic hard spheres immersed in a thermal bath and compare Langevin-dynamics simulation results for the radial distribution function $g(r)$ and the static structure factor $S(q)$ with predictions of an equilibrium-inspired rational function approximation (RFA). The equilibrium hard-sphere RFA is supplied with nonequilibrium input for the contact value and a reduced isothermal-compressibility-like quantity, yielding analytical expressions for $g(r)$ in Laplace space and for $S(q)$. We find that the RFA gives a very good description of the short- and intermediate-range structure of the suspension over a broad range of densities, drag coefficients, and inelasticities. It reproduces $g(r)$ substantially better than the Percus-Yevick approximation in inelastic states, especially near contact, and gives a good account of $S(q)$ except at the smallest wave numbers. There, simulations show a drag-dependent enhancement over the RFA prediction, indicating additional long-wavelength nonequilibrium correlations beyond the present equilibrium-like description. These results show that an equilibrium-based hard-sphere approach provides an accurate description of the particle-scale structure of the present Langevin model with inelastic hard spheres (except in the smallest-$q$ region), and suggest that similar equilibrium-inspired approaches may also be useful for related nonequilibrium hard-sphere suspension models, including multicomponent systems.

### [76] [Plastic smoothing of rough surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18208)
*B. N. J. Persson*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的有效功率谱（effective power spectra）方法，用于描述塑性变形后的粗糙表面，并将其整合进Persson接触力学理论（Persson contact mechanics theory），通过对比实验结果解释了塑性变形后表面粗糙度的不同演化模式（高斯型 vs. 偏斜型）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当两个金属块被挤压时，接触区域的微凸体（asperity）通常会发生塑性变形（plastic deformation），进而影响接触刚度（contact stiffness）、电阻、热阻和界面流体流动等许多摩擦学（tribology）性质。因此，需要一种能够描述塑性变形后表面形貌（surface topography）的有效方法。

Method: 提出了一种新的方式，用于获得塑性变形表面的有效功率谱，并将其应用于Persson接触力学理论中。随后，利用该塑性修正后的功率谱（plastically modified power spectra）计算表面高度形貌，并与Yusof和Ripin的实验结果进行对比。

Result: 对比实验结果显示，该方法能够再现塑性变形对表面形貌的影响。同时发现，某些表面在塑性变形后仍保持与变形前相似的高斯型粗糙度（Gaussian roughness），仅振幅减小；而另一些表面则呈现出高度偏斜的粗糙度（skewed roughness）。

Conclusion: 论文讨论了塑性变形后表面粗糙度呈现不同演化模式（高斯型 vs. 偏斜型）的原因，指出所提出的有效功率谱方法可有效用于描述塑性变形后的表面，并为接触力学理论提供输入。

Abstract: When two metal blocks are squeezed together the stresses in the asperity contact regions are usually so large that the asperities deform plastically, at least at short length scales. Many tribology properties of contacts, such as the contact stiffness and the electric and thermal contact resistance, and the fluid flow at interfaces, depend on the surface topography and are hence modified by the plastic flow. Here I present a new way to obtain an effective power spectra of plastically deformed surfaces to be used in the Persson contact mechanics theory. I also present results for the surface height topography obtained using the plastically modified power spectra, and compare to the experimental results of Yusof and Ripin, who studied the influence of plastic flow on the topography for a smooth steel surface squeezed against a rough steel surface. Finally, I discuss why some surfaces after plastic deformation have similar Gaussian roughness as before plastic deformation, only with smaller roughness amplitude, while other surfaces shows very skewed roughness after plastic deformation.

</details>

### [77] [Two-color solitons in Kerr third harmonic generation model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16435)

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文研究谐振克尔三次谐波产生（resonant Kerr third-harmonic generation）模型中的双色二维空间局域光模，发现两种局域态族，其动力学行为不遵循普适临界功率，而取决于谐波间的功率分布，并揭示了新的坍缩机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用计算工具（computational tools）对谐振克尔三次谐波产生模型中的双色二维空间局域光模进行数值研究。

Result: 识别出两种不同的局域态族：基频主导族（fundamental-dominated family）充当同时坍缩（collapse）与联合衍射（diffraction）之间的动力学分隔线（dynamical separatrix），而三次谐波主导族（third-harmonic-dominated family）则无此行为。此外，发现伴随三次谐波强振荡的谐振坍缩事件，揭示了标准克尔自聚焦（Kerr self-focusing）中不存在的坍缩机制。

Conclusion: 双色二维局域光模的动力学不由普适临界功率（universal critical power）决定，而依赖于谐波间的功率分布；谐振克尔三次谐波产生模型中存在超越标准克尔自聚焦的新坍缩机制。

Abstract: We investigate two-color, two dimensional spatially localized light modes in a resonant Kerr third-harmonic generation model. Using computational tools, we identify two distinct families of localized states. Unlike the single-component 2D nonlinear Schrödinger equation and previously studied non-resonant two-color systems, the dynamics are not dictated by a universal critical power, but depend on the distribution of power between the harmonics. The "fundamental-dominated" family acts as a "dynamical separatrix" between simultaneous collapse and joint diffraction, whereas the "third-harmonic-dominated" family does not. We further identify resonant collapse events accompanied by strong oscillations of the third harmonic, revealing a collapse mechanism absent from standard Kerr self-focusing.

### [78] [Multisine electrochemical impedance spectroscopy for Li-ion battery characterisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17832)
*Noël Hallemans,Heiko Seel-Mayer,Peter Keil,Stephen R. Duncan,David A. Howey*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文展示了在商用恒电位仪上对锂离子电池进行宽频范围（20 mHz 至 1 kHz）的高保真多正弦（multisine）电化学阻抗谱（EIS）测量，并与单正弦（single-sine）EIS进行了对比，同时在不同工作条件下（充放电、弛豫、温度变化）测量了宽带多正弦阻抗，揭示了该方法在电池动力学、材料性质、电荷转移过程及热性能方面的新见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电化学阻抗谱（electrochemical impedance spectroscopy, EIS）是一种有价值的非侵入式电池表征工具，传统上采用不同频率的正弦波顺序注入（单正弦法），但该方法实验时间较长，难以在运行工况下测量。多正弦（multisine）激励法可缩短实验时间并支持在工作条件下进行阻抗测量，因此需要系统验证其在高保真条件下的有效性并与传统单正弦法进行对比。

Method: 使用商用恒电位仪（commercial potentiostat）在锂离子电池上实施高保真多正弦EIS测量，频率范围覆盖20 mHz至1 kHz；同时进行单正弦（single-sine）EIS作为对照，并在线性性（linearity）和稳态性（stationarity）条件下对两种技术进行验证比较。此外，在充放电、弛豫（relaxation）及温度变化等不同工作条件下测量宽带多正弦阻抗。

Result: 多正弦EIS能在宽频范围内实现与单正弦EIS相当的高保真阻抗测量，同时显著缩短实验时间；该方法可在充放电、弛豫及温度变化等实际运行条件下稳定工作，为电池动力学、材料性质、电荷转移过程及热性能提供了新的测量数据。

Conclusion: 多正弦EIS是一种高保真、高效的阻抗测量方法，能够在运行工况下提供超出传统单正弦法的电池特性洞察，有助于深入理解电池的动力学行为、材料特性、电荷转移过程及热性能。

Abstract: Electrochemical impedance spectroscopy (EIS) is a valuable tool for non-invasive battery characterisation as it provides a compact data representation of physical processes over a wide range of time scales. Commonly, sinusoids at different frequencies are injected sequentially (single-sines). Alternatively, a multisine excitation (a sum of sines) is advantageous for reducing experiment time and allowing impedance to be measured during operational conditions (e.g.\ charging, discharging, relaxation, and during temperature changes). In this work, we demonstrate high-fidelity multisine EIS measurements on Li-ion cells over a wide frequency range (20 mHz to 1 kHz) taken with a commercial potentiostat, and compare these to single-sine EIS, discussing the advantages of both techniques and how to verify the conditions of linearity and stationarity. We also measure broadband multisine impedance at different operating conditions (during charging/discharging, relaxation, and temperature changes), showing how this tool gives new insights into battery dynamics, material properties, charge transfer processes, and thermal performance.

</details>

Conclusion: 实空间几何曲率为调控超导电流提供了可控机制，有望推动曲率电子学（curvature electronics）在超导器件中的应用。

Abstract: Real-space geometric curvature in magnetic thin films introduces a controllable mechanism for tailoring the pathways of superconducting steady-state Josephson currents via the proximity effect. We present a generalized Green's function method for calculating diffusive transport in arbitrarily curved surfaces, and show how the competing mechanisms of curvature and distance regulate conversion between different superconducting pairings in a proximity-coupled ferromagnet. We show how this dictates the distribution of current density, with the possibility of curvature-controlled current density manipulation, induced eddy currents and current reversal.

### [80] [A Disconnected Superconducting Regime at the Parent Limit of Infinite-Layer Nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16684)
*Chihao Li,Yutong Chen,Yaolong Bian,Yihao Zhang,Jiahao Ye,Zhitong An,Xingtian Sun,Yu Fan,Zhihui Chen,Zhanze Wang,Jinglei Zhang,Haichao Xu,Rui Peng,Donglai Feng*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究发现，未掺杂的化学计量比PrNiO₂薄膜即表现出本征超导电性（零电阻和抗磁性），并通过异质结工程排除了界面起源；该超导相存在于空穴掺杂浓度3%以内，与约20%二价掺杂形成的传统超导穹顶（superconducting dome）之间存在非超导间隔区，且表现出显著更强的上临界场各向异性，表明无限层镍酸盐并非单纯的铜氧化物（cuprate）类似物，而是具有独立的超导物理机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无限层镍酸盐（infinite-layer nickelates）长期以来被视为铜氧化物超导体（cuprate superconductors）的类似物，其超导电性被认为需要通过约10–20%的阳离子替代（cation substitution）来诱导。该研究旨在检验未掺杂化学计量比PrNiO₂是否存在本征超导电性，并揭示其与已知超导穹顶之间的关系。

Method: 研究采用化学计量比且未经阳离子替代的PrNiO₂薄膜进行输运和磁性测量，通过异质结工程（heterostructure engineering）排除界面效应，并系统比较三价与二价替代（trivalent vs. divalent substitution）对超导电性的影响，结合角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）进行电子结构表征。

Result: 未掺杂的PrNiO₂薄膜表现出本征超导电性（零电阻和抗磁性），且该超导电性并非源于界面效应。三价替代样品的零电阻超导电性稳定存在，而二价替代则迅速抑制超导电性。该超导相被限制在从本征态开始不超过3%的空穴掺杂（hole doping）范围内，并在相图（phase diagram）中与约20%二价掺杂形成的超导穹顶之间存在非超导间隔区。此外，该超导相表现出显著更强的上临界场各向异性（upper-critical-field anisotropy）。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了无限层镍酸盐中存在一个独立的超导相（separated superconducting regime），表明无限层镍酸盐并非仅仅是铜氧化物超导体的类比材料，而是具有独特的超导物理（distinct superconducting physics）。这一发现挑战了现有认知，为理解镍基超导体的微观机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: Infinite-layer nickelates have been widely viewed as cuprate analogs in which superconductivity emerges and forms a superconducting dome centered around 10-20% cation substitution. Here we show that pristine and stoichiometric PrNiO2, without cation substitution, exhibits intrinsic superconductivity characterized by zero resistance and diamagnetism in uncapped films. Through heterostructure engineering, we further exclude an interfacial origin of the superconductivity. Remarkably, zero-resistance superconductivity is consistently observed in trivalent-substituted PrNiO2, whereas it is rapidly suppressed by dilute divalent substitution. Combined with angle-resolved photoemission studies, these results indicate that such a new superconducting regime is confined to within 3% additional hole doping from pristine PrNiO2. Furthermore, this phase is separated from the previously established superconducting dome around ~ 20% divalent doping by a non-superconducting region in the phase diagram, and is further distinguished by a remarkably stronger upper-critical-field anisotropy. These findings establish a unique separated superconducting regime, suggesting that infinite-layer nickelates are not merely cuprate analogs but host distinct superconducting physics.

</details>


### [81] [Unconventional superconductivity in ScIr$_2$ chiral crystal with a kagome lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16689)
*Keqi Xia,Jianzhou Zhao,Igor Plokhikh,Marisa Medarde,Yang Xu,Qingfeng Zhan,Dariusz Jakub Gawryluk,Toni Shiroka,Tian Shang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究报告了ScIr₂₋ₓSiₓ家族中非常规超导（unconventional superconductivity）的证据，通过μ子自旋谱学（muon-spin spectroscopy）测量与能带结构计算相结合的方法，发现其超导配对符合双能隙模型且至少有一个能隙存在节点，表明非常规超导特性。该体系同时存在近费米能级的平带（flat bands）和手性链（chiral chain），为研究非常规超导、平带与手性之间的相互作用提供了罕见平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: kagome晶格材料因其能带拓扑（band topology）、自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）、磁性与电子关联（electronic correlations）之间的相互作用而展现出丰富的量子现象。尽管其磁性已被广泛研究，但由于缺乏合适的候选材料，这类体系中非常规超导（unconventional superconductivity）的探索仍十分有限。

Method: 研究采用μ子自旋谱学（muon-spin spectroscopy）测量与能带结构计算（band-structure calculations）相结合的方法，对ScIr₂₋ₓSiₓ家族材料进行表征。

Result: 母体ScIr₂经历从高温立方相到低温菱方相的结构相变，但Ir kagome层基本保持（仅轻微畸变）。Si替代抑制了结构相变，但超导配对仍可由双能隙模型（two-gap model）良好描述，其中至少一个能隙存在节点，表明非常规超导电性。ScIr₂的低温相含有Ir手性链（chiral chain），可归类为拓扑手性晶体（topological chiral crystal）。

Conclusion: ScIr₂₋ₓSiₓ家族中非常规超导的起源可归因于费米能级附近出现的独特平带（flat bands），这些平带导致强电子关联（strong electronic correlations）。该体系为研究非常规超导、平带与手性之间的相互作用提供了一个有趣而罕见的平台。

Abstract: Materials with a kagome lattice host exotic quantum phenomena driven by the interplay between band topology, spin-orbit coupling, magnetism, and electronic correlations. While magnetism of kagome materials has been widely investigated, their unconventional superconductivity (SC) remains largely unexplored due to the limited availability of suitable materials. Here, we report evidence of unconventional SC in the ScIr$_{2-x}$Si$_{x}$ family by combining muon-spin spectroscopy measurements with band-structure calculations. The parent ScIr$_2$ undergoes a structural phase transition from a high-$T$ cubic- to a low-$T$ rhombohedral phase, while the Ir kagome layer remains, albeit slightly distorted. Although the structural transition is suppressed by Si substitution, the superconducting pairing of ScIr$_{2-x}$Si$_{x}$ remains well described by a two-gap model. Since at least one of the gaps has nodes, this indicates an unconventional SC. Its unconventional nature can be explained by the distinct flat bands occurring near the Fermi level, leading to strong electronic correlations in the ScIr$_{2-x}$Si$_{x}$ family. Moreover, the low-$T$ phase of ScIr$_2$ exhibits an Ir chiral chain; therefore, it can be classified as a topological chiral crystal. Overall, the unusual properties of the ScIr$_{2-x}$Si$_{x}$ family make it an interesting, albeit rare, system for studying the interplay between unconventional SC, flat bands, and chirality.

</details>


### [82] [Marginal-Fermi-Liquid-like Behavior without Pseudogap in Infinite-Layer Nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16852)
*Yu Fan,Zhitong An,Xiang Ding,Xingtian Sun,Yutong Chen,Zhihui Chen,Shenglin Tang,Chihao Li,Jiahao Ye,Timur Kim,Haichao Xu,Rui Peng,Donglai Feng*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究利用角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）解析了无限层镍酸盐超导薄膜La0.8Ca0.2NiO2及其母体LaNiO2的低能谱函数，发现动量选择性关联和边缘费米液体（marginal Fermi liquid）散射可在没有铜氧化物型赝能隙（pseudogap）的情况下存在，为识别高温超导正常态的关键电子特征提供了基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在空穴掺杂铜氧化物（cuprates）中，赝能隙形成、奇异金属行为和非常规超导电性三者紧密交织但关系尚未厘清。无限层镍酸盐（nickelates）提供了具有类铜Ni dx2−y2费米面（Fermi surface）与多能带电子自由度（multiband electronic degrees of freedom）的独特3d9平台，可用于探究上述问题。

Method: 采用角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）解析超导La0.8Ca0.2NiO2及母体LaNiO2薄膜的低能谱函数，测量电子自能（self-energy）Im Σ(ω)的动量依赖行为及低能谱权重（low-energy spectral weight）的分布特征。

Result: 在La0.8Ca0.2NiO2中，电子自能Im Σ(ω)近似随能量线性变化，其斜率从(π/2, π/2)向(π, 0)增大，表现出动量依赖的边缘费米液体散射。两种薄膜从对角方向向(π, 0)方向均出现低能谱权重的渐进抑制，母体LaNiO2中抑制更显著。但整个费米面周围仍存在有限费米能级谱权重，且未观察到指示赝能隙的前沿位移（leading-edge shift）或回弯（back-bending）现象。

Conclusion: 动量选择性关联和边缘费米液体散射可以在不出现可探测的铜氧化物型赝能隙的情况下发生，这为确定高温超导正常态的必要电子特征提供了基准。

Abstract: Pseudogap formation, strange-metal behavior and unconventional superconductivity are closely intertwined in hole-doped cuprates, yet their relationship remains unresolved. Infinite-layer nickelates offer a distinct 3d9-derived platform to address this question by combining a cuprate-like Ni dx2-y2 Fermi surface with multiband electronic degrees of freedom. Here we use angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy to resolve the low-energy spectral function of superconducting La0.8Ca0.2NiO2 and parent LaNiO2 thin films. In La0.8Ca0.2NiO2, the electronic self-energy Im Sigma(omega) is approximately linear in energy and its slope increases from (pi/2, pi/2) to (pi, 0), revealing momentum-dependent marginal-Fermi-liquid-like scattering. Both films show a progressive suppression of low-energy spectral weight from the diagonal direction toward (pi, 0), with stronger suppression in parent LaNiO2. However, finite Fermi-level spectral weight persists around the entire Fermi surface, with no leading-edge shift or back-bending indicative of pseudogap formation in either the electron pocket or the cuprate-like hole band. Our results demonstrate that momentum-selective correlations and marginal-Fermi-liquid-like scattering can occur without a detectable cuprate-like pseudogap, providing a benchmark for identifying the essential normal-state electronic ingredients of high-temperature superconductivity.

</details>


### [83] [Spatial resolution and point spread function of high-resolution scanning SQUID microscopy probes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17414)
*Jan Ullmann,Katharina Kress,Timur Weber,Boris Gross,Daniel Jetter,Reinhold Kleiner,Martino Poggio,Dieter Koelle*

TL;DR: 本文通过模拟磁通耦合，建立了悬臂梁上超导量子干涉器件（SQUID-on-lever）探针的点扩散函数（PSF）数学模型，并通过单个磁性斯格明子（skyrmion）的测量实验验证了该PSF与空间分辨率的准确性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过模拟超导量子干涉器件（SQUID）与磁通源的耦合，建立悬臂梁上超导量子干涉器件（SQUID-on-lever, SOL）探针点扩散函数（PSF）的数学描述；并利用单个磁性斯格明子（skyrmion）的实测磁通响应，与仿真结果进行对比验证。

Result: 实测的单个磁性斯格明子（skyrmion）磁通响应与仿真得到的磁通响应高度一致，从而验证了所计算的点扩散函数（PSF）与空间分辨率的正确性。

Conclusion: 本研究为使用悬臂梁上超导量子干涉器件（SQUID-on-lever, SOL）探针进行磁显微成像提供了完整的磁灵敏度和空间分辨率描述，证实了通过仿真计算得到的点扩散函数（PSF）能够准确表征实际探针的性能。

Abstract: Superconducting quantum interference devices (SQUIDs) show exceptional sensitivity to magnetic flux. In scanning SQUID microscopy (SSM), SQUID size and its distance to the sample are minimized in order to map weak magnetic fields with best possible spatial resolution. SQUID-on-lever (SOL) architectures have proven especially effective as SSM probes due to their small sensor size, robustness, and ease of integration with conventional atomic force microscopy hardware. In order to optimize magnetic microscopy carried out with SOL probes and to accurately reconstruct the magnetic fields that they measure, it is essential to know their point spread function (PSF). The size and shape of this PSF are determined by magnetic flux focusing effects, which depend on the characteristic length-scales of the superconductor and the sensor geometry. By simulating the coupling to sources of magnetic flux, this work provides a mathematical description of the SOL PSF, which contains a full description of the probe's magnetic sensitivity and spatial resolution. We then use measurements of a single magnetic skyrmion to measure the magnetic flux response of a real SOL. We demonstrate excellent agreement with flux responses that are obtained from simulations, thereby confirming the calculated PSF and spatial resolution.

</details>


### [84] [Interface-Confined Superconductivity with Thickness-Independent Superfluid Stiffness in (Pb,Sn)Te/FeTe Bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17539)
*Zi-Jie Yan,Hongtao Rong,Yiyuan Luo,Yufei Zhao,Pu Xiao,Zihao Wang,Lok-Kan Lai,Annie G. Wang,Zhiyuan Xi,Yanxing Li,Xiaoyu Wei,Ke Wang,Binghai Yan,Chih-Kang Shih,Cui-Zu Chang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）生长Pb1-xSnxTe/FeTe双层膜，发现界面超导（interface-induced superconductivity）对邻近层的拓扑（topology）、对称性（symmetry）和电子结构（electronic structure）不敏感，超导主要源于FeTe层的改性，并提供了可调多狄拉克表面态（multiple Dirac surface states）与界面超导共存的实验平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FeTe基异质结中的界面超导有望实现拓扑超导（topological superconductivity），但邻近层的拓扑、对称性和电子结构在其中的具体作用尚未明确，因此需要系统研究这些因素对超导性的影响。

Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）生长Pb1-xSnxTe/FeTe双层膜；利用角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）追踪Pb1-xSnxTe层从平庸绝缘体（trivial insulator）到拓扑晶体绝缘体（topological crystalline insulator）的演化；通过电输运测量和双线圈互感（double-coil mutual-inductance）测量表征超导特性。

Result: 在整个组分范围内均观测到稳健的超导性，超导转变温度（superconducting transition temperature）恒为约12 K；超流刚度（superfluid stiffness）在拓扑相变（topological phase transition）前后相当，且对组分层厚度变化不敏感，表明超导被限制在界面附近。

Conclusion: FeTe基异质结中的超导性对邻近层的拓扑、晶体对称性和电子结构基本不敏感，超导主要源于FeTe层的改性；界面限制超导与可调多狄拉克表面态的共存为探索拓扑超导和多马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes）相互作用提供了通用平台。

Abstract: Interface-induced superconductivity in FeTe-based heterostructures provides a promising route toward topological superconductivity, yet the roles of the neighboring layers topology, symmetry, and electronic structure remain unresolved. In this work, we employ molecular beam epitaxy to grow Pb1-xSnxTe/FeTe bilayers and use angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy to track the evolution of the Pb1-xSnxTe layer from a trivial insulator to a topological crystalline insulator hosting multiple Dirac surface states. Electrical transport measurements reveal robust superconductivity throughout the entire composition range, with a nearly constant superconducting transition temperature of ~12 K despite substantial changes in the electronic structure and topology of Pb1-xSnxTe. Double-coil mutual-inductance measurements further reveal comparable superfluid stiffness across the topological phase transition and nearly thickness-independent superfluid stiffness despite large variations in the constituent-layer thicknesses, demonstrating that superconductivity is confined near the interface. These results establish that superconductivity in FeTe-based heterostructures is largely insensitive to the topology, crystal symmetry, and detailed electronic structure of the neighboring layer, supporting a primary origin in modifications to the FeTe layer. The coexistence of interface-confined superconductivity and tunable multiple Dirac surface states in Pb1-xSnxTe/FeTe bilayers provides a versatile platform for exploring topological superconductivity and interactions among multiple Majorana zero modes.

</details>

Method: 开发了非谐超导密度泛函理论（anharmonic superconducting density functional theory, ah-SCDFT），将非谐修正系统性地整合到标准SCDFT中，仅在有限的超导计算收敛步骤中引入适度的计算开销增加。

Abstract: First-principles studies of superconductivity often neglect anharmonic effects (AHE), despite their crucial role in achieving quantitative accuracy in many materials. To bridge this gap, we introduce a general computational approach, termed anharmonic superconducting density functional theory (ah-SCDFT) which systematically incorporates anharmonic corrections into standard SCDFT. This approach allows for high-fidelity predictions of superconducting properties with only a modest increase in computational cost for a limited number of superconducting calculation convergence steps. We demonstrate the effectiveness and reliability of ah-SCDFT by applying it to the prototypical superconductor MgB2, accurately reproducing its superconducting behavior under both ambient conditions and applied pressure in excellent agreement with experiment. Our results establish ah-SCDFT as a powerful, efficient, and broadly applicable approach for quantitatively reliable studies of superconductivity and a promising tool for the prediction of new superconducting materials.

Abstract: We investigate the nonlinear behavior of a superconducting microwave resonator subjected to a dissipative mechanism where the associated quality factor (Q factor) decreases with increasing dissipated power, leading to a dissipative feedback effect. By modifying the Rothwarf-Taylor equations, we establish a macroscopic quasiparticle heating (QPH) model that directly links the quality factor to the microwave readout power. The key finding is the identification of a distinctive oval-shaped distortion in the resonance circle in the complex plane. This distortion serves as a practical experimental signature for identifying the readout power regime in which QPH dominates the loss, under conditions where other nonlinear mechanisms are sufficiently weak. To validate the model, we design and fabricate a niobium (Nb) half-wavelength coplanar waveguide (CPW) resonator and conduct systematic bath temperature and readout power sweeps. The model provides a well fit to the observed oval-shaped resonance circle distortion across a wide range of operating conditions, confirming the QPH mechanism as the primary source of the dissipative non-linearity in the parameter space investigated.

### [87] [A Voltage-Controlled Josephson Frequency Comb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17992)
*Giorgio De Simoni,Francesco Giazotto*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 所提出的约瑟夫森场效应晶体管频率梳发生器可作为紧凑且可扩展（compact and scalable）的微波源，用于低温量子信息处理（cryogenic quantum information）和传感（sensing）应用。其通过门电极实现直接电控的能力克服了传统约瑟夫森梳状结构的局限性。

Abstract: Microwave frequency combs constitute promising resources for quantum technologies, cryogenic electronics, and multiplexed sensing architectures. In this work, we propose a frequency-comb generator based on a Josephson field-effect transistor operated in a relaxation-oscillation regime. The device comprises a gate-tunable ballistic superconductor-semiconductor-superconductor junction embedded in a resistively shunted circuit, in which electrostatic control of the carrier density enables in situ tuning of both the critical current and the Josephson inductance. Time-domain circuit simulations indicate that the resulting oscillator produces coherent voltage pulses whose Fourier spectrum forms a microwave frequency comb. In contrast to conventional Josephson-based comb architectures, the proposed platform provides direct electrical control of the comb spacing, emission frequencies, and modal power distribution via a gate electrode. For a representative Al/InAs implementation, we demonstrate continuous frequency coverage in the technologically relevant 1-10 GHz range. Furthermore, the concept is shown to be compatible with higher-$T_c$ superconductors, underscoring its potential as a compact and scalable microwave source for cryogenic quantum information and sensing applications.

### [88] [Symmetry-Based Microscopic Theory of the Unconventional Pairing Mechanism in La$_5$Ni$_3$O$_{11}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18094)
*Guan-Hao Feng,Jun Quan*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文针对混合镍氧化物La₅Ni₃O₁₁中观察到的约64 K高温超导现象，发展了一套基于对称性的唯象方法，结合电荷自洽DFT+DMFT计算，揭示了其双能隙超导特性：主导的d_{z²}轨道间层间配对和次主导的d_{x²-y²}轨道面内配对，并将超导转变温度低于La₃Ni₂O₇（约80 K）的原因归因于层间配对贡献的减弱。

Method: 采用基于对称性的唯象方法（phenomenological symmetry-based approach），结合电荷自洽密度泛函理论加动力学平均场理论（charge self-consistent density functional theory plus dynamical mean-field theory, DFT+DMFT）方法，系统分析La₅Ni₃O₁₁的低能物理。

Conclusion: 基于统一图像讨论了镍氧化物超导体中双层NiO₂平面的可能配对机制及γ口袋（γ pocket）在超导中的作用。

Abstract: Recent experiments report high-temperature superconductivity in the hybrid nickelate $\mathrm{La}_5\mathrm{Ni}_3\mathrm{O}_{11}$, which is composed of alternating stacks of bilayer $\mathrm{La}_3\mathrm{Ni}_2\mathrm{O}_7$ and monolayer $\mathrm{La}_2\mathrm{NiO}_4$. However, the superconducting transition temperature $T_c \approx 64~\mathrm{K}$ for $\mathrm{La}_5\mathrm{Ni}_3\mathrm{O}_{11}$ is remarkably lower than the $80~\mathrm{K}$ observed for pressurized $\mathrm{La}_3\mathrm{Ni}_2\mathrm{O}_7$. Thus, an unified microscopic theory is required to address the difference in the pairing mechanisms between these systems. Here, we develop a phenomenological symmetry-based approach to systematically analyze the low-energy physics in $\mathrm{La}_5\mathrm{Ni}_3\mathrm{O}_{11}$, which is obtained by a charge self-consistent density functional theory plus dynamical mean-field theory method. We show that the superconductivity in $\mathrm{La}_5\mathrm{Ni}_3\mathrm{O}_{11}$ exhibits a two-gap nature, consisting of a leading interlayer pairing between the $d_{z^2}$ orbitals and a subleading intralayer pairing between the $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbitals. The reduction of $T_c$ can be attributed to the diminished contribution of the interlayer pairing, as reflected by the hopping parameter ratio $|t_{\perp}^z/t_{\parallel}^{x}|$. Base on this unified picture, we discuss the possible pairing mechanism and the role of $γ$ pocket for the superconductivity in the bilayer NiO$_2$ planes of nickelate superconductors.

### [89] [Structural and Vibrational Properties of D$_3$Se from First Principles: Anharmonic Quantum and Isotope Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18095)
*Wenjie Ma,Yao Ma,Mi Pan,Pugeng Hou,Francesco Belli*

TL;DR: 本文通过结合第一性原理计算与随机自洽谐波近似（stochastic self-consistent harmonic approximation），研究D₃Se在Im\overline{3}m相于60-200 GPa下的振动与超导性质。结果表明，离子量子效应与非谐效应显著重整化声子谱、稳定晶格至至少70 GPa，并降低超导临界温度约3-16 K。在75 GPa下，通过Migdal-Eliashberg理论得到T_c ≈ 154 K。非谐效应还将同位素系数α从0.44抑制至0.29，大幅偏离BCS极限0.5，揭示非谐性从根本上主导该体系的同位素效应。

These effects introduce significant renormalization to the phonon spectra and stabilize the lattice down to at least 70 GPa, well below the harmonic prediction of >110 GPa. Ultimately, the phonon renormalizations alter the electron-phonon coupling, introducing a decrease in the superconducting critical temperature by about 3-16 K across the studied pressure range with respect to standard calculations. Including anharmonic phonons within the Migdal-Eliashberg theory yields $T_c \approx 154$ K at 75 GPa (with $μ^* = 0.1$, $λ = 3.0$), highlighting D3Se as a promising high-Tc superconductor at moderate pressures. Examining the role of anharmonicity in the isotope effect, we find that at 200 GPa it suppresses the isotope coefficient $α$ to 0.29 one third below the harmonic value (0.44) which approaches the BCS limit of 0.5. This dramatic reduction demonstrates that anharmonicity fundamentally governs the isotope effect on this system. The stark discrepancy between anharmonic and harmonic descriptions underscores the need for targeted experimental efforts to resolve the origin of the persistent theory-experiment discrepancy in compressed hydrides.

### [90] [Superconductivity in MgHCu3 perovskite revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18117)
*Piotr Szkudlarek,Wojciech Grochala*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 晶体和电子结构对k点网格和泛函选择不敏感，但声子及声子相关性质对网格密度和泛函选择极其敏感。对于不同的Gaussian展宽，计算得到的TC值在约10至31 K的宽范围内变化，均未超过40 K的经典极限。

Abstract: We reexamine the crystal structure, electronic structure, lattice dynamics, phonon dispersion, electron-phonon coupling, and superconducting properties of MgHCu3 perovskite using the PBEsol and PBE functionals. This perovskite phase was recently proposed to exhibit superconductivity with the critical superconducting temperature, TC, of 42 K, which falls slightly over the classical 40 K limit for the phonon driven superconductivity. We show that although the crystal and electronic structure of this hypothetical compound are quite robust with respect to the k point mesh and functional used, yet the phonons and phonon related properties are extremely sensitive to the density of the grid chosen as well as functional used for calculations. Correspondingly, the values of the critical superconducting temperature calculated here for different Gaussian broadenings vary in a broad range of ca. 10 to 31 K and they do not exceed the classical limit. We suggest that the properties of this and many other high TC hydrides claimed should be thoroughly scrutinized using a variety of functionals, and benchmarked with experiment, to provide more reliable values of TC.

### [91] [Tunable Superconductivity Mediated by Heavy-Electron Plasmons: Band-Structure and Quantum-Geometric Engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18157)

Motivation: 传统超导电性依赖于晶格振动（声子）作为配对胶水，其能量尺度受限于化学与原子质量。等离子体激元（plasmon）作为电子的集体振荡，可通过电子结构工程调控，但控制最优等离子体介导配对的原理尚不明确。

Method: 在随机相位近似（random-phase approximation, RPA）和Eliashberg理论框架下，对最小金属模型计算最优超导临界温度（$T_c$），分析等离子体能量尺度与延迟效应（retardation）导致的排斥抑制之间的竞争关系。

Result: 仅通过等离子体通道，最优$T_c$仅约0.1 K；引入中等强度的声子吸引后，$T_c$提升两个数量级至20 K以上。平带体系中的带间等离子体（interband plasmon）由重带量子度量（quantum metric）调控，而轻带的量子几何可抑制静态屏蔽（static screening）并增强净吸引。层间距会迅速削弱配对，因此同一层中镜像对称性不同的轻、重电子体系是更有前景的平台。

Conclusion: 研究为平带体系在超导电性中确立了新角色：平带并非直接承载配对电子，而是作为可调谐的配对媒介，其集体电荷激发可将超导能量尺度设定在远超自身窄带宽的范围。

Abstract: Conventional superconductivity derives its pairing glue from lattice vibrations, tying its characteristic scales to chemistry and atomic masses. Plasmons$-$the collective oscillations of electrons$-$can instead be reshaped through electronic structure engineering, but the principles governing optimal plasmon-mediated pairing remain unclear. Here, we establish such principles for two-carrier systems in which heavy-electron plasmons mediate the pairing of light electrons. Within the random-phase approximation and Eliashberg theory, we calculate the optimal $T_c$ of minimal metallic models and show that it is controlled by a competition between the plasmon energy scale and retardation-driven suppression of the repulsion, yielding optimal carrier densities and band masses. While the plasmon channel alone reaches only $T_c\sim$ 0.1 K, a moderate phonon attraction cooperates with it, boosting $T_c$ by two orders of magnitude to above 20 K. However, the band flattening needed for slow metallic plasmons also favors the development of competing orders. We therefore consider an insulating system in which coherent interband transitions between flat bands generate gapped interband plasmons without free carriers. The heavy-band quantum metric governs the dispersion and electron-plasmon pairing strength of the interband plasmon, while the quantum geometry of the light band suppresses static screening and enhances the net attraction. Because layer separation rapidly weakens pairing, we propose systems with coexisting light and heavy electrons living in different mirror-symmetry sectors of the same layer as promising platforms. Our results establish a new role for flat-band systems in superconductivity: rather than hosting the paired electrons themselves, they can serve as a tunable pairing mediator whose collective charge excitations set the superconducting energy scale beyond their narrow bandwidth.

</details>


### [92] [Nonreciprocal Superconducting Transport from Chiral Edge States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18159)
*Jin-Xing Hou,Yan-Song Song,James Jun He,Song-Bo Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文揭示拓扑系统中的边界控制手性边缘态是超导非互易输运（nonreciprocal superconducting transport）的一种重要但此前被忽视的微观机制，并通过笼目反铁磁体（kagome antiferromagnets）中的约瑟夫森结验证了非互易信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导非互易输运因能实现无耗散整流而受到广泛关注，但其微观起源通常被归因于体态电子态（bulk electronic states）；本文旨在探索拓扑系统中边界控制的手性边缘态（chiral edge states）作为替代机制的可能性。

Method: 以手性笼目反铁磁体（chiral kagome antiferromagnets）为研究对象，通过面外自旋倾斜（out-of-plane spin canting）或自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）打开高陈数体能隙（high-Chern-number bulk gap），产生多个手性边缘模（chiral edge modes）；利用依赖于子格的边界终止（sublattice-dependent boundary termination）选择边缘态的单谷特征（single-valley character）。

Result: 边界不对称性（boundary asymmetry）导致相对边缘处出现非对称边缘谱，并在垂直于边缘取向的约瑟夫森结（Josephson junctions）中产生可观测的非互易信号，包括非对称Andreev谱（asymmetric Andreev spectra）、约瑟夫森二极管效应（Josephson diode effect）以及反常Fraunhofer干涉图案（anomalous Fraunhofer interference patterns）。

Conclusion: 这些发现拓宽了对超导非互易性（superconducting nonreciprocity）的微观理解，并指出边界工程（boundary engineering）可作为实现超导二极管器件（superconducting diode devices）的可调谐途径。

Abstract: Nonreciprocal superconducting transport enables dissipationless rectification and has attracted considerable interest, yet its microscopic origin is typically sought in bulk electronic states. Here, we show that boundary-controlled chiral edge states in topological systems provide a simple yet largely overlooked mechanism for nonreciprocal superconducting transport. Focusing on chiral kagome antiferromagnets, we demonstrate that out-of-plane spin canting or spin-orbit coupling opens a high-Chern-number bulk gap, giving rise to multiple chiral edge modes. Strikingly, sublattice-dependent boundary termination selects a single-valley character for the edge states, leading to asymmetric edge spectra at opposite edges. This boundary asymmetry directly yields observable nonreciprocal signatures in Josephson junctions oriented transverse to the edges, including asymmetric Andreev spectra, Josephson diode effect, and anomalous Fraunhofer interference patterns. These findings broaden the microscopic understanding of superconducting nonreciprocity and highlight boundary engineering as a tunable route toward superconducting diode devices.

</details>

### [93] [Gaussian Reformulation of the Feynman Path Integral for Quantum Statistical Mechanics with Results for the Second Virial Coefficient of $^4$He](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16301)
*Phil Attard*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 论文将量子统计力学的费曼路径积分重新表述为每个位置构型邻域的高斯采样方法。利用格点上的环形聚合物统计（ring polymer statistics）确定方差，通过威格纳-柯克伍德对易函数（Wigner-Kirkwood commutation function）的高温展开确定均值。该方法避免了传统路径积分量子蒙特卡罗中每个构型需要多个温度节点以及统计平均中数值抵消的问题。氦气第二维里系数的解析与模拟结果与实验测量吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统路径积分量子蒙特卡罗方法在处理每个构型时需引入多个温度节点，且在统计平均中依赖数值抵消，这些问题限制了计算效率与精度，因此需要发展更简洁、稳定的采样方案。

Method: 将费曼路径积分（Feynman path integral）重新表述为每个位置构型邻域的高斯采样。从格点上的环形聚合物统计导出方差，从威格纳-柯克伍德对易函数的高温展开（high temperature expansion）导出均值。该方法无需为每个构型设置多个温度节点，也避免了统计平均中的数值抵消。

Result: 针对氦气第二维里系数（second virial coefficient）给出了解析和模拟结果，并与实验室测量数据进行了比较。

Conclusion: 所提出的路径积分高斯采样方法有效地克服了传统路径积分量子蒙特卡罗方法在多温度节点与数值抵消方面的缺陷，且对氦气第二维里系数的预测与实验一致，验证了方法的可行性。

Abstract: The Feynman path integral for quantum statistical mechanics is reformulated as Gaussian sampling of the neighborhood of each position configuration. The variance and mean are obtained from ring polymer statistics on a lattice, and from the high temperature expansion of the Wigner-Kirkwood commutation function, respectively. The algorithm avoids multiple temperature nodes for each configuration and the need for numerical cancelation in the statistical averages, which are problematic for conventional path integral quantum Monte Carlo. Analytic and simulation results for the second virial coefficient of helium are compared to laboratory measurements.

</details>


### [94] [Representation-Dependent Machine Learning of the Isotropic-Nematic Transition in the Lebwohl-Lasher Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16481)
*Maninder Kaur,Aojie Xue,David P Landau*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了机器学习检测相变时输入表示（input representation）对称性的影响。以三维Lebwohl-Lasher模型的弱一级各向同性-向列相变为例，发现无监督学习（如主成分分析和卷积自编码器）在原始分子构型上无法识别相变，但使用旋转不变（rotationally invariant）的局部关联表示后能够成功检测；而有监督的三维卷积神经网络则能从原始构型中准确预测标量序参量（scalar order parameter）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验机器学习检测相变不仅依赖于学习算法（learning algorithm），还依赖于输入表示是否保持系统的对称性（symmetries）。

Method: 采用无监督方法（主成分分析PCA和卷积自编码器CAE）与有监督方法（三维卷积神经网络CNN）对Lebwohl-Lasher模型进行相变检测，对比原始分子构型（raw molecular configurations）与旋转不变的局部关联表示（local-correlation representation）两种输入形式的效果。

Result: 在原始构型上，PCA和CAE无法识别相变，而CNN在给定序参量标签时能准确预测；在旋转不变的局部关联表示上，PCA和CAE均能恢复相变敏感特征（transition-sensitive signatures）和双峰共存分布（bimodal coexistence distributions）。

Conclusion: Lebwohl-Lasher模型将无监督相发现（unsupervised phase discovery）与有监督序参量回归（supervised order-parameter regression）区分开来，表明在具有取向有序（orientationally ordered）的系统中，无监督机器学习需要尊重对称性的输入表示。

Abstract: Machine-learning detection of phase transitions depends not only on the learning algorithm, but also on whether the input representation preserves the symmetries of the system. We examine this for the weak first-order isotropic--nematic transition of the three-dimensional Lebwohl--Lasher model, whose apolar and continuously degenerate nematic phase makes raw molecular configurations a challenging input for unsupervised learning. Principal component analysis (PCA) and a convolutional autoencoder (CAE) fail to identify the transition from raw configurations because rotationally equivalent nematic states can appear far apart in the input space. When the same configurations are transformed into a rotationally invariant local-correlation representation, both methods recover transition-sensitive signatures and bimodal coexistence distributions. A supervised three-dimensional convolutional neural network (CNN), by contrast, accurately predicts the scalar order parameter from raw configurations when given order-parameter labels. The Lebwohl-Lasher model therefore separates unsupervised phase discovery from supervised order-parameter regression and shows that symmetry-respecting input representations are needed for unsupervised machine learning in orientationally ordered systems.

</details>


### [95] [Glauber dynamics phase transitions in athermal random field Blume-Capel and Blume-Emery-Grifitths models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16561)
*Sumedha,Aldrin B E*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在完全图（complete graph）上求解了有无外磁场条件下Glauber动力学（Glauber dynamics）与平衡态的两个模型。研究发现：高斯随机场（Gaussian random field）的方差R类似于温度，存在临界值R_c，低于该值时稳态依赖于初始态，高于该值时平衡态与非平衡稳态重合。论文还分析了Blume-Emery-Griffiths模型中的阻挫（frustration）与迟滞回线（hysteresis loop）的多种形状。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究随机场模型（random field model）中Glauber动力学稳态与平衡态之间的差异，探究方差R在其中的作用以及初始态依赖性和相变行为。

Method: 在完全图上解析求解Glauber动力学模型和平衡态模型，比较有无外磁场情况下的稳态行为；引入排斥性双二次相互作用（repulsive bi-quadratic interaction）以引入阻挫。

Result: R低于临界值R_c时稳态依赖初始态，高于R_c时平衡态与非平衡稳态重合；R类似温度，可准确得到连续和一级相变的位置；对于Blume-Emery-Griffiths模型，R_c可变为零，且随R增大可能发生从R_c=0到√(2/π)的交叉（crossover）；有外磁场时一级相变区域出现迟滞，回线形状包括矩形、六边形、平行四边形、细腰形和双迟滞回线。

Conclusion: 随机场方差R在Glauber动力学中扮演类似温度的角色，是调控稳态行为的关键参数；迟滞回线的面积依赖于R，而形状由R=0时的模型行为决定；Blume-Emery-Griffiths模型展现出丰富的相图，且显著依赖初始态。

Abstract: We solve the two models for Glauber dynamics and in equilibrium, both in the presence and absence of the external magnetic field on a complete graph. We compare the steady state of the Glauber dynamics with equilibrium and find that for low values of variance $R$ of the Gaussian random field, the steady state of the Glauber dynamics depends on the initial state. Beyond a critical value $R_{c}$ the equilibrium and non equilibrium steady states coincide. The variance $R$ in random field models behaves similar to the temperature. The location of both the continuous and first order transitions can be obtained exactly for the Glauber dynamics steady state. The frustration is introduced by considering repulsive bi-quadratic interaction for Blume-Emery-Griffiths model. We also. consider repulsive bi-quadratic interaction and show that $R_c$ can become zero depending on the value of the crystal field. Interestingly, we also find that even when a system has $R_c=0$ at the start of quasi-static evolution with Glauber dynamics, with increasing $R$, in some regime of the couplings, the model undergoes a crossover to a random field Ising model universaility with $R_c$ changing from $0$ to $\sqrt{\frac{2}π}$. In the presence of uniform magnetic field, regions of first order transition exhibit hysteresis under Glauber dynamics. These models exhibit rectangular, hexagonal, parallelogram, wasp-waisted, and double hysteresis loops. We derive the shapes of hysteresis loops analytically giving the equation for the value of the coercive field and show that while the area under the hysteresis loop depends on $R$, the shape is determined by the behavior of the models at $R=0$. In particular, in the case of Blume-Emery-Griffiths model the hysteresis plots have regions of continuous and first order transitions both, resulting in a rich phase diagram that depends non-trivially on the initial state.

</details>


### [96] [Occupation-condensation transition of a sublinearly vertex-reinforced random walk on regular tree](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16971)
*Bon A Koo,Edward Ju*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究顶点强化随机游走（vertex-reinforced random walk）在有根b叉树上的凝聚相变（condensation transition）现象。当强化参数β低于临界值β_c时，游走者的占据测度（occupation measure）扩散分布，范围线性增长；当β超过临界值时，单个顶点占据O(1)比例的时间，而游走范围以log t速率缓慢增长。通过可逆性（reversibility）分析，发现β_c正比于b-1，不同分支数b=2,3,4的数据在除以b-1后高度重合。临界点附近的占据数呈现非自平均（non-self-averaging）且双峰分布（bimodal）的共存现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解顶点强化随机游走在指数增长图（如树）上的行为，特别是强化（reinforcement）与图结构扩张之间的竞争如何导致凝聚相变，并区分此类凝聚与有限范围局域化（finite-range localization）的本质差异。

Method: 在有根b叉树（rooted b-ary tree）上定义顶点强化随机游走，其转移概率正比于1+βn^{a}，其中n为历史访问次数，a∈(0,1)为记忆强度参数。通过数值模拟使用四种估计量定位相变阈值，并利用冻结环境下的可逆性（reversibility）推导边电导（edge conductances）c_{uv}=w_u w_v与平稳测度μ_v∝w_v∑_{u∼v}w_u，将逃逸前沿置于有偏游走的分支数判据（branching-number criterion）下分析。

Result: 发现β_c(a,b)处存在尖锐的凝聚相变：低于β_c时占据范围线性增长，高于β_c时单个顶点凝聚O(1)比例的访问时间，范围以log t速率缓慢增长而非有界。四种估计量在t=3×10^7的观测时间内定位到相同阈值且无系统漂移。可逆性分析预测β_c∝b-1，b=2,3,4的数据在除以b-1后误差在百分之几以内。临界点附近占据数呈现非自平均与双峰分布的共存现象。

Conclusion: 顶点强化随机游走在树上的凝聚相变与有限范围局域化有本质区别，其阈值可由分支数判据定量预测。a=1/2仅作为凝聚剖面（condensed profile）的边际指数（marginal exponent）出现，而临界行为具有热力学相变中两相共存的特征。

Abstract: A vertex-reinforced random walk steps to a neighbour with probability proportional to $1+βn^{a}$, where $n$ counts previous visits to that neighbour and $a\in(0,1)$ sets the memory strength. On the rooted $b$-ary tree the exponential growth of the vertex set drives the walk outward while the reinforcement pulls it back. We report a sharp condensation transition of the occupation measure at a finite $β_c(a,b)$: below it the occupation spreads and the range grows linearly; above it a single vertex holds an $O(1)$ fraction of the time, stable in the observation time, while the range keeps growing very slowly, at a rate better described by $\log t$ than by any power. We do not find the range to be bounded, and keep this condensation distinct from finite-range localization. Four estimators locate the same threshold, which shows no systematic drift out to $t=3\times10^{7}$. In a frozen environment the walk is reversible, with edge conductances $c_{uv}=w_{u}w_{v}$, $w_{v}=1+βn_{v}^{a}$, and measure $μ_{v}\propto w_{v}\sum_{u\sim v}w_{u}$ describing the condensed core, whose neighbour coupling we test directly. Reversibility places the escape at the frontier within the branching-number criterion for biased walks on trees, predicting $β_c\propto b-1$; the measured lines for $b=2,3,4$ collapse under division by $b-1$ to a few percent (bootstrap). The value $a=1/2$ that governs the walk on $\mathbb{Z}$ enters only as the marginal exponent of the condensed profile. Near $β_c$ the occupancy is non-self-averaging and bimodal, a coexistence-type phenomenology.

</details>


### [97] [On the Information Required for Feedback Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16639)
*Matthew P. Leighton,Jose M. Betancourt,Thierry Emonet,Benjamin B. Machta,Michael C. Abbott*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了在信息受限条件下随机系统的反馈控制问题，推导了从受控系统到控制器所需的信息率下界，并得到了最优控制协议的显式形式——即概率性地时间反演被动动力学，最终将理论应用于非线性粒子定位、微生物导航和信息引擎等场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物系统从微观到宏观层面以及许多工程问题都需要在信息有限的条件下对含噪声系统进行控制。本研究旨在建立信息受限反馈控制的理论框架，以揭示信息率与系统控制性能之间的基本权衡关系。

Method: 针对达到目标稳态的随机系统，论文推导了从受控系统到控制器所需信息率（information rate）的下界。对于状态无关被动动力学的系统，该下界由一个显式最优控制协议达到，该协议通过概率性地时间反演（time-reverse）被动动力学来实现。

Result: 该框架能够为广泛的信息受限控制问题生成性能-信息帕累托前沿（performance-information Pareto frontier）。论文通过非线性粒子定位、微生物导航以及实验实现的信息引擎三个应用案例展示了所获结果的有效性。

Conclusion: 研究建立了信息率下界与最优控制协议之间的明确联系，为理解生物系统中信息受限的噪声控制以及设计工程反馈控制器提供了统一的理论工具。

Abstract: Biological systems across scales, along with many engineering problems, must control noisy systems with limited information. Here we study information-limited feedback control of stochastic systems to achieve target steady states, and derive a lower bound on the information rate from controlled system to controller. This framework allows us to obtain performance-information Pareto frontiers for wide-ranging control problems with limited information. For systems with state-independent passive dynamics, the bound is saturated by an explicit optimal control protocol which probabilistically time-reverses the passive dynamics. We showcase these results through applications to nonlinear particle localization, microbial navigation, and experimentally realized information engines.

</details>

### [99] [A Unified Discrete and Continuous Theory of Core-Halo Complexity Maximizers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17907)
*Akshat Sharma*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文为离散和连续概率空间中的广义统计复杂度最大化问题建立了统一的变分框架，证明最优解必然具有两水平（core-halo）结构，并给出了完整的解析刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前研究表明，在有限离散系统中，最大化统计复杂度（statistical complexity）的分布呈现两水平结构，但缺乏一个同时适用于离散和连续概率空间的统一处理框架。

Method: 基于Shannon熵（Shannon entropy）和Rényi熵（Rényi entropy）构造广义统计复杂度，建立一般性变分框架（variational framework），推导出同时适用于离散概率质量和连续概率密度的公共驻值方程（stationary equation）。

Result: 证明每个驻值解（stationary solution）恰好具有两个概率水平，形成通用的核心-光环结构（core-halo structure）；优化问题可简化为单一重数参数（multiplicity parameter）；全局复杂度最大值由最小允许核心（smallest admissible core）实现，在离散情形对应单一主导状态，在连续极限下对应无穷小核心。

Conclusion: 该框架为广义统计复杂度提供了统一的数学基础，完整解析刻画了复杂度最大化分布，潜在应用涵盖统计力学（statistical mechanics）、信息论（information theory）及复杂系统（complex systems）分析。

Abstract: The maximization of statistical complexity has long been associated with the emergence of probability distributions lying between perfect order and complete disorder. While previous studies have shown that complexity-maximizing distributions exhibit a two-level structure in finite discrete systems, an analogous unified treatment for both discrete and continuous probability spaces has remained unavailable. In this work, we develop a general variational framework for a generalized statistical complexity constructed from Shannon and Renyi entropies. We derive a common stationary equation governing both discrete probability masses and continuous probability densities and prove that every stationary solution necessarily possesses exactly two probability levels, establishing a universal core-halo structure. We further demonstrate that the optimization problem reduces to a single multiplicity parameter and prove that the global complexity maximum is attained by the smallest admissible core, corresponding to a single dominant state in the discrete case and an infinitesimal core in the continuous limit. These results provide a complete analytical characterization of the complexity-maximizing distributions and reveal a common mathematical structure underlying complexity optimization in both discrete and continuous settings. The framework establishes a unified foundation for generalized statistical complexity with potential applications in statistical mechanics, information theory, and the analysis of complex systems.

</details>


### [100] [Floquet Driving of Enzymatic Reactions: Counting Statistics and Long-Time Currents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17072)
*Yuki Watanabe,Yuki Ishiguro,Takashi Oka*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文为经典随机过程开发了一套弗洛凯理论（Floquet formalism），用于计算周期性时间调制下的粒子流及其计数统计，并以离散驱动的米氏酶促反应模型（Michaelis-Menten-type reaction model）为例验证了理论表达式，揭示了高频极限下周期性驱动对化学反应速率的有效重整化效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光遗传学（optogenetics）等人工控制化学反应系统的技术迅速发展，使得理解时间依赖控制下的反应动力学日益重要。当反应速率的调制具有时间周期性时，需要一套系统性的理论框架来分析此时的粒子流和统计行为。

Method: 基于福克形式体系（Floquet formalism），针对经典随机过程引入计数场（counting field），推导了第一累积量（first cumulant）和相应粒子流的普适表达式。粒子流通过有效弗洛凯生成元（effective Floquet generator）和踢出态（kicked state）表示，并进一步给出了高、低频极限下的渐近表达式。随后将理论应用于离散弗洛凯驱动（discrete Floquet driving）——一种非微扰的阶跃式协议，构建了由G蛋白激活和抑制的环磷酸腺苷（cAMP）生产的离散驱动米氏-门顿型反应模型。

Result: 得到了离散驱动米氏-门顿模型中周期性切换催化活性所产生的长时产物粒子流的解析表达式和数值结果。在高频极限下，周期性驱动的效应可等效为化学反应速率的有效修改。

Conclusion: 该研究为周期性驱动的化学反应提供了弗洛凯分析（Floquet analysis）的理论基础，有助于理解和设计时间调制下的化学反应系统。

Abstract: Technologies for artificially controlling chemical reaction systems, such as optogenetics, are rapidly advancing, making it increasingly important to understand reaction dynamics under time-dependent control. When the modulation of reaction rates is periodic in time, the Floquet formalism provides a systematic framework. We develop a Floquet theory for classical stochastic processes that enables the calculation of the current and its counting statistics under such periodic modulation. In particular, we formulate the theory in terms of a counting field and derive general expressions for the first cumulant and the corresponding current. The current is expressed using the effective Floquet generator and the kicked state, and we further obtain general asymptotic expressions for the current in both the high- and low-frequency regimes. As a concrete example to test our analytical expressions, we then apply the results to discrete Floquet driving -- a non-perturbative, stepwise protocol. The setup is motivated by a biochemical system known as cyclic adenosine monophosphate (cAMP) production, which is an enzymatic reaction activated and inhibited by G-proteins. This is formulated as a discretely driven Michaelis--Menten-type reaction model, in which the catalytic activity is switched on and off abruptly in time, and we obtain analytical expressions and numerical results showing how periodic switching of reaction rates generates a long-time product current. In particular, in the high-frequency limit, we show that the effect of the periodic driving can be interpreted through an effective modification of the chemical reaction rates. These results provide a basis for Floquet analysis of periodically driven chemical reactions.

### [101] [Adverse Selection with Quality Variance: A Maximum-Entropy Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17239)
*Zhi-Lei Zhang,Tan-Ji Zhou,C. P. Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文将逆向选择（adverse selection）建模为质量分布的动态截断（dynamic truncation）过程：买方设定一个与当前平均质量成正比的支付上限，超出该上限的卖方退出市场，这一迭代过程最终收敛到稳定状态。该方法揭示了阻止完全逆向选择的机制，分析了质量方差和价格溢价对市场恶化的影响，并通过最大熵基准（maximum-entropy benchmark）数值展示了质量方差与支付率如何共同决定市场退化程度及最终稳定质量平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统逆向选择模型中仅用平均质量描述市场，无法回答市场退化速度以及质量分布如何演化这两个关键问题。本文旨在通过引入质量分布的动态截断机制，解决上述不足。

Method: 将逆向选择建模为质量分布的动态截断过程：买方设定一个与当前平均质量成正比的上界（比例系数为 ξ > 1），质量超过该上界的卖方拒绝出价并退出市场；保留的市场由截断后的条件分布（conditional distribution）刻画，该演化过程不断迭代直至市场质量达到稳定状态。

Result: （i）识别出阻止完全逆向选择（市场质量下降到最低质量下限的完整过程）的机制；（ii）更大的质量方差（quality variance）或更小的价格溢价（price premium）会提高平均质量恶化的上界；（iii）最大熵基准的数值结果表明质量方差和支付率（payment rate）共同决定市场恶化程度与最终稳定质量平台。

Conclusion: 该统计方法阐明了市场干预减缓逆向选择的途径：提高买方的支付率、降低质量方差，或提高最低质量下限（minimum quality floor）。

Abstract: The adverse-selection mechanism in markets explains how asymmetric information between buyers and sellers can drive high-quality goods out of the market, thereby causing market deterioration. In its simplest formulation, only the mean quality is used to describe the market, and this is insufficient to determine how fast the market deteriorates or how the quality distribution evolves. To resolve the two problems, we describe the adverse selection as a dynamic truncation of the quality distribution: buyers set an upper bound proportional to the mean quality by a rate $ξ$ that is larger than unity, and sellers whose quality exceeds this upper bound reject an offer and exit the market. The retained market is then characterized by the conditional distribution obtained after this truncation, and the corresponding evolution process is iterated until market quality reaches a stable state. This statistical approach gives three results. (i) We identify a mechanism for preventing complete adverse selection, defined as the process where the quality of the market is driven down to the minimum quality floor. (ii) A larger quality variance or a smaller price premium, defined as the amount by which the payment upper bound exceeds the current mean quality, raises the upper bound on the deterioration in mean quality. (iii) A maximum-entropy benchmark shows numerically how quality variance and the payment rate jointly determine market deterioration and the final stable quality platform. This approach also clarifies how market interventions can slow adverse selection: they may raise buyers' payment rate, reduce quality variance, or increase the minimum quality floor.

</details>


### [102] [Richards' equation as a hydrodynamic limit: Chapman--Enskog reduction of the continuum kinetic equation for unsaturated soil water](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17358)
*Riccardo Rigon*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 基于前期论文中提出的孔隙填充分布（pore-filling distribution）动力学理论，本文通过Chapman-Enskog约化从连续介质动力学方程推导出Richards方程，建立了Darcy尺度渗流方程与孔隙尺度统计力学之间的微观基础，并首次从第一性原理导出了双渗透率/多渗透率模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宏观非饱和渗流理论（如Richards方程）通常将空间与时间两个极限混为一谈，缺乏从孔隙尺度动力学出发的严格推导。本文旨在通过动力学理论分离这两个极限，为Richards方程提供微观基础，并从第一性原理解释多重渗透率模型（dual-/multiple-permeability models）的起源。

Method: 对前期论文导出的连续介质动力学方程（continuum kinetic equation, CKE）$d_t g + \text{div} F = C[g]$进行Chapman-Enskog约化（Chapman-Enskog reduction），控制参数为Damköhler数Da（重分布时间与强迫时间之比），类似于从Boltzmann方程到Navier-Stokes方程的约化路径。线性化的重分布算子J在质量内积（mass inner product）下为自伴且负半定，其核为一维，对应唯一的不变量（水）。Chapman-Enskog层级在每一阶都反演同一个J，仅源项变化。通过平均场约化恢复标准积分公式，串行路径修正给出Mualem异质性惩罚。

Result: 得到了四个结果：（1）平衡步定义持水曲线（retention curve）；（2）线性化水量收支与体间源项设定一阶方程；（3）该方程的可解性条件即为质量守恒，亦即Richards方程；（4）响应函数给出宏观通量，将导水率K识别为一阶输运系数（类比于黏性系数）。当孔径分布为双峰时，弛豫谱出现间隙；投影到谱带并在带内做Chapman-Enskog约化，带间弛豫保留至O(1)项，即可从第一性原理导出双渗透率/多渗透率模型，交换系数由带间连通性决定。当Da非小量时，展开失效，需直接求解完整CKE。

Conclusion: 本文建立了从孔隙尺度动力学到宏观Richards方程及其多渗透率推广的严格数学桥梁，阐明了空间极限（几何收缩至REV点）与时间极限（Chapman-Enskog约化）各自的作用。该框架不仅统一了传统非饱和流理论，还提供了从第一性原理导出并修正Mualem模型及多渗透率模型的理论依据，为Da非小量条件下的非平衡输运指明了完整CKE这一研究方向。

Abstract: Richards' equation for unsaturated water flow is derived from the kinetic theory of the pore-filling distribution g(r,x,t) of a companion paper. It separates two limits that macroscopic theory usually conflates. The spatial limit is purely kinematic: contracting the representative elementary volume (REV) to a point yields the closed continuum kinetic equation (CKE) d_t g + div F = C[g], with F a pore-resolved pre-closure flux and C[g] the occupancy-gated redistribution operator. The dynamics lies in the temporal limit, the subject of this paper: a Chapman-Enskog (CE) reduction of the CKE controlled by the Damkohler number Da (redistribution time over forcing time), the structural analogue of the passage from Boltzmann to Navier-Stokes. The linearized redistribution operator J is self-adjoint and negative semidefinite in the mass inner product, with a one-dimensional kernel fixing a single invariant (water) and hence one macroscopic equation; the CE hierarchy inverts the same J at every order, only the source changing. Four results follow: the equilibrium step defines the retention curve; the linearized water budget plus the inter-REV source set the first-order equation; its solvability is mass conservation, i.e. Richards' equation; and the response function gives the macroscopic flux, identifying the conductivity K as a first-order transport coefficient, the counterpart of viscosity. Mean-field reduction recovers the standard integral formula; the serial-path correction gives Mualem's heterogeneity penalty. A bimodal pore-size distribution opens a gap in the relaxation spectrum; projecting onto the bands and applying CE within each, with cross-band relaxation surviving at O(1), derives the dual- and multiple-permeability models from first principles, the exchange coefficient set by inter-band connectivity. When Da is not small the expansion breaks down and the full CKE is needed.

</details>


### [103] [Large scale behavior in the Kuramoto-Sivashinsky equation: The Schwinger-Dyson route](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17915)
*Olivier Coquand*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用 Schwinger-Dyson 框架证明，Kuramoto-Sivashinsky 方程在红外极限下能维持稳定标度（scaling）的唯一解具有负有效粘度（negative effective viscosity），且该性质是波方程的一般属性，不依赖于重整化群（renormalization group）流的具体截断或数值方案的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究 Kuramoto-Sivashinsky 方程在大尺度（large scale）下的性质，旨在不依赖特定重整化群截断或数值方案的前提下，证明负有效粘度是该方程在红外极限（infrared limit）下维持稳定标度的普遍性质。

Method: 采用 Schwinger-Dyson 框架（Schwinger-Dyson framework）进行分析，在最小假设（minimal set of hypotheses）下推导红外极限中标度解的必要条件。

Result: 证明了在红外极限下能维持稳定标度的唯一解具有负有效粘度，且该结论不依赖于重整化群流的具体截断或特定数值格式的限制。

Conclusion: 负有效粘度是 Kuramoto-Sivashinsky 方程在红外区域的一般属性（general property），表明该性质本质上源于波方程本身，而非某种特定近似或数值处理的人为产物。

Abstract: The present paper is a study of the large scale properties of the Kuramoto-Sivashinsky equation. By using a Schwinger-Dyson framework, we aim to provide a proof that the only solutions that can sustain a stable scaling in the infrared limit have a negative effective viscosity (in the Kuramoto-Sivashinsky sense) with a minimal set of hypotheses, thereby showing that this constitutes a general property of the wave equation that does not depend on a specific set of truncations of a renormalisation group flow, or limitations of a given numerical scheme for example.

### [104] [Expansion of a free Fermi gas released from an isotropic trapping potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18007)
*J M Luck,P L Krapivsky*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用半经典方法研究了无相互作用费米子（fermions）在各向同性囚禁势（isotropic trapping potential）突然释放后的弹道膨胀（ballistic expansion）行为，推导了大粒子数极限下晚期膨胀轮廓的普适表达式，并揭示了动量分布与空间分布的边缘标度指数为 $d/a$，从而推广了 Wigner 半圆律（Wigner semi-circle law）和 Thomas-Fermi 分布（Thomas-Fermi distribution）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究无相互作用费米子在囚禁势突然释放后的弹道膨胀动力学，特别是大粒子数极限下的晚期行为，以揭示其普适标度性质。

Method: 采用半经典方法（semi-classical techniques），在任意维度 $d$ 和任意幂次势（power-law potentials）指数 $a$ 下，推导大费米子数体系膨胀云团的晚期轮廓。

Result: 得到了膨胀云团晚期时空轮廓的显式表达式，并发现动量分布与空间分布的边缘指数为 $d/a$，实现了对 Wigner 半圆律和 Thomas-Fermi 分布的普适推广。

Conclusion: 无相互作用费米子在各向同性幂律囚禁势下的弹道膨胀表现出由 $d/a$ 标度指数描述的普适行为，该结果适用于任意维度和任意幂次势指数。

Abstract: We consider a system of non-interacting fermions prepared in the many-body ground state of an isotropic trapping potential in any dimension, and investigate the ballistic expansion of the fermionic cloud after the potential is suddenly released. Using semi-classical techniques, we derive the full late-time profile of the expanding cloud in the regime when the fermion number is large. We thus obtain explicit expressions for power-law potentials with arbitrary exponent $a$ and in all dimensions $d$. The momentum distribution and the spatial profile of the cloud exhibit a universal edge exponent $d/a$, thus generalizing the Wigner semi-circle law and the Thomas-Fermi distribution.

### [105] [Thermal and viscous contrast in quantum Hall scanning-probe images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16315)
*P. Shubham Parashar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个基于朗道能级投影、沃德恒等式（Ward identity）、磁化减除热电输运、斯托克斯-欧姆反演（Stokes-Ohm inversion）和有限尖端费舍尔信息（finite-tip Fisher information）的量子霍尔（quantum Hall，QH）扫描成像功能泛函框架，在两个互补输运区域分别推导出缺陷诱导的热电和电霍尔对比度解析表达式，并指出霍尔奇成像本身不足以直接作为霍尔粘度（Hall viscosity）的测量指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子霍尔扫描图像常被直接解读为局域势、温度或粘度的地图，但实际上探针记录的是输运算子的有限分辨率泛函。现有解读忽略了这一泛函结构的复杂性，需要建立定量框架以区分电、热电和粘性响应通道。

Method: 采用朗道能级投影（Landau-level projection）、粒子数沃德恒等式（particle-number Ward identity）、磁化减除热电输运（magnetization-subtracted thermoelectric transport）、流体动力学斯托克斯-欧姆反演（hydrodynamic Stokes-Ohm inversion）以及有限尖端费舍尔信息（finite-tip Fisher information）构建统一泛函框架。

Result: 在强场锐朗道能级区域，光滑标量缺陷的热电和电霍尔对比度满足 δα_{xy}^{tr}/δσ_{xy}=(E_c-μ)/(eT)，去除热磁化电流后，在保持的长波阶下轨道形状因子、缺陷几何与公共尖端核函数相互抵消，热电对比度零点被能量加权锚定在 E_c=μ 处。在流体动力学区域，可测量的 q^2 张量振幅混合多种通道，霍尔奇图像本身不能直接作为霍尔粘度测量。在代表性石墨烯几何中，Schur 补拟合对边界滑移最为敏感，条件单标准差灵敏度约为 68 平方纳米（SNR0=200）。

Conclusion: 该框架将量子霍尔纳米成像（quantum Hall nanoscopy）的视觉解读转化为针对电、热电和粘性响应通道的定量可观测性检验。

Abstract: Quantum Hall scanning images are often read as maps of a local potential, temperature, or viscosity, whereas a probe records a finite-resolution functional of a transport operator. We formulate this functional using Landau-level projection, a particle-number Ward identity, magnetization-subtracted thermoelectric transport, a hydrodynamic Stokes-Ohm inversion, and finite-tip Fisher information. Two results follow in complementary transport regimes. In the strong-field, sharp-Landau-level regime, the defect-induced thermoelectric and electrical Hall contrasts of a smooth scalar defect obey $δα_{xy}^{tr}/δσ_{xy}=(E_c-μ)/(eT)$. At the retained long-wavelength order, the orbital form factor, defect geometry, and common tip kernel cancel after the heat-magnetization current is removed, so the zero of the thermoelectric contrast is pinned by energy weighting at $E_c=μ$ rather than by defect shape. In the hydrodynamic regime, the measurable $q^2$ tensor amplitudes mix Hall, longitudinal, transverse, boundary, electrothermal, and kinetic channels, so a Hall-odd image is not by itself a Hall-viscosity measurement. For a representative graphene geometry, a Schur-complement fit against the stated nuisance library yields a conditional one-standard-deviation sensitivity of approximately 68 square nanometers at SNR0 = 200, with boundary slip the limiting nuisance. The framework turns visual interpretation of quantum Hall nanoscopy into a quantitative observability test for electrical, thermoelectric, and viscous response channels.
