### [106] [Observation of Critical Current Minimum in Super-Honeycomb Josephson Junction Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16500)
*Melissa Mikalsen,Alexander-Georg Penner,Samuel D. Escribano,Nadav Drechsler,Arunav Bordoloi,Jacob Issokson,Felix von Oppen,Yuval Oreg,Javad Shabani*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验和理论模拟，研究了超导体-半导体约瑟夫森结阵列（superconductor-semiconductor Josephson junction arrays）中涡旋晶格（vortex lattice）的集体量子现象。在相邻结间距小于安德烈夫束缚态（Andreev bound states, ABS）相干长度（ξ_ABS）的强耦合条件下，在方形和超级蜂窝（super-honeycomb）两种晶格中观测到不同填充因子（filling factor）下的临界电流峰。超级蜂窝阵列在外加平面内磁场（in-plane field）增大时，在填充因子 f=1 处出现独特的临界电流极小值（critical current minimum），而方形阵列和大间距超级蜂窝阵列则没有该特征，表明该现象由超级蜂窝涡旋的几何结构与结间长程杂化（inter-junction hybridization）共同导致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导体-半导体约瑟夫森结阵列是一个独特可调的集体量子现象研究平台，尤其在相邻结间距小于安德烈夫束缚态相干长度（ξ_ABS > d_JJ）时，局域安德烈夫束缚态可在晶格中杂化。本文旨在探究不同几何构型（方形阵列、超级蜂窝阵列）及不同耦合强度下此类阵列中的涡旋行为与临界电流特征。

Method: 制备了三种不同的Al-InAs约瑟夫森结阵列：一个方形阵列（square array）、一个超级蜂窝阵列（super-honeycomb array），两者均满足强耦合条件（ξ_ABS > d_JJ）；以及一个大间距超级蜂窝控制器件（control device），满足弱耦合条件（ξ_ABS ≲ d_JJ）。在外加垂直磁场（out-of-plane field）和旋转平面内磁场（rotating in-plane field）下测量临界电流（critical current）响应，并结合受挫XY模型（frustrated XY model）进行数值模拟。

Result: 在外加垂直磁场下，临界电流峰出现在有理填充因子（rational filling factors）处，反映稳定的涡旋晶格构型。超级蜂窝晶格中，涡旋在不同填充因子下局域于不同的非全等（non-identical）元胞（plaquettes），与受挫XY模型模拟一致。旋转平面内磁场产生周期性临界电流振荡，反映InAs量子阱中的Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit coupling）。在填充因子 f=1 处，仅强耦合超级蜂窝阵列在外加平面内磁场强度增大时表现出明显的临界电流极小值，方形阵列和大间距超级蜂窝阵列均无此特征。

Conclusion: 超级蜂窝阵列在 f=1 处出现的临界电流极小值是由超级蜂窝涡旋晶格的独特几何结构和长程结间杂化（long-range inter-junction hybridization）共同导致的。这一发现表明，通过改变晶格几何与耦合强度，可在约瑟夫森结阵列中调控集体量子行为，尤其是受抑制的临界电流特征。

Abstract: Superconductor-semiconductor Josephson junction arrays are a uniquely tunable platform for studying collective quantum phenomena, particularly in the regime where localized Andreev bound states can hybridize across the lattice when the physical separation between adjacent junctions is smaller than their coherence length ($ξ_{\text{ABS}}>d_{\text{JJ}}$). Here, we investigate three distinct Al-InAs Josephson junction arrays: a square array and super-honeycomb array fabricated within this ${ξ_{\text{ABS}}>d_{\text{JJ}}}$ regime, as well as a larger-spacing super-honeycomb control device designed such that $ξ_{\text{ABS}}\lesssim\!~d_{\text{JJ}}$. Under an out-of-plane field, critical current peaks emerge at rational filling factors, reflecting stable vortex configurations in the lattices. In the super-honeycomb lattice, vortices localize to distinct non-identical plaquettes at different filling factors, as predicted by frustrated XY model simulations. A rotating in-plane field yields periodic critical current oscillations that reflect the Rashba spin-orbit coupling inherent to the InAs quantum well. Surprisingly, at $f = 1$, the closely spaced super-honeycomb array exhibits a distinct critical current minimum as the magnitude of the in-plane field increases, a signature absent in the square array and large-spacing super-honeycomb array. These results indicate that this signature is jointly influenced by the unique geometry of the super-honeycomb vortex lattice and by long-range inter-junction hybridization.

</details>


### [107] [Topological magnon noises](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16574)
*Shuang Liang,Tengyue Zhao,Yu-Hang Li,Hua Jiang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文基于拓扑磁振子绝缘体的自旋哈密顿量，发展了一套温度梯度驱动下铁磁绝缘体中磁振子输运（magnon transport）的综合理论，推导了磁振子电流和噪声的公式，并发现吉尔伯特阻尼（Gilbert damping）会破坏磁振子守恒，从而深刻改变噪声间的互易关系、约翰逊-奈奎斯特公式（Johnson-Nyquist formula）以及透射系数与散粒噪声（shot noise）之间的定量关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立温度梯度驱动下铁磁绝缘体中磁振子输运的完整形式理论（formalism），为计算磁振子霍尔角（magnon Hall angle）、法诺因子（Fano factor）以及定量关联磁振子电导（magnon conductance）与噪声提供理论框架。

Method: 基于拓扑磁振子绝缘体（topological magnon insulator）的自旋哈密顿量（spin Hamiltonian），推导了磁振子流和相应磁振子噪声（magnon noise）的解析表达式。

Result: 发现吉尔伯特阻尼（Gilbert damping）的存在导致磁振子流不守恒，从而显著改变了局域与非局域噪声间的互易关系、电导与热噪声之间的约翰逊-奈奎斯特公式，以及透射系数与散粒噪声之间的定量关系。

Conclusion: 吉尔伯特阻尼破坏了磁振子流的守恒性，使得传统电子输运中的噪声—电导关系在磁振子系统中发生根本性修正，需重新审视磁振子输运中的涨落—耗散关系。

Abstract: We develop a comprehensive formalism for magnon transport in ferromagnetic insulators driven by a temperature gradient. The formulas for magnon current and corresponding magnon noise are derived herein based on the spin Hamiltonian of a topological magnon insulator, which enables us to calculate the magnon Hall angle, to provide an explicit expression for the Fano factor, and to reaffirm the quantitative relations between magnon conductance and magnon noise. We find that the magnon current is not conserved in the presence of the Gilbert damping. Consequently, the reciprocal relation between the local and nonlocal noises, the Johnson-Nyquist formula between the conductance and the thermal noise, and the relation between the transmission coefficient and the shot noise are profoundly altered.

### [108] [Distributed Topological Charge and Spinorial Holonomy in Yukawa-Regularized Graphene Disclinations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16835)
*A. M. de M. Carvalho,G. Q. Garcia,E. Brito,C. Furtado*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种Yukawa型正规化（Yukawa-type regularization）方法，将圆锥几何（conical geometry）中的奇异顶点替换为光滑的曲率分布，在保持缺陷渐近拓扑结构的前提下，获得了共形因子、曲率和拓扑荷的精确表达式，并展示了尺度依赖的拓扑荷与半径依赖的几何相位（holonomy）之间的直接联系。进一步分析了该背景中无质量狄拉克准粒子（massless Dirac quasiparticles）的动力学，证明正规化核心在保持缺陷渐近拓扑特征的同时修正了自旋联络（spin connection），为石墨烯类系统中的几何与拓扑效应研究提供了有限核心扩展框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 圆锥几何是描述向错（disclinations）的标准模型，但其将曲率集中于奇异顶点，无法处理实际材料中缺陷核心的有限尺寸效应。因此需要引入一种光滑的正规化方案，以更真实地描述缺陷核心的几何与拓扑性质。

Method: 采用Yukawa型正规化替代圆锥几何中的顶点奇异性，通过光滑曲率分布保持缺陷的渐近拓扑结构。推导了共形因子、曲率和封闭拓扑荷的精确解析表达式。在此基础上，研究无质量狄拉克准粒子在该背景中的动力学行为。

Result: 获得了正规化几何中共形因子、曲率和拓扑荷的精确解析解。发现拓扑荷具有尺度依赖性，相应的几何相位依赖于半径，建立了分布曲率与几何相位之间的直接联系。在狄拉克准粒子动力学方面，正规化核心修正了自旋联络，但保留了缺陷的渐近拓扑特征。

Conclusion: 该工作为传统圆锥描述提供了有限核心扩展，为研究石墨烯类系统中的几何与拓扑效应建立了自然框架。

Abstract: Conical geometries provide the standard description of disclinations, but they concentrate the curvature at a singular apex. We introduce a Yukawa-type regularization that replaces this singularity by a smooth curvature distribution while preserving the asymptotic topology of the defect. Exact expressions are obtained for the conformal factor, curvature, and enclosed topological charge. The resulting geometry exhibits a scale-dependent topological charge and a corresponding radius-dependent holonomy, establishing a direct connection between distributed curvature and geometric phases. We further investigate the dynamics of massless Dirac quasiparticles in this background and show that the regularized core modifies the spin connection while preserving the asymptotic topological signature of the defect. These results provide a finite-core extension of the conventional conical description and offer a natural framework for studying geometric and topological effects in graphene-like systems.

### [109] [Colored $Δ_T$ noise probes the topological character of edge modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17354)
*Sachiraj Mishra,Colin Benjamin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出将有彩色Δ_T噪声（colored Δ_T noise），即有限频率Δ_T噪声，作为探测量子霍尔（quantum Hall）和量子自旋霍尔（quantum spin Hall）系统中边模（edge-mode, EM）输运的探针。研究表明，手性（chiral）、自旋守恒螺旋（spin-conserving helical）和自旋翻转螺旋（spin-flip helical, 平庸）边模在适当偏压协议下展现出截然不同的有色Δ_T噪声特征，且这些特征在电子-空穴不对称性（electron-hole asymmetry）影响下仍能保持区分性。有色Δ_T噪声还表现出频率依赖的符号反转，这是白噪声（white noise）所不具备的。零温有色量子散粒噪声（colored quantum shot noise）对手性边模为零，对自旋守恒螺旋边模随频率改变符号，而对自旋翻转螺旋边模始终为正。这些结果确立了有色Δ_T噪声作为一种鲁棒且实验可及的互补探针，用于识别介观拓扑系统中的不同类型边模输运。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直流电导和噪声测量往往掩盖了有限频率下的非平衡电流涨落和动力学输运特性，因此需要一种能够直接探测本征热涨落（intrinsic thermal fluctuations）且消除焦耳热效应（Joule heating）的探针。有色Δ_T噪声在零平均电荷电流条件下仅由温度和电压偏压驱动，为解决这一问题提供了可能。

Method: 论文从理论上分析了有色Δ_T噪声在不同边模类型（手性、自旋守恒螺旋、自旋翻转螺旋）下的谱特征，并通过引入量子点接触（quantum point contact）考虑能量依赖的散射，研究了电子-空穴不对称性对有限频率谱的修正。同时，对零温有色量子散粒噪声也进行了对比分析。

Result: 不同边模类型在有色Δ_T噪声下呈现显著可区分的特征：手性、自旋守恒螺旋和自旋翻转螺旋边模在适当偏压协议下谱特征各异。有色Δ_T噪声展现出频率依赖的符号反转，这是白Δ_T噪声（ω=0）所不具备的。零温有色量子散粒噪声对手性边模恒为零，对自旋守恒螺旋边模随频率改变符号，而对自旋翻转螺旋边模始终为正。电子-空穴不对称性会显著改变有限频谱，但不会抹除上述区分性特征。

Conclusion: 有色Δ_T噪声是一种鲁棒且实验可及的探针，能够作为互补手段区分手性、自旋守恒螺旋和自旋翻转螺旋（平庸）边模输运，尤其适用于自旋守恒螺旋与自旋翻转螺旋边模的区分，后者的有色Δ_T噪声保留了特征性的符号反转。

Abstract: We investigate colored $Δ_T$ noise, i.e., finite-frequency $Δ_T$ noise, as a probe of edge-mode (EM) transport in quantum Hall and quantum spin Hall systems. Colored $Δ_T$ noise probes finite-frequency nonequilibrium current fluctuations and dynamical transport properties that are often obscured in DC measurements of conductance and noise. Since $Δ_T$ noise is driven solely by a temperature and voltage bias under zero average charge current conditions, it eliminates current-induced Joule heating and directly probes intrinsic thermal fluctuations. We show that chiral, spin-conserving helical, and spin-flip helical (trivial) EMs exhibit distinct colored $Δ_T$-noise signatures under appropriate bias protocols. Incorporating energy-dependent scattering through a quantum point contact, we demonstrate that electron-hole asymmetry significantly modifies the finite-frequency spectrum while preserving these distinguishing features. Notably, colored $Δ_T$ noise exhibits a frequency-dependent sign reversal absent in the corresponding white ($ω=0$) $Δ_T$ noise. We further investigate zero-temperature colored quantum shot noise and find that it vanishes identically for chiral EMs, whereas the spin-conserving helical response changes sign with frequency. By contrast, spin-flip helical (trivial) EMs exhibit a positive colored shot-noise spectrum. However, the corresponding colored $Δ_T$ noise retains its characteristic sign reversal, providing a robust distinction between spin-conserving helical and spin-flip helical (trivial) EM transport. These results establish colored $Δ_T$ noise as a robust, experimentally accessible, complementary probe for identifying chiral, spin-conserving helical, and spin-flip helical (trivial) EM transport in mesoscopic topological systems.

</details>


### [110] [Vacancy-Induced Topological Phase Transition via Valley Annihilation in an Anisotropic Honeycomb Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16965)
*Anna Hassine,Amit Goft,Boris Rotstein,Eric Akkermans*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明，在原本对所有参数都拓扑平庸的蜂窝晶格（honeycomb lattice）中，单个缺失原子（空位）可以驱动拓扑相变（topological phase transition），并使其缺陷缠绕数（defect winding number）ν₃在临界各向异性比为t'/t=2时从±1跳变为0，该相变由体Lifshitz转变（bulk Lifshitz transition）驱动，可在局域态密度中以波前位错（wavefront dislocations）的形式直接观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统拓扑相变通常需要整体调控晶格参数或对称性破缺，而本文旨在探索单个点缺陷（point defect）——即一个原子空位（vacancy）——是否足以在原本拓扑平庸的体系中诱导出拓扑相变，并研究其背后的机制与可观测效应。

Method: 采用二维蜂窝晶格模型，引入各向异性最近邻跃迁比t'/t作为调控参数。利用Nielsen-Ninomiya费米子加倍定理（fermion-doubling theorem）分析完整晶格的拓扑平庸性；通过引入单个空位作为内边界（internal boundary），计算缺陷缠绕数ν₃并分析其随t'/t的变化；使用逆参与率（inverse participation ratio, IPR）表征零模（zero mode）的空间局域化程度。

Result: 完整晶格因Dirac谷（Dirac valleys）成对出现且拓扑荷（topological charge）完全抵消而恒为拓扑平庸。单个空位打破这种抵消，在t'/t<2时产生缺陷缠绕数ν₃=∓1。当t'/t=2时，两个Dirac谷合并湮灭，赝自旋（pseudospin）自由度数从m=2降至m=1，违反非平庸缠绕数所需条件d+D+1=2m，导致ν₃=0，发生拓扑相变。零模从代数衰减（~1/r）转变为更强的空间约束，IPR在临界点达到尖锐极小值。

Conclusion: 该相变发生在固定对称性类别BDI内，完全由体Lifshitz转变驱动，且仅通过空位缺陷才能观测到。局域态密度中的波前位错可直接成像ν₃，为石墨烯（graphene）及光子、冷原子类比系统提供了实验上可实现的探测手段。

Abstract: A single missing atom can drive a topological phase transition in a lattice that is otherwise trivial for all values of its parameters. We demonstrate this in a two-dimensional honeycomb lattice with anisotropic nearest-neighbor hopping ratio $t'/t$. The pristine lattice is topologically trivial for all $t'/t$ by the Nielsen-Ninomiya fermion-doubling theorem: Dirac valleys appear in pairs whose topological charges cancel identically in any bulk invariant. A single vacancy breaks this cancelation, acting as an internal boundary with defect winding number $ν_3=\mp 1$ for $t'/t<2$. At $t'/t=2$, the two Dirac valleys merge and annihilate; the number of active pseudospinor degrees of freedom drops from $m=2$ to $m=1$, violating the condition $d+D+1=2m$ required for a non-trivial winding number. The winding number collapses to $ν_3=0$: a topological phase transition within a fixed symmetry class (BDI), driven entirely by a bulk Lifshitz transition and observable only through the vacancy. The defect zero mode crosses over from algebraic (${\sim}1/r$) to stronger spatial confinement, with its inverse participation ratio reaching a sharp minimum at criticality. Wavefront dislocations in the local density of states provide a direct, spatially resolved image of $ν_3$, accessible in graphene and in photonic and cold-atom analogs.

</details>


### [111] [Quantum-metric-driven light-induced ferrovalley state in d-wave altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17049)
*Shihao Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出d波交错磁体（d-wave altermagnets）可作为隔离量子度规（quantum metric）与贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的理想平台，利用线偏振非共振光驱动轨道选择性的铁谷相（ferrovalley phase），通过纯量子度规介导的带隙重整化实现量子度规的直接测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子度规与贝里曲率在量子材料中几乎总是共存，二者贡献难以分离，这成为量子材料研究中的一个核心难题。

Method: 利用Magnus展开（Magnus expansion）和精确Floquet对角化（exact Floquet diagonalization）方法，分析线偏振非共振光对d波交错磁体的驱动效应。

Result: 线偏振非共振光可通过纯量子度规介导的带隙重整化（band-gap renormalization）驱动轨道选择性的铁谷相，且在任何阶数下均无贝里曲率贡献；轨道选择性源于d_{xz}与d_{yz}轨道间的度规各向异性（metric anisotropy）。

Conclusion: d波交错磁体为量子度规效应的隔离、调控和读出提供了纯净且可调的平台，所得谷带隙差可直接定量度量量子度规，并可通过自旋分辨ARPES和光学泵浦-探测谱（pump-probe spectroscopy）进行实验观测。

Abstract: Isolating the quantum metric from the Berry curvature remains a central challenge in quantum materials, as the two geometric quantities nearly always coexist and their contributions are difficult to disentangle. We show that d-wave altermagnets, whose real Hamiltonian possesses strictly vanishing Berry curvature, constitute an ideal platform for overcoming this obstacle. Using the Magnus expansion and exact Floquet diagonalization, we demonstrate that linearly polarized off-resonant light drives an orbital-selective ferrovalley phase through a purely quantum-metric--mediated band-gap renormalization, with no Berry curvature contribution at any order. The orbital selectivity originates from the hopping anisotropy, which generates a pronounced metric anisotropy between the $d_{xz}$ and $d_{yz}$ orbitals, and the gap reduction is expressed analytically in terms of the quantum metric. The resulting valley gap difference provides a direct, quantitative measure of the quantum metric, accessible to spin-resolved ARPES and optical pump-probe spectroscopy. This establishes d-wave altermagnets as a pristine, tunable platform in which quantum metric effects can be isolated, controlled by light polarization, and read out through valley polarization.

</details>


### [112] [Geometry contribution to sound attenuation in double-Weyl semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17064)
*Varsha Subramanyan,Shi-Zeng Lin,Avadh Saxena*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文发现，在双外尔半金属（double Weyl semimetals）中，应变（strain）不与外尔节点发生轴向耦合（axial coupling），而是通过形变费米面（Fermi surface）的几何结构来主导声衰减（sound attenuation），并指出这一几何贡献是简单外尔半金属（simple Weyl semimetals）中完全不存在的新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究关注简单外尔半金属中应变通过轴向耦合对声衰减的反常贡献，但双外尔半金属中缺乏该耦合机制，其声衰减的来源尚未明确。

Method: 基于对称性分析（symmetry analysis）和费米面几何形变的物理图像，通过理论推导论证双外尔半金属中应变作为破缺对称性的指向场（director field）如何作用于每个外尔节点周围的费米面。

Result: 双外尔半金属中声衰减的唯一来源是应变引起的费米面几何形变，不存在轴向耦合；识别出一种在简单外尔半金属中完全缺失的几何贡献（geometric contribution）。

Conclusion: 双外尔半金属与简单外尔半金属的声衰减机制根本不同，前者由费米面几何形变主导，后者由轴向耦合主导。

Abstract: The axial coupling of strain to the nodes of the simple Weyl semimetals leads to anomalous contributions to sound attenuation in such materials. However, in double Weyl semimetals, there is no such axial coupling. Strain instead couples as a symmetry-breaking director field that deforms the Fermi surface around each Weyl node. In this work, we show that absence of axial coupling in double Weyl semimetals implies a very different mechanism of relaxation due to sound. The deformed geometry of the Fermi surface is the only source of sound attenuation under these conditions. Thus, we identify a geometric contribution to sound attenuation in double Weyl semimetals that is entirely absent in simple Weyl semimetals.

### [113] [Spin-valley-layer coupling with dual control via stacking and electric field in antiferromagnetic bilayer Janus YIBr](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17199)
*Bo-Wen Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculation）和有效低能模型（effective low-energy model），研究了六种不同堆叠方式的双层Janus YIBr反铁磁二维半导体结构，揭示了堆叠方式对易磁化轴方向、狄拉克（Dirac）色散关系以及自旋-谷-层耦合（spin, valley and layer coupling）的影响，并发现外电场可调控费米能级附近的空穴自旋、谷和层自由度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁二维半导体的改性和增强被认为对实现新颖电子性质和促进有前景的应用至关重要，因此需要深入理解其微观机制。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculation）和有效低能模型（effective low-energy model）对六种不同堆叠方式的双层Janus YIBr结构进行分析。

Result: 磁各向异性能（magnetic anisotropy energy）计算显示易磁化轴方向随堆叠方式改变；能带计算揭示价带中至少在0.3 eV宽的能量窗口内存在狄拉克相对论色散关系（Dirac relativistic dispersion relation）；自旋、原子性质和贝里曲率（Berry curvature）分析表明存在自旋-谷-层耦合，可实现自旋劈裂（spin splitting）、谷极化（valley polarization）和量子谷霍尔绝缘体（quantum valley Hall insulators）。

Conclusion: 外电场可用于控制费米能级附近空穴的自旋、谷和层自由度，这些发现对未来探索双层Janus结构的新奇性质、调控方法和更多功能具有参考价值。

Abstract: The modification and enhancement of antiferromagnetic two-dimensional semiconductor is considered crucial for realizing novel electronic properties and facilitating promising applications. For this purpose, we investigate six antiferromagnetic 2D bilayer Janus YIBr structures with different stacking variations by means of first-principles calculation and an effective low-energy model. The calculation of magnetic anisotropy energy shows that the direction of easy axis varies with different stacking. First-principles-calculated energy bands reveal that there is a Dirac relativistic dispersion relation in the valence band in a wide energy window of 0.3 eV at least. The calculations for spin, atom properties and Berry curvature description show that there is spin, valley and layer coupling with spin splitting, valley polarization and quantum valley Hall insulators can be achieved in the bilayer Janus structures. Further analyses of the effect of external electric field can be used to control spin, valley and layer of the hole near the Fermi level. These can be useful in future exploration for novel properties, control methods and more functionalities in bilayer Janus structures.

### [114] [Layer Edelstein Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17209)
*Binchang Zhou,Pan Zhou,Baoru Pan,Yuzhong Hu,Songmin Liu,Lizhong Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在双层系统中由电流驱动的普遍自旋现象——层埃德尔斯坦效应（layer Edelstein effect, LEE），定义为在面内电荷电流驱动下、可通过外加电场调控的层分辨自旋磁化。通过最小双层 k·p 理论、对称性分析和第一性原理计算，论文证明了该效应在非磁性双层堆积系统中普遍存在，并展示了两种普遍表现形式：对称性直接要求的显式层间自旋磁化，以及在外电场作用下对称性降低时激活的分量。第一性原理计算在 MoSSe、MoTe₂ 和 WTe₂ 双层堆积系统中验证了该效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电控磁学是实现下一代自旋电子学（spintronics）功能的基本途径。现有研究在层霍尔效应（layer Hall effect）方面已有进展，但其在自旋领域的自然对应效应——即如何在电荷电流驱动下实现层分辨的自旋极化控制——尚缺乏统一的理论框架和普适性理解。

Method: 采用最小双层 k·p 理论建立 LEE 的一般存在性；结合对称性分析与一般双层堆积框架，推导出模型无关的对称性判据；通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）在 MoSSe、MoTe₂ 和 WTe₂ 双层堆积系统中进行数值验证。

Result: 建立了 LEE 的对称性理论框架，证明其在广泛的非磁性双层堆积系统中普遍允许存在。LEE 具有两种普遍表现形式：由对称性直接决定的显式层间相反自旋磁化分量，以及在外电场作用下因对称性降低而激活的分量。第一性原理计算在三种代表性材料体系中确认了该效应并展示了实验可行性。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了 LEE 作为双层系统中由对称性支配的普遍响应（generic symmetry-governed response），为通过电学方法产生和操控层分辨自旋极化（layer-resolved spin polarization）提供了统一的概念框架。

Abstract: Electrical control of magnetism represents a fundamental route toward next-generation spintronic functionalities. In this Letter, we introduce a universal current-induced spin phenomenon in bilayer systems, termed the layer Edelstein effect (LEE), which serves as the natural counterpart of the layer Hall effect in real space. It is defined by the emergence of layer-resolved spin magnetizations with opposite components on the top and bottom layers, driven by an in-plane charge current and controllable by an external electric field. We establish the general existence of the LEE using a minimal bilayer $k \cdot p$ theory. By combining symmetry analysis with a general bilayer stacking framework, we derive a model-independent symmetry criterion demonstrating that the LEE is generically allowed in a broad class of nonmagnetic bilayer stacking systems. We further show that the LEE admits two universal manifestations: explicit layer-opposite spin magnetization components mandated directly by symmetry, and components become activated upon symmetry reduction by external electric fields. First-principles calculations on stacked bilayer MoSSe, MoTe$_2$ and WTe$_2$ confirm the predicted effect and illustrate their experimental feasibility. Our work establishes the LEE as a generic symmetry-governed response of bilayer systems, providing a unified conceptual framework for electrically generating and manipulating layer-resolved spin polarization.

</details>


### [115] [A field theory approach to Breit-type Hamiltonians in gapped Dirac systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17361)
*Xinhong Zhou,T. H. Hansson,Varsha Subramanyan,Qing-Dong Jiang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种基于路径积分（path integral）的场论方法，用于推导带隙狄拉克系统（gapped Dirac systems）在矢量与轴矢规范场（vector and axial gauge fields）耦合下的Breit型低能哈密顿量（low-energy Hamiltonian）。通过将质量隙视为大能量标度并积分出狄拉克旋量的高能分量，获得了低能自由度的薛定谔描述。在轴矢规范场存在时，哈密顿量中出现了传统电磁情形中无对应的额外矢量-轴矢耦合项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Breit哈密顿量方法主要适用于普通电磁（矢量）规范场，缺乏对轴矢规范场（axial gauge fields）耦合情形的系统处理。本文旨在建立一种统一的路径积分场论框架，以统一处理矢量与轴矢规范场下带隙狄拉克系统的低能有效哈密顿量。

Method: 采用路径积分（path-integral）场论方法，将质量隙视为大能量标度，通过积分掉狄拉克旋量（Dirac spinor）的高能分量，获得描述剩余低能自由度的正则薛定谔（canonical Schrödinger）描述。该方法可逐阶（order by order）展开，得到低能有效哈密顿量。

Result: 对于普通狄拉克方程（ordinary Dirac equation），该方法逐阶重现了传统的Breit哈密顿量（Breit Hamiltonian）。在存在轴矢规范场时，得到的哈密顿量包含额外的矢量-轴矢耦合项（vector-axial couplings），这类耦合在传统电磁情形中不存在。方法在三维和二维狄拉克模型上得到验证，并展示了与带隙外尔系统（gapped Weyl systems）的相关性。

Conclusion: 该方法为处理矢量与轴矢规范场耦合的带隙狄拉克系统提供了系统的低能有效理论框架。轴矢规范场可产生传统电磁场中不存在的低能输运特征（low-energy transport signatures），这对于研究带隙外尔系统（gapped Weyl systems）中的动力学轴矢场（dynamical axial fields）具有重要物理意义。

Abstract: We develop a path-integral-based field theory for deriving Breit-type low-energy Hamiltonians for gapped Dirac systems coupled to both vector and axial gauge fields. Treating the mass gap as the large energy scale, we integrate out the high-energy component of the Dirac spinor and obtain a canonical Schrödinger description for the remaining low-energy degrees of freedom. For the ordinary Dirac equation, our method reproduces the conventional Breit Hamiltonian order by order. In the presence of axial gauge fields, however, the resulting Hamiltonian contains additional vector-axial couplings that have no analogue in the traditional electromagnetic case. We illustrate the method using three- and two-dimensional Dirac models and discuss its relevance to gapped Weyl systems, where dynamical axial fields can generate distinctive low-energy transport signatures.

</details>


### [116] [Symmetry-isolated magnetoelectric electro-optic effects in noncentrosymmetric metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17392)
*C. O. Ascencio,D. J. P. de Sousa,Seungjun Lee,Tony Low*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文分类了时间反演对称非中心对称金属中贝里曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipole）D、回旋磁张量（gyrotropic magnetic tensor）K 和磁电电光张量（magnetoelectric electro-optic tensor）G 的对称性约束形式，识别出11个空间群（space groups）中D和K对称性为零而G非零，并通过第一性原理计算和斜入射几何光学分析提供了分离D和G驱动的电光信号的实验路径。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过对称性分析分类D、K和G在时间反演对称（time-reversal symmetric）、非中心对称金属中的形式；使用第一性原理计算（first-principles based calculations）验证代表性材料中D和K为零而G非零且可通过费米能级（Fermi level）移动调控；设计斜入射几何（oblique-incidence geometry）以区分D和G驱动的电光响应特征。

Result: 识别出11个空间群中D和K因对称性为零而G保持非零；第一性原理计算证实了代表性材料中这一现象；斜入射几何下，D驱动响应产生螺旋度偶（helicity-even）吸收或增益修正，G驱动响应耦合s和p光学扇区并产生偏置诱导的圆二色性（bias-induced circular dichroism）具有sinθcosθ角度依赖性。

Conclusion: 所识别的空间群和实验构型为分离D和G驱动的电光效应提供了互补路径，为实验上直接观测非中心对称金属中与G相关的磁电电光效应提供了清晰的实验方案。

Abstract: We classify the symmetry-constrained forms of the Berry curvature dipole $\mathbf{D}$, gyrotropic magnetic tensor $\mathbf{K}$, and magnetoelectric electro-optic (EO) tensor $\mathbf{G}$, which describe metallic optical and EO effects in time-reversal symmetric, noncentrosymmetric metals. We identify 11 space groups (SGs) in which $\mathbf{D}$ and $\mathbf{K}$ vanish by symmetry while $\mathbf{G}$ remains allowed, thereby providing a more direct route to observing the recently predicted magnetoelectric EO effects associated with $\mathbf{G}$. First-principles based calculations confirm that $\mathbf{D}$ and $\mathbf{K}$ vanish for representative materials, while $\mathbf{G}$ remains allowed and tunable via Fermi level shifting. We further show that the choices of SG and experimental configuration provide complementary paths for isolating $\mathbf{G}$-driven EO effects, including cases where $\mathbf{D}$ and $\mathbf{K}$ are also symmetry-allowed. In an oblique-incidence geometry, the $\mathbf{D}$-driven response produces a helicity-even absorption or gain correction, whereas the $\mathbf{G}$-driven response couples the $s$ and $p$ optical sectors and produces a bias-induced circular dichroism with a characteristic $\sinθ\cosθ$ angular dependence. This provides a direct experimental route for separating the $\mathbf{D}$- and $\mathbf{G}$-driven EO signatures in noncentrosymmetric metals.

### [117] [Tilted Anisotropic Dirac Fermions in an Exponentially Decaying Magnetic Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17676)
*Sushmita Saha,Alestin Mawrie*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用各向异性缩放将非各向同性系统映射为各向同性系统的参数；进而应用洛伦兹变换将实验室坐标系下的各向异性问题转化为加速系（boosted frame）中的标准各向同性狄拉克方程；在加速系中求解指数衰减磁场问题；最后通过逆变换将能谱和量子化条件变换回实验室坐标系。

Result: 得到了一个隐含的朗道量子化条件，该条件中的引导中心参数内禀地依赖于能量。识别了物理可容许态（physically admissible states）所需满足的条件。验证了在均匀磁场极限下，本形式可正确恢复倾斜各向异性狄拉克费米子的已知朗道能谱。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个统一的洛伦兹协变框架，可用于描述倾斜各向异性狄拉克材料在指数衰减磁场中的朗道量子化行为。该工作为理解非均匀磁场下狄拉克费米子的量子现象提供了理论工具。

Abstract: We develop an analytical theory of Landau quantization for tilted anisotropic Dirac fermions in an exponentially decaying magnetic field. Using anisotropy scaling and a Lorentz transformation, we recast the laboratory-frame problem into the isotropic Dirac equation in the boosted frame, where the exponentially decaying magnetic-field problem admits an exact solution. Transforming the boosted-frame spectrum back to the laboratory frame yields an implicit quantization condition with an intrinsically energy-dependent guiding-center parameter. We identify the conditions for physically admissible states. We further show that the formalism recovers the known uniform-field spectrum of tilted anisotropic Dirac fermions in the appropriate limit. Our results establish a unified Lorentz-covariant framework for describing Landau quantization in tilted anisotropic Dirac materials in the presence of an exponentially decaying magnetic field.

### [118] [Depth Determination of Individual Shallow NV-Centers via Spin-Lock NMR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17734)
*Aaron Daniel,Beat Bürgler,Patrick Maletinsky,Patrick Potts*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于Spin-Lock NMR的替代方法，用于定量确定金刚石中单氮-空位（NV）中心的深度。与传统的XY8动态去耦序列相比，该方法避免了亚谐波响应和仪器分辨率限制，通过调节Spin-Lock拉比频率至1H拉莫尔频率实现Hartmann-Hahn共振，并基于马尔可夫主方程导出定量拟合函数，从而直接关联测量谱与NV深度。实验表明该方法与XY8协议结果高度一致，并可用于研究金刚石表面常出现的1H核自旋信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 浅层电子自旋（如金刚石中的氮-空位（NV）中心）的定量量子传感需要准确知道自旋在材料表面下的深度。现有基于XY8动态去耦序列的1H核磁共振（NMR）方法存在两个问题：有限宽度脉冲导致亚谐波响应（包括来自附近13C自旋的干扰），以及仪器分辨率有限，只能稀疏采样窄带1H NMR线形。因此需要一种更精确、无谐波模糊的替代方法。

Method: 引入Spin-Lock NMR作为单NV深度确定的新方法。通过将Spin-Lock拉比频率（Rabi frequency）调谐至1H拉莫尔频率（Larmor frequency），使NV探针通过Hartmann-Hahn共振（Hartmann-Hahn resonance）测量1H NMR信号，从而避免脉冲去耦序列的谐波模糊，并显著提高仪器分辨率。从马尔可夫主方程（Markovian master equation）推导出定量Spin-Lock NMR拟合函数，直接关联测量谱与NV深度。

Result: 该方法在多个NV中心上得到的深度估计值与基于XY8的协议结果高度一致，验证了Spin-Lock NMR作为定量单NV深度确定的稳健替代方案。进一步应用该方法研究了金刚石表面常报道存在的1H核自旋信号（即使在没有浸没油的情况下）。

Conclusion: Spin-Lock NMR是定量单NV深度确定的一种稳健替代方法，具有避免谐波模糊、分辨率更高、与现有方法一致性好等优点，并可推广至对金刚石表面固有1H核自旋信号的研究。

Abstract: Quantitative quantum sensing with shallow electron spins, such as those hosted by nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers in diamond, requires accurate knowledge of the spin's depth below the host material's surface. A widely used approach infers this depth from the 1H nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) signal of immersion oil on the diamond surface that can be detected using dynamical decoupling sequences such as XY8. However, finite-width pulses make XY8 sensitive to subharmonic responses, including unwanted contributions from nearby 13C spins, and its instrument-limited spectral resolution provides only sparse sampling of the narrow 1H NMR lineshape. Here, we introduce Spin-Lock NMR as an alternative approach to single-NV depth determination. By tuning the Spin-Lock Rabi frequency to the 1H Larmor frequency, the NV probes the 1H NMR signal through the Hartmann-Hahn resonance without the harmonic ambiguities of pulsed decoupling sequences and with substantially higher instrument-limited spectral resolution. We derive a quantitative Spin-Lock NMR fit function from a Markovian master equation that directly relates the measured spectrum to the NV depth. Our approach yields NV depth estimates in excellent agreement with the established XY8-based protocol across multiple NV centers and establishes Spin-Lock NMR as a robust alternative for quantitative single-NV depth determination. To demonstrate its applicability, we employ our method to investigate the 1H nuclear spin signal that is regularly reported to be present on diamond, even in the absence of immersion oil.

### [119] [Impurity-induced Inverse Faraday Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17802)
*A. A. Kopasov,A. A. Bespalov,A. S. Mel'nikov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从量子力学角度描述了二维电子气（2D electron gas）中非磁性点杂质周围的光致直流电流态和磁场。基于含时薛定谔方程（time-dependent Schrödinger equation）的二阶微扰解，发现垂直于二维系统平面的直流磁场分量呈随机磁通分布，绑定在杂质位置附近。空间平均的直流磁场在远离样品边缘处不消失，因此该逆法拉第效应（inverse Faraday effect）机制与基于弛豫时间近似的流体动力学或动力学方程方法给出的标准图像有本质区别。该机制在二维和三维系统中均普遍适用，且内部直流磁场可能引发光致霍尔效应（photoinduced Hall effect）和法拉第旋转（Faraday rotation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于弛豫时间近似（relaxation time approximation）的流体动力学或动力学方程方法仅预测光致电流沿样品边缘流动，无法描述无序系统中杂质附近产生的体电流和内部直流磁场。本文旨在提出一种新的量子力学描述，以解释圆偏振光照射下无序二维电子气中杂质附近的光致直流电流和磁场分布。

Method: 基于含时薛定谔方程，在电磁波振幅的二阶微扰论（second-order perturbation theory）框架下求解，获得光致直流电流态和磁场的量子力学描述。

Result: 发现垂直于二维系统平面的直流磁场分量呈类似于随机磁通（random magnetic fluxes）的分布，绑定在杂质位置附近。空间平均的直流磁场在远离样品边缘处不为零，与标准理论预测的仅沿边缘流动的电流图像显著不同。

Conclusion: 该光致整流电流（rectified currents）绕杂质中心形成的机制对二维和三维系统均普遍适用。内部直流磁场可导致探测电磁信号的光致霍尔效应和法拉第旋转。

Abstract: We provide a quantum-mechanical description of the photoinduced dc current states and magnetic fields around nonmagnetic point impurities in a two-dimensional (2D) electron gas irradiated by a circularly polarized electromagnetic wave. Based on the solution of the corresponding time-dependent Schrodinger equation within the second-order perturbation theory in the electromagnetic wave amplitude we find that the resulting dc magnetic field component perpendicular to the plane of the 2D system is distributed like in a set of random magnetic fluxes bound to the positions of impurities. As a result, the spatially averaged dc magnetic field does not vanish far from the sample edges and, thus, our scenario of the inverse Faraday effect in disordered systems differs strongly from the standard one based on the relaxation time approximation within the hydrodynamic or kinetic equation approaches which would give only the photoinduced currents flowing along the sample edges. The predicted mechanism for formation of rectified currents flowing around the impurity centers is shown to be generic both for 2D and three-dimensional systems. The internal dc magnetic field can give rise to the photoinduced Hall effect and Faraday rotation for a probing electromagnetic signal.

### [120] [Physics-constrained machine learning for decoding multi-nanobubble configurations in graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17866)
*Jihye Kim,Taegeun Song,Nojoon Myoung*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种物理约束的机器学习框架，通过电子态密度（DOS）谱图逆向解码多个石墨烯纳米泡（graphene nanobubbles）的构型，利用多泡DOS谱的加和性原理，实现复杂构型的准确重建并对噪声具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从电子谱图中识别多个石墨烯纳米泡（graphene nanobubbles）非常困难，因为不同纳米泡的应变诱导特征（strain-induced features）彼此重叠，传统方法难以区分。

Method: 基于物理约束的机器学习框架：利用之前全量子输运计算（full quantum-transport calculations）验证的多泡态密度（DOS）等于各单泡谱归一化之和的加和关系（additive relation），将其编码为紧凑的神经分解模型（neural decomposition model）。对每个目标谱独立优化基系数，所得权重直接识别组成该谱的几何构型。

Result: 该方法能够准确重建复杂度递增的纳米泡构型，对于重复出现的组成泡、不完整的基字典（basis dictionary）以及模拟测量噪声（simulated measurement noise）均表现出鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该框架为表征应变工程（strain-engineered）石墨烯纳米结构提供了一条可解释的路径，并可能推广至其他具有加和光谱响应（additive spectral responses）的量子材料。

Abstract: Identifying multiple graphene nanobubbles from electronic spectra is challenging because their strain-induced features overlap. We develop a physics-constrained machine-learning framework that decodes nanobubble configurations from density-of-states (DOS) spectra. For spatially separated nanobubbles, previous full quantum-transport calculations established that the multi-bubble DOS is numerically equivalent to the normalized sum of the constituent single-bubble spectra. We encode this validated additive relation in a compact neural decomposition model. For each target spectrum, the basis coefficients are optimized independently, and the resulting weights directly identify the constituent geometries. The method accurately reconstructs configurations of increasing complexity and remains robust to repeated constituents, incomplete basis dictionaries, and simulated measurement noise. The framework provides an interpretable route for characterizing strain-engineered graphene nanostructures and may extend to other quantum materials with additive spectral responses.

</details>


### [121] [Stripe-Order Altermagnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17997)
*Zheng-Yang Zhuang,Zhongbo Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于条纹序（stripe order）的交变磁（altermagnetism）新机制，该机制由自旋反转镜面对称性（spin-reversing mirror）主导，而非传统奈尔序（Néel order）反铁磁体中的旋转对称性，并揭示了相应的条纹交变磁相与反交变磁相及其输运特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的交变磁机制主要依赖于奈尔序反铁磁体中的自旋反转旋转（spin-reversing rotations），未能涵盖基于镜面对称性的新类型；本文将建立由自旋反转镜面对称性主导的条纹序交变磁理论，以扩展交变磁的分类框架。

Method: 使用两轨道模型（two-orbital models）分析条纹自旋序与轨道序的耦合；采用随机相位近似（random-phase approximation, RPA）计算，研究强跳迁各向异性（hopping anisotropy）下近半填充（near half filling）区域的条纹序交变磁稳定性。

Result: 发现两种相：条纹交变磁相（stripe altermagnet）具有镜面选择的向列自旋分裂（mirror-selected nematic spin splitting），以及条纹反交变磁相（stripe anti-altermagnet）具有自旋简并能带（spin-degenerate bands）；在合适的翘曲结构（buckled structures）中，反交变磁相可支持类铁电（ferroelectric-like）的自旋分裂电控；RPA计算表明条纹序交变磁在强跳迁各向异性下于近半填充区域占优。

Conclusion: 自旋反转镜面对称性使得与镜面平行或垂直的电场仅产生纯横向自旋电流（purely transverse spin current），为条纹序交变磁提供直接的输运诊断手段。

Abstract: Altermagnetism combines compensated magnetic order with nonrelativistic spin splitting, yet established mechanisms predominantly rely on spin-reversing rotations in Néel-order antiferromagnets. Here we establish stripe-order altermagnetism governed instead by a spin-reversing mirror, placing it outside the usual rotation-based $l$-wave classification. Using two-orbital models, we show that the interplay of stripe spin and orbital orders yields two phases: a stripe altermagnet with mirror-selected nematic spin splitting and a stripe anti-altermagnet with spin-degenerate bands. The latter can support ferroelectric-like electrical control of spin splitting in suitable buckled structures. Random-phase-approximation (RPA) calculations show that stripe-order altermagnetism is favored near half filling under strong hopping anisotropy. The spin-reversing mirror further enforces a purely transverse spin current for an electric field parallel or normal to the mirror plane, providing a direct transport diagnostic.

</details>


### [122] [Resonant excitations via low frequency pumping in driven magnon systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18073)
*Jan Mathis Giesen,Alexandre Abbass Hamadeh,Imke Schneider,Philipp Pirro,Sebastian Eggert*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用Floquet理论分析铁磁自旋波（magnons）在微波泵浦下的共振激发，特别是驱动频率低于自旋波能量时的参量共振（parametric resonances）。研究建立了理论框架，能解析预测YIG等铁磁/亚铁磁薄膜中共振区域和共振阈值随阻尼、振幅和频率的变化。共振区域由准能（quasi-energies）的异常点（exceptional points）分隔，结果与微磁模拟吻合。阈值振幅随阻尼呈特征幂律（powerlaw）变化，可实现低频驱动下对选定波数的定向激发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对驱动频率低于自旋波能量时的非线性共振行为理解不足，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用Floquet理论（Floquet theory）分析微波泵浦下铁磁自旋波的共振激发，结合理论框架解析预测共振区域与阈值，并通过微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulations）进行验证。

Result: 共振区域可通过准能的异常点（exceptional points）分隔；阈值振幅随阻尼呈特征幂律关系。

Conclusion: 低频驱动可在较大参数区域内激发参量共振，实现对特定波数自旋波的定向激发。

Abstract: We analyse resonant excitations of ferromagnetic magnons via microwave pumping using Floquet theory. Special focus is put on driving frequencies that are below the corresponding magnon energy, which can be excited in large parameter regions via parametric resonances. We develop a theoretical framework that analytically predicts the regions of resonances and resonance thresholds in thin films of ferro- and ferri-magnetic materials like YIG as a function of damping, amplitude and frequency. Resonance regions are separated by exceptional points of the quasi-energies and the results are compared with micromagnetic simulations. The corresponding threshold amplitudes can be estimated from a characteristic powerlaw with damping, leading to the possibility of targeted exciatations at selected wavenumbers using low frequency drive.

</details>


### [123] [Contrasting $Γ$- and K-Valley Moiré Physics in Twisted Monolayer/Bilayer WSe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18212)
*Jackson Kuklin,Ning Mao,Milan Mandigo-Stoba,Edgar Elias,Tianci Song,Connor Engel,Pola Pietrzkowski,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Daniel Rhodes,Yang Zhang,Qianhui Shi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本工作识别出扭曲单层/双层WSe₂作为一个可通过位移场调控在K谷和Γ谷分别实现莫尔物理的平台，揭示了不同轨道特征（orbital character）在相同莫尔填充因子下产生截然不同的关联量子相。K谷表现为弱绝缘体（接近反铁磁态），而Γ谷展现出显著的Pomeranchuk效应，靠近Mott转变；在填充因子ν=1/3时，K谷形成稳健的广义Wigner晶体，Γ谷则位于结晶边界附近且同样呈现Pomeranchuk效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子轨道特征（electronic orbital character）在决定关联效应、自旋-轨道耦合、维度以及凝聚态体系的量子相中起核心作用。二维莫尔材料虽已成为高度可调谐的关联现象研究平台，但轨道自由度的角色在很大程度上仍未得到探索。

Method: 通过实验上的位移场调控（displacement-field tuning），在扭曲单层/双层WSe₂体系中分别实现了K谷与Γ谷的莫尔物理，利用两种谷不同的轨道特征对比其在相同莫尔填充因子下的关联相行为。

Result: 在填充因子ν=1时，K谷态为弱绝缘体，对应van Hove奇点附近的反铁磁态（antiferromagnetic state），与扭曲双层WSe₂观测结果一致；Γ谷态则显示出显著的Pomeranchuk效应，靠近Mott转变（Mott transition）。在ν=1/3时，K谷形成稳健的广义Wigner晶体（generalized Wigner crystal），Γ谷位于结晶边界附近并再次呈现Pomeranchuk效应，温度或磁场的增加可增强局域化。

Conclusion: 本工作强调了轨道特征在定义莫尔体系量子相中的关键作用，并指出Γ谷是一个有前景的平台，可用于探索量子相变附近的关联现象，其中竞争相和增强的涨落可能催生非常规量子相。

Abstract: Electronic orbital character plays a central role in determining electronic correlations, spin-orbit coupling, dimensionality, and ultimately the quantum phases of condensed-matter systems. Two-dimensional moiré materials have emerged as highly tunable platforms for exploring correlated phenomena, but the role of orbital degrees of freedom remains largely unexplored. Here, we identify twisted monolayer/bilayer WSe$_2$ as a platform in which displacement-field tuning enables moiré physics to be realized in both the $K$ and $Γ$ valleys. The distinct orbital characters of these valleys give rise to contrasting correlated phases at moiré filling factors $ν=1$ and $ν=1/3$. At $ν=1$, the $K$-valley state is a weak insulator, consistent with an antiferromagnetic state near a van Hove singularity in the intermediate-coupling regime, similar to that observed in twisted bilayer WSe$_2$. In contrast, the $Γ$-valley state exhibits a pronounced Pomeranchuk effect, consistent with proximity to a Mott transition. At $ν=1/3$, the $K$ valley hosts a robust generalized Wigner crystal, whereas the $Γ$-valley state lies near the crystallization boundary and again exhibits a Pomeranchuk effect, with localization enhanced by increasing temperature or magnetic field. Our work highlights the importance of orbital character in defining quantum phases in moiré systems, and identify the $Γ$ valley as a promising platform for exploring correlated phenomena near quantum phase transitions, where competing phases and enhanced fluctuations may give rise to unconventional phases.

</details>


### [124] [Position-dependent tight-binding model for Li impurities in monolayer and bilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18214)
*Hernan Aguirre,Hernan L. Calvo,Eduardo M. Perassi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过发展一个半经验紧束缚模型（semi-empirical tight-binding model）来研究锂离子吸附在单层石墨烯（MLG）以及插层在AB堆叠双层石墨烯（BLG）中的电子结构，模型参数通过拟合密度泛函理论（DFT）计算确定，能够准确再现费米能级附近的电子能带，并揭示锂离子引入的微扰具有强烈局域化特征，且单层与双层石墨烯的杂质势空间轮廓存在系统性差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 锂吸附和插层会显著改变石墨烯基材料（graphene-based materials）的低能电子性质，理解这些改性对研究锂离子在石墨电极中的输运与存储至关重要。

Method: 发展了一个依赖于锂离子位置的半经验紧束缚模型（semi-empirical tight-binding model），通过拟合不同构型、高度及超胞尺寸下的密度泛函理论（DFT）计算来确定模型参数。

Result: 该模型准确复现了单层石墨烯（MLG）和双层石墨烯（BLG）费米能级附近的电子能带，并清晰解释了对称性破缺（symmetry breakings）、谷间混合（intervalley mixing）及能隙打开（band-gap openings）等杂质诱导的能带改性。锂离子引入的微扰高度局域化，效应随超胞尺寸增大而减弱；拟合参数进一步揭示MLG与BLG在杂质势空间轮廓上存在系统性差异。

Conclusion: 所得结果为研究稀锂杂质提供了高效的理论框架，并可作为未来研究锂离子在石墨烯基材料中扩散及杂质诱导输运现象的有用起点。

Abstract: Lithium adsorption and intercalation can significantly modify the low-energy electronic properties of graphene-based materials, making their characterization relevant for understanding Li-ion transport and storage in graphitic electrodes. In this work, we investigate the electronic structure of a Li ion adsorbed on monolayer graphene (MLG) and intercalated within AB-stacked bilayer graphene (BLG). To this end, we develop a semi-empirical tight-binding model that incorporates Li-position dependence. Its parameters are determined by fitting to density-functional-theory calculations for different configurations, heights, and supercell sizes. The obtained model accurately reproduces the electronic bands near the Fermi level for both MLG and BLG and provides a transparent interpretation of the impurity-induced modifications in terms of symmetry breakings, intervalley mixing, and band-gap openings. We find that the perturbation introduced by the Li ion is strongly localized and that its effect decreases with increasing supercell size. The fitted parameters further reveal systematic differences between MLG and BLG in the spatial profile of the impurity potential. The obtained results provide an efficient framework for studying dilute Li impurities and constitute a useful starting point for future investigations of Li diffusion and impurity-induced transport phenomena in graphene-based materials.

### [125] [Non-Abelian Gauge Field Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18215)
*Ivan Velkovsky,Carlos Camacho,Tomoki Ozawa,Hannah Price,Bryce Gadway*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文通过主动机械晶格（active mechanical lattice）实验实现了可调的非阿贝尔规范场（non-Abelian gauge field），并展示了其与非厄米动力学（non-Hermitian dynamics）的相互作用，包括方向依赖的Wilson圈（Wilson loops）和非厄米皮肤模（non-Hermitian skin modes）的局域化切换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非阿贝尔规范场在描述与内部自由度（如自旋）耦合的粒子运动行为中起关键作用，但实验上实现可控的非阿贝尔规范场仍具挑战。本文旨在通过主动机械晶格平台，实验实现可调的非阿贝尔规范场，并进一步探索其与非厄米动力学的相互作用。

Method: 利用成对振子（oscillators）编码每个格点上的局域赝自旋（pseudo-spin），通过实时测量和反馈（real-time measurement and feedback）设计格点间自旋依赖的跃迁（spin-dependent hoppings），从而在主动机械晶格中实验实现可调的非阿贝尔规范场。

Result: 实验提取了Wilson圈可观测量，证实产生了真正的非阿贝尔规范场。在二维（2D）晶格中，展示了非厄米性可导致单原胞（single plaquette）的方向依赖Wilson圈；在一维（1D）系统中，展示了非阿贝尔规范势可切换非厄米皮肤模在链两端的局域化位置。

Conclusion: 本工作建立了主动机械晶格作为灵活可编程的平台，用于探测非阿贝尔规范场并探索其与非厄米动力学的相互作用。

Abstract: Non-Abelian gauge fields play a key role in describing the behavior of particles whose motion is coupled to internal degrees of freedom, such as their spin. Here, we experimentally realize a tuneable non-Abelian gauge field in an active mechanical lattice by using pairs of oscillators to encode a local pseudo-spin for each site, with inter-site spin-dependent couplings engineered via real-time measurement and feedback. We experimentally extract Wilson-loop observables in our set-up and hence demonstrate that we can create a genuinely non-Abelian gauge field. We then exploit the controllability of our mechanical lattice to engineer non-reciprocal hoppings to explore non-Hermitian non-Abelian gauge potentials. For a two-dimensional (2D) lattice, we demonstrate that the non-Hermiticity can manifest in direction-dependent Wilson loops for a single plaquette, while for a one-dimensional (1D) system, we show that a non-Abelian gauge potential can switch the localization of non-Hermitian skin modes between opposite ends of a chain. Our work establishes active mechanical lattices as a flexible and programmable platform for probing non-Abelian gauge fields and exploring their interplay with non-Hermitian dynamics.

### [126] [An Unsupervised Search for Novel Instrumental Glitches in LIGO O4a: Multi-Scale Sensitization, Empirical Physical Vetoes, and Rate Upper Limits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18136)
*Luca Cirfeta*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文介绍 DANTE V3，这是针对 LIGO、Virgo、KAGRA 第四次观测运行（O4）早期未建模异常的系统性研究。通过多尺度几何框架提取了 10,372 个候选事件，引入块自助领域偏移防御（block-bootstrap Domain Shift Defense, DSD）以应对探测器噪声流形的不平稳领域偏移。经过背景重校准、物理环境监测交叉相关防御和物理归一化交叉相关检验后，未发现任何重合事件，表明这些候选事件不具备离散形态凝聚性，并给出了新型未编录仪器形态率的 90% 频率论泊松上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: O4 观测运行中 Advanced LIGO、Virgo 和 KAGRA 探测器灵敏度空前提高，导致无监督流水线极易受到探测器噪声流形非平稳领域偏移（non-stationary domain shift）的影响。因此需要对未建模异常进行系统的纵向研究并建立有效的防御机制。

Method: 扩展至多尺度几何框架（multi-scale geometric framework，0.5 s 至 4.0 s）以增强形态敏感性；引入块自助领域偏移防御（block-bootstrap Domain Shift Defense, DSD）对抗矢量量化原生背景指标；执行物理环境监测（physical environment monitoring, PEM）交叉相关防御及物理归一化交叉相关检验。

Result: 提取 10,372 个唯一候选事件，28.3% 在重校准后幸存；全局拓扑分析显示幸存者缺乏离散形态凝聚性，聚合成单一宏观簇而无紧凑子结构；形态“扩散性”比较方法被证明存在混淆并被弃用；PEM 防御中一个候选因控制线耦合被否决，另一个幸存为未编录仪器异常；交叉相关检验未发现任何重叠事件；给出 90% 频率论泊松上限：$R_{90} \le 5.83 \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$ (H1) 和 $R_{90} \le 5.64 \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$ (L1)。

Conclusion: 在无监督引力波天文学中，原生背景重校准和物理辅助否决机制是绝对必要的。DANTE V3 的研究结果强调了领域偏移防御和物理交叉检验对避免虚假探测的关键作用。

Abstract: The fourth observing run (O4) of Advanced LIGO, Virgo, and KAGRA presents unparalleled sensitivity, rendering unsupervised pipelines highly vulnerable to the non-stationary domain shift of the detectors' noise manifolds. We present DANTE V3, concluding a longitudinal investigation into unmodeled anomalies during early O4a. By expanding to a multi-scale geometric framework (0.5 s to 4.0 s), we amplify morphological sensitivity, extracting 10,372 unique candidates. To mitigate domain-shift artifacts, we introduce a block-bootstrap Domain Shift Defense (DSD) against a vector-quantized native background index. While 28.3% of candidates survive recalibration, global topological analysis reveals they lack discrete morphological cohesion. The survivors coalesce into a single macro-cluster without compact substructure; we show explicitly that morphological "diffusivity" comparisons used previously are confounded and retire them. Pristine background is even more monolithic (100% in one cluster vs 99.77% for survivors): this topology is a property of the embedding geometry, not of anomaly status. Executing a definitive physical environment monitoring (PEM) cross-correlation defense using an empirically calibrated null, one singleton is vetoed by a control-line coupling, while another survives as an uncatalogued instrumental outlier. Replacing the embedding-similarity cross-detector coincidence test with a physical normalized cross-correlation test, we find no coincident events among 8,749 candidates. We quote 90% frequentist Poisson upper limits on the rate of novel uncatalogued instrumental morphologies -- $R_{90} \le 5.83 \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$ (H1) and $R_{90} \le 5.63 \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$ (L1). This underscores the absolute necessity of native background recalibration and physical auxiliary vetoes in unsupervised gravitational-wave astronomy.

</details>

### [127] [Transverse Charge Distribution as a Probe of Nucleon Transversity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16392)
*Wanchen Li,Xiaohui Liu,Ding Yu Shao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了横向电荷分布（transverse charge distribution）作为一种自旋敏感的电荷流探针，用于碎裂过程（fragmentation）和核子层析（nucleon tomography）。该可观测量的测量仅依赖带电粒子径迹方向和电荷符号，无需量热能量测量。该分布可分解为无极化电荷单极子和手征奇性的横向电荷偶极子，其中偶极子由Collins效应（Collins effect）控制并直接耦合到横向性（transversity）。将该形式应用于RHIC上的横向极化p↑p碰撞，发现电荷加权可抑制无极化单极子背景，并使来自相反电荷强子的自旋依赖偶极子相干叠加，从而显著增强方位角不对称性，为提取横向性提供了一条理论上干净且实验上精确的纯径迹途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的碎裂函数和核子层析方法通常依赖于量热能量测量，在实验上存在复杂性。本文旨在提出一种仅基于带电粒子径迹测量的自旋敏感探针，以更简洁的方式探测夸克碎裂过程中的电荷流动以及核子内部结构，特别是为提取横向性（transversity）提供新的实验途径。

Method: 引入横向电荷分布作为可观测量的概念；推导其在领头扭度（leading twist）下的算符乘积展开（OPE）为荷重共线矩（charge-weighted collinear moments）；将形式应用于RHIC上横向极化p↑p碰撞的物理场景；通过电荷加权（charge weighting）技术抑制无极化背景并增强自旋依赖信号。

Result: 横向电荷分布分解为无极化电荷单极子和手征奇性横向电荷偶极子；单极子由电荷守恒固定，偶极子由Collins效应控制并直接耦合到横向性。在横向极化p↑p碰撞中，电荷加权技术导致来自相反电荷强子的自旋依赖偶极子相干叠加，从而显著增强方位角不对称性（azimuthal asymmetries）。

Conclusion: 横向电荷分布为碎裂过程和核子层析提供了一种理论上干净且实验上精确的自旋敏感探针。基于纯径迹（track-only）的测量方式绕过了量热能量测量的需求，并且通过电荷加权显著增强了自旋依赖信号，为提取横向性建立了可靠的实验途径。

Abstract: We introduce the transverse charge distribution as a spin-sensitive charge-flow probe for fragmentation and nucleon tomography. By measuring the angular distribution of net electric charge around a fragmenting quark, this observable relies entirely on the tracking of charged-particle directions and charge signs, strictly bypassing the need for calorimetric energy measurements. At leading twist, the distribution decomposes into an unpolarized charge monopole and a chiral-odd transverse charge dipole. We derive the operator product expansion of these distributions onto charge-weighted collinear moments: the monopole is fixed by charge conservation, while the dipole is governed by the Collins effect and couples directly to transversity. Applying this formalism to transversely polarized $p^\uparrow p$ collisions at RHIC, we show that charge weighting suppresses the unpolarized monopole background and causes the spin-dependent dipoles from oppositely charged hadrons to add coherently. This coherence strongly enhances the resulting azimuthal asymmetries, establishing a theoretically clean and experimentally precise track-only avenue for extracting transversity.

</details>

Method: 构建了一个基准门户模型，假设暗扇区与标准模型仅有微弱耦合（feeble coupling）。通过轴子类中介子与暗π介子之间的混合机制生成信号，并分析了由此产生的位移衰变（displaced-decay）特征。

Result: 识别出长寿命的味对角暗π介子可产生位移衰变信号，该信号在电子-离子对撞机上无需硬触发条件即可被探测，适合用来记录软末态粒子，从而为暗强子化动力学提供互补性探针。

Conclusion: 电子-离子对撞机因其独特的软粒子探测能力，能够对GeV能标禁闭的暗非阿贝尔规范体系进行有效搜索，位移衰变信号可作为该暗扇区模型的关键实验特征。

Abstract: We study a dark non-Abelian gauge sector with GeV-scale confinement. The dark sector is assumed to couple only feebly to the Standard Model, while its low-energy spectrum may contain long-lived flavor-diagonal dark pions. Signals of these states are particularly well suited to the Electron-Ion Collider (EIC), where the absence of a hard trigger requirement and the capability to record soft final-state particles offer a complementary probe of dark hadronization dynamics. Abstract: The QCD axion with charm-only Peccei-Quinn coupling evades the isospin-violation problem of light-quark models in $χ$PT. Since $m_c>Λ_{\rm QCD}$, we employ heavy meson chiral perturbation theory (HMChPT) to constrain this GeV-scale axion, including its CP-even radial partner $σ$ and the axion $a$. In HMChPT, $σ$ enters at leading order with $O(1)$ coupling, while $a$ couples only at $O(1/m_c)$ and manifests via axion-pion mixing with $θ_{aπ}\simeq f_π/f_a\sim0.04$. We analyze $D$-meson masses, $D$-$D^*$ splitting, charmonium, $D$-$D$ scattering, $B_s$ mixing, rare $D$ decays, and the channels $K^+\toπ^+a$, $B\to K a$. No fatal HMChPT constraint emerges, unlike the $χ$PT isospin issue. One can find that the branching ratios of the decays $Υ(3S)\to B_c\ellν_\ell$ are the largest among those of considered semileptonic decays and can amount to $10^{-9}$; As to the nonleptonic decays, $Υ(3S)\to B_cρ$ and $Υ(3S)\to B_cD^{(*)}_s$ have the largest branching ratios, which reach up to $10^{-10}$. ### [131] [Attractodynamics in 0+1D](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16393)
*Jean F. Du Plessis,Bruno Scheihing-Hitschfeld,Rachel Steinhorst*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出“吸引子动力学（attractodynamics）”，一种围绕远离平衡态吸引子构建的宏观理论，并通过0+1维模型验证其相对于完整动力学演化的可改进描述能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流体力学（hydrodynamics）仅适用于局部热平衡附近的动力学，而许多物理系统在远离平衡态时仍表现出吸引子行为。作者希望发展一种能系统描述远离平衡态吸引子附近动力学的宏观理论框架。

Method: 从0+1维开始，选取一个已知各向异性远离平衡态吸引子解的模型，建立理想的吸引子动力学方程（ideal attractodynamic equations）以及包含领先瞬态残差（leading transient residual）的扩展形式，并与完整的动理学演化（full kinetic evolution）进行直接比较。

Result: 理想的吸引子动力学能够捕捉吸引子流形附近的演化，而引入领先的离吸引子矩（off-attractor moments）可扩展一致性的范围，直至有限截断失效。这表明该层级结构提供了对近吸引子动力学的可改进描述。

Conclusion: 该0+1维示例明确了构建局域3+1维吸引子动力学所需的要素，并表明吸引子动力学可作为不依赖于底层动理学描述的宏观理论独立存在。

Abstract: Hydrodynamics is a macroscopic theory of long-wavelength dynamics around local thermal equilibrium. We develop attractodynamics, the analogous construction around a far-from-equilibrium attractor. Dynamics near a far-from-equilibrium attractor retains some non-hydrodynamic microscopic information, which attractodynamics systematically organizes. We move towards this general structure by starting in 0+1D, and consider a model for which an anisotropic far-from-equilibrium attractor solution is exactly known. This setting provides a clean benchmark in which the ideal attractodynamic equations and a leading transient residual extension can be compared directly with the full kinetic evolution. The resulting hierarchy gives an improvable description of near-attractor dynamics: the ideal theory captures evolution close to the attracting manifold, while retaining the leading off-attractor moments extends the regime of agreement until the finite truncation breaks down. This example identifies the ingredients needed for local 3+1D attractodynamics and for macroscopic attractodynamic theories not derived from an underlying kinetic description.

### [132] [Light-front diagnostics in the 't Hooft model: II. Boundary cancellations, ERBL spectral sums, and analyticity of the EMT form factor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16426)
*Arkadiy I. Syamtomov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 论文在't Hooft模型的大N_c极限下，通过完整构造广义部分子分布（GPD）的第二阶矩，研究了光前重叠（light-front overlap）中近前向能量-动量张量（EMT）信息的解析结构，证明了边界指数、共振对数等奇异性在ERBL与DGLAP两个支撑区域之间的抵消机制，并提取了稳定的曲率与纵向迹半径等物理量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对角光前重叠本身并非局域矩阵元（local matrix element），但其包含近前向能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor, EMT）信息。论文旨在通过完整构造广义部分子分布（generalized parton distribution, GPD）的第二阶矩，厘清ERBL与DGLAP两个支撑区域的组合方式，并解析其中边界指数和共振对数等奇异结构的物理含义与抵消机制。

Method: 在大N_c极限下的't Hooft模型（'t Hooft model）中，论文完成了GPD第二阶矩的ERBL（Efremov-Radyushkin-Brodsky-Lepage）贡献部分，系统地追踪了两个支撑区域（support regions）如何结合。通过分析边界指数（boundary exponents）导致的分数幂次（fractional powers）和β=1/2处共振对数（resonant logarithms），检验了包括领头与次领头指标族（indicial families）干涉在内的抵消行为，并利用中间态分解（intermediate-state decomposition）研究极点强度（pole strength）的重新分布。

Result: 证明了边界指数和共振对数等奇异性在两区域间完全抵消；在共振点处，双重与单对数的抵消还产生了一个逆质量平方求和规则（inverse-mass-squared residue sum rule）。在共振点之上，两区域组合为有限四阶系数，使得完整的EMT形状因子（form factor）在曲率阶（curvature order）上解析。ERBL扇区不影响斜率（slope），但对曲率（curvature）及更高阶导数至关重要。提取了稳定的规范曲率（canonical curvature）与重曲率（heavy curvature），给出了第二、第三轻激发态的系统性包络估计（systematic envelopes），以及纵向迹半径（longitudinal trace radius）。

Conclusion: ERBL与DGLAP两支撑区域的奇异结构在完整GPD矩中精确抵消，保证了EMT形状因子的解析性。这一机制在't Hooft模型中得到了严格验证，且从中提取的曲率与迹半径等物理量具有稳定性与系统性意义，为理解光前重叠中非局域矩阵元的结构提供了重要参考。

Abstract: A diagonal light-front overlap contains near-forward energy-momentum-tensor (EMT) information but is not itself a local matrix element. In the large-$N_c$ 't Hooft model we complete the second GPD moment with its ERBL contribution and follow how the two support regions combine. Boundary exponents generate fractional powers and, at $β=1/2$, resonant logarithms in the separate terms. We show that these structures cancel, including the interference of the leading and next indicial families. At the resonance, cancellation of the double and single logarithms also yields an inverse-mass-squared residue sum rule; above it, the two regions combine into a finite fourth-order coefficient. The complete EMT form factor is therefore analytic through curvature order. The ERBL sector leaves the slope unchanged but is essential for curvature and higher derivatives. We extract stable canonical and heavy curvatures, estimates with systematic envelopes for the second and third light excitations, and the longitudinal trace radius. The intermediate-state decomposition further shows how constituent mass and excitation redistribute pole strength and generate removable poles and interference zeros.

### [133] [Detailed study of the dual symmetry of dense quark matter within the effective action formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17190)
*T. G. Khunjua,K. G. Klimenko,R. N. Zhokhov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在无质量(3+1)维NJL模型和QCD模型框架下，研究了由$u$、$d$夸克（三色）组成的致密夸克物质的相图对称性，发现体系在重子数化学势（baryon chemical potential）$\mu_B$、同位旋化学势（isospin chemical potential）$\mu_I$、手征化学势（chiral chemical potential）$\mu_5$和手征同位旋化学势（chiral isospin chemical potential）$\mu_{I5}$共同存在时，拉格朗日量在所谓对偶变换（dual transformation）$\mathcal{D}$下不变，且路径积分测度也保持不变，因此整个热力学势具有对偶对称性（dual symmetry）。该对偶对称性意味着手征对称性破缺（chiral symmetry breaking, CSB）相和带电π介子凝聚（charged pion condensation, PC）相在$(μ_B,μ_I,μ_5,μ_{I5})$相图中呈对偶共轭排列。这是无质量致密QCD的一个基本性质，对QCD相图研究具有重要意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究由$u$、$d$夸克（三色）组成的致密夸克物质在多种化学势（$\mu_B,\mu_I,\mu_5,\mu_{I5}$）共同作用下的相图对称性，并验证该对称性是否在路径积分层面成立，从而揭示CSB相与带电PC相之间的内在对偶关系。

Method: 在无质量(3+1)维Nambu–Jona-Lasinio (NJL)模型和量子色动力学（QCD）模型框架下，分析引入四种化学势后拉格朗日量的对称性，并进一步检验配分函数的路径积分测度在对偶变换$\cal D$下的不变性，从而证明完整热力学势的对偶对称性。

Result: 在$\mu_B,\mu_I,\mu_5,\mu_{I5}$存在时，NJL模型和QCD模型的拉格朗日量及路径积分测度均在对偶变换$\cal D$下保持不变；因此相图中CSB相与带电PC相呈对偶共轭（对称）排列。

Conclusion: CSB相与带电PC相之间的对偶对称性是无质量致密QCD的一个基本性质，应在QCD相图的任何近似框架下均成立，并对手征对称性破缺与超导等多体现象的研究具有重要意义。

Abstract: The symmetry properties of the phase diagram of dense quark matter composed of $u$ and $d$ quarks with three colors have been investigated in the framework of massless (3+1)-dimensional Nambu--Jona-Lasinio (NJL) and QCD models. It turns out that in the presence of baryon $μ_B$, isospin $μ_I$, chiral $μ_5$ and chiral isospin $μ_{I5}$ chemical potentials, the Lagrangians of these models are invariant under the so-called dual transformation ${\cal D}$. In this paper, it has been shown that the path integration measure of the corresponding partition functions is also invariant under ${\cal D}$. Consequently, the entire NJL model (or QCD) thermodynamic potentials are dually symmetric. In particular, it means that in the total $(μ_B,μ_I,μ_5,μ_{I5})$-phase portraits of these models the chiral symmetry breaking (CSB) and charged pion condensation (PC) phases are arranged dually conjugate (or symmetrically) to each other. Dual symmetry between CSB and charged PC phases of quark matter is a fundamental property of massless dense QCD; it should be observed in the framework of any approximation to the QCD phase diagram, and have important implications for studies of the phase structure.

### [134] [Breaking the Democratic Limit in the Generalized Friedberg-Lee Model: Implications for Neutrino Masses and Mixing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17258)
*N. Razzaghi*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准FL框架中的民主极限（democratic limit）虽然理论上深刻，但预测了简并质量谱（degenerate mass spectrum）和零反应堆角（θ₁₃=0），已被实验排除。因此需要在高对称极限与实验观测之间建立桥梁，在保持理论自洽性的前提下实现可观测的中微子混合与质量分裂。

Method: 基于广义Friedberg-Lee（FL）框架，在奇异点Point D（α=β=-1/3）处引入最小且系统性的微扰（perturbation），该微扰保持扭曲Friedberg-Lee（TFL）对称性，避免使用ad hoc参数，从而在受控方式下打破魔幻对称性（magic symmetry）和μ-τ对称性（μ-τ symmetry）。

Result: 模型预测倒置质量序（inverted mass hierarchy，m₃=0）、非零反应堆角θ₁₃、最大大气混合角（maximal atmospheric mixing）、显著的狄拉克CP相位（Dirac CP phase）以及本征CP破缺（intrinsic CP violation）。中微子质量和Jarlskog不变量（Jarlskog invariant）的数值范围与全局拟合数据高度一致。

Conclusion: 该工作在TFL对称性方案内为中微子味物理学（neutrino flavor physics）提供了一个具有理论动机的坚实基础，表明通过受控对称性破缺可以将高对称极限与实验观测自然统一。

Abstract: We investigate a generalized Friedberg--Lee (FL) framework for neutrino masses, focusing on the singular parameter space at Point D ($α= β= -1/3$). At this limit, the neutrino mass matrix exhibits a democratic texture governed by the $S_3$ permutation symmetry. Although theoretically profound, the exact democratic limit is phenomenologically excluded as it predicts a degenerate mass spectrum and a vanishing reactor angle ($θ_{13}=0$). To reconcile this high-symmetry limit with experimental observations, we introduce a minimal and systematic perturbation that preserves the Twisted Friedberg--Lee (TFL) symmetry. This mechanism effectively lifts the mass degeneracy and breaks the magic and $μ$--$τ$ symmetries in a controlled manner. Our derivation avoids \textit{ad hoc} parameters, establishing a robust framework that yields a realistic inverted mass hierarchy ($m_3=0$), a non-zero $θ_{13}$, and intrinsic CP violation. We demonstrate that the model predicts maximal atmospheric mixing and a significant Dirac CP phase. The obtained numerical ranges for the neutrino masses and the Jarlskog invariant show excellent agreement with global fit data, providing a theoretically motivated foundation for neutrino flavor physics within the TFL scheme.

</details>


### [135] [Theoretical uncertainties in reconstructing model parameters with gravitational waves from supercooled phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18233)
*Maciej Kierkla,Marek Lewicki,Philipp Schicho,Daniel Schmitt,Bogumila Swiezewska*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文比较了两种重求和方案（高温有效场论 vs. 菊花重求有效势）对经典尺度不变U(1)_X模型中引力波信号重构的影响，发现菊花重求方案因理论误差主导重构不确定性而被强烈排除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未来干涉仪可能探测到来自宇宙一阶相变的引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）信号，但从信号反推底层的粒子物理模型需要对微观物理到频谱的映射具有理论控制。对于经典尺度不变的（classically scale-invariant）标准模型扩展，这一映射对核化率（nucleation rate）的量子与热修正处理非常敏感。

Method: 以经典共形U(1)_X模型为代表，扫描其参数空间并比较两种重求和（resummation）方案：一是高温有效场论（high-temperature effective field theory），在双圈水平匹配并包含对反弹作用量（bounce action）的次领头阶（next-to-leading-order, NLO）修正，核化率前因子（prefactor）由完整单圈泛函行列式给出；二是常用的菊花重求有效势（daisy-resummed effective potential），前因子按量纲估计。通过Fisher矩阵（Fisher-matrix）分析LISA探测器注入GW信号的方式来重构基本模型参数。

Result: 菊花重求方案的理论误差主导了重构不确定性，因此该方案被强烈排除（strongly disfavored）。

Conclusion: 对于产生强过冷相变（strongly supercooled transitions）和强GW信号的经典尺度不变模型，必须采用更高精度的理论方案（如高温有效场论加NLO修正）才能可靠地从未来GW观测中反演粒子物理参数。

Abstract: Future interferometers may detect a gravitational-wave (GW) signal from a cosmological first-order phase transition. Reconstructing the underlying particle-physics model from such a signal requires theoretical control over the map from microphysics to the spectrum. For classically scale-invariant extensions of the Standard Model, which generically predict strongly supercooled transitions and strong GW signals, this map depends sensitively on the treatment of quantum and thermal corrections to the nucleation rate. Taking the classically conformal ${\rm U}(1)_X$ model as representative of this class, we scan its parameter space and compare two resummation schemes. The first is a high-temperature effective field theory, matched at two-loop level and including next-to-leading-order corrections to the bounce action, with the nucleation-rate prefactor given by the full one-loop functional determinants. The second is a commonly employed daisy-resummed effective potential, with the prefactor estimated on dimensional grounds. Reconstructing the fundamental model parameters through a Fisher-matrix analysis of injected GW signals at LISA, we find that the daisy-resummation scheme is strongly disfavored, as its theoretical error dominates over the reconstruction uncertainty.

</details>

### [136] [Schema-Bound LLM Control of Scientific Instrumentation through Model Context Protocol Skills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17012)
*Roberto dos Reis,Vinayak P. Dravid*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过模型上下文协议（Model Context Protocol, MCP）将本地大语言模型（LLM）连接到科学仪器的可行方法，包括模式绑定的工具表面、供应商中立的适配器模式、持久化生命周期及MCP注册技能，从而为闭环自主仪器研究提供了可测试、可复现的受控基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（large language models, LLMs）能够规划工具驱动的科学工作，但科学仪器仍然难以与这类智能体连接：供应商应用程序接口（API）可能仅在内采集主机进程中加载，设施可能禁止云托管智能体，而自然语言接口可能生成物理上不合理的参数。因此需要一种本地的、受约束的、可验证的连接方法。

Method: 方法通过模型上下文协议（Model Context Protocol, MCP）集成四个要素：(1) 模式绑定的工具表面（schema-bound tool surface），在适配器派发前根据物理边界验证请求；(2) 供应商中立的、主机进程内的适配器模式（adapter pattern），将语言端推理与仪器端执行分离；(3) 面向长时间运行实时处理任务的持久化生命周期（persistent lifecycle）；(4) MCP提示注册的技能（MCP-prompt-registered skills），将类型化工具组合为可复用的多步协议。

Result: 开源源码参考服务器实现了30个类型化工具、5种实时任务类型和6项技能，并通过物理合理模拟器（physics-plausible simulator）实现相同协议表面。120项独立于硬件的测试全部确定性通过；15项本地LLM集成测试因模型非确定性在12–15项之间通过。一次初步单次探测（非基准测试，无置信区间）显示，五种开源工具调用LLM可在无云依赖的情况下本地驱动该模式绑定接口。

Conclusion: 该方法为闭环自主仪器研究（closed-loop agentic instrumentation research）提供了一个受边界约束、可测试且可复现的基础。尽管存在模型非确定性和初步探测的局限性，但整体框架在软件层面通过了完整验证。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can plan tool-mediated scientific work, but scientific instruments remain difficult to connect to such agents: vendor APIs may load only inside acquisition host processes, facilities may prohibit cloud-hosted agents, and natural-language interfaces can emit physically unreasonable arguments. We present a method for connecting local LLMs to scientific instruments through the Model Context Protocol (MCP). It combines: (1) a schema-bound tool surface that validates requests against physical bounds before adapter dispatch; (2) a vendor-neutral, host-process adapter pattern separating language-side reasoning from instrument-side execution; (3) a persistent lifecycle for long-running live-processing jobs; and (4) MCP-prompt-registered skills that compose typed tools into reusable multi-step protocols. Our open-source reference server exposes 30 typed tools, 5 live-job types, and 6 skills through a physics-plausible simulator implementing the same protocol surface. Validation is software-only: all 120 hardware-independent tests pass deterministically, while 15 local-LLM integration tests pass 12-15 of 15 across runs because of model nondeterminism. A preliminary single-run probe across five open tool-calling LLMs indicates that the schema-bound interface can be driven locally by small open-weight models without cloud dependency; it is not a benchmark and has no confidence intervals. The method provides a bounded, testable, and reproducible foundation for closed-loop agentic instrumentation research.

### [137] [Scalar glueball-$s\bar{s}$ mixing in one flavor lattice QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17294)
*Long-Cheng Gui,Wei Sun,Ying Chen,Ming Gong,Geng Li,Zhaofeng Liu*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 该论文利用 $N_f=1$ 各向异性晶格量子色动力学（lattice QCD）模拟，通过广义本征值问题（GEVP）求解标量胶球（scalar glueball）与 $s\overline{s}$ 介子的混合，得到两个最低本征态质量分别为 $1.290(20)\,\mathrm{GeV}$ 和 $1.777(49)\,\mathrm{GeV}$，混合角 $|θ| \approx 40.7(2.7)^\circ$，混合能 $x_s = 239(24)$ MeV，表明标量扇区中存在显著的胶球-奇异夸克偶素混合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了理解实验上观测到的同位旋标量标量介子的内部结构，需要非微扰地定量研究标量胶球与 $s\overline{s}$ 介子之间的混合效应。

Method: 采用 $N_f=1$ 各向异性 $16^3 \times 128$ 格点系综（格距 $a_s\approx 0.148\,\rm{fm}$），在 $J^\text{PC} = 0^{++}$ 道中构建优化的胶球和 $s\overline{s}$ 标量算符，通过求解广义本征值问题（GEVP）提取质量本征态及其与两类算符的耦合强度。

Result: 两个最低本征态质量为 $m_1 = 1.290(20)\,\mathrm{GeV}$ 和 $m_2 = 1.777(49)\,\mathrm{GeV}$；混合角 $|θ| \approx 40.7(2.7)^\circ$；混合能 $x_s = 239(24)$ MeV。

Conclusion: 标量扇区中存在强烈的胶球-$s\overline{s}$ 混合，该结果为理解实验同位旋标量标量介子的性质提供了重要非微扰输入；混合能的连续极限及其夸克质量依赖性有待后续研究。

Abstract: We investigate the mixing between the lowest-lying scalar glueball and the $s\overline{s}$ meson in $N_f=1$ lattice quantum chromodynamics (QCD) utilizing an anisotropic $16^3 \times 128$ lattice ensemble at a lattice spacing $a_s\approx 0.148\,\rm{fm}$. By solving a generalized eigenvalue problem (GEVP) for the optimized glueball and $s\overline{s}$ scalar operators in the $J^\text{PC} = 0^{++}$ channel, the masses of the two lowest-lying eigenstates are determined to be $m_1 = 1.290(20)\,\mathrm{GeV}$ and $m_2 = 1.777(49)\,\mathrm{GeV}$. By extracting the couplings of these mass eigenstates to the glueball and $s\bar{s}$ operators, we determine a substantial mixing angle $|θ| \approx 40.7(2.7)^\circ$ and a large mixing energy $x_s = 239(24)$ MeV. These results indicate a strong glueball-$s\bar{s}$ mixing in the scalar sector, providing important non-perturbative inputs for understanding the nature of the experimental isoscalar scalar mesons. The continuum limit of the mixing energy and its quark mass dependence need to be investigated in the future.

### [138] [Renormalization of meson susceptibilities and RG-invariant symmetry ratios in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17816)
*Ting-Wai Chiu*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文分析了有限温度QCD中具有精确手征对称性的品格公式下介子磁化率的紫外发散结构，揭示了由温度相减消除的加性发散和由重整化因子Z_Γ²控制的乘法发散，并证明由温度相减后的对称伙伴磁化率构成的比值κ_AB是重整化群不变且方案无关的精确量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解有限温度QCD中介子磁化率（meson susceptibilities）的紫外发散结构，并构建一个重整化群不变且方案无关（renormalization-group invariant and scheme-independent）的可观测量，以精确研究手征对称性（chiral symmetry）恢复及其与U(1)_A反常的相互作用。

Method: 采用具有精确手征对称性的品格QCD（lattice QCD）公式，通过温度相减（temperature subtraction）分离加性发散（additive divergences），并利用重整化因子Z_Γ²处理乘法发散（multiplicative renormalization）。基于对称伙伴之间Z因子相等的性质Z_A = Z_B，构造比值κ_AB = (χ_A^reg - χ_B^reg) / (χ_A^reg + χ_B^reg)。

Result: 加性发散包含来自恒等算符（identity operator）的主幂律发散α_Γ/(2a²)和依赖于质量的对数项∝ m² ln(1/(am))，且精确手征对称性禁止了所有依赖于质量的幂律发散。推导了所有介子道的完整Z因子链，并对比了与Wilson费米子（Wilson fermions）的发散结构差异——后者因显式手征对称性破缺导致手征奇性（chiral-odd）幂律发散混合并破坏Z_A = Z_B的等量关系。

Conclusion: 构造的对称性比值κ_AB是重整化群不变且方案无关的精确可观测量，适用于任意风味数和质量，不受自发对称性破缺或U(1)_A反常影响。该构造依赖于精确手征对称性带来的Z_A = Z_B等量关系，在Wilson费米子中不再成立。

Abstract: We analyze the ultraviolet divergence structure of meson susceptibilities in finite-temperature QCD, for lattice formulations with exact chiral symmetry. The bare susceptibility separates into additive divergences and a multiplicative renormalization $Z_Γ^{2}$. The additive divergences are temperature-independent, and are removed by the temperature subtraction. They consist of the leading power divergence $α_Γ/(2a^2)$ from the identity operator, together with a mass-dependent logarithmic term $\propto m^2\ln(1/(am))$. The latter is present already for chirally symmetric fermions. Exact chiral symmetry forbids all mass-dependent \emph{power} divergences of the susceptibility. The multiplicative factor $Z_Γ^{2}$ has a logarithmic dependence on the lattice spacing, controlled by the operator anomalous dimension. We show that the symmetry ratio $κ_{AB} = (χ_A^{\rm reg} - χ_B^{\rm reg})/ (χ_A^{\rm reg} + χ_B^{\rm reg})$, built from temperature-subtracted susceptibilities of symmetry partners, is exactly renormalization-group invariant and scheme-independent. The additive divergence is removed by the subtraction, and the multiplicative factor cancels through the equality $Z_A = Z_B$. This equality holds for any number of flavors and any quark masses in a mass-independent scheme, unaffected by spontaneous symmetry breaking or the $U(1)_A$ anomaly. We derive the complete $Z$-factor chains for all meson channels and contrast the divergence structure with that of Wilson fermions, for which the explicit chiral-symmetry breaking induces a chiral-odd power-divergent mixing and spoils the equality $Z_A = Z_B$ on which the construction relies.

</details>

### [139] [Two-dimensional solitons in extended GPE models with Lee-Huang-Yang corrections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16820)
*G. N. Koutsokostas,F. Bristy,E. C. Psychogiou,G. A. Bougas,G. C. Katsimiga,S. I. Mistakidis,P. G. Kevrekidis,D. J. Frantzeskakis*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文基于扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程，采用多尺度渐近方法推导出Kadomtsev-Petviashvili和Davey-Stewartson可积模型，构造了量子液滴背景上的线孤子、团孤子、环孤子和dromion等多种二维孤子解，并通过数值模拟检验了其动力学鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子液滴（quantum droplet）环境中二维孤子（solitary wave）的存在性与动力学，探索平均场（mean-field）与量子涨落（quantum fluctuation）竞争下前所未有的多维孤子解结构。

Method: 采用多尺度渐近方法（multiscale asymptotic methods）推导背景调制度稳定区间的有效非线性可积模型，对应Kadomtsev-Petviashvili方程和Davey-Stewartson方程；在此基础上构造近似解析解，并通过数值模拟监测解的动力学鲁棒性（dynamical robustness）。

Result: 构造出线孤子（line soliton）、代数局域的团孤子（lump soliton）、环孤子（ring soliton）和指数局域的dromion四种嵌入液滴背景的二维孤子解。线孤子、团孤子和环孤子与理论预测最为接近，虽因小振幅辐射（radiation）而逐渐偏离；dromion与分析波形偏离最大，但大致保持其形状。

Conclusion: 揭示出平均场与量子涨落竞争模型中前所未有的多维孤子解，这些结果适用于当前的超冷原子（ultracold atom）实验。

Abstract: We investigate the existence and dynamics of two-dimensional solitary waves in a quantum droplet environment described by the extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation featuring logarithmic mean-field and Lee-Huang-Yang interactions. In the modulationally stable regime of the background, we employ suitable multiscale asymptotic methods to derive effective nonlinear integrable models corresponding to the Kadomtsev-Petviashvili and Davey-Stewartson equations. Based on these reduced models, we construct approximate analytical solutions describing line solitons, algebraically localized lump solitons, ring solitons, and exponentially localized dromions embedded on the droplet background. The dynamical robustness of these solutions is monitored through numerical simulations. Line, lump and ring solitons stay closest to the theoretical predictions, although progressively deviate due to the emergence of small-amplitude radiation, while dromions depart from their analytical waveform the most, although they roughly maintain their shape. Our results unveil unprecedented multidimensional soliton solutions in models featuring the competition of mean-field and quantum fluctuations and as such are amenable to current ultracold atom experiments.

### [140] [Coexistence of long- and quasi-long range spatial order in 1D quantum quasicrystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17334)
*A. Mendoza-Coto,M. Grossklags,J. Stefaniak,T. Donner,F. Piazza*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 准晶（quasicrystal）中仅有一个 Goldstone 模（phonon 或 phason）在自发对称破缺后获得能隙（gapped），而另一个保持无能隙（gapless），导致一维系统中长程有序（long-range order）与准长程有序（quasi-long-range order）共存。该机制可通过光学腔（optical cavity）中的超冷玻色原子（ultracold bosonic atoms）实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索准晶中独有的自发对称破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）机制：两个不可公度波矢（incommensurate wave vectors）对应的两个 Goldstone 模——声子（phonon）与相位子（phason）——是否可能被不等价地破坏，即仅其中一个获得能隙。

Method: 通过理论分析展示：在准晶中，由于两个竞争波矢的存在，平移对称性（translational invariance）自发破缺后可出现一种新机制——仅使一个 Goldstone 模（对应某个波矢）获得能隙，而另一个保持无能隙。在一维情形下，利用超冷玻色原子在光学腔中的系统进行物理实现。

Result: 发现一种准晶独有的现象：一个 Goldstone 模被能隙化（gapped），另一个保持无能隙（gapless）。在一维中，这导致有能隙波矢方向呈现长程有序（long-range order），无能隙波矢方向因持续涨落（sustained fluctuations）呈现准长程有序（quasi-long-range order）。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了一种准晶特有的对称性破缺机制，即两个 Goldstone 模可被不等价地破坏，并给出了一维光腔-超冷原子系统的具体实现方案，为准晶中非平凡有序现象的探索提供了新途径。

Abstract: Quasicrystals exhibit long-range positional order without periodicity, arising from multiple incommensurate wave vectors. In self-assembled quasicrystals, the spontaneous breaking of translational invariance gives rise to two Goldstone modes-phonons and phasons-associated with two competing wave vectors. Here, we demonstrate a unique scenario exclusive to quasicrystals: a mechanism that gaps out only one Goldstone mode (associated with one wave vector), while the other remains gapless. In one dimension, this leads to the coexistence of long-range order at the gapped wave vector and quasi-long-range order at the gapless one, due to sustained fluctuations. We show that this phenomenon can be realized using ultracold bosonic atoms in optical cavities.

### [141] [Quantitative Theory for the Amplitude of Fluorescence Quantum Beats from Geminate Triplet-Pair Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16461)
*Zachary Rex,Bách Ph\d{a}m Xuân,Gerald Curran,Ivan Biaggio*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文从表征三重态激子动力学的完整参数集出发，推导了红荧烯（rubrene）和并四苯（tetracene）中来自双子三重态激子融合（geminate triplet-exciton fusion）的荧光量子拍振幅。研究发现，在并四苯中该振幅依赖于裂变时间（fission time），而在红荧烯中则取决于三重态输运的维度（dimensionality）。动力学蒙特卡洛（Kinetic Monte Carlo）模拟在裂变时间约200皮秒和各向同性输运条件下再现了并四苯的实验数据，在沿鱼骨轴（herringbone axis）三重态跳跃时间约250皮秒和各向异性输运条件下再现了红荧烯的实验数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解有机半导体中三重态激子融合产生的荧光量子拍振幅，揭示其与裂变时间、输运维度等微观动力学参数之间的定量关系。

Method: 从完整参数集解析推导量子拍振幅，结合动力学蒙特卡洛（Kinetic Monte Carlo）模拟，对红荧烯和并四苯两种材料分别进行参数化拟合，并与实验数据对照。

Result: 在并四苯中，量子拍振幅依赖于裂变时间；在红荧烯中则不依赖于裂变时间，而是由三重态输运的维度决定。模拟表明并四苯的裂变时间约为200皮秒且三重态输运为各向同性；红荧苯的三重态沿鱼骨轴跳跃时间约为250皮秒且输运为各向异性。

Conclusion: 量子拍振幅在不同材料中受不同主导因素控制，该差异可通过裂变时间与输运维度的组合来定量解释，表明该方法可作为探测有机半导体中三重态动力学的有效工具。

Abstract: We derive the amplitude of quantum-beats in the fluorescence from geminate triplet-exciton fusion in rubrene and tetracene from the full set of parameters that characterize triplet exciton dynamics. We find that the amplitude depends on the fission time in tetracene, but does not do so in rubrene, where it is determined by the dimensionality of triplet transport. Kinetic Monte Carlo simulations reproduce the experimental data in both materials, for a fission time of the order of 200 ps and isotropic triplet transport int tetracene, and for a triplet hopping time along the herringbone axis of 250 ps and anisotropic transport in rubrene.

</details>


### [142] [Microscopic Origin of Dephasing in Solids from First-Principles Electron-Phonon Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17109)
*Atsushi Yamada,Kazuhiro Yabana*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文在实时含时密度泛函理论（real-time TDDFT）框架下，基于时间域的 Williams-Lax 框架，揭示了电子-声子相互作用（electron-phonon interactions）是固体中有效退相干（dephasing）的微观起源。该方法在金属中自然产生类似 Drude 的阻尼，在电介质中则能产生清晰的高次谐波谱（high-harmonic spectra），无需引入超短现象学退相时间。通过将超胞动力学映射到原胞密度矩阵，发现退相干主要由布居数动力学（population dynamics，即对角元）主导，而非非对角相干性（off-diagonal coherence）的衰减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解固体中退相干的微观起源是凝聚态物理与超快光学领域的关键问题；传统的现象学退相时间缺乏微观基础，限制了第一性原理模拟的预测能力。

Method: 在实时含时密度泛函理论（real-time TDDFT）框架内，采用时间域 Williams-Lax 框架描述电子-声子相互作用；通过将超胞（supercell）动力学映射到原胞（primitive-cell）密度矩阵来解析退相干的机制。

Result: 在金属中，该方法从单一无序构型即可产生类似 Drude 的阻尼行为；在电介质中，同一机制可得到干净的高次谐波谱，无需引入超短现象学退相时间。退相干主要由密度矩阵对角元（布居数动力学）主导，而非对角元（非对角相干性）的衰减仅起次要作用。

Conclusion: 电子-声子相互作用为固体中的有效退相干提供了微观第一性原理解释，并表明退相干的驱动力主要来自布居数动力学，这为超快现象的第一性原理模拟提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Electron-phonon interactions provide a microscopic origin of effective dephasing in solids within real -time TDDFT via a time-domain Williams-Lax framework. In metals, Drude -like damping emerges from a single disordered configuration; in dielectrics, the same mechanism yields clean high-harmonic spectra without introducing ultrashort phenomenological dephasing times. Mapping supercell dynamics onto a primitive-cell density matrix reveals that dephasing is governed primarily by population dynamics (diagonal elements) rather than by the decay of off-diagonal coherence.
