### [143] [Spin-Independent Dissipation Induces Emergent Spin Mobility Polarization in Donor-Double-Stranded DNA-Acceptor Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17189)
*Hengrui Yang,Yu Xiong,Weitang Li,Zhigang Shuai*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文通过供体-双链DNA-受体模型和林德布拉德方程（Lindblad equation），定义自旋迁移率极化（spin mobility polarization）并揭示一种由耗散驱动的通用手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）机制：自旋无关的弛豫将螺旋自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）产生的瞬态不对称锁定为稳态极化，且弱SOC呈现“一个增强、一个抑制”的反直觉模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）效应虽经大量实验验证，但其微观机制仍存在争议，缺乏统一的物理解释。

Method: 采用供体-双链DNA-受体模型，结合林德布拉德方程（Lindblad equation）描述开放量子系统动力学；通过自旋分辨均方位移（spin-resolved mean-square displacement）定义自旋迁移率极化，并将弛豫固定在一个周转平台（turnover plateau）上。

Result: 自旋无关的弛豫（spin-independent relaxation）将螺旋自旋-轨道耦合（helical SOC）带来的瞬态不对称锁定为稳态极化；弱SOC（预期效应微弱）反而呈现“一个增强、一个抑制”（one enhanced, one suppressed）的反直觉自旋极化模式；改变螺旋手性可交换两种自旋的极化方向。

Conclusion: 本文定义了自旋迁移率极化作为一种有效探针，并给出了一种通用的耗散驱动（dissipation-driven）CISS机制。

Abstract: Despite extensive experiments, chiral-induced spin selectivity (CISS) remains debated. Using a donor-double-stranded DNA-acceptor model and Lindblad equation, we define spin mobility polarization via spin-resolved mean-square displacement and fix relaxation on a turnover plateau. Spin-independent relaxation locks the transient asymmetry from helical spin-orbit coupling (SOC) into a steady polarization. Weak SOC, expected to have little effect, boosts one spin but suppresses the other instead, in a "one enhanced, one suppressed" pattern. Flipping the helix exchanges them. The work defines mobility polarization as a probe and gives a generic dissipation-driven mechanism for CISS.

### [144] [Suppression of Non-Hermitian Skin Effect by Pseudomagnetic Field in Honeycomb Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17703)
*Kai Shao,Kun Luo*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文研究了在非厄米蜂窝晶格（non-Hermitian honeycomb lattice）中，赝磁场（pseudomagnetic fields, PMFs）如何通过两种不同机制（单调递增应变与空间调制增益/损耗）抑制非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect, NHSE），并发现该机制对边界细节不敏感，适用于多种边缘终止类型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管非厄米趋肤效应（NHSE）已在多种经典波平台中实现，但时间反演对称性得以保留的赝磁场（PMFs）与NHSE之间的相互影响尚缺乏充分研究。

Method: 论文在非厄米蜂窝晶格（non-Hermitian honeycomb lattice）中，分别通过单调递增应变（monotonically increasing strain）和空间调制的增益与损耗（spatially modulated gain and loss）两种机制产生赝磁场（PMFs），并利用数值模拟分析其对NHSE的抑制效果。

Result: 两种方案均显示，PMFs可通过将趋肤模式（skin modes）驱动至体态（bulk），有效抑制NHSE，同时伴随趋肤拓扑面积（skin topological area）的缩减以及周期边界条件下复能谱（complex-energy spectrum）的收缩。该抑制机制对边界细节不敏感，在锯齿型（zigzag）、胡须型（bearded）、扶手椅型（armchair）及细枝型（twig）等多种边缘终止下均成立。

Conclusion: 赝磁场（PMFs）被确立为一种多功能且有效的非厄米趋肤效应（NHSE）控制手段，并为在光子与声学超材料（photonic and acoustic metamaterials）以及拓扑电路（topolectrical circuits）等人工平台中的可行实现提供了方向。

Abstract: Magnetic suppression of the non-Hermitian skin effect (NHSE) offers a viable route for its control. While the NHSE has been realized in various classical-wave platforms, only pseudomagnetic fields (PMFs), which preserve time-reversal symmetry, can be engineered in such systems; however, their interplay with the NHSE remains underexplored. Here, we investigate this interplay in a non-Hermitian honeycomb lattice by considering two distinct mechanisms for generating PMFs: monotonically increasing strain and spatially modulated gain and loss. We show that in both scenarios, PMFs can efficiently suppress the NHSE by driving skin modes into the bulk, accompanied by a reduction of the skin topological area and a contraction of the complex-energy spectrum under periodic boundary conditions. This mechanism is insensitive to boundary details and holds for various edge terminations, including zigzag, bearded, armchair, and twig edges. Our results establish PMFs as a versatile and effective means to control the NHSE, and point toward feasible implementations in a broad range of artificial platforms, including photonic and acoustic metamaterials as well as topolectrical circuits.

### [145] [Spin relaxation in $X$-wave magnets with $X=p, d, f, g, i$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17807)
*Lijie Liu,Mingbo Dou,Xu Chen,Xianjie Wang,M. Ye. Zhuravlev,A. V. Nikolaev,L. L. Tao*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文在D’yakonov-Perel’机制框架下，系统研究了具有Rashba自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的X波磁体（X = p, d, f, g, i）中的自旋弛豫（spin relaxation），计算了任意奈尔矢量（Néel vector）方向的自旋弛豫时间矩阵，并揭示了自旋弛豫率与动量弛豫时间、Rashba及交变磁自旋劈裂（altermagnetic spin-split）强度成正比的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋弛豫会导致自旋退相干（spin decoherence）和有限的自旋寿命（spin lifetime），对自旋电子学（spintronic）器件有害；为获得长自旋寿命，亟需阐明自旋弛豫机制及其影响因素。

Method: 在D’yakonov-Perel’机制框架下，针对具有Rashba自旋轨道耦合的X波磁体，计算了任意奈尔矢量方向的自旋弛豫时间通用矩阵，并以奈尔矢量沿[001]方向为例进行了具体分析。

Result: 对于d、f、g、i波磁体，自旋弛豫时间倒数矩阵呈现各向异性（anisotropic）且为对角矩阵；对于p波磁体，推导出自旋时间演化的解析表达式。所有X波磁体的自旋弛豫率与动量弛豫时间（momentum relaxation time）、Rashba及交变磁自旋劈裂强度成正比。

Conclusion: 研究结果为深入理解X波磁体中的自旋弛豫机制提供了新的认识，对实现适用于自旋电子学器件的长自旋寿命具有指导意义。

Abstract: Spin relaxation results in the spin decoherence and a finite spin lifetime, which are detrimental to spintronic devices. To achieve a long spin lifetime desirable for spintronic devices, elucidating the spin relaxation mechanism and factors influencing the spin lifetime is of vital importance. Here, we investigate the spin relaxation in $X$-wave magnets ($X=p, d, f, g, i$) with Rashba spin-orbit coupling within the framework of D'yakonov-Perel' mechanism. We calculate the general matrix of the spin relaxation time for an arbitrary Néel vector direction of the $X$-wave magnet. As an illustration, we study the spin relaxation for the Néel vector along the $[001]$ direction. It is found that the reciprocal spin-relaxation-time matrices are anisotropic and diagonal for the $d$-, $f$-, $g$- and $i$-wave magnets. For the $p$-wave magnet, we derive the analytical expressions for the temporal evolution of spins. Moreover, the spin relaxation rate is proportional to the momentum relaxation time, Rashba and altermagnetic spin-split strengths for all $X$-wave magnets. Our results shine more light on the fundamental understanding of the spin relaxation mechanism in $X$-wave magnets.

### [146] [On a super-Virasoro group, a semigroup of annuli, and Gauss--Berezin integral operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17168)
*Yury A. Neretin*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文构建了与Neveu-Schwarz李超代数（Neveu-Schwarz Lie superalgebra）对应的超群（supergroup）NS(𝒜)及其复化半群Γ(𝒜)，后者元素为带有接触结构（contact structures）的1|1维超环（superannuli），其乘法为超环的粘合。在参数满足某些不等式条件下，证明了NS(𝒜)的酉表示可延拓为Γ(𝒜)的表示。文章不假设读者具备李超代数和超群的先验知识。

Result: 给出了超群NS(𝒜)的多种显式描述，并构造了其复化半群Γ(𝒜)。在参数满足特定不等式时，证明了NS(𝒜)的酉表示可以延拓为Γ(𝒜)的表示。

Conclusion: 通过Grassmann化和复化半群构造，建立了Neveu-Schwarz超群酉表示与超环粘合结构之间的联系，为超共形理论中的表示论提供了新的代数工具。

Abstract: Denote by ${\mathcal A}$ the Grassmann algebra with a countable number of generators, by ${\mathcal A}_{\overline 0}$, ${\mathcal A}_{\overline 1}$ its even and odd parts. We consider supergroups as groups over $\mathcal A$.
  Consider the Neveu--Schwarz Lie superalgebra $\mathfrak{ns}= \mathfrak{ns}_{\overline 0}\oplus \mathfrak{ns}_{\overline 1}$. Consider its Grassmannization $\mathfrak{ns}(\mathcal{A}):= (\mathfrak{ns}_{\overline 0}\otimes {\mathcal A}_{\overline 0}) \oplus (\mathfrak{ns}_{\overline 1}\otimes {\mathcal A}_{\overline 1})$ and the corresponding supergroup $\mathrm{NS}(\mathcal {A})$. We describe this group explicitly in different ways. Next, we define a complexification $Γ({\mathcal A})$ of $\mathrm{NS}({\mathcal A})$. It is a semigroup, whose elements are superannuli of dimension $1|1$ equipped with contact structures; the multiplication is gluing of such superannuli. Under some inequalities for parameters, we show that unitary representations of $\mathrm{NS}({\mathcal A})$ admit extensions to representations of $Γ(\mathcal {A})$. We do not assume that the reader has prior knowledge of Lie superalgebras and supergroups.

Abstract: Stochastic resetting has evolved from a simple model of diffusive search acceleration into a general framework for predicting, inferring, and controlling stochastic dynamics far from equilibrium. Its defining features, i.e., the creation of non-equilibrium steady states and the acceleration of first-passage kinetics, are increasingly relevant across physical chemistry, from biological restart mechanisms to molecular simulations and colloidal experiments. We review the renewal theory underlying stochastic resetting and show how it enables prediction of reset dynamics from properties of the underlying process, while also allowing the latter to be inferred from the resetting-accelerated dynamics. We then discuss applications to state preparation, enhanced sampling, kinetic inference, and training and sampling of machine learning models. Finally, we review recent advances in adaptive resetting, environmental feedback, many-body dynamics, and thermodynamic costs of resetting. ### [148] [Interpolative Separable Density-Fitting for Transcorrelated Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17314)
*Ke Liao,Yifan Cheng,Werner Dobrautz,Tianyu Zhu,Ali Alavi*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合插值可分密度拟合（ISDF）近似与有效二体（xTC）处理的 transcorrelated（TC）方法（ISDF-xTC-CCSD），通过低秩表示大幅降低三体算符的存储与积分成本，并利用多GPU实现和自微分技术实现大基组下的高效构建。在线性氢链和苯分子基态能量计算中，该方法在热力学极限和完备基组（CBS）极限附近均达到与最先进多体参考一致的高精度（约1 mHa/atom），且CBS外推显著优于传统耦合簇方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统transcorrelated（TC）方法虽能通过相似变换将Jastrow关联因子引入哈密顿量以加速向完备基组（CBS）极限的收敛，但三体算符的存储与积分成本过高，限制了其在大体系与灵活多中心关联子中的应用。因此需要发展一种低秩近似策略来压缩TC积分，并配合高效计算实现以适用于大规模体系。

Method: 采用插值可分密度拟合（ISDF）近似对网格评估的TC积分进行压缩，结合有效二体（xTC）处理将三体算符近似为二体算符，从而大幅降低存储和积分成本。同时引入多GPU实现与关联子的自动微分（automatic differentiation），使得大基组下TC框架的构建成为可行例程。最终形成的ISDF-xTC-CCSD方法在耦合簇单双激发（CCSD）水平上进行计算。

Result: 在线性氢链上，该方法在联合热力学极限与CBS极限下（基组达cc-pV5Z）与最先进多体参考的误差约为1 mHa/atom。在苯分子基态能量计算中，支持多达1200个轨道（cc-pCV5Z），达到CCSD水平的最高精度，且其CBS外推结果显著比传统耦合簇方法更稳健。

Conclusion: ISDF-xTC-CCSD方法使transcorrelated框架得以实用化地应用于大体系和灵活多中心关联子，在保持高精度的同时大幅降低了计算成本，尤其在大基组CBS外推中展现出优于传统耦合簇方法的稳定性。

Abstract: The transcorrelated (TC) method dramatically accelerates the convergence of correlated calculations toward the complete-basis-set (CBS) limit by folding a Jastrow correlator into the Hamiltonian via a similarity transformation, incorporating the electron--electron cusp into the effective interaction. We make the TC framework practical for large systems and flexible, multi-center correlators by compressing the grid-evaluated TC integrals with the interpolative separable density-fitting (ISDF) approximation, combined with the effective two-body (xTC) treatment of the three-body operator. This low-rank representation reduces storage and integration costs by orders of magnitude, and a multi-GPU implementation with automatic differentiation of the correlator makes the construction routine for large basis sets. We demonstrate the resulting ISDF-xTC-CCSD method on the linear hydrogen chain, reaching the joint thermodynamic and CBS limits with basis sets up to cc-pV5Z in agreement with state-of-the-art many-body references to within about 1~mHa/atom, and on the benzene ground-state energy with up to 1200 orbitals (cc-pCV5Z), where the method attains state-of-the-art accuracy at the coupled cluster singles and doubles level and its CBS extrapolation is markedly more robust than that of conventional coupled-cluster methods.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发一个高效、可扩展的软件套件，以克服第四代 HDNNP 中长程相互作用与电荷平衡计算的高计算复杂度（原本为 $\mathcal{O}(N^3)$），并使所有世代 HDNNP 的训练与评估均能达到线性或准线性缩放。

Method: 采用准线性缩放平面波方法加速 QEq 计算（复杂度降至 $\mathcal{O}(N\log^2 N)$）；使用优化内存管理消除长程相互作用带来的训练开销；基于现代 Fortran（2003/2008 标准）实现，并采用混合 MPI/OpenMP 并行化方案；设计模块化库架构以便绑定外部软件，已提供与 LAMMPS 及 ASE 的原生接口。

Result: QEq 计算复杂度从 $\mathcal{O}(N^3)$ 降至 $\mathcal{O}(N\log^2 N)$，使所有世代 HDNNP 均实现线性或准线性缩放；4G-HDNNP 的训练效率与局部相互作用 HDNNP 相当；通过详细基准测试验证了该软件的高效性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: RuNNer 2.0 可在从本地工作站到大规模 HPC 集群等多种 CPU 环境下高效运行，其内置的委员会式不确定性量化（committee-based uncertainty quantification）及完整接口支持，使其成为面向多代 HDNNP 的统一计算平台。

Abstract: We present RuNNer 2.0, the "Ruhr University Neural Network energy representation", a highly optimized software suite for training and evaluating high-dimensional neural network potentials (HDNNPs) of the second, third, and fourth generation. Long-range electrostatics and charge equilibration (QEq) for the description of non-local charge transfer in fourth-generation (4G) HDNNPs are accelerated by quasi-linear-scaling plane-wave methods, reducing QEq computational complexity from $\mathcal{O}(N^3)$ to $\mathcal{O}(N\log^2 N)$ such that linear or quasi-linear scaling is achieved across all HDNNP generations. An optimized memory management strategy eliminates the training overhead traditionally associated with long-range interactions, allowing 4G-HDNNPs to be trained with the same efficiency as their local counterparts. Developed in modern Fortran (2003/2008 standards), combined with a hybrid MPI/OpenMP parallelization scheme, RuNNer 2.0 has been designed to run efficiently in any CPU environment, from cost-effective local workstations to massive HPC clusters. Its modular library architecture facilitates straightforward binding to external simulation software; native interfaces to LAMMPS and the Atomic Simulation Environment (ASE) provide full access to all its features, including built-in committee-based uncertainty quantification. The high efficiency and scalability of the RuNNer 2.0 ecosystem are demonstrated through detailed benchmarks.

</details>

### [150] [Holographic CFT Thermodynamics as a Bridge Between the Weak Gravity and Weak Cosmic Censorship Conjectures for EMPYM--AdS Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16216)
*Saeed Noori Gashti,Behnam Pourhassan,Izzet Sakalli,Saheb Soroushfar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过标量场扰动下黑洞的吸积过程，验证了Einstein–Maxwell–power–Yang–Mills–AdS黑洞族满足弱宇宙监督猜想（WCCC）与弱引力猜想（WGC），并发现非阿贝尔Yang–Mills场降低了有效荷质比阈值，同时在全息CFT热力学框架下导出了扩展第一定律与Euler关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弱宇宙监督猜想（WCCC）和弱引力猜想（WGC）是量子引力理论中约束奇点与带电物质行为的基本判据，研究它们在具有非阿贝尔规范场和反德西特（AdS）背景的黑洞族中是否成立，对理解全息对偶及量子引力的自洽性具有重要意义。

Method: 在全息CFT热力学中，以中心荷C和CFT体积Vol为独立变量，导出含Yang–Mills电荷与非线性指数γ变化的扩展第一定律及闭合Euler关系，并通过机器精度验证状态方程。对标量扰动，通过视界能量与电荷通量确定超辐射阈值ω<q̃_sφ̃_h，利用质量–能量关系μ_s=ω将其转化为荷质比约束q̃_s/μ_s>r_min/Q̃；对极值与近极值构型展开度规函数f(r)至最小值附近，分析吸积过程对f_min符号的影响。

Result: 吸积过程保持f_min非正，从而视界得以幸存，宇宙监督成立。Yang–Mills场将有效荷质比阈值降低至Reissner–Nordström值（1）以下。热容量局部稳定性分析定位了Davies点。在整个参数范围内，EMPYM黑洞族在标量扰动下遵守宇宙监督，WGC仅确定演化方向（朝向或远离极值）。

Conclusion: EMPYM黑洞族在全息CFT热力学框架下同时满足WCCC与WGC，非阿贝尔Yang–Mills场对荷质比阈值的压低效应揭示了规范场构型在量子引力约束中的关键作用。

Abstract: The weak cosmic censorship conjecture (\WCCC) and the weak gravity conjecture (\WGC) sit at the heart of how singularities and charged matter are constrained in any consistent theory of quantum gravity. We study both conjectures for Einstein--Maxwell--power--Yang--Mills--AdS (\EMPYM) black holes, a family in which a non-Abelian power-law Yang--Mills field, a Maxwell field, and a negative cosmological constant act together. Working in holographic conformal field theory (CFT) thermodynamics, we treat the central charge $C$ and the CFT volume $\Vol$ as independent variables and obtain an extended first law that carries variations of the Yang--Mills charge and of the nonlinearity exponent $γ$. A closed Euler relation follows, and we check it together with the full set of equations of state to machine precision. The perturbation is a charged massive scalar minimally coupled to the Maxwell sector. Its horizon energy and charge fluxes fix the superradiance threshold $ω<\tilde{q}_s\tildeφ_h$, and the mass--energy relation $μ_s=ω$ turns this into the bound $\tilde{q}_s/μ_s>r_{\min}/\tilde{Q}$. Expanding the metric function $f(r)$ about its minimum for extremal and near-extremal configurations, we find that absorption keeps $f_{\min}$ non-positive, so the horizon survives. The Yang--Mills sector lowers the effective charge-to-mass threshold below the Reissner--Nordström value of unity, while a local stability analysis locates a Davies point in the heat capacity. Across the parameter range examined the \EMPYM\ family respects cosmic censorship under scalar perturbations, with the \WGC\ fixing only the direction of evolution toward or away from extremality.

### [151] [Universality of Magic in Local Quantum Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16403)
*Valentin Benedetti,Atish Dabholkar,Marcello Dalmonte*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，在离散局域量子场论实现中的任何稳定子态（stabilizer state）在连续极限下均无法流向真空或任何在短距离上类似真空的态。其论证基于纠缠谱（entanglement spectrum）在稳定子态中是平坦的，而在局域QFT中由于任意子区域对应的冯·诺依曼代数（von Neumann algebra）具有type III₁性质，循环分离态（cyclic and separating state）的纠缠谱是非平坦的。该结果意味着模拟物理相关QFT态必然需要超越稳定子态和克利福德操作（Clifford operation）的量子资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究稳定子态在局域量子场论（quantum field theory, QFT）连续极限下能否近似真空态或短距离类真空态，从而厘清经典可模拟量子态与真实QFT物理态之间的根本差异。

Method: 利用稳定子态纠缠谱平坦与局域QFT中循环分离态纠缠谱非平坦的对立性质，后者源于任意子区域冯·诺依曼代数的type III₁结构，通过代数量子场论（algebraic QFT）论证给出严格证明。

Result: 任何离散实现中的稳定子态在连续极限下均无法成为真空或短距离类真空态；模拟真实QFT态必须引入超越稳定子态和克利福德操作的量子资源。

Conclusion: 该结果为全息对偶（holography）等领域提供了重要启示：经典可模拟的稳定子框架不足以描述连续QFT中的基本物理态。

Abstract: We show that no stabilizer state in a discrete realization of a local quantum field theory can flow in the continuum to the vacuum or to any state that resembles the vacuum at short distances. The argument rests on the fact that the entanglement spectrum is flat for stabilizer states but non-flat for cyclic and separating states in a local QFT as a consequence of the type III$_1$ nature of the von Neumann algebras associated with arbitrary subregions. Our result implies that simulating physically relevant QFT states necessarily requires quantum resources beyond stabilizer states and Clifford operations. We comment on the implications for holography.

</details>


### [152] [Recursive construction of scalar one-loop integrals in dimensional regularisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16416)
*Paul Mork*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于Schläfli双曲单纯形微分公式，推导出标量单圈费曼积分在维度正则化下的递推结构。该递推将N点积分的洛朗系数与更低阶、含更多外线的积分系数联系起来，以ε=0项（几何上对应双曲空间单纯形体积，已知可用多重对数表示）为种子，迭代得到任意阶ε展开系数，并首次给出任意质量、离壳欧氏运动学下六边形积分的O(ε)系数显式闭合多重对数表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标量单圈费曼积分（scalar one-loop Feynman integrals）在维度正则化下的ε展开系数具有重要的理论意义，但高阶系数的系统计算缺乏统一构造方法。本文旨在建立一种普适的递推算法，使得所有阶次的洛朗系数均可通过多重对数（multiple polylogarithms, MPLs）闭式表达，从而克服现有方法的局限性。

Method: 利用Schläfli关于双曲单纯形的微分公式（Schläfli's differential formula for hyperbolic simplices），导出维度正则化下标量单圈积分的递推关系。该递推将N点积分的洛朗系数约化到更低阶、但具有更多外线的积分系数；种子项由ε=0贡献给出，其在双曲空间中的几何解释为单纯形体积，已知可用多重对数表示。迭代该递推即可逐阶构造任意质量和运动学下的高阶ε展开系数。

Result: 证明了维度正则化下标量单圈积分的所有洛朗展开系数均可表达为多重对数（MPLs）的有限组合。作为超越现有结果的首个应用，给出了任意质量和离壳欧氏运动学下六边形积分的O(ε)系数显式闭合多重对数表达式。

Conclusion: 本文建立的递推结构为计算标量单圈积分任意阶ε展开提供了一种系统性的构造性算法，且严格保证了整个展开类处于多重对数函数类中。这一结果拓展了维度正则化微扰计算的理论工具，并为进一步研究高圈积分提供了潜在的几何化视角。

Abstract: We derive a novel recursive structure for dimensionally regularised scalar one-loop Feynman integrals based on Schläfli's differential formula for hyperbolic simplices. The recursion relates the Laurent coefficients in the dimensional regulator $\varepsilon$ of an $N$-point integral to lower-order coefficients of integrals with additional external legs. The construction is seeded by the $\varepsilon=0$ contributions, which admit a geometric interpretation as volumes of simplices in hyperbolic space and are known in terms of multiple polylogarithms (MPLs). Iterating the recursion therefore provides a constructive algorithm for computing arbitrary orders in the $\varepsilon$-expansion of scalar one-loop integrals with arbitrary masses and kinematics, while remaining entirely within the class of MPLs. In particular, this establishes that all coefficients in the Laurent expansion of dimensionally regularised scalar one-loop integrals can be expressed in terms of MPLs. As a first application beyond existing results, we obtain an explicit closed MPL expression for the $\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon)$ coefficient of the scalar hexagon with arbitrary masses and off-shell Euclidean kinematics.

</details>


### [153] [A unified expansion of Einstein's gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16459)
*Arkachur Bhattacharya,Pushkar Soni*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一框架，通过含参数(s,n)和收缩参数ε的扩展方法，将伽利略引力（Galilean gravity）、卡罗尔引力（Carroll gravity）等非洛伦兹引力理论（non-Lorentzian gravity theories）纳入统一的协变形式，并进一步导出弦卡罗尔引力（String Carroll gravity），用于描述一般非极端黑洞的近视界几何。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献中，不同类型的非洛伦兹引力理论（如伽利略引力与卡罗尔引力）被分别处理，缺乏统一视角。本文旨在建立一个单一的统一扩展框架（unified framework of expansion），以涵盖这些不同的理论。

Method: 通过庞加莱代数（Poincaré algebra）在切空间中的收缩，引入参数(s,n)和收缩参数ε，构造统一的平坦几何（unified flat geometry）及其统一代数（unified algebra）。在ε→0极限下保持参数未固定，并利用该设置系统地按ε的偶次幂展开爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量（Einstein-Hilbert action），形成引力的统一扩展（unified expansion）。

Result: 该统一扩展在首阶由(s,n)确定，可重现爱因斯坦引力、伽利略引力、卡罗尔引力等多类引力理论。进一步提出了弦卡罗尔引力（SC gravity），其中局部度规具有两个零本征值。通过具体例子确认，一般非极端黑洞的近视界区域构成SC引力的解。

Conclusion: 统一扩展框架为研究非洛伦兹引力提供了系统化工具；弦卡罗尔引力能够描述非极端黑洞的近视界几何，为理解一般黑洞视界附近的物理开辟了新的途径。

Abstract: Non-Lorentzian theories of gravity, most common of which are Galilean and Carrollian gravity, arise from General relativity under suitable scalings. General relativity can be obtained by gauging the Poincaré algebra. A convenient formulation of non-Lorentzian gravity follows the contraction of the Poincaré algebra in the tangent space to its non-Lorentzian counterparts, e.g. Galilean and Carrollian algebras. In existing literature, different non-Lorentzian theories of gravity have been addressed separately. In this paper, we introduce a single unified framework of expansion to address all these different theories. We show that different scalings can be unified into a single covariant form parametrized by $(s,n)$, alongside the contraction parameter $ε$. Keeping these parameters unfixed in the limit $ε\to 0$ defines a $\textit{unified flat geometry}$ and its $\textit{unified algebra}$, which reduces to a specific non-Lorentzian geometry for a particular choice of $s$ and $n$. Using this setup in the tangent space, we systematically expand the Einstein-Hilbert action in even powers of $ε$, which we call a $\textit{unified expansion}$ of Einstein's gravity, whose leading-order theory is fixed by $(s,n)$. This reproduces various classes of gravitational theories, including Einstein gravity (the trivial case), Galilean gravity, Carroll gravity, all of which can be extracted from this expansion. Using the expansion, we then formulate String Carroll (SC) gravity, where the local metric has two vanishing eigenvalues. The near-horizon region of generic non-extremal black holes has been recently shown to be a SC geometry. By considering explicit examples, we confirm that these near-horizon geometries constitute solutions of SC gravity, paving the way of understanding physics near the horizon of generic black holes in terms of SC gravity.

</details>


### [154] [Quantum phases at high chemical potential in 2-flavor matrix-QC$_2$D](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16774)
*Nirmalendu Acharyya,Prasanjit Aich,Arkajyoti Bandyopadhyay,Sachindeo Vaidya*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过变分法分析两色两味QCD矩阵模型（matrix-QCD$_{2,2}$）在大重子数化学势（$μ_{_B}$）、同位旋化学势（$μ_{_I}$）和/或手征化学势（$c$）下的基态，发现调谐剩余参数会引发量子相变（QPTs），形成由重子数$B$和同位旋$I$标记的复杂相图，其中多个LOFF类相自发破缺旋转对称性，其基态包含类似库珀对的自旋-1双（反）夸克，且夸克携带的旋转分数占自旋的显著部分甚至几乎全部。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究两色两味QCD矩阵模型在强化学势（重子数、同位旋和手征化学势）下的基态性质，旨在揭示中间到强杨-米尔斯耦合区域中的量子相变行为与相结构。

Method: 采用变分技术（variational techniques）对角化哈密顿量，分析大化学势区域中简化的哈密顿量的基态性质。

Result: 在$μ_{_B}$与$c$或$μ_{_B}$与$μ_{_I}$主导的区域，调谐剩余参数可引发量子相变（QPTs），形成复杂相网；多数LOFF类基态带有非零自旋，自发破缺旋转对称性；基态费米子成分为自旋-1双（反）夸克，类似库珀对；夸克旋转分数显著，某些情况下几乎占满总自旋。

Conclusion: 上述结果与Splittorff-Son-Stephanov早期有效场论预言一致，证实了强化学势下两色两味QCD矩阵模型中存在丰富的量子相变和对称性破缺现象。

Abstract: We investigate the matrix model of two-color two-flavor QCD (matrix-QCD$_{2,2}$) in regimes with large baryon ($μ_{_B}$), isospin ($μ_{_I}$), and/or chiral ($c$) chemical potentials. In these regimes, the Hamiltonian simplifies considerably, making it possible to investigate the ground state for intermediate and strong Yang-Mills coupling. By diagonalizing the Hamiltonian using the variational techniques, we show that in regimes where $μ_{_B}$ and $c$ (or $μ_{_B}$ and $μ_{_I}$) dominate, tuning the remaining parameters leads to quantum phase transitions (QPTs). These transitions form a complex web of phases, each of which has a ground state uniquely labelled by baryon number $B$ and isospin $I$. Several of these phases are LOFF-like, characterized by a ground state carrying non-zero spin and hence spontaneously breaking rotational symmetry. These results are consistent with older effective field theory predictions by Splittorff-Son-Stephanov \cite{Splittorff:2000mm}. The fermionic content of these LOFF-like ground states consists of spin-1 di-(anti-) quarks which are analogous to Cooper pairs. We compute the spin-fraction carried by the quarks and find that it constitutes a significant portion -- in some cases nearly the entirety -- of the total spin.

</details>


### [155] [Kibble-Zurek Mechanism and Current-Phase Relation in a Holographic Josephson Junction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16804)
*Zhi-Hong Li,Huai-Fan Li,Hai-Qing Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过全息超导环中的约瑟夫森结，基于Kibble-Zurek机制研究其电流-相位关系，发现正弦型关系周期性出现，并识别了临界电流与几何参数及温度之间的依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索全息超导环中约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）的电流-相位关系（current-phase relation），尤其是从随机和非平衡动力学（stochastic and non-equilibrium dynamics）角度出发，依据Kibble-Zurek机制（Kibble-Zurek mechanism）进行系统研究。

Method: 采用空间调制的电荷密度来构建弱连接（weak link），在多种几何和热力学参数范围内研究电流-相位关系，分析临界电流（critical current）与结的宽度、陡度和深度等几何参数的关联。

Result: 正弦型电流-相位关系因几何结构的紧致形状而周期性出现；临界电流与结的几何参数（宽度、陡度和深度）存在明确关系；临界电流随最终温度呈特征指数衰减，反映了强耦合（strong-coupling）区域中序参量的热退化。

Conclusion: 建立了全息约瑟夫森器件的稳健理论框架，为高温超导体（high-$T_c$ superconductors）的非平衡动力学提供了可实验检验的预测。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive study of the current-phase relation of the Josephson junction in a holographic superfluid ring, realized from the stochastic and non-equilibrium dynamics according to the Kibble-Zurek mechanism. By employing a spatially modulated charge density to engineer a weak link, the current-phase relation is investigated in a range of geometric and thermodynamic parameters. The seminal sinusoidal relation between the current and the phase emerges periodically due to the compact shape of the geometry. We also identify the relations between the critical current and the geometric parameters of the junction: the width, steepness and depth. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the critical current exhibits a characteristic exponential decaying against the final temperature, reflecting the thermal degradation of the order parameter in a strong-coupling regime. Our results establish a robust framework for holographic Josephson devices, offering experimentally testable predictions for the non-equilibrium dynamics of high-$T_c$ superconductors.

</details>


### [156] [Electric field fluctuations and renormalization group flows in a self-interacting scalar field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16932)
*Melanie Martínez,Enrique Muñoz,Marcelo Loewe*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过复 λφ4 模型研究自相互作用带电标量场在具有经典随机涨落的背景电场中的行为，利用复制技巧（replica trick）对电场涨落进行统计平均，推导出重整化群方程（renormalization group equations）及耦合流图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究经典随机噪声对带电标量场论物理参数的影响，特别是在弱电场和超强电场两种极端情形下的效应。

Method: 将随机背景电场通过协变导数（covariant derivative）纳入Schwinger传播子；利用复制技巧（replica trick）对电场涨落进行统计平均；通过平均过程得到带电电流之间的有效相互作用及其耦合常数。

Result: 得到了该理论的外衣传播子（dressed propagators）、相互作用顶点（interaction vertices）以及重整化群方程（renormalization group equations），并给出了耦合常数流图（streamplots）。平均过程中产生了带电电流间的有效相互作用，其耦合常数正比于电场涨落自关联函数（auto-correlation function）的幅度。

Conclusion: 随机电场涨落会诱导带电电流间的有效相互作用，该效应可通过重整化群分析在耦合参数空间中加以刻画。

Abstract: We consider a self interacting charged scalar field represented by the complex λφ4 model, embedded in a background electric field exhibiting classical stochastic fluctuations. We studied the effects of the classical stochastic noise on the physical parameters of the scalar field theory, for both weak and ultra strong electric field regimes. The stochastic background electric field is included in the Schwinger propagator through the covariant derivative, and the generating functional of the theory is found by means of the replica trick in order to compute the statistical average over electric fluctuations. As a result of the averaging process, an effective interaction between charged currents emerges, with a coupling constant proportional to the magnitude of the auto-correlation function of the electric field fluctuations. We obtained the dressed propagators, the interaction vertices, and the renormalization group equations of the theory, along with the corresponding streamplots in the manifold of interaction couplings.

</details>


### [157] [Non-Abelian Thirring model at large $N$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17246)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过非阿贝尔玻色化（non-Abelian bosonization）方法研究了半单群G在水平k下的Thirring模型，计算了其电流和复合电流算符的两点关联函数至λ的三阶，在二次卡西米尔（quadratic Casimir）c_G大值近似下提取了β函数和反常维度（anomalous dimensions），结果表明不存在阶数为k/c_G的额外临界点，支持Destri & de Vega的结论但反驳了Dashen & Frishman关于存在阶数为1/c_G的额外不动点的主张。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用半单群G在水平k下的非阿贝尔玻色化Thirring模型，引入形变参数λ。在群的伴随表示（adjoint representation）中二次卡西米尔c_G取大值的假设下，将电流和复合电流算符的两点关联函数（two-point correlation functions）计算至λ的三阶。从关联函数中提取β函数和算符的 anomalous dimensions。

Result: 计算结果表明不存在阶数为k/c_G的额外临界点（additional critical point）。该结果与Destri & de Vega在费米子非阿贝尔Thirring模型中的发现一致，但与Dashen & Frishman声称存在阶数为1/c_G的额外不动点（additional fixed point）的主张相矛盾。

Conclusion: 本文通过玻色化方法提供的计算结果否定了Dashen & Frishman关于额外不动点的论断，证实了Destri & de Vega的结论，即非阿贝尔Thirring模型中不存在阶数为k/c_G的额外临界点。

Abstract: We consider the non-Abelian bosonized Thirring model for a semi-simple group $G$ at level $k$, with deformation parameter $λ$. We compute the two-point correlation functions of current and composite current operators to cubic order in $λ$, assuming large values of the quadratic Casimir $c_G$ of the group $G$ in the adjoint representation. From these, we extract the $β$-function and the anomalous dimensions of both the current and composite current operators, showing the absence of an additional critical point of order $k/c_G$. Our findings align with those of Destri & de Vega for the Fermionic non-Abelian Thirring model, but contradict the claim in Dashen & Frishman regarding the existence of an additional fixed point of order $1/c_G$.

### [158] [The Information Content of Krylov Observables: A Machine Learning Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17346)
*Ritam Basu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文使用机器学习量化三种Krylov空间可观测量的信息含量，发现归一化Wigner负性（normalized negativity）χ(t)蕴含的二阶矩信息盈余是量子混沌的特征信号，并给出了解析机制与定量界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究表明归一化负性χ(t)可作为二阶矩探针（second-moment infall probe），但不同Krylov空间可观测量之间的信息层次关系尚不明确，尤其是何种特征能区分混沌（chaos）与可积动力学（integrable dynamics）。

Method: 在小残差网络（small residual networks, 16–32神经元）和提升树（boosted trees）上，对约57,000条标记演化数据进行训练；数据覆盖GUE、GOE、Poisson系综，可积SL(2,ℝ)/CFT扇区，以及混沌插值H(ε)=H_SL(2,ℝ)+ε·R₀·W_GUE。训练目标包括热场温度（thermofield temperature）、精细谱型因子（fine spectral form factor, SFF）、e^S平台、对称类识别以及(h,α)简并参数恢复。

Result: 任一可观测量均可高精度（R²≈0.999）确定热场温度；但均无法重构精细谱型因子（R²≈0.18），平滑目标也无改善；e^S平台可恢复（R²=0.861），主要由扩展复杂度前20%部分贡献。单一曲线以98%准确率识别对称类。可积扇区中可观测量信息等价；负性对(h,α)简并消歧最优（N→h: R²=0.999）。沿混沌插值，χ相对于C的非对称间隙（asymmetry gap）随混沌增强而从+0.33增至+0.77，而原始N的间隙衰减至零。

Conclusion: 归一化负性χ(t)携带的二阶矩信息盈余是混沌的特征信号，本文为其提供了解析机制与定量上界，指出精细谱型因子严格优于所有二阶矩可观测量，后者无法捕获谱形因子（SFF）的dip-ramp物理。

Abstract: We employ machine learning to quantify the information carried by three Krylov-space observables: the spread complexity $\mathcal{C}(t)$, the discrete Wigner negativity $N(t)$, and the normalized negativity $χ(t)=N(t)/|S(t)|$, with $S(t)$ the survival amplitude, recently proposed as a second-moment infall probe (arXiv:2607.04065). Small residual networks (16-32 neurons) and boosted trees are trained on half of $\sim 57{,}000$ labeled evolutions spanning the GUE, GOE and Poisson ensembles, the integrable $SL(2,\mathbb{R})$/CFT sector, and the chaos interpolation $H(\varepsilon)=H_{SL(2,\mathbb{R})}+\varepsilon R_0 W_{GUE}$. Either moment determines the thermofield temperature at $R^2\simeq 0.999$. Neither reconstructs the fine spectral form factor ($R^2\simeq 0.18$ in every ensemble); smoothing the target does not repair this, and windows wide enough to help erase the dip-ramp physics itself: the SFF strictly refines both moments. The coarse $e^S$ plateau is nevertheless recovered at $R^2=0.861$, mostly from the first 20% of $\mathcal{C}(t)$. A single curve identifies the symmetry class at up to 98% accuracy. In the integrable sector the observables are informationally equivalent, as exact negative-binomial slaving demands, while the negativity best resolves the $(h,α)$ degeneracy ($N\to h$: 0.999). Along the interpolation the asymmetry gap of $χ$ over $\mathcal{C}$ switches on with chaos, growing from +0.33 to +0.77 as the level statistics cross to GUE, while the raw-$N$ gap decays to zero. The second-moment informational surplus is therefore a signature of chaos, carried specifically by the normalized negativity, and we derive an analytical mechanism and a quantitative bound for it.

</details>

### [160] [The next-to-next-to-leading order BFKL eigenvalue at odd conformal spin in planar N=4 super Yang-Mills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17608)
*Alex Prygarin,Claudelle Capasia Madjuogang Sandeu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文以封闭形式给出了平面N=4超杨-米尔斯理论中奇数共形自旋n的三圈（次次领头阶）BFKL本征值，其表达式为嵌套调和和与有理函数的有限组合，并通过直接Mellin提取从三圈被积函数中精确导出原子表，部分系数闭合为调和和，其余核层通过有限数据全纯递推或数值验证处理，在nu=0处与独立量子谱曲线结果自旋对自旋一致至n=91。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在平面N=4超杨-米尔斯（planar N=4 super Yang-Mills）理论的背景下，精确计算高圈BFKL（Balitsky-Fadin-Kuraev-Lipatov）本征值对于理解可积性和散射振幅的对偶性具有重要意义，但目前三圈（three-loop）水平上奇数共形自旋（odd conformal spin）n的封闭形式表达式尚未完整给出。

Method: 从Caron-Huot-Herranen三圈被积函数（three-loop integrand）出发，通过直接Mellin提取（direct Mellin extraction）精确导出奇数自旋n≥3的原子表（atom table），以有理算术形式给出；n=1作为边界块（boundary block）提供。系数由1、π²和ζ₃的有理倍数构成，部分系数槽通过Nielsen积分（nested harmonic sums）和两阶梯距离（two ladder distances）上的调和和（harmonic sums）闭合，剩余五核层通过有限数据全纯递推（finite-data holonomic recurrence）或数值验证处理。

Result: 在47个系数槽中，有40个在固定初等基下闭合为两个阶梯距离上的调和和；剩余核层中有一个网格满足有限数据全纯递推，其余核的全体自旋规则尚未闭合。超出显式调和和的系数权重阶梯在nu=0处塌缩为深度为一的digamma和trigamma函数。在nu=0处，截距（intercepts）通过n=91与独立量子谱曲线（Quantum Spectral Curve）结果自旋对自旋一致。每个奇数自旋的本征值严格无乘积项，对应于Kotikov-Lipatov厄米可分离形式（hermitian-separable form）的加性情形，携带1+(-1)^n的次领头反常项在奇数n处消失。

Conclusion: 本文为平面N=4超杨-米尔斯理论的奇数共形自旋提供了封闭形式的三圈BFKL本征值，虽未声称得到n均匀形式（n-uniform form），但通过解析与数值方法验证了大部分核闭合。伴随论文提供了完整推导与表达式，其中十六个核闭合中有十一个得到证明，五个经数值验证。

Abstract: We present the three-loop (next-to-next-to-leading order) BFKL eigenvalue of planar N=4 super Yang-Mills at odd conformal spin n in closed form, as a finite combination of nested harmonic sums and rational functions of z=(|n|-1)/2 + i nu. For each odd n>=3 the atom table is extracted exactly, in rational arithmetic, from the Caron-Huot-Herranen three-loop integrand by direct Mellin extraction; a shipped command regenerates it on demand, with n=1 a supplied boundary block. The coefficients are rational multiples of 1, pi^2 and zeta_3; in a fixed elementary basis, forty of the forty-seven coefficient slots close as harmonic sums of the two ladder distances (all-spin form conjectural, the split a property of the basis), while the residual five-kernel layer includes one grid obeying a finite-data holonomic recurrence, an all-n rule for the rest still open. Beyond the explicit harmonic sums the coefficient-weighted ladder collapses onto depth-one digamma and trigamma functions. At nu=0 the intercepts reproduce the independent Quantum Spectral Curve values spin by spin through n=91. At each odd spin the eigenvalue is strictly product-free, the additive case of the Kotikov-Lipatov hermitian-separable form; the next-to-leading anomalous term carrying 1+(-1)^n is absent at odd n. No n-uniform form is claimed. Derivations (eleven of sixteen kernel closures proven, five verified numerically) and complete expressions are given in a companion paper.

</details>


### [161] [The next-to-next-to-leading order BFKL eigenvalue at odd conformal spin in planar N=4 super Yang-Mills: closed form, coefficient structure, and arithmetic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17613)
*Alex Prygarin,Claudelle Capasia Madjuogang Sandeu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文以闭合形式给出平面N=4超杨-米尔斯理论（planar N=4 super Yang-Mills）中奇数共形自旋（odd conformal spin）n的三圈（next-to-next-to-leading order, NNLO）BFKL本征值（BFKL eigenvalue），由有限组合的连续嵌套调和和（continued nested harmonic sums）与有理函数构成，并报告了一种算术障碍（arithmetic obstruction）：异常网格系数在计算范围内每个n=p+2（n-2为素数）处招募新的分母素数，该有限定律已被证明并推测持续存在，导致其生成函数不能是代数或全局有界（globally bounded）。偶数自旋被推测包含于同一母函数中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高能散射（high-energy scattering）中，BFKL（Balitsky-Fadin-Kuraev-Lipatov）方程描述小x区域（small-x regime）的胶子演化，其本征值（eigenvalue）是理解Regge极限（Regge limit）下散射振幅的关键对象。N=4超杨-米尔斯理论作为共形场论（conformal field theory）的典范模型，其BFKL本征值的高阶精确计算对检验AdS/CFT对偶（AdS/CFT correspondence）中的可积性（integrability）结构至关重要。

Method: 从Caron-Huot-Herranen三圈被积函数（three-loop integrand）出发，在有理算术（rational arithmetic）中精确提取每个奇数自旋的原子表（atom table）；通过一个移位的命令（shipped command）为任意奇数n≥3重新生成该表，n=1作为提供的边界块（boundary block）。一个再求和的主生成函数（resummed master generating function）（已验证至n=17及m=9,11,13,15,21,31）未被用于逐自旋表格的生成。通过在整数移位阶梯（integer-shifted ladder）上引入参数z=(|n|-1)/2+iν，将本征值表达为连续嵌套调和和与有理函数的有限组合。

Result: 在ν=0处，截距（intercepts）逐自旋复现了独立的量子谱曲线（Quantum Spectral Curve）数值，验证至n=91。系数为1、π²和zeta_3的有理倍（rational multiples）；在固定初等基（fixed elementary basis）中，47个槽（slots）中的40个以两个阶梯距离（ladder distances）的调和和闭合（全自旋形式为推测性）。剩余五核层（residual five-kernel layer）包含一个服从全纯递归（holonomic recurrence）的网格；调和和分离后，系数加权阶梯坍缩为两个深度为一的多伽马超越函数（depth-one polygamma transcendentals）。

Conclusion: 发现一种算术障碍：异常网格系数在每个n=p+2（n-2为素数）处引入新的分母素数，该有限定律已获证明并推测持续存在；在此延续假设下，其生成函数数据不能是代数或全局有界的。偶数自旋被推测包含于同一母函数中。每个奇数自旋的本征值是无乘积形式（product-free case）的Kotikov-Lipatov厄米可分离形式（hermitian-separable form）。

Abstract: We present the three-loop (next-to-next-to-leading order) BFKL eigenvalue of planar N=4 super Yang-Mills at odd conformal spin n in closed form, as a finite combination of continued nested harmonic sums and rational functions of z=(|n|-1)/2 + i nu on an integer-shifted ladder. For each odd spin the atom table is extracted exactly, in rational arithmetic, from the Caron-Huot-Herranen three-loop integrand; a shipped command regenerates it for any odd n>=3, with n=1 a supplied boundary block. A resummed master generating function, conjectured to reproduce those integrands at every spin (verified through n=17 and at m=9,11,13,15,21,31), is not used for the per-spin tables. At nu=0 the intercepts reproduce the independent Quantum Spectral Curve values spin by spin through n=91. The coefficients are rational multiples of 1, pi^2 and zeta_3; in a fixed elementary basis, forty of the forty-seven slots close as harmonic sums of the two ladder distances (all-spin form conjectural). The residual five-kernel layer includes one grid obeying a holonomic recurrence; once the harmonic sums are separated the coefficient-weighted ladder collapses onto two depth-one polygamma transcendentals. We report an arithmetic obstruction: the exceptional-grid coefficients recruit a new denominator prime at each n=p+2 (n-2 prime) through the computed range, a finite law we prove and conjecture to continue; on that continuation their generating data cannot be algebraic or globally bounded. Even spins are conjecturally contained in the same master. At each odd spin the eigenvalue is the product-free case of the Kotikov-Lipatov hermitian-separable form. A companion Letter announces the result.

</details>


### [162] [Hypercomplex formulation of dissipative scalar electrodynamics and phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17626)
*B. R. López-Raymundo,R. Cartas-Fuentevilla*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过超复标量电动力学（hypercomplex scalar electrodynamics）框架，将耗散（dissipation）作为由扩展局域规范对称性 U(1)×SO(1,1) 决定的内在动力学性质引入，推导了广义金兹堡-朗道（Ginzburg-Landau）方程，并证明了系统在穿过临界温度时必然经历不连续的一级相变（first-order phase transition），同时揭示了双曲对称性（hyperbolic symmetry）在有效四次耦合为负时引起的结构不稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 与不变量（invariants）相关的系数约束禁止了混合态（mixed states）的共存，形式上确认了双临界点（bicritical point）的存在；系统在穿过临界温度时被迫发生不连续的一级相变；当有效四次耦合（effective quartic couplings）取负值时，自由能（free energy）下方无界，产生渐近不稳定性方向（asymptotic directions of instability）。

Conclusion: 基于超复标量电动力学和 U(1)×SO(1,1) 规范对称性的框架，耗散可作为内禀动力学属性出现；该框架预言了一级相变的必然性以及负四次耦合情形下的结构不稳定性，为理解耗散系统中规范对称性与相变行为的关系提供了新视角。

Abstract: A hypercomplex formulation of scalar electrodynamics is developed, in which dissipation emerges as an intrinsic dynamic property dictated by the extended local gauge symmetry U(1)XSO(1,1). By constructing an effective free-energy functional, we derive the generalized Ginzburg-Landau equations and analyze the thermodynamic stability of the system. Our analysis of the vacuum state up to the fourth order reveals that the constraint on the coefficients associated with the invariants prohibits the coexistence of mixed states, formally establishing the existence of a bicritical point. Consequently, upon crossing the critical temperature, the system is forced to undergo a discontinuous first-order phase transition. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the hyperbolic symmetry induces a structural instability when the effective quartic couplings take negative values, rendering the free energy unbounded from below and creating asymptotic directions of instability.

### [163] [Analytic HTEE in Moving Plasmas and Its Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17721)
*Mohammad Ali-Akbari*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在 AdS₃/CFT₂ 对偶框架下，研究了洛伦兹助推的 (1+1) 维等离子体中的全息类时间纠缠熵（holographic timelike entanglement entropy, HTEE），通过解析求解极值曲面方程，发现存在临界助推速度，低于该速度时极值曲面转折点为纯虚数，熵的实部随助推速度变化；高于该速度时，极值曲面变为纯实数，标志着从 HTEE 到类空间真实鞍点（spacelike-like real saddle）的转变，并在零速度极限下恢复已知的静态 BTZ 黑洞结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非平衡或运动态等离子体中的纠缠结构，特别是类时间纠缠熵在助推背景下的行为，以拓展对全息纠缠熵在洛伦兹助推下的理解。

Method: 利用 AdS₃/CFT₂ 对偶，采用洛伦兹助推的 BTZ 黑洞（Lorentz-boosted BTZ black hole）作为背景，解析求解耦合的极值曲面方程，推导出 HTEE 的闭式表达式。

Result: 发现一个临界助推速度：低于该速度时，极值曲面转折点为纯虚数，HTEE 出现普适虚部贡献，实部随助推速度变化；高于该速度时，物理上允许的极值曲面变为纯实数，系统过渡到类空间真实鞍点。零速度极限下恢复静态 BTZ 结果。

Conclusion: 助推速度可诱导 HTEE 向类空纠缠熵的转变，临界速度标志着极值曲面分支的终结与鞍点类型的切换，揭示了助推背景中全息纠缠熵的丰富相结构。

Abstract: We investigate the holographic timelike entanglement entropy of a boosted $(1+1)$-dimensional plasma within the AdS$_3$/CFT$_2$ correspondence, considering a Lorentz-boosted BTZ black hole background. We solve the coupled extremal-surface equations analytically and obtain a closed-form expression for the HTEE. We show that below a critical boost velocity, the turning points of the extremal surface are purely imaginary, leading to the universal imaginary contribution to the entropy, while the real part acquires a nontrivial dependence on the boost velocity. Moreover, we identify a critical boost velocity at which the complex extremal-surface branch terminates. Beyond this critical velocity, the physically admissible extremal surfaces become purely real, signalling a transition from the holographic timelike entanglement entropy to a spacelike-like real saddle that is geometrically similar to the standard holographic entanglement entropy. The known static BTZ result is recovered in the zero-velocity limit, as expected.

</details>


### [164] [Leading Yukawa terms in the three-loop anomalous dimension and four-loop $β$-function of ${\cal N}=1$ supersymmetric theories for various renormalization prescriptions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17848)
*Ratmir Jumanov,Konstantin Stepanyantz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文计算了任意可重整化的𝒩=1超对称理论中物质超场反常维度的三圈阶贡献（正比于Yukawa耦合的六次方），并基于此计算了相应的四圈阶规范β-函数，探讨了其方案依赖性，构造了使重整化群函数形式最简的“最小”重整化方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在𝒩=1超对称规范理论中，NSVZ关系在采用高协变导数（higher covariant derivatives）正则化配合最小对数减除（minimal subtractions of logarithms）时对所有阶成立。为了验证该关系并研究重整化群函数的方案依赖性问题，需要计算更高圈的贡献。

Method: 采用高协变导数正则化方法，计算了任意可重整化𝒩=1超对称理论中物质超场反常维度（anomalous dimension）的三圈阶贡献（正比于Yukawa耦合的六次方），并覆盖了多种重整化方案（renormalization prescriptions）。在此基础上，进一步计算了相应的四圈阶规范β-函数（gauge β-function）。

Result: 得到了物质超场反常维度的三圈阶贡献，以及相应的四圈阶规范β-函数；揭示了这些函数的方案依赖性；构造了使重整化群函数形式最简的“最小”重整化方案（minimal renormalization prescription），同时保持了超对称推导出的规范β-函数与Yukawa β-函数的精确方程的有效性。

Conclusion: 在高协变导数正则化框架下，通过构造“最小”方案可实现对NSVZ关系的多圈验证，并简化重整化群函数的形式。

Abstract: For an arbitrary renormalizable ${\cal N}=1$ supersymmetric theory with a single gauge coupling regularized by higher covariant derivatives we calculate the three-loop contribution to the anomalous dimension of the matter superfields proportional to the sixth powers of Yukawa couplings for a wide class of renormalization prescriptions. Next, taking into account that in the case of using the higher covariant derivatives supplemented by minimal subtractions of logarithms the NSVZ relation is valid in all orders, we calculate the corresponding four-loop contribution to the gauge $β$-function and investigate its scheme dependence. In particular, we construct the so-called ``minimal'' renormalization prescription for which the renormalization group functions have the simplest possible form provided that the exact equations for the gauge and Yukawa $β$-functions following from supersymmetry remain valid.

### [165] [Dynamical Timelike Entanglement Entropy in an Evaporating Schwarzschild--AdS Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17874)
*Digen Das,Prabwal Phukon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了蒸发中的Schwarzschild–AdS黑洞的类时间纠缠熵（timelike entanglement entropy, tEE）动力学框架，利用绝热推广的Kruskal构造和累积热相位Φ(t)描述蒸发过程，并发现非均匀的Page时间间隔、相位延迟与振幅调制等动力学特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的类时间纠缠熵（tEE）研究局限于静态背景，尚未推广到动态黑洞（如蒸发黑洞）场景，使人们对引力系统中时间量子关联在非平衡过程中的行为缺乏理解。

Method: 通过有效Stefan–Boltzmann描述将霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）耦合到外部吸收浴（absorptive bath）来模拟蒸发，得到时变视界半径r_h(t)和表面引力κ(t)；基于演化视界的近 horizon Rindler 结构，对静态Kruskal构造进行绝热推广，定义累积热相位Φ(t)=∫_0^t κ(t') dt'作为静态相位κt的替代，并引入绝热参数A(t)验证构造的有效性。

Result: 绝热参数A(t)在感兴趣区域内始终较小（≲0.012），在视界穿过临界半径r_h=l/√3时精确为零；动态tEE连续追踪蒸发过程，导出的动态Page时间间隔呈非均匀分布，并伴随相位延迟（phase delay）和振幅调制（amplitude modulation）；动态熵依赖于κ(t)的完整累积历史，而非瞬时值，因此保留了对整个蒸发过程的记忆。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了蒸发黑洞中时间量子关联的第一性原理动力学框架，揭示了非静态引力系统中时间纠缠结构的新特征，为未来更广泛的动态黑洞研究提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Timelike entanglement entropy (tEE) has recently emerged as a novel probe of temporal quantum correlations in gravitational systems. Existing studies are largely restricted to static backgrounds. In this work we extend the construction of tEE to an evaporating Schwarzschild--AdS black hole. The evaporation is modeled through an effective Stefan--Boltzmann description of Hawking radiation coupled to an external absorptive bath, yielding a time-dependent horizon radius ($r_h(t)$) and surface gravity $κ(t)$. We derive, from the near-horizon Rindler structure of the evolving horizon, an adiabatic generalization of the static Kruskal construction, obtaining the accumulated thermal phase $Φ(t)=\int_0^tκ(t')\,dt'$ as the natural replacement for the static phase $κt$. The validity of this construction is governed by an explicit adiabatic parameter $\mathcal A(t)$, which we verify numerically remains small ($\lesssim0.012$) throughout the regime of interest. It vanishes exactly where the horizon crosses the critical radius $r_h=l/\sqrt3$ identified independently from the static thermodynamics. Using $Φ(t)$, we construct a dynamical timelike entanglement entropy that continuously tracks the evaporation process and derive the corresponding dynamical Page-like times. Unlike the uniformly spaced Page-like times of the static geometry, evaporation induces non-uniform temporal spacing, together with a progressive phase delay and amplitude modulation of the oscillatory tEE. Because the dynamical entropy depends on the full accumulated history of $κ(t)$ rather than its instantaneous value alone, it retains a memory of the entire evaporation process. These results establish a first-principles dynamical framework for investigating temporal quantum correlations in evaporating black holes.

</details>


### [166] [Comments on holographic spread complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18024)
*Zhehan Li,Jia Tian*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了将扩散复杂度（spread complexity）增长率与探针径向动量联系起来的全息提议，通过直接量子化AdS探针并利用外推字典（extrapolation dictionary）给出了更普遍的推导。研究发现，在平直时空和德西特时空中，该提议的成立依赖于特定的相干态结构与表示选择，而非仅仅依赖于半经典极限的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在识别全息提议中“扩散复杂度增长率与体探针径向动量相关”这一论断的隐含假设，并澄清经典探针动力学如何从量子动力学中涌现。

Method: 采用直接量子化反德西特（AdS）时空中的探针，并利用外推字典进行推导；同时将提议置于“复杂度=任何东西（complexity=anything）”框架中进行解释。此外，在平直时空和德西特（de Sitter）时空中检验该提议的普适性。

Result: 在平直时空中，物理哈密顿量不保持相干态结构，扩散复杂度测量的是波包的色散展宽而非经典动量。在德西特时空中，静态块（static-patch）能量表示中的半经典波包表现出相同的色散行为；而适应于主序列表示（principal-series representation）的相干态则能展现扩散复杂度的指数增长，其增长率的时间依赖性与经典径向动量一致。

Conclusion: 半经典极限本身不足以建立动量-复杂度关系（momentum–complexity relation）；该关系的成立依赖于特定的相干态构造与表示选择。

Abstract: We revisit the holographic proposal relating the growth rate of spread complexity to the radial momentum of a bulk probe, aiming to identify its underlying assumptions and clarify how classical probe dynamics emerges from quantum dynamics. By quantizing AdS probes directly and using the extrapolation dictionary, we provide a more general derivation of the proposal. In particular, we interpret it as a concrete realization of a classical complexity observable and its quantization in the ``complexity=anything'' framework. Since probe dynamics is not intrinsically tied to the AdS/CFT correspondence, we also examine the proposal in flat and de Sitter spacetimes. In flat spacetime, the physical Hamiltonian does not preserve the coherent-state structure, and spread complexity measures the dispersive broadening of the wave packet rather than classical momentum. In de Sitter space, generic semiclassical wave packets in the static-patch energy representation show the same dispersive behavior. By contrast, coherent states adapted to the principal-series representation can exhibit exponential growth of spread complexity, with a growth rate that has the same time dependence as the classical radial momentum. These examples indicate that a semiclassical limit alone is not sufficient for a momentum--complexity relation.

</details>


### [167] [Non-injective field redefinitions and quantum inequivalence in scalar theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18166)
*Bin Zhu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究通过常单位雅可比（constant unit Jacobian）多项式场重定义（polynomial field redefinition）从自由有质量多重态拉回得到的标量理论，发现尽管局部每个真空等价于自由理论，全局上由于场空间度量不完备、原像数目变化及位置算子谱多重性（spectral multiplicity）非常数，导致无法实现全局幺正的场重定义和正则的Weyl指数化（Weyl exponentiation），从而区分了局部微扰等价与全局量子等价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解通过非线性场重定义（特别是非单射多项式映射）构造的标量理论在局部与全局之间的差异，探究是否存在全局幺正性（global unitarity）障碍，以区分微扰等价与真正的量子等价。

Method: 以一个三变量非单射映射（Alpöge最近提出的映射）为主要例子，进行线性归一化后构造了一个三标量sigma模型（sigma model），并分析其场空间几何、真空结构及运动方程（equation of motion）的局部与全局性质。此外还分析了带有一般五次纤维（generic quintic fiber）的四标量映射以验证机制的普遍性。

Result: 每个局部真空由三个质量为m的自由模式描述，运动方程在局部化为自由Klein–Gordon方程（Klein–Gordon equation）。但全局上场空间度量不完备（incomplete），目标空间上实原像（real preimage）数目变化，且对易位置算子（commuting position operators）具有非恒定的联合谱多重性（joint spectral multiplicity）。这些性质排除了场重定义的全局幺正实现以及正则典范动量（formal canonical momenta）的正则Weyl指数化。

Conclusion: 两个例子共同表明，局部微扰等价（perturbative equivalence）与全局量子等价（global quantum equivalence）是分离的：在选定的局部叶上成立的微扰等价并不保证整个场空间的全局量子等价。

Abstract: We study scalar theories obtained by pulling a free massive multiplet back through a polynomial field redefinition with constant unit Jacobian. Our main example uses the three-variable noninjective map recently announced by Alpöge. After a linear normalization, it defines a three-scalar sigma model with a flat, unit-volume field-space metric and three isolated vacua. Each vacuum is locally described by three free modes of mass m, and the exact equations of motion reduce locally on each sheet to free Klein--Gordon equations. The global theory is nevertheless not a single free theory: the field-space metric is incomplete, the number of real preimages changes across target space, and the commuting position operators have nonconstant joint spectral multiplicity. This rules out a global unitary implementation of the field redefinition and a regular Weyl exponentiation of the formal canonical momenta. We then analyze a four-scalar map with a generic quintic fiber. It exhibits the same mechanism with an additional field that controls the fiber polynomial. The two examples separate perturbative equivalence on a chosen local sheet from global quantum equivalence of the full field space.

</details>


### [168] [Gravitational Vacuum Polarization: Decoupling and the Conformal Anomaly](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18180)
*Emil Mottola*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文给出了任意质量 $m$ 和曲率耦合参数 $\xi$ 的量子标量场应力张量关联函数 $\langle T^{ab}T^{cd}\rangle$ 的紧凑形式，重点分析了 $m\to\infty$ 极限下的退耦（decoupling）以及 $m\to 0$ 时共形反常（conformal anomaly）的红外起源。研究验证了协变守恒的Ward恒等式（Ward Identity, WI），揭示了自旋-2和自旋-0两个张量通道的形式因子在维数正规化（dimensional regularization）下的行为，并指出 $\xi=1/6$ 情况下自旋-0形式因子无需紫外正规化即可直接满足退耦。其虚部定义了一个满足紫外有限求和规则的谱函数，实部在无质量极限下唯一确定了 $\square R$，质量平方依赖描述了Wilson重整化群流（Wilsonian renormalization group flow）到长距离有效场论。在 $m=0$ 时，自旋-0谱函数在零能量处退化为狄拉克 $\delta$ 函数，表明存在由引力低能有效理论中共形反常导致的标量Goldstone集体激发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在给出量子标量场应力张量关联函数 $\langle T^{ab}T^{cd}\rangle$ 的紧凑解析形式，厘清其在 $m\to\infty$ 大质量退耦极限与 $m\to 0$ 小质量共形反常红外起源两个极端下的行为，并解决一般曲率耦合参数 $\xi$ 下退耦条件不满足的问题。

Method: 采用 $n$-维正规化计算单圈有效作用量（one-loop effective action）对度规的二阶变分，从中提取应力张量关联函数 $\langle T^{ab}T^{cd}\rangle$。利用协变守恒的Ward恒等式验证关联函数结构，将其分解为自旋-2（无迹）和自旋-0（有迹）两个张量通道，每个通道乘以相应的洛伦兹不变形式因子（form factor）。对 $n=4$ 处的极点项进行最小减除（minimal subtraction），并对结果进行修正以恢复退耦性质。

Result: 发现对一般的 $\xi\neq 1/6$，$n=4$ 时经过最小减除的形式因子不能满足退耦条件，但可通过简单修正实现退耦。$\xi=1/6$ 情况具有特殊重要性：自旋-0形式因子在 $n=4$ 时完全有限，无需紫外正规化或减除，且直接满足退耦。其虚部定义的谱函数对任意 $m$ 服从紫外有限的求和规则；实部在无质量极限下唯一确定 $\square R$；$m^2$ 依赖性描述了从紫外到红外的Wilson重整化群流。当 $m=0$ 时，自旋-0谱函数在零能量处成为狄拉克 $\delta$ 函数。

Conclusion: 在 $m=0$ 时，自旋-0谱函数的狄拉克 $\delta$ 函数行为证明了引力低能有效理论中由于共形反常而存在无质量标量Goldstone集体激发（massless scalar Goldstone collective excitation），该激发是共形对称性自发破缺的体现。

Abstract: A compact form of the stress tensor $\langle T^{ab}T^{cd}\rangle$ correlation function of a quantum scalar field of arbitrary mass $m$ and curvature coupling $ξ$ is presented, with particular emphasis on decoupling in the $m\to\infty$ limit and infrared origin of the conformal anomaly as $m \to 0$. The Ward Identity (WI) of covariant conservation is verified for the full second order metric variation of the one-loop effective action, of which $\langle T^{ab}T^{cd}\rangle$ is part, including local contact terms. This WI is satisfied by two tensors, one spin-2 (traceless) and the second spin-0 (traceful), each multiplied by a Lorentz invariant form factor computed in $n$-dimensional regularization. Minimal subtraction of pole terms at $n =4$ produces form factors that fail to satisfy decoupling for general $ξ\neq 1/6$, but can be simply amended to do so. Particular interest attaches to the $ξ=1/6$ case, in which the spin-0 form factor at $n =4$ is completely finite, requires no UV regularization or subtractions, and satisfies decoupling directly. Its imaginary part defines a spectral function that obeys a UV finite sum rule for any $m$, while its real part unambiguously determines the $\square R$ in the massless limit. Its $m^2$ dependence describes a Wilsonian renormalization group flow to an effective field theory limit at large distances. At $m= 0$ the spin-0 spectral function becomes a Dirac $δ$-function at zero energy, demonstrating the existence of a massless scalar Goldstone collective excitation due to the conformal anomaly in the low energy effective theory of gravity.

</details>


### [169] [All Tree-Level Massive Cosmological Correlators via Spectral Gluing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18223)
*Jonathan Gräfe,Denis Werth*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发现，德西特时空中大质量宇宙关联子（cosmological correlators）树图级别的超几何结构（hypergeometric structure）实际上隐藏着极简的数学基础：通过谱表示（spectral representation）和谱胶合算法（spectral gluing algorithm），这些关联子可由Lauricella广义超几何函数族（Lauricella generalised hypergeometric functions）的基本构件通过图组合学（graph combinatorics）拼接而成，且去除动力学传播子（dynamical propagators）后，剩余的超几何运动学依赖坍缩为有理函数（rational functions）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大质量宇宙关联子在树图层面已展现出丰富的超几何结构，反映了粒子在德西特时空中的畸变传播；本文旨在揭示这种表观复杂性背后隐藏的简单数学结构。

Method: 利用谱表示计算任意树图级别的大质量标量场关联子，将其分解为Lauricella广义超几何函数族的基本构件，再通过谱积分（spectral integrals）胶合；发展了一种谱胶合算法，通过初等图组合学计算这些积分，得到显式级数表示（series representations），该算法自然生成了对应微分方程的解，并利用图湮灭算子（graph annihilators）发现了广义超几何函数间的新恒等式。

Result: 发现了一种新的广义超几何函数恒等式族，揭示了意外的简化：剥离动力学传播子后，剩余的超几何运动学依赖坍缩为有理函数；大质量关联子的刚性超几何解析结构由图组合学决定。

Conclusion: 大质量宇宙关联子的超几何结构隐藏着由图组合学决定的简单性，暗示了某种内在几何原理，大质量关联子的性质由此自然涌现。

Abstract: Massive cosmological correlators exhibit a rich hypergeometric structure already at tree level, reflecting the distorted propagation of particles in de Sitter spacetime. In this paper, we reveal that this apparent complexity conceals a remarkably simple underlying mathematical structure. Using the spectral representation, we compute arbitrary tree-level correlators of scalar fields with generic masses and show that they are constructed from fundamental building blocks belonging to the family of Lauricella generalised hypergeometric functions, glued together by spectral integrals. We develop a spectral gluing algorithm that evaluates these integrals through elementary graph combinatorics, yielding explicit series representations that resum the dependence on internal energies away from soft limits. This algorithm naturally generates solutions to the differential equations satisfied by massive correlators as expansions in the corresponding eigenfunctions. Acting with a set of graph annihilators, we uncover a new class of magical identities among generalised hypergeometric functions, revealing an unexpected simplification: once the dynamical propagators are stripped away, the remaining hypergeometric kinematic dependence collapses to rational functions. Our results expose a hidden simplicity in the rigid hypergeometric analytic structure dictated by graph combinatorics, and hint at an intrinsic geometric principle from which properties of massive correlators naturally emerge.

</details>

### [170] [A Measure-Theoretic Approach to Spontaneous Stochasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16328)
*Wandrille Ruffenach,Eric Simonnet,Nicolas Valade*

Main category: nlin.CD

TL;DR: 本文引入了一种测度论（measure-theoretic）形式体系，将自发随机性（spontaneous stochasticity, SpSt）理解为一种测度选择原则（measure-selection principle），并在有限维系统中建立了可达性定理、奇异性分析与重整化群视角，揭示了无粘非唯一性如何通过正则化极限产生非狄拉克统计分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自发随机性（SpSt）是否存在充分发展的湍流中仍是一个重大未解问题，且除少数特定系统外，SpSt一直缺乏通用的数学定义。因此，本文旨在为SpSt提供一种一般的数学形式体系，以统一理解其产生机制。

Method: 引入测度论形式体系，将SpSt视为一种测度选择原则：给定无粘问题、适定正则化与一个环境测度（ambient measure），研究该测度在正则化流（regularized flow）下的前推（pushforward）收敛性质；强SpSt发生当前推测度收敛到非狄拉克概率律（non-Dirac probability law）。此外，利用Dini型方向增长（Dini-type directional growth）检测无粘动力学中的奇异集，并引入重整化（半）群观点将极限统计学视为统计吸引子（statistical attractors）。

Result: 建立了中心可达性定理（attainability theorem）：只要无粘问题非唯一，任何支撑在无粘状态集上的概率测度都可以通过适当的正则化作为极限律被选取。识别了无粘动力学中的奇异集作为非唯一性的必要障碍。阐明了SpSt与初始数据敏感性（sensitivity to initial data）之间的关系，澄清了湍流启发的有限时间分离判据的范围与局限。

Conclusion: 本文为自发随机性提供了一个统一的测度论框架，揭示了环境测度、无粘奇异性、正则化尺度与初始数据敏感性在SpSt涌现中的相互作用。该工作将经典确定性选择替换为统计选择（statistical selection），为深入理解湍流及其他非唯一系统中的自发随机性奠定了数学基础。

Abstract: Spontaneous stochasticity (SpSt), originating in Richardson's picture of turbulent dispersion and Lorenz's Eulerian view of finite-time loss of predictability, was later formulated under this name by Gawędzki and collaborators and developed in shell models by Mailybaev and collaborators. Whether it occurs in fully developed turbulence remains a major open question.
  Beyond a few specific classes of systems, however, SpSt has lacked a general mathematical definition. We introduce a measure-theoretic formalism in which it is understood as a measure-selection principle. Given an inviscid problem, a well-posed regularization, and an ambient measure, we study the pushforward of that measure by the regularized flow. Strong SpSt occurs when these pushforward measures converge to a non-Dirac probability law, replacing classical deterministic selection by statistical selection.
  For finite-dimensional systems, we establish several structural results. Our central attainability theorem shows that, whenever the inviscid problem is nonunique, any probability measure supported on the set of inviscid states can be selected as the limiting law of a suitable regularization. We also identify singular sets in the inviscid dynamics, detected through Dini-type directional growth, as necessary obstructions underlying nonuniqueness. We analyze the relation between SpSt and sensitivity to initial data, clarifying the scope and limitations of turbulence-inspired finite-time separation criteria. Finally, we develop a renormalization-(semi)group viewpoint in which limiting statistics arise as statistical attractors. Explicit examples illustrate how ambient measures, inviscid singularities, regularization scales, and initial-data sensitivity interact in the emergence of SpSt.

</details>

### [171] [Temporal Correlations Between Fuzzy Dark Matter and Baryonic Matter in Virialized Core-Halo Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16917)
*Ivan Alvarez-Rios,Francisco S. Guzman*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过三维薛定谔-泊松-欧拉（Schrödinger-Poisson-Euler）系统模拟，检验模糊暗物质（Fuzzy Dark Matter, FDM）干涉驱动的颗粒状涨落与耦合气体成分之间的时间相关性。结果表明，气体对FDM的全局引力势有响应，但与干涉驱动的颗粒结构之间不存在强时间相关性，暗示通过重子物质局域时间涨落直接探测FDM颗粒性的能力有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模糊暗物质（FDM）预言的干涉驱动颗粒结构会产生时变引力场，可能对重子物质产生可观测的动力学效应。本文旨在检验这种涨落是否在FDM与耦合气体成分之间产生可测量的时间相关性。

Method: 作者利用三维薛定谔-泊松-欧拉（Schrödinger-Poisson-Euler）系统，对耦合的FDM-气体构型进行演化模拟。FDM成分通过多合并（multimerger）构型初始化，弛豫至核-晕（core-halo）结构；重子成分建模为理想气体。维里化后，通过相关函数（correlation functions）和谱诊断（spectral diagnostics）分析两者的时间涨落。

Result: FDM密度场呈现含显著高频成分的涨落，而气体则形成更平滑、寿命更长的相干结构。尽管气体对FDM晕产生的引力势有动力学响应，但FDM干涉驱动涨落与气体动力学之间不存在强时间相关性，该行为在探测的气体温度范围内一致。

Conclusion: 重子物质响应的是维里化晕的全局引力势，而非FDM依赖于相位的详细颗粒结构。这种弱时间耦合可能限制通过局域重子时间涨落直接探测FDM颗粒性的可行性。

Abstract: Fuzzy Dark Matter (FDM) predicts the existence of virialized halos with interference-driven granular structure generated by the wave nature of ultralight bosons. Since these fluctuations produce time-dependent gravitational fields, they can be proposed as a potential source of observable dynamical effects on baryonic matter. In this work we test whether such fluctuations generate measurable temporal correlations between FDM and a coupled gas component. We evolve coupled FDM-gas configurations with the Schrödinger-Poisson-Euler system in three dimensions. The FDM component is initialized through multimerger configurations that relax toward core-halo structures, while the baryonic component is modeled as an ideal gas. After virialization, we analyze the temporal fluctuations of both components through correlation functions and spectral diagnostics. The FDM density field shows fluctuations with significant high-frequency content, whereas the gas develops smoother and longer-lived coherent structures. Although the gas dynamically responds to the gravitational potential generated by the FDM halo, we find no strong temporal correlation between the interference-driven fluctuations of FDM and the gas dynamics. This behavior persists across the explored range of gas temperatures. Our results indicate that baryonic matter reacts to the global gravitational potential of the virialized halo rather than to the detailed phase-dependent granular structure of FDM. This weak temporal coupling may limit the possibility of directly detecting FDM granularity through local baryonic temporal fluctuations.

</details>

### [172] [Theoretical derivation of blood velocity from TOF-MRA based artery centerline](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16498)
*Abrar Faiyaz*

Main category: physics.med-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于物理信息（physics-informed）的计算框架，通过解析扩展Bloch方程为Bloch-McConnell流动方程，建立纵向磁化空间衰减与流体速度之间的数学关系，从而直接从标准TOF-MRA信号中提取局部血流速度，无需额外相位对比扫描。通过MATLAB模拟含合成噪声的变几何管道（渐缩管与局灶狭窄管）流动，并采用基于双Tikhonov正则化的全局逆优化方法稳定求解不适定的渡越时间积分，成功恢复了逐点真实速度，包括渐进加速和狭窄射流。该工作为从结构MRA图像中提取定量功能血流动力学指标提供了理论证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: TOF-MRA广泛用于结构性血管成像，但要获取血流速度等功能性血流动力学（functional hemodynamics）信息，通常需要额外的相位对比（phase-contrast）扫描，增加了扫描时间。现有方法假设流速恒定，无法处理真实血管中的变速度情况。因此，需要一种无需额外扫描、能从标准TOF-MRA信号中直接提取变流体速度的理论框架。

Method: 首先，将Bloch方程解析扩展为Bloch-McConnell流动方程（Bloch-McConnell flow equations），建立纵向磁化（longitudinal magnetization）空间衰减与流体速度之间的数学关系。然后，在MATLAB中开发仿真框架，模拟两种变几何管道（连续渐缩管与局灶狭窄管）在合成扫描仪噪声下的流体流动。最后，采用基于双Tikhonov正则化（Dual-Tikhonov regularization）的全局逆优化（global inverse optimization）方法，通过主动惩罚高频数值振荡并保持结构曲线刚度，稳定求解不适定的渡越时间积分（transit time integral）。

Result: 计算仿真成功恢复了真实逐点速度（ground-truth point-wise velocities），准确追踪了逐渐的血流动力学加速（gradual hemodynamic accelerations）以及尖锐的狭窄射流（sharp stenotic jets）。验证了该方法在变几何和噪声条件下提取局部速度的有效性。

Conclusion: 该理论框架提供了一个稳健的数学概念验证（proof-of-concept），表明可以从标准结构MRA成像中提取定量、局部的功能血流动力学指标，为无需额外扫描时间的高级流量量化（flow quantification）奠定了基础。

Abstract: Time-of-flight magnetic resonance angiography (TOF-MRA) is widely used for structural vascular imaging, but extracting functional hemodynamics like blood velocity typically requires supplementary phase-contrast scans. This study proposes a novel, physics-informed computational framework to extract variable fluid velocity directly from standard TOF-MRA signal profiles. We analytically expand the Bloch equations into Bloch-McConnell flow equations, establishing a mathematical relationship between the spatial decay of longitudinal magnetization and fluid velocity. To validate this derivation and overcome the limitations of constant-velocity assumptions, a MATLAB simulation framework was developed to model fluid flow in two variable-geometry flowing tube cases i.e continuous tapering and focal stenosis -under synthetic scanner noise. A global inverse optimization approach utilizing Dual-Tikhonov regularization was deployed to stably invert the ill-posed transit time integral, actively penalizing high-frequency numerical ringing while preserving structural curve stiffness. The computational sim-ulations successfully recovered ground-truth point-wise velocities, accurately tracking gradual hemodynamic accelerations and sharp stenotic jets. This theoretical framework provides a robust mathematical proof-of-concept that quantitative, localized functional hemodynamic metrics can be extracted from standard structural MRA imaging, estab-lishing a foundation for advanced flow quantification without requiring additional scan time.

</details>

### [173] [Exploring Brain Networks Using Noninvasive Electrophysiological Measurements: Methods and Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17602)
*Richard Leahy,Takfarinas Medani*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了基于脑电图（EEG）和脑磁图（MEG）进行脑网络分析的方法学基础与实用工作流程，涵盖物理原理、源重建、连接性指标、分析管道及新兴方向，为非侵入式电生理学在脑网络研究中的应用提供了概念基础与实践指南。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EEG与MEG能以毫秒级时间分辨率非侵入式测量大脑活动，为研究大规模脑网络中的功能性和有效性相互作用提供了独特手段。然而，其分析涉及从物理原理到源重建、体积传导校正等一系列复杂方法学问题，亟需系统性的方法学梳理与实践指导。

Method: 本文以综述形式展开，首先回顾EEG与MEG的物理原理及其互补优势与局限；随后阐述正问题与逆问题（forward and inverse problems），包括个体头模型构建、源重建技术（source reconstruction techniques）及精确解剖建模的重要性。针对体积传导（volume conduction）和信号泄漏（signal leakage）问题提出了缓解策略及源空间连接性分析最佳实践。综述了常用的功能性和有效性连接性指标，如相干性（coherence）、相位同步指标、振幅包络相关（amplitude envelope correlation）、格兰杰因果（Granger causality）、动态因果模型（dynamic causal modeling）和传递熵（transfer entropy），并分析了各项指标的假设、优势与局限。此外，介绍了端到端分析管道（end-to-end analysis pipelines），重点强调Brainstorm及开源软件在可重复研究中的作用。

Result: 本文呈现了EEG/MEG脑网络分析从物理原理到应用实践的完整知识体系，系统梳理了各类连接性度量方法的适用场景与局限性，并介绍了时变连接性（time-varying connectivity）、跨频相互作用（cross-frequency interactions）及基于网络的分析（network-based analyses）等新兴方向。

Conclusion: 本文为非侵入式电生理学在健康和疾病状态下研究人类脑网络组织提供了概念基础与实用指南，有助于研究人员和高年级学生理解和运用EEG/MEG进行脑网络映射与解释。

Abstract: Electroencephalography (EEG) and magnetoencephalography (MEG) provide noninvasive measurements of brain activity with millisecond temporal resolution, enabling the investigation of functional and effective interactions within large-scale brain networks. This chapter presents a comprehensive overview of the methodological foundations and practical workflows for EEG/MEG-based brain network analysis. We first review the physical principles underlying EEG and MEG, emphasizing their complementary strengths and limitations. We then describe the forward and inverse problems, including subject-specific head modeling, source reconstruction techniques, and the importance of accurate anatomical modeling for reliable source localization. Strategies for mitigating volume conduction and signal leakage are discussed, together with best practices for source-space connectivity analysis. The chapter reviews widely used functional and effective connectivity measures, including coherence, phase synchronization metrics, amplitude envelope correlation, Granger causality, dynamic causal modeling, and transfer entropy, highlighting their assumptions, advantages, and limitations. Modern end-to-end analysis pipelines are presented, with particular emphasis on Brainstorm and complementary open-source software for reproducible EEG/MEG research. Finally, we discuss emerging approaches, including time-varying connectivity, cross-frequency interactions, and network-based analyses, illustrating how noninvasive electrophysiology contributes to understanding brain organization in health and disease. The chapter provides both conceptual foundations and practical guidance for researchers and advanced students seeking to map and interpret human brain networks using EEG and MEG.

</details>

### [174] [Study of $χ_{\mathrm{c}}$ production in pPb collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\mathrm{NN}}}$ = 8.16 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17847)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 基于CMS实验在质心能量为每核子对8.16 TeV的质子-铅（proton-lead, pPb）碰撞中采集的数据，测量了瞬发P波粲偶素（charmonium）态χc1(1P)和χc2(1P)的产额，并报导了二者的截面比。该比值对事件带电粒子多重性、J/ψ的快度（rapidity）和横动量（transverse momentum, pT）均不敏感，且与质子-质子（pp）碰撞结果一致，表明pPb碰撞中未出现显著的相对修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究粲偶素态在核环境中的产生行为，特别是P波态χc在质子-铅（proton-lead, pPb）碰撞中的截面比，以探究冷核物质效应（cold nuclear matter effects）对重夸克偶素（quarkonium）产生的相对影响。

Method: 基于CMS实验收集的175 nb⁻¹积分亮度数据，在每核子对质心能量√s_NN = 8.16 TeV的pPb碰撞中，通过χc → J/ψ γ衰道重建χc态；J/ψ用μ⁺μ⁻对重建，γ通过其转换产生的e⁺e⁻对重建。

Result: 在|y(J/ψ)| < 2.4、6.5 < pT(J/ψ) < 30 GeV范围内，报导了χc2与χc1的产额截面比；该比值独立于事件带电粒子多重性、J/ψ的快度和横动量，且与√s = 7 TeV的pp碰撞结果一致。

Conclusion: χc2-to-χc1比值在pPb碰撞中未表现出显著的相对核修饰效应，这与ψ(2S)-to-J/ψ比值的行为形成对比，暗示不同粲偶素态在核环境中可能受到不同的修正机制。

Abstract: Production of prompt P-wave charmonium states $χ_\mathrm{c1}$(1P) and $χ_\mathrm{c2}$(1P) is studied in proton-lead (pPb) collisions at a center-of-mass energy per nucleon pair of $\sqrt{\smash[b]{s_{_{\mathrm{NN}}}}}$ = 8.16 TeV. The analysis is based on data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 175 nb$^{-1}$ collected by the CMS experiment at the CERN LHC. The $χ_\mathrm{c}$ states are measured via their decay $χ_\mathrm{c}$ $\to$ J$/ψ\,γ$. The J$/ψ$ meson is reconstructed via its decay to a muon pair, while the photon is reconstructed through its conversion to an electron-positron pair. The ratio of production cross sections times branching fractions for the two charmonium states, [$σ(χ_\mathrm{c2}) \mathcal{B}(χ_\mathrm{c2}$ $\to$ J$/ψ\, γ$)] / [$σ(χ_\mathrm{c1}) \mathcal{B}(χ_\mathrm{c1}$ $\to$ J$/ψ\, γ)$], is reported in the rapidity range $\vert y($J$/ψ)\vert$ $\lt$ 2.4 for the transverse momentum range 6.5 $\lt$ $p_{\mathrm{T}}$(J$/ψ$) $\lt$ 30 GeV. The $χ_\mathrm{c2}$-to-$χ_\mathrm{c1}$ ratio is found to be independent of event charged-particle multiplicity, as well as of the rapidity and $p_\mathrm{T}$ of the J$/ψ$. The consistency of this ratio with proton-proton measurements at $\sqrt{s}$ = 7 TeV indicates an absence of strong relative modification for $χ_\mathrm{c}$ states in pPb collisions, in contrast to the behavior observed in the $ψ$(2S)-to-J$/ψ$ ratio.

</details>


### [175] [First measurement of $\mathbf{\rm Ξ_{\rm c}^{0}}$ production in $\mathbf{Pb}-\mathbf{Pb}$ collisions at $\mathbf{\sqrt{\textit{s}_{\rm NN}}}$ = 5.02 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17903)
*ALICE Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: ALICE合作组首次在核-核（nucleus-nucleus）碰撞中测量了粲重子（charm baryon）$Ξ_{\mathrm c}^{0}$的产额，在Pb-Pb对撞中观测到其核修正因子（nuclear modification factor, $R_{\mathrm{AA}}$）在低横动量（transverse momentum, $p_{\mathrm T}$）区间高达3，创下粲强子（charm hadron）测量之最，但现有模型虽能描述$R_{\mathrm{AA}}$，却系统性低估了产额及多种重子-介子产额比（yield ratio）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: $Ξ_{\mathrm c}^{0}$重子的产生及其横动量微分谱对高能重离子碰撞中形成的夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）内的强子化过程（hadronization process）和奇异数产生（strangeness production）高度敏感，然而此前在核-核碰撞中尚未有相关测量。

Method: 利用ALICE探测器在$\sqrt{s_{\mathrm{NN}}}=5.02~\mathrm{TeV}$的Pb-Pb碰撞数据，在中心快度区（midrapidity, $|y|<0.5$）重建$Ξ_{\mathrm c}^{0}$重子，分别针对0–10%和30–50%中心度（centrality）区间，在横动量范围$3<p_{\mathrm T}<12~\mathrm{GeV}/c$和$4<p_{\mathrm T}<12~\mathrm{GeV}/c$内测量其产额和核修正因子$R_{\mathrm{AA}}$。

Result: $Ξ_{\mathrm c}^{0}$的核修正因子$R_{\mathrm{AA}}$在$3<p_{\mathrm T}<4~\mathrm{GeV}/c$区间内最高达到约3，是迄今所有粲强子中观测到的最大值。模型预测与实测$R_{\mathrm{AA}}$基本一致，但在所测$p_{\mathrm T}$区间内系统性地低估了产额以及$Ξ_{\mathrm c}^{0}/\mathrm{D}^{0}$、$Ξ_{\mathrm c}^{0}/Λ_{\mathrm c}^{+}$和$Ξ_{\mathrm c}^{0}/\mathrm{D}^{+}_{\mathrm s}$的产额比。

Conclusion: 首次在核-核碰撞中测量$Ξ_{\mathrm c}^{0}$产额并揭示其$R_{\mathrm{AA}}$在低$p_{\mathrm T}$区间显著增强，表明现有强子化模型对含奇异数粲重子的产生机制描述尚不充分，需要进一步的理论改进。

Abstract: The ALICE Collaboration reports the first measurement of the production of prompt $Ξ_{\mathrm c}^{0}$ baryons in nucleus$-$nucleus collisions by analyzing data from $\mathrm{Pb}-\mathrm{Pb}$ collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\mathrm{NN}}}~=5.02~\mathrm{TeV}$. The production and transverse-momentum ($p_{\mathrm T}$) differential spectra of $Ξ_{\mathrm c}^{0}$ are particularly sensitive to the hadronization process and to strangeness production in the quark--gluon plasma formed in high-energy heavy-ion collisions. The $Ξ_{\mathrm c}^{0}$ baryons are reconstructed at midrapidity ($|y|<0.5$) in the transverse-momentum intervals $3<p_{\mathrm T}~<12~\mathrm{GeV}/c$ and $4<p_{\mathrm T}~<12~\mathrm{GeV}/c$ in the 0$-$10\% and 30$-$50\% centrality intervals, respectively. The nuclear modification factor ($R_{\mathrm{AA}}$) reaches values up to 3 in the interval $3<p_{\mathrm T}~<4~\mathrm{GeV}/c$, which is the largest value measured so far for charm hadrons. Model predictions are compatible with the measured $R_{\mathrm{AA}}$, while, in the measured $p_{\mathrm T}$ intervals, they underestimate the production yield as well as the measured $Ξ_{\mathrm c}^{0}/\mathrm{D}^{0}$, $Ξ_{\mathrm c}^{0}/Λ_{\mathrm c}^{+}$, and $Ξ_{\mathrm c}^{0}/\mathrm{D}^{+}_{\mathrm s}$ yield ratios.

</details>

# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [176] [Relativistic bound-state solutions for a non-central Schi{ö}berg-type hyperbolic potential with double ring-shaped angular terms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16265)
*Shakir. M. Nagiyev,Vatan H. Badalov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究在Klein-Gordon方程中引入含双环状角势垒的非中心Schiöberg型双曲势，通过奇异相互作用（singular interactions）改变波函数允许定义域，从而重塑量子谱。标量和矢量耦合相等使径向与角度动力学可分离。角度方程精确求解，径向方程借助Greene-Aldrich近似处理，得到Jacobi多项式波函数和隐式相对论量子化条件。赤道面上的反平方奇点将位形空间分割为反射相关的扇区，各扇区角谱相同。在一扇区内将势垒降至零时，仅保留奇宇称态，而常规全域问题则恢复两种宇称。非相对论极限恢复Schrödinger谱。对NaH和Na₂，低振动能级与实验合理吻合，近解离偏离揭示渐近局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索奇异相互作用（singular interactions）通过改变波函数允许定义域来重塑量子谱的物理机制，具体在Klein-Gordon方程中研究含双环状角势垒的非中心Schiöberg型双曲势（non-central Schiöberg-type hyperbolic potential with double ring-shaped angular barriers）下的相对论量子行为。

Method: 利用相等标量和矢量耦合（equal scalar and vector couplings）实现径向与角度动力学的分离；角度方程精确求解，径向方程采用Greene-Aldrich近似（Greene-Aldrich approximation）处理，获得Jacobi多项式波函数（Jacobi-polynomial wavefunctions）和隐式相对论量子化条件（implicit relativistic quantization condition）。

Result: 赤道面反平方奇点（equatorial inverse-square singularity）将位形空间分割为反射相关扇区，各扇区角谱相同；势垒降至零时仅保留奇宇称态，而非全域问题的双宇称恢复。非相对论极限恢复Schrödinger谱。对NaH和Na₂的计算显示，低振动能级与实验合理吻合，近解离区域存在偏差。

Conclusion: 奇异相互作用可通过改变波函数定义域有效调控相对论量子谱，该机制在Klein-Gordon框架下得到解析验证；低能级与实验的吻合支持模型适用性，而近解离偏差提示该势模型在渐近区域的局限性。

Abstract: Singular interactions can reshape quantum spectra by changing admissible wavefunction domains. In this study, we investigate this mechanism in the Klein--Gordon equation for a non-central Schiöberg-type hyperbolic potential with double ring-shaped angular barriers. Equal scalar and vector couplings separate the radial and angular dynamics. We solve the angular equation exactly and treat the radial equation with the Greene--Aldrich approximation, obtaining Jacobi-polynomial wavefunctions and an implicit relativistic quantization condition. The equatorial inverse-square singularity splits configuration space into reflection-related sectors with identical angular spectra. Reducing the barrier to zero within one sector retains only odd-parity states, unlike the regular full-domain problem, which restores both parities. The nonrelativistic limit recovers the Schr{ö}dinger spectrum. For NaH and Na$_2$, low-lying vibrational energies agree reasonably with experiment, whereas near-dissociation deviations reveal asymptotic limitations.

</details>


### [177] [The Quantum Correction to Gaussian Information Geometry is the Killing Form of the Symplectic Algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16376)
*Christian Kerskens*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文严格证明了量子Bures度量的对偶形式与Fisher-Rao信息度量的对偶形式之差恒等于辛代数$\mathfrak{sp}(2n,\mathbb R)$的Killing型（Killing form）的拉回，该差在Cartan分解（Cartan decomposition）上的符号解释了量子度量在纯态边界处的各向异性硬化，并通过相丛上的伪黎曼度量（pseudo-Riemannian metric）的Schur补（Schur complement）实现了这一修正，避免了最小耦合方案的不可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Bures-Wasserstein传输度量、Fisher-Rao信息度量与量子Bures度量各自已被充分研究，但它们之间的相互关系因定义所涉及的算子方程而模糊不清。本文旨在澄清这些对偶度量之间的精确差异及其几何意义。

Method: 作者从逆变（contravariant）（对偶）度量出发，通过将度量差识别为辛代数$\mathfrak{sp}(2n,\mathbb R)$的Killing型的拉回（通过同构$X\mapsto\Omega X$），并在Cartan分解上分析其符号。进一步，通过相丛上的伪黎曼度量的Schur补构造，避免了通过最小耦合（minimal coupling）到主联络（principal connection）的实现路径。

Result: 对偶量子Bures度量与对偶Fisher-Rao度量之差精确等于迹形式（trace form），即与Killing型成比例，且该差独立于协方差矩阵。该形式在紧致子代数$\mathfrak u(n)$上为负（导致发散），在非紧致补空间上为正，再现了量子度量在纯态边界处的各向异性硬化。数值验证了所有恒等式。

Conclusion: 三个经典度量之间的模糊关系得以澄清：对偶量子Bures度量与对偶Fisher-Rao度量的差由辛代数的Killing型给出，并通过相丛上的Schur补几何实现，而最小耦合方案被排除。

Abstract: On the admissible cone $\mathcal C_Ω=\{Σ\in\mathrm{Sym}^+(2n):Σ+iΩ\ge0\}$ of Gaussian covariance matrices, the classical Bures--Wasserstein transport metric, the Fisher--Rao information metric, and the quantum Bures metric are individually well understood, but their mutual relationship is obscured by the operator equations defining them. Working with the contravariant (dual) metrics, we show that the exact difference between the dual quantum Bures metric and the dual Fisher--Rao metric is independent of the covariance matrix: it is identically the trace form, proportional to the Killing form, of the symplectic algebra $\mathfrak{sp}(2n,\mathbb R)$, pulled back through the isomorphism $X\mapstoΩX$. The signature of this form on the Cartan decomposition reproduces the anisotropic stiffening of the quantum metric at the pure-state boundary: it is negative on the compact subalgebra $\mathfrak u(n)$, which carries the divergence, and positive on the noncompact complement. Because the correction is quadratic in the momenta, a no-go lemma shows it cannot arise from minimal coupling to a principal connection. We realize it instead through a Schur complement of a pseudo-Riemannian metric on a phase bundle, whose base reduction is the quantum Bures metric and whose horizontal metric is the classical-limit Fisher--Rao metric. All identities are verified numerically to working precision.
