### [178] [Hamiltonian Lift of Bures--Wasserstein Covariance Dynamics with a Spectral Floor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16380)
*Christian Kerskens*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文在正定锥 Sym$^+_n$ 上构造了一个有限维哈密顿提升（Hamiltonian lift）的协方差动力学，将 Bures–Wasserstein 度量下的耗散梯度流嵌入一个保守的相空间框架，并揭示了光谱底限（spectral floor）所诱导的局域刚度标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 正定锥上的协方差动力学通常由梯度流（gradient flow）描述，但梯度流编码了耗散松弛（dissipative relaxation），却掩盖了底层的相空间结构（phase-space structure）。该论文旨在恢复这一缺失的相空间结构。

Method: 在配备 Bures–Wasserstein 度量的 Sym$^+_n$ 上构造有限维哈密顿提升（Hamiltonian lift）。利用自然力学拉格朗日量导出正则动量 $Π=\tfrac12 L_Σ[\dotΣ]$（其中 $L_Σ$ 为 Lyapunov 算子），并得到显式哈密顿量 $\mathcal{H}(Σ,Π) = 2{\rm tr}(ΠΣΠ)+V(Σ)$。通过添加 Rayleigh 耗散（Rayleigh dissipation），在过阻尼极限（overdamped limit）下恢复 Bures–Wasserstein 梯度流。

Result: 对于含光谱底限（spectral floor）和迹控制（trace-control）势能的系统，各向同性平衡（isotropic equilibrium）附近的二次涨落哈密顿量（quadratic fluctuation Hamiltonian）分离了迹模（trace mode）和迹零模（traceless mode）。基线刚度（baseline stiffness）在平衡协方差逼近光谱底限时发散，行为为 $(s-ν)^{-2}$。

Conclusion: 该构造为受约束的 Bures–Wasserstein 协方差松弛识别了一个保守母系统（conservative parent system），并确定了光谱底限所诱导的局域刚度标度（local stiffness scale）。

Abstract: Covariance dynamics on the positive-definite cone are commonly described by gradient flows, which encode dissipative relaxation but obscure the underlying phase-space structure. We construct a finite-dimensional Hamiltonian lift of covariance dynamics on Sym$^+_n$ equipped with the Bures--Wasserstein metric. The natural mechanical Lagrangian yields canonical momentum $Π=\tfrac12 L_Σ[\dotΣ]$, where $L_Σ$ is the Lyapunov operator, and explicit Hamiltonian $\mathcal{H}(Σ,Π) = 2{\rm tr}(ΠΣΠ)+V(Σ)$. Adding Rayleigh dissipation recovers the Bures--Wasserstein gradient flow in the overdamped limit. For a spectral-floor and trace-control potential, the quadratic fluctuation Hamiltonian around the isotropic equilibrium separates trace and traceless modes; the baseline stiffness diverges as $(s-ν)^{-2}$ as the equilibrium covariance approaches the floor. The construction identifies a conservative parent system for constrained Bures--Wasserstein covariance relaxation and fixes the local stiffness scale induced by the spectral floor.

### [179] [Uncountably many inequivalent maximally entangled measurements for two qutrits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16396)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于三维空间中连续族对称信息完备集（SIC）构造一个单参数连续族的两量子三态最大纠缠测量基。通过分析生成该族测量基的局域酉基（local unitary bases），验证基间的局域酉不等价性，并构造野误差基（wild error bases）实例。

Result: 成功构造了一个单参数连续族的两量子三态最大纠缠测量基，并证明该族中任意两个基在局域酉操作下不等价。在最小可能维度（两量子三态）下构造了首个野误差基实例。

Conclusion: 高维（两量子三态）系统中存在连续不等价的最大纠缠测量基族，且该族导致不同测量基在量子信息相关场景中表现出性能差异。这一发现揭示了高维纠缠测量基结构的丰富性，并通过野误差基的构造为量子信息理论提供了新工具。

Abstract: Every two-qubit measurement basis composed of maximally entangled eigenstates can be transformed into the Bell basis via local unitary operations. For higher dimensions, in contrast, there exist inequivalent bases composed of maximally entangled eigenstates. Here, we provide a single-parameter family of two-qutrit maximally entangled measurement bases, and demonstrate that none of the bases are equivalent to each other under local unitaries. These bases are constructed from the continuous family of symmetric informationally complete sets of states in dimension three. By studying the local unitary bases that generate the family of two-qutrit maximally entangled measurement bases, we construct the first examples of wild error bases in the smallest dimension where these can exist. Finally, we discuss how distinct measurements in the family lead to differences in performance in several scenarios relevant in quantum information.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用施瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）背景下的量子大气模型，构建受霍金辐射影响的二分Werner态，计算并分析几何量子失协在物理可及区域（physically accessible region）与不可及区域（physically inaccessible region）中的行为，并考察Hartle-Hawking常数（Hartle Hawking constant）与事件视界半径（event horizon radius）的调控效应。

Result: 物理可及区域中几何量子失协随归一化径向距离增加呈先减后增的非单调变化，而物理不可及区域呈现完全相反的趋势；几何量子失协的显著极值恰好出现在霍金辐射峰值强度对应位置。Hartle-Hawking常数越大，量子关联再分配效应越强；事件视界半径越大，该效应越被抑制。

Conclusion: 霍金辐射导致的量子关联在可及与不可及区域间呈现相反的再分配模式，且再分配强度受Hartle-Hawking常数与事件视界半径的相反调控。

Abstract: We investigate the geometric quantum discord of bipartite Werner states influenced by Hawking radiation in the quantum atmosphere of a Schwarzschild black hole. We find that the geometric quantum discord in the physically accessible region exhibits a nonmonotonic behavior: it first decreases and then increases as the normalized radial distance increases, while the discord in the physically inaccessible region shows the exact opposite trend. A pronounced extremum of geometric quantum discord occurs precisely at the position corresponding to the peak intensity of Hawking radiation. Furthermore, we find that the Hartle Hawking constant and the event horizon radius exert opposite effects on the strength of quantum correlation redistribution: a larger Hartle Hawking constant enhances the redistribution effect, whereas a larger event horizon radius suppresses it.

### [181] [Relativistic quantum teleportation protected by the anti-Unruh effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17216)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Unruh-DeWitt探测器（Unruh-DeWitt detector）模型，令参与方Rob与有质量标量场（massive scalar field）发生局部相互作用，同时Alice保持惯性系（inertial frame），分析不同探测器能隙（energy gap）下纠缠与隐形传态保真度的变化。

Result: 小探测器能隙下纠缠随加速度单调递增；大能隙下纠缠在低加速区因Unruh效应先下降，随后在高加速区因反Unruh效应恢复并增强，有效探测器温度（effective detector temperature）降低导致量子相干性（quantum coherence）恢复，隐形传态保真度随加速度增加并在高加速区趋近于1。

Conclusion: 反Unruh效应能够保护并恢复量子信息，为缓解相对论性量子关联退化提供了一种潜在机制。

Abstract: We investigate standard quantum teleportation in a relativistic setting where one participant, Rob, undergoes uniform acceleration while Alice remains inertial. Rob interacts locally with a massive scalar field modeled by an Unruh-DeWitt detector. We show that for small detector energy gaps, the entanglement shared between Alice and Rob increases monotonically with acceleration. For larger gaps, entanglement initially decreases at low accelerations due to the Unruh effect, but is subsequently restored and enhanced at higher accelerations as a consequence of the anti-Unruh effect. This behavior is associated with a reduction of the effective detector temperature, leading to a recovery of quantum coherence previously lost to the field. As a result, the teleportation fidelity increases with acceleration and approaches unity in the high-acceleration regime. Our results demonstrate that the anti-Unruh effect can protect and recover quantum information, providing a potential mechanism to mitigate relativistic degradation of quantum correlations.

### [182] [Sensing relativistic quantum fields with minimally perturbing local measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17920)
*F. Daem,L. Ballesteros Ferraz,A. Zampeli,A. Matzkin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种在相对论性量子场论（relativistic quantum field theory）中对局域测量进行最小扰动的框架，通过弱耦合指针（weakly coupled pointers）以非破坏方式感知场的局域性质，并利用因果允许的Kraus更新（causally admissible Kraus updates）构建操作协议。在三个应用案例（因果结构探测、超临界势中的粒子产生计数、纠缠态与非纠缠态的区分）中展示了该方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文建立一个最小扰动框架：通过弱耦合指针来感知场的局域性质，并将测量信息编码在依赖于场态后选择（postselection）的条件期望值（conditional expectation values）中。操作协议采用因果允许的Kraus算符更新（Kraus updates），与近期相对论性测量理论保持一致，并明确考虑“不可能测量”相关的因果限制。

Result: 通过三个应用展示框架的有效性：（1）类空性探测器（spacelikeness detector），用于因果结构感知（causal-structure sensing）；（2）超临界势（supercritical potential）中粒子产生密度（particle-creation densities）的计数；（3）对场纠缠态（entangled states）与混合态（mixtures）的非破坏性区分。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架为相对论性量子场论中的局域测量提供了因果自洽的最小扰动方案，能够在满足因果约束的前提下实现对场性质的非破坏性感知，并在多个物理场景中展现出实用价值。

Abstract: We develop a framework for minimally perturbing local measurements in relativistic quantum field theory, with the aim to sense local properties of the field in a non-destructive manner. The field properties are sensed by weakly coupled pointers and encapsulated in conditional expectation values dependent on a postselection of the field state. Our operational protocol uses causally admissible Kraus updates for the field, in line with recent relativistic measurement theories, keeping in mind restrictions related to ``impossible measurements''. We illustrate our approach with three applications: a spacelikeness detector for causal-structure sensing, counting particle-creation densities in a supercritical potential and non-destructive discrimination between entangled states of the field and mixtures.

### [183] [New bound on $S_{1}\times S_{2}$-setting Bell locality of a nonseparable Werner state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18050)
*Elena R. Loubenets*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在给定测量设置数 $S_{1}, S_{2}$ 的关联场景下，两量子态（two-qudit）沃纳态（Werner state）是否展现贝尔非局域性（Bell nonlocality）的问题。作者推导出一个新的充分条件，使得维度 $d \leq \min\{S_{1}, S_{2}\}$ 的不可分沃纳态在所有 $S_{1} \times S_{2}$ 设置关联场景下满足所有贝尔不等式（Bell inequalities），即具有 $S_{1} \times S_{2}$ 设置贝尔局域性（Bell locality）。该条件超越了Werner和Barrett此前给出的局域性条件。此外，论文以算子形式明确证明了Terhal等人的优化结果：当 $d > \min\{S_{1}, S_{2}\}$ 时，任何不可分沃纳态都是 $S_{1} \times S_{2}$ 设置贝尔局域的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子应用中，判断一个贝尔非局域两量子态（Bell nonlocal two-qudit state）在给定广义量子测量（generalized quantum measurements）数目 $S_{1}, S_{2}$ 的关联场景下是否展现非局域性，是一个重要问题。现有关于不可分沃纳态（nonseparable Werner state）的局域性条件存在局限性，需要更一般化的分析。

Method: 本研究采用解析方法推导一个新的充分条件。该条件适用于维度 $d \leq \min\{S_{1}, S_{2}\}$ 的不可分沃纳态，使其在所有 $S_{1} \times S_{2}$ 设置关联场景下满足任意谱类型（离散或连续）的贝尔不等式。同时，采用算子形式（operator terms）对Terhal等人的半规划（semi-programming）优化结果进行了显式证明。

Result: 得到了一个新的通用局域性条件（locality condition），该条件在多种 $S_{1}, S_{2} \geq 1$ 取值下超越了Werner和Barrett此前针对不可分沃纳态给出的局域性条件。此外，以算子形式明确证明了：任何维度 $d > \min\{S_{1}, S_{2}\}$ 的不可分沃纳态都是 $S_{1} \times S_{2}$ 设置贝尔局域的。

Conclusion: 本文获得的新的局域性条件对贝尔非局域性理论以及基于贝尔非局域性的量子应用均具有重要意义。这些结果拓展了对沃纳态在受限测量设置场景下局域性行为的理解。

Abstract: In many quantum applications it is important to know whether or not a Bell nonlocal two-qudit state exhibits its nonlocality under correlation scenarios with some given numbers $S_{1},S_{2}\geq1$ of generalized quantum measurements at two sites. In the present article, we find analytically a new general condition sufficient for a nonseparable Werner state with a dimension $d\leq\min\{S_{1},S_{2}\}$ to satisfy all Bell inequalities under every $S_{1}\times S_{2}$-setting correlation scenario with outcomes of an arbitrary spectral type, discrete or continuous $-$ that is, to be $S_{1}\times S_{2}$-setting Bell local, for short. For a variety of $S_{1},S_{2}\geq1$ values, this new general locality condition is beyond Werner's and Barrett's locality conditions for a nonseparable Werner state. We also prove explicitly in the operator terms the optimization result by Terhal et. el. [Phys. Rev. Lett. \textbf{90,} 157903 (2003)] via semi-programming that every nonseparable Werner state with a dimension $d>\min\{S_{1},S_{2}\}$ is $S_{1}\times S_{2}$ -setting Bell local. The new results of the present article are important both for Bell nonlocality theory and for quantum applications based on Bell nonlocality.

### [184] [Dissipative Stabilization of Floquet-Engineered Many-Body Order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16391)
*Shreyas Raman,Robin Schafer,Alicia J. Kollar,Anushya Chandran*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出通过静态耦合的耗散辅助系统（dissipative auxiliaries）对Floquet驱动系统进行冷却，使其稳定在Floquet工程哈密顿量的低能态，从而在稳态中实现无平衡态对应的动力学有序（如离散时间晶体序）。高驱动频率和弱耦合下过剩能量密度可控，并可通过费米黄金定则（Fermi's Golden Rule）的速率理论描述。数值结果验证了该方案在横场Ising链和长程Ising链中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Floquet驱动可实现哈密顿量与量子门工程，并产生无平衡态对应的动力学有序相；然而在良好隔离的系统中，这些现象本质上是瞬态的。因此，如何将瞬态的Floquet有序相稳定为稳态是一个关键挑战。

Method: 引入与系统静态耦合的耗散辅助系统（dissipative auxiliaries），通过耗散过程将驱动系统冷却到Floquet工程哈密顿量的低能态附近。利用基于费米黄金定则（Fermi's Golden Rule）的速率理论（rate theory）描述高驱动频率和弱耦合条件下的过剩能量密度。在Floquet工程横场Ising链和长程Ising链中进行数值模拟验证。

Result: 数值结果表明，在Floquet工程横场Ising链的两个相中均实现了鲁棒的冷却效果；在长程Ising链的稳态中观察到了周期加倍的磁化响应，即离散时间晶体序（discrete time-crystalline order）。

Conclusion: 该工作为驱动-耗散系统（driven dissipative systems）的稳态提供了稀有的解析分析工具，展示了通过耗散辅助冷却稳定Floquet工程有序相的可行性。

Abstract: Floquet driving underlies Hamiltonian and gate engineering, and produces dynamical orders with no equilibrium counterpart. These phenomena are, however, transient in well-isolated systems. We show that statically coupled dissipative auxiliaries cool the system toward low-energy states of the Floquet-engineered Hamiltonian, stabilizing orders in the steady state. The excess energy density is controllably small at high drive frequency and weak coupling and is captured by rate theory based on Fermi's Golden Rule. We numerically confirm robust cooling in a Floquet-engineered transverse-field Ising chain in both phases, and demonstrate discrete time-crystalline order, with a period-doubled magnetization response, in the steady state of a long-range Ising chain. Our results provide a rare analytical handle on the steady states of driven dissipative systems.

### [185] [$p$-Body $\simeq$ Range $p-1$: Exact Order-Range Mapping and Dual-Unitarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16642)
*Tanay Pathak*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个具有连续p体相互作用的周期驱动（kicked）一维自旋-1/2伊辛模型，建立了精确的Floquet相互作用阶数-范围映射（order-range mapping），将p体模型映射到最大范围为p-1的两体伊辛模型，并通过进一步调节驱动强度得到p体对偶幺正（dual-unitary）模型族，进而精确求解了可解初始态下的纠缠动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过在特定的相互作用强度下对p体伊辛模型进行周期驱动（periodically kicking），建立Floquet演化算符的精确阶数-范围映射（order-range mapping）：p体模型映射到具有最大作用范围p-1且耦合常数完全确定的两体伊辛模型。进一步调节驱动强度，使映射后的模型成为对偶幺正（dual-unitary）模型。以p=3为最小示例说明映射的非平凡结构，并推广至所有奇数p。

Result: 建立了精确的Floquet阶数-范围映射，给出了p体相互作用到有限范围两体相互作用的显式对应关系；提供了显式的p体对偶幺正模型族；对一类可解初始态，精确求解了任意时刻的纠缠动力学（entanglement dynamics），并展示了以p=3为例的非平凡映射结构。

Conclusion: 研究为系统性地构造和研究p体对偶幺正Floquet模型提供了一条系统化路径，揭示了高体相互作用在周期驱动系统中可映射为低体有效模型的精确结构，有助于深入理解纠缠演化与量子混沌。

Abstract: We introduce and study a periodically kicked version of a one-dimensional spin-$1/2$ Ising model with contiguous $p$-body interactions. At specific interaction strengths of the model, we establish an exact Floquet interaction $\textit{order-range}$ mapping: the Floquet evolution operator of the $p$-body Ising model is exactly mapped to a two body Ising model with interactions having maximum range $p-1$ and exactly determined couplings. Upon further tuning the kicking strength, the mapped model becomes dual-unitary, thus providing an explicit family of $p$-body dual unitary models. We then determine exact entanglement dynamics of the $p$-body model for a class of solvable initial states at all times. We further illustrate the nontrivial structures that can emerge from the $\textit{order-range}$ mapping using a minimal example of $p=3$ and generalize it for all odd $p$. These findings provide a systematic route to constructing and studying $p$-body dual-unitary Floquet models.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受可编程光镊阵列实验进展的启发，本文旨在为近等边原子三聚体建立一个精确可解的形空间理论框架，探索其在量子信息处理中的应用潜力。

Method: 采用Kendall形球上的Higgs振子模型，构建非共振谱格点；通过固定角动量下的相对驻极分析，识别对称性选择的双重态结构；引入相位相干形模驱动和里德伯介导的条件相位作为操控手段。

Result: 固定角动量的相对驻极极小化子支撑在两个相邻的可容许格点上；对称性选择的双重态与更高分支之间存在有限分支间隙。

Conclusion: 该理论框架与操控方案为构建几何量子比特和实现纠缠操作提供了一条可行的候选路径，有望在可编程量子系统中发挥作用。

Abstract: Motivated by programmable tweezer arrays, we develop an exactly solvable shape-space theory for near-equilateral atomic trimers. The Higgs oscillator on Kendall's shape sphere gives a nonresonant spectral lattice whose fixed-angular-momentum relative-stationary minimizers are supported on two adjacent admissible sites. These symmetry-selected doublets are separated from higher relative-stationary branches by a finite branch gap. With phase-coherent shape-mode driving and Rydberg-mediated conditional phases, they furnish a candidate route to geometric qubits and entangling operations.

### [187] [Chiral Entangled-State Generation through Dissipative Quantum Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17302)
*Huixia Gao,Konghao Sun,Yiwen Han,Lei Xiao,Dengke Qu,Kunkun Wang,Xiang Zhan,Wei Yi,Peng Xue*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合耗散稳态工程与绝热通道的通用协议，通过参数空间中的手性路径实现纠缠态制备，并在光子系统中实验验证了其高保真度、抗噪声及可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观念中，耗散（dissipation）被认为会破坏量子纠缠（quantum entanglement）；已有研究通过设计量子跳跃（quantum jump）过程将耗散转化为制备纠缠态的工具。本文旨在超越这一范式，展示耗散量子动力学中一种新型纠缠产生机制。

Method: 结合驱动-耗散稳态工程（driven-dissipative steady-state engineering）与绝热通道（adiabatic passage），提出一种通用协议：通过参数空间中的演化路径手性（chirality）来决定最终的纠缠态。该方案可进一步扩展至多体纠缠（multipartite entanglement）。实验上，通过量子朗之万方程（quantum Langevin equation）模拟一对光子的李乌维尔动力学（Liouvillian dynamics），验证了手性制备的可行性与抗噪性。

Result: 实验证实，通过手性动力学（chiral dynamics）可在噪声环境下高保真度（high fidelity）和高纠缠并发度（concurrence）地制备多种纠缠态。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了参数手性动力学（parametric chiral dynamics）作为一种可扩展且鲁棒的纠缠产生工具，为量子信息领域的应用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Dissipation, though often detrimental to quantum entanglement, can be manipulated for the preparation of entangled states, wherein ingeniously designed quantum jump processes drive the system toward the desired steady state. Here we venture beyond this paradigm, and demonstrate a new type of entanglement generation in dissipative quantum dynamics. Combining driven-dissipative steady-state engineering and adiabatic passage, we propose a general protocol where the final entangled state depends on the chirality of the evolution path in the parameter space, a scheme that is further extendable to multipartite entanglement. By simulating the Liouvillian dynamics through the quantum Langevin equation for a pair of photons, we experimentally confirm the noise-resistant chiral preparation of various entangled states with high fidelity and concurrence. Our work establishes parametric chiral dynamics as a scalable and robust tool for controllable entanglement generation, paving the way for its applications in quantum information.

### [188] [Neural Gauge-P Representation for Open Quantum Dynamics of Interacting Bosons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17534)

Conclusion: 神经规范-$P$表示法展现了在非平衡开放量子多体动力学（nonequilibrium open quantum many-body dynamics）中实现精确、长时间模拟的潜力。

Abstract: Simulating the nonequilibrium dynamics of interacting open quantum systems remains challenging beyond small system sizes. Quantum phase-space representations provide a scalable approach, but their useful simulation time can be limited by broad distribution tails and the associated boundary terms. We introduce the neural gauge-$P$ representation for open bosonic systems, in which stochastic gauges are parameterized by neural networks and optimized using exact moment equation residuals. For the driven-dissipative Bose--Hubbard model in both single-site and square-lattice settings, the neural gauge-$P$ representation remains accurate during long-time evolution toward the steady state, whereas the corresponding ungauged representation becomes unreliable at substantially earlier times. These results demonstrate the potential of the neural gauge-$P$ representation for accurate simulations of nonequilibrium open quantum many-body dynamics.

### [189] [Strong Quantum Mpemba Effect from Exact Slow-Mode Selection in Constrained Rydberg Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17975)
*Mingdi Xu,Kaixiang Lu,Xiang-Ping Jiang,Haiping Hu,Lei Pan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现，在多体系统中，如果系统对最慢的衰减通道“视而不见”，反而能够实现更快的弛豫——这一机制在受局域退相位约束的里德伯链（Rydberg chains）中产生了稳健的强量子Mpemba效应（strong quantum Mpemba effect）。关键结论是，对于单自旋翻转约束哈密顿量，局域退相位使哈密顿量自身成为精确的左Liouvillian慢模；而能量期望为零的平移不变态能够移除这一慢通道，迫使系统通过更快模式弛豫。研究进一步表明，该机制也存在于(2,3)模型和更远距离的blockade族中，并提出精确慢模选择（exact slow-mode selection）而非特殊疤痕波函数（scar wave functions），是约束开放量子系统中异常快速弛豫的一般组织原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索多体系统能否因对最慢衰减通道“视而不见”而实现更快弛豫，即是否存在一种内在机制驱动强量子Mpemba效应。

Method: 以受局域退相位约束的里德伯链为模型系统，分析约束单自旋翻转哈密顿量（constrained single-spin-flip Hamiltonians）下的Liouvillian慢模结构，通过能量期望为零的平移不变态移除慢通道，并与热态（thermal state）对比，检验弛豫速率的差异。

Result: 局域退相位使哈密顿量自身成为精确的左Liouvillian慢模（$\mathcal L^\dagger(H)=-γH$）；热态保留该慢通道，而能量期望为零的平移不变态（包括零能量疤痕本征态、$|0\cdots0\rangle$乘积态和$Z_2$猫态）则移除该通道，从而产生强量子Mpemba效应。该机制在PXP链、(2,3)模型及更长程blockade族中均稳健存在。

Conclusion: 精确慢模选择（exact slow-mode selection）而非特殊疤痕波函数，是约束开放量子系统中异常快速弛豫的一般组织原理。

Abstract: Can a many-body state relax faster because it is blind to the slowest decay channel? We show that this mechanism gives rise to a robust strong quantum Mpemba effect in locally dephased constrained Rydberg chains. The key observation is that, for constrained single-spin-flip Hamiltonians, local dephasing turns the Hamiltonian itself into an exact left Liouvillian slow mode,
  $\mathcal L^\dagger(H)=-γH$.
  A thermal state generically retains this slow channel, whereas translationally invariant states with vanishing energy expectation remove it and are forced to relax through faster visible modes. This exact selection rule produces a strong quantum Mpemba effect in the locally dephased PXP chain, including for a zero-energy scar eigenstate, the $|0\cdots0\rangle$ product state, and a translation-invariant $Z_2$ cat state. We further show that the same mechanism persists in the $(2,3)$ model and in the longer-range blockade family. Our results identify exact slow-mode selection, rather than special scar wave functions, as a general organizing principle for anomalously fast relaxation in constrained open quantum systems.

</details>

### [190] [An Implicit Time-Domain Harmonic Balance Method for Radio-Frequency Capacitively Coupled Plasma Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18103)
*Yuze Zhu,Yufeng Wei,Yue Zhang,Kun Xu*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次将时域谐波平衡（time-domain harmonic balance, HB）方法成功扩展到完全耦合的漂移-扩散-泊松系统（drift-diffusion-Poisson system）中，用于射频电容耦合等离子体（RF CCPs）的高精度快速模拟；通过算子分裂策略避免全局雅可比矩阵的存储，在保持数值稳定性的同时，相比传统双时间步进（DTS）方法实现了超过10倍的加速，且宏观相对误差低于0.3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 射频电容耦合等离子体（RF CCPs）的快速精确模拟对现代等离子体反应器的迭代设计与参数优化至关重要，但传统时间推进方法（time-marching methods）受限于冗长的物理瞬态过程，计算效率低下。

Method: 首次将时域谐波平衡（time-domain harmonic balance, HB）方法扩展到包含完整电子能量输运的漂移-扩散-泊松系统（drift-diffusion-Poisson system）；采用时空算子分裂策略（spatiotemporal operator-splitting strategy），依次执行空间隐式松弛（spatial implicit relaxation）与单元局部时间反演（cell-local temporal inversion），避免全局雅可比矩阵（global Jacobians）的组装与存储。

Result: 在平行板氩气CCP基准测试中，保留8次谐波（eight harmonics）的HB解在所有时域配点（temporal collocation points）上的宏观相对误差严格低于0.3%；在纯串行单核执行中，HB方法相比完全收敛的DTS基线实现了超过10倍的加速，比最粗糙的时间推进配置仍快5倍以上。

Conclusion: 时域谐波平衡（HB）框架为实际RF等离子体模拟提供了一种物理上严格、内存高效且高度加速的新范式，完全避免了传统时间推进方法所需的物理瞬态过程。

Abstract: Fast and accurate fluid simulation of radio-frequency capacitively coupled plasmas (RF CCPs) is of great importance for the iterative design and parameter optimization of modern plasma reactors. This study presents the first successful extension of the time-domain harmonic balance (HB) method to a fully coupled drift-diffusion-Poisson system with complete electron-energy transport for RF plasma simulations. To resolve the severe numerical stiffness arising from highly nonlinear energy-dependent kinetics and dense phase-coupling, a highly efficient spatiotemporal operator-splitting strategy is employed. By sequentially executing a spatial implicit relaxation and a cell-local temporal inversion, this strategy entirely avoids the memory-intensive assembly of global Jacobians while preserving robust numerical stability. The proposed method is rigorously validated against a standard parallel-plate argon CCP benchmark. Evaluated across all discrete temporal collocation points, the HB solution demonstrates that retaining eight harmonics perfectly resolves both the quasi-steady bulk plasma and the highly nonlinear transient sheath dynamics, yielding macroscopic relative errors strictly below 0.3% compared to conventional dual-time stepping (DTS) solutions. Beyond its high physical fidelity, the time-domain HB method completely bypasses the prohibitive physical transients required by conventional time-marching methods. Evaluated on a purely sequential single-core execution, the HB method delivers a greater than 10-fold speedup over fully converged DTS baselines and remains over 5 times faster than the coarsest time-marching configurations. These results establish the time-domain HB framework as a physically rigorous, memory-efficient, and highly accelerated paradigm for practical RF plasma simulations.

</details>

### [191] [Fitting the topology of synthetic particle systems with a novel graph representation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17680)
*Martin Alexander Memmesheimer,Claudia Redenbach*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粒子材料的宏观性质取决于其微观粒子的形状与排列，现有的粒子生成模型主要关注单粒子形状与尺寸，难以准确拟合粒子系统的拓扑结构。此外，所需的大规模三维体素图像（3D voxel images）使得传统的持久同调计算方法在计算上不可行。

Method: 本文引入了一种新颖的粒子系统图表示（graph representation），将持久同调的计算从图像域（image domain）转移到图域（graph domain），从而大幅降低计算开销。该方法作为合成图像的后处理步骤，独立于具体的粒子生成方法。

Result: 所提方法能够改善合成粒子系统与真实粒子系统之间的拓扑一致性和几何一致性，同时保留粒子尺寸分布（particle size distribution）等形态学特征。

Conclusion: 该工作为粒子系统合成数据的拓扑拟合提供了一种高效且通用的后处理方案，有望揭示结构-性质关系（structure-property relations）。

Abstract: The shape and arrangement of particles in a material determine its macroscopic properties. Most particle generation models focus on single-particle characteristics like shape and size. We aim at fitting the topology of the particle system using tools from persistent homology. However, the large size of the required 3D image data makes existing methods computationally infeasible. We bridge this gap by introducing a novel graph representation of particle systems and transferring the computation of persistent homology from the image domain to the graph domain. This yields a postprocessing method for synthetic images of particle systems, that is independent of the underlying generation method and improves topological and geometrical agreement with real particle systems while preserving morphological characteristics such as the particle size distribution.

### [192] [On the collapse of three point vortices on surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16490)
*Theodore D. Drivas,Boris A. Khanikati,Valeriya A. Khanikati*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 该论文研究了三维点涡（point vortex）系统在曲面上发生有限时间坍缩（collapse）的普适性问题。在欧几里得平面和球面上，坍缩是自相似（self-similar）的；在双曲面上则不存在任何解析测地距离变量下的自相似坍缩；而对于任意嵌入三维欧氏空间的光滑曲面，则存在近乎自相似的坍缩解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 点涡是描述二维理想流体动力学的重要简化模型。已知在欧几里得平面上，三涡配置可以发生有限时间内的自相似坍缩。本文旨在探究这一现象在弯曲曲面（如球面和双曲平面）上的推广程度与存在条件。

Method: 通过理论分析，分别对常曲率曲面（零曲率的平面、正曲率的球面、负曲率的双曲平面）上的三涡动力学方程进行解析研究，考察自相似坍缩解的存在性。此外，利用局部几何逼近方法，分析任意光滑嵌入曲面上的近似自相似坍缩行为。

Result: 自相似坍缩是零常曲率（平面）和正常曲率（球面）曲面的普适特征；在双曲平面上，对于由测地距离的任意解析函数定义的距离变量，自相似坍缩解均不存在；但对于任意光滑嵌入曲面，存在近乎自相似的三涡坍缩解。

Conclusion: 点涡坍缩的自相似性强烈依赖于曲面的曲率符号：非负常曲率曲面上具有普适性，负曲率曲面上则被禁止，而一般光滑曲面上以近似形式存在。

Abstract: Point vortices represent an important reduced model describing two-dimensional ideal fluid dynamics. It is well known that there exist three-vortex configurations on the Euclidean plane $\mathbb{R}^2$ that exhibit finite-time singularities, i.e., collapse to a single point. Moreover, in $\mathbb{R}^2$, such collapses occur only self-similarly. Here, we investigate the extent to which this phenomenon persists on curved surfaces. We show that self-similar collapse is a universal feature of surfaces of nonnegative constant curvature, namely the plane and the sphere. In contrast, on the hyperbolic plane, it is shown that self-similar collapsing solutions do not exist with respect to any distance variable defined by an analytic function of the geodesic distance. Finally, we establish the existence of nearly self-similar collapse of three vortices on arbitrary smooth surfaces embedded in $\mathbb{R}^3$.

</details>


### [193] [An SPH model with physically prescribed parameters for droplet dynamics on complex surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16670)
*Zhonghua Qiao,Yifan Wei,Xianmin Xu*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于物理的、高效的平滑粒子流体动力学（smoothed particle hydrodynamics, SPH）模型，用于模拟不同润湿性复杂表面上的液滴动力学。该模型采用单相液滴建模策略，通过SPH核函数近似界面长程相互作用，以压力表示短程相互作用，并建立了分子间势能与宏观表面张力系数之间的显式关系，减少了对经验参数校准的依赖。静态润湿和液滴撞击模拟验证了该方法能准确捕捉复杂动态润湿行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂表面上变润湿性液滴动力学的数值模拟对工程应用和基础研究具有重要意义，但现有数值方法在精确捕捉界面相互作用、保持物理一致性和计算效率方面仍面临挑战。

Method: 开发了一种基于物理且高效的平滑粒子流体动力学（SPH）模型：采用单相液滴建模策略降低计算成本；在界面处，使用SPH核函数近似长程相互作用，以压力表示短程相互作用；并基于此建立了分子间势能与宏观表面张力系数之间的显式关系，减少了经验参数校准的依赖。

Result: 静态润湿模拟中平衡接触角与Young–Dupré方程吻合良好；润湿和液滴撞击的进一步模拟表明该方法能够捕捉复杂的动态润湿行为。

Conclusion: 所提出的SPH模型在保持物理一致性和计算效率的同时，能够准确模拟复杂表面上的液滴动力学行为，为相关工程和基础研究提供了可靠工具。

Abstract: Numerical simulation of droplet dynamics on complex surfaces with varying wettability is of great significance to both engineering applications and fundamental research. However, existing numerical methods still face challenges in accurately capturing interfacial interactions while preserving physical consistency and computational efficiency. In this work, a physically grounded and efficient smoothed particle hydrodynamics (SPH) model is developed for droplet dynamics simulation. To reduce computational cost, a single-phase droplet modeling strategy is employed. At the interface, long-range interactions are approximated using the SPH kernel function, whereas short-range interactions are represented through pressure. Based on this treatment, an explicit relationship between the intermolecular potential energy and the macroscopic surface tension coefficient is further established, thereby reducing reliance on empirical parameter calibration. The proposed method is first validated through static wetting simulations, where the equilibrium contact angles agree well with the Young--Dupré equation. Further simulations of wetting and droplet impact demonstrate that the method is capable of capturing complex dynamic wetting behaviors.

</details>


### [194] [Physically Consistent Outflow Boundary Conditions for Global Stability Analysis of Bluff Body Wakes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17864)
*Guangyao Cui,Amit Sigawi,Michael Karp*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文采用基于有限差分离散的矩阵形成法（matrix-forming method）对钝体尾流（bluff body wake）进行全局线性稳定性分析（global linear stability analysis），重点评估了出口边界条件对计算域大小和结果精度的影响，发现Robin边界条件可以显著缩短所需计算域而不降低精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在钝体尾流的全局线性稳定性分析中，出口边界条件的选择直接影响计算域尺寸的选取与结果的准确性。本文旨在通过合理设置边界条件，在不引发出口附近虚假振荡（spurious oscillation）的前提下，尽可能缩小计算域，从而提升计算效率。

Method: 采用基于有限差分离散的矩阵形成法，针对不可压缩钝体尾流（如圆柱和大攻角翼型）进行全局线性稳定性分析。系统评估了多种常用出口边界条件，包括Dirichlet、Neumann、外推（extrapolation）、无应力（stress-free）、海绵层（sponge layer）以及引入局部线性稳定性分析（local linear stability analysis）预测的Robin条件。

Result: 在临界雷诺数（critical Reynolds number）以下，即使全局模态（global mode）线性稳定，尾流中仍可能存在显著的远场下游空间增长。不同雷诺数下，Robin边界条件均能在大幅缩短的计算域内实现全局模态的稳健收敛（robust convergence）。

Conclusion: Robin条件显著提升了全局稳定性分析的计算效率，矩阵形成法可进一步推广至时间周期流的Floquet分析（Floquet analysis）及可压缩构型等更复杂的稳定性分析场景。

Abstract: Global linear stability analysis of bluff body wake flows is performed using the matrix-forming method based on finite-difference discretization. Particular emphasis is placed on the influence of outflow boundary conditions, with the aim of minimizing the required computational domain size without degrading accuracy or inducing spurious oscillations near the outlet. This study focuses on incompressible wakes behind bluff bodies such as cylinders and airfoils at high angle of attack, especially in regimes where global modes exhibit downstream spatial amplification. It is shown that below the critical Reynolds number -- where the global mode remains linearly stable -- significant spatial growth can persist far downstream, even when the wake is nearly absent. This behavior underscores the importance of imposing a physical boundary condition at the outlet. Several commonly used outflow boundary conditions are evaluated, including Dirichlet, Neumann, extrapolation, stress-free, sponge layer, and the Robin condition that incorporates predictions from local linear stability analysis at the outlet. The results demonstrate that, for different $Re$ cases, the Robin condition enables robust convergence of global modes within substantially truncated domains, thereby improving the efficiency of global stability analysis. These findings highlight the broader applicability of the matrix-forming approach for complex stability analyses, including Floquet analysis of time-periodic flows and extensions to compressible configurations.

</details>


### [195] [Transition to chaos in two-dimensional Rayleigh-Bénard convection: the role of the magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17918)
*Francis F. Franco,Gabriel de T. Paula,Roman Chertovskih,Dalton N. Oliveira,Erico L. Rempel*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究外部磁场对二维瑞利-贝纳德对流（RBC）的影响，发现磁场会显著增强行波卷（traveling rolls）的动力行为，并通过磁重联（magnetic reconnection）导致对流卷分裂/破碎，从而可能触发二维湍流的转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究外加磁场对二维瑞利-贝纳德对流数值模拟的影响，尤其是在混沌转变过程中的作用。

Method: 先在没有磁场的情况下建立基线RBC模型，随后引入背景磁场，对比分析不同约化瑞利数（reduced Rayleigh number）下系统从行波卷到混沌的转变过程，并通过速度场分析揭示拓扑变化机制。

Result: 纯流体动力学情况下，系统经历吸引子合并危机（attractor-merging crisis）后由行波卷转变为混沌行波卷；引入磁场后，行波卷动力学显著增强，对流卷更易分裂/破碎；鞍点与对流卷中心碰撞使系统恢复原始拓扑，同时磁重联导致一个磁涡旋分裂为两个。

Conclusion: 磁场通过对流卷分裂/破碎及磁重联机制，可能促进二维湍流的转变，且该过程在时间上呈间歇性发生。

Abstract: The impact of an externally imposed magnetic field on numerical simulations of two-dimensional Rayleigh-Bénard convection (RBC) is investigated. Initially, the RBC model is examined in the absence of a magnetic field to establish a baseline. Then, a background magnetic field is introduced, and its influence on the transition to chaos is explored. For the purely hydrodynamic case and a range of the reduced Rayleigh number, the system exhibits traveling rolls which, after an attractor-merging crisis, give way to chaotic traveling rolls. Upon imposing a background magnetic field, there is a notable increase in the occurrence of traveling roll dynamics. Furthermore, the presence of the magnetic field favors the splitting/breaking of convective rolls, indicating a possible mechanism for transition to two-dimensional turbulence, with the structure of the convection cell being disrupted. A detailed analysis of the velocity field reveals that the collision between a saddle point and the center of a convective roll restores the system's original topology, with two symmetric kinetic vortices. During this collision, a magnetic vortex splits in two as a result of a magnetic reconnection. This behavior occurs intermittently in time.

### [196] [Projection-Lift Equivalence and Dissipation-Tight Compactness for Continuum-State FENE-Markov Fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16993)
*Sai Peng*

TL;DR: 本文研究不可压缩FENE哑铃模型与可逆马尔可夫算子的耦合系统，证明在零质心扩散条件下状态平均是精确的因子映射，且系统解的存在性、多重性与唯一性完全由其标量FENE投影决定；同时构造了正扩散情形下的全局弱解，并证明了相关极限过程的强收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究耦合内部状态（internal state）的不可压缩FENE哑铃模型的数学结构，特别是状态平均的因子映射性质及其对解的唯一性与多重性的影响，并解决大数据下非唯一性问题。

Method: 结合正则拉格朗日流（regular Lagrangian flow）的稳定性与相对熵估计（relative-entropy estimate），处理同时变化的矩阵漂移（matrix drifts）与跃迁速率（jump rates）；利用无迹矩阵纤维演化（trace-free matrix fibre evolution）驱动状态提升（state lift）。

Result: 零质心扩散下系统解的存在性、多重性与唯一性完全由标量FENE投影决定，内部态动力学不产生额外的大数据非唯一性；正质心扩散下独立构造了全局大数据弱解，确认了相同的非线性项；证明了完整密度在标量极限后的强收敛性，以及阻力、态依赖活性、奇异应力与非原子Jeffreys生产项的极限传递。

Abstract: We consider incompressible FENE dumbbells coupled to a reversible Markov operator on a compact continuum of internal states. At zero centre-of-mass diffusion we prove that state averaging is an exact factor map and that a Lagrangian state lift is its unique inverse on the natural energy-solution classes. Thus existence, multiplicity, and uniqueness of the state-resolved system are precisely those of its scalar FENE projection; the internal-state dynamics creates no additional large-data nonuniqueness. The lift is driven by a trace-free matrix fibre evolution and permits nonlinear local activities, including rates with linear dependence on the singular Kramers stress.We also prove a sequential form of this structure. For state-resolved regularizations with relative-entropy-prepared initial fibres and no viscous dissipation defect, the complete densities converge strongly without reconstructing them after the scalar limit. Consequently the full drag,state-dependent activity, singular stress, and non-atomic Jeffreys production all pass to the limit. The argument combines stability of regular Lagrangian flows with a relative-entropy estimate for simultaneously varying matrix drifts and jump rates. A stationary oscillation shows that the preparation cannot follow from the natural entropy bounds alone. With positive centre-of-mass diffusion we independently construct global large-data weak solutions and identify the same nonlinear terms. An explicit infinite-rank kernel proves that these results are not finite-species reductions.

### [197] [Couette Flow with Robin Boundary Condition (I): the viscosity-independent friction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17468)
*Siming He,Binqian Niu,Weiren Zhao*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文是该系列的第一篇，研究固体-流体边界摩擦因子 α 对 Couette 流稳定性的影响。在 Robin 型边界条件下，证明了当黏性系数 ν 远小于 α 且初始扰动满足一定小条件时，系统是渐近稳定的，并且无黏阻尼（inviscid damping）和增强耗散（enhanced dissipation）成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究固体-流体边界处摩擦因子 α 对 Couette 流稳定性的影响，特别是 Robin 型边界条件下系统的渐近行为。

Method: 考虑有界周期通道 $\mathbb{T} \times [-1,1]$ 中 Couette 流在 Robin 型边界条件（$u^2|_{y=\pm 1}=0$, $[α\partial_n u^1+u^1]|_{y=\pm 1}=f$）下的稳定性问题，其中 α 为摩擦因子，n 为单位外法向量。通过分析初始扰动满足 $\|ω_{\rm in}\| \leq εν^{1/3}$ 的条件，建立稳定性结果。

Result: 对于给定的摩擦因子 α，当流体黏性系数 ν 远小于 α（ν ≪ α）且初始扰动足够小时，系统是渐近稳定的。此外，无黏阻尼（inviscid damping）和增强耗散（enhanced dissipation）也成立。

Conclusion: Robin 边界条件下的摩擦因子 α 在黏性系数足够小时能够保证 Couette 流的渐近稳定性，并伴随无黏阻尼和增强耗散现象。

Abstract: This article is the first paper in the series. In this series of articles, we will examine the influence of the friction factor $α$ at the solid--fluid boundary on the stability of Couette flow. Specifically, we consider the stability of Couette flow in a bounded periodic channel $\mathbb{T} \times [-1,1]$ under Robin-type boundary conditions ($u^2|_{y=\pm 1} = 0$, $[α\partial_n u^1 + u^1]|_{y=\pm1} = f $), where $α$ is the friction factor and $n$ is the unit outer normal vector. In this article, we prove that for a given friction factor $α$, as long as the fluid viscosity coefficient $ν\ll α$ is sufficiently small, the system is asymptotically stable if the initial perturbation satisfies $\|ω_{\rm in}\| \leq εν^{1/3}$. Moreover, inviscid damping and enhanced dissipation hold.

### [198] [Finite Potential Energy for Entire Solutions of the Planar Ginzburg--Landau Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17490)
*Hongge Chen,Juncheng Wei,Haicheng Yan,Wen Yang*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了所有满足无穷远处趋于单位模条件的二维Ginzburg–Landau方程光滑整体解的势能有限，从而解决了Brezis公开问题2.5。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该工作旨在解决Brezis提出的公开问题2.5，即证明Ginzburg–Landau方程在无穷远处模趋近于1的光滑整体解具有有限的势能（potential energy）$\int_{\mathbb{R}^2}(1-|u|^2)^2\dd x<+\infty$。

Method: 针对携带非零环量且仅以$|x|^{-1}$衰减的无旋模式（curl-free mode）这一核心困难——该模式不在$L^2$中且不具有单值势——作者通过在$L^2$梯度修正上取极小化构造了一个满足齐次方程且继承相同环量的比较场（comparison field）。结合Kelvin变换（Kelvin inversion）与拟线性椭圆方程的De Giorgi–Nash–Moser理论，得到了最优衰减$O(|x|^{-1})$。对于Ginzburg–Landau解，利用Bernstein估计和Jacobi形式的强制性（coercivity）在外区域相位方程中产生$L^2$强迫项，进而获得相位场的$L^4$估计。

Result: 得到的$L^4$界蕴含$1-|u|^2\in L^2(\mathbb{R}^2)$，从而势能有限。

Conclusion: 该结果完整解决了Brezis公开问题2.5，确认了二维Ginzburg–Landau方程光滑整体解的势能必然有限。

Abstract: We prove that every smooth entire solution $ u\colon\mathbb{R}^2\to\mathbb{R}^2 $ of the Ginzburg--Landau equation $ -Δu=u(1-|u|^2) $ with $ |u(x)|\to1 $ as $ |x|\to\infty $ has finite potential energy, i.e., \begin{equation*} \int_{\mathbb{R}^2}(1-|u|^2)^2\dd x<+\infty, \end{equation*} thereby resolving Brezis' Open Problem 2.5 in \cite{BrezisProblems}. The main difficulty stems from the possible presence of a curl-free mode that carries nonzero circulation and decays only like $ |x|^{-1} $; such a mode lies outside $ L^2 $ and does not admit a single-valued potential. By minimizing over $ L^2 $ gradient corrections, we construct a comparison field that solves the homogeneous equation and inherits the same circulation. The Kelvin inversion, combined with the De Giorgi--Nash--Moser theory for quasilinear elliptic equations, then produces the optimal decay $ O(|x|^{-1}) $. For a Ginzburg--Landau solution, the Bernstein estimate and the coercivity of the Jacobi form produce an $ L^2 $ forcing term in the exterior phase equation. The resulting $ L^4 $ bound on the phase field implies $1-|u|^2\in L^2(\mathbb{R}^2)$, and therefore the potential energy is finite.

</details>


### [199] [Minimizers and Weak Solutions for Singular Born--Infeld Type Functionals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17794)
*Tengyang Liu,Ruifeng Zhang*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究Born–Infeld型奇异泛函极小元与弱解之间的关系。通过单调逼近方法处理泛函的固有奇异性，证明极小元的梯度永不触及奇异边界，进而得到极小元的存在唯一性及变分不等式。在径向电荷分布条件下，极小元是唯一的弱解，并建立了极小元的C^1与C^2正则性及严格类空条件的一致估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Born–Infeld理论（Born–Infeld theory）中的奇异泛函在静电学背景下自然满足有限梯度界$|\nabla\phi|\le 1$，但其极小元与弱解之间的严格关系尚不清晰。本文旨在为更广泛的一类Born–Infeld型奇异泛函建立统一的变分分析与正则性框架，澄清极小元与弱解的等价性。

Method: 提出一种单调逼近方法（monotonic approximation method）处理泛函$\mathcal{L}(s)$在$s\to (1/2)^-$处的奇异性；通过分析极小元梯度的边界行为，证明其永不触及奇异边界$|\nabla\phi|^2=1$；在径向电荷分布假设下，将极小元与弱解进行对比验证。

Result: 证明了极小元的梯度始终严格远离奇异边界，从而得到极小元的存在唯一性及对应的变分不等式（variational inequality）；在径向电荷密度$\rho$条件下，极小元是唯一的弱解；建立了极小元的$C^1$与$C^2$正则性，并给出了严格类空条件（strict spacelikeness）$|\nabla\phi_0|\le 1-\varepsilon$中$\varepsilon>0$的显式刻画，该参数依赖于空间维数、空间区域及电荷密度。

Conclusion: 本文的结果将经典Born–Infeld理论推广到一般Born–Infeld型奇异泛函类，为这类奇异泛函与系统的变分分析和正则性提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the relation between minimizers and weak solutions for a class of singular functionals arising from Born--Infeld type theories $\mathcal{L}(s)$. In the setting of an electrostatic field $s=\frac{1}{2}|\nablaφ|^2$, $\mathcal{L}(s)$ satisfies $\lim_{s\to(1/2)^-}\mathcal{L}(s)=+\infty$, which naturally enforces the finite gradient bound $|\nablaφ|\le 1$, also called the truncation threshold. For a prescribed extended charge density $ρ$, we consider the relation between the weak solution of the system \begin{equation} \begin{cases} -{\rm div}\left(b\left(\frac12|\nablaφ|^2\right)\nablaφ\right)=ρ,& \text{in }\mathbb{R}^N,\\ b(s)=\mathcal{L}'(s),\quad\lim_{s\to\frac12^-} b(s)=+\infty,\\ \lim_{|x|\to\infty}φ(x)=0 \end{cases} \end{equation} and the minimizer $φ_0$ of the singular functional. We propose a monotonic approximation method to handle the intrinsic singularities of $\mathcal{L}(s)$. We prove that the gradient of the minimizer never touches the singular boundary $|\nablaφ|^2=1$; this structural result yields a key integrability property, the existence and uniqueness of the minimizer, and the corresponding variational inequality. Under the additional assumption that $ρ$ is radially distributed, we show that the minimizer is the unique weak solution. Furthermore, we establish the $C^1$ and $C^2$ regularity of the minimizer under suitable integrability conditions on $ρ$, and provide a uniform estimate for the strict spacelikeness condition $|\nablaφ_0|\le 1-ε$, where the parameter $ε>0$ is explicitly characterized in terms of the spatial dimension, the spatial region, and $ρ$. Our results extend the classical Born--Infeld theory to a general class of singular Born--Infeld type theories, thereby providing a unified framework for the variational analysis and regularity of such singular functionals and systems.

</details>


### [200] [Euler-Poisson equations with velocity-dependent damping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18035)
*Olga S. Rozanova*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究带幂律速度相关阻尼系数的排斥性Euler-Poisson方程，发现一维情形下全局光滑解的初始数据集合得以扩大，但其他维度（除四维外）中阻尼无法改善解的光滑性质，稳态的任意小扰动仍会导致爆破（blow up），尽管振荡幅度衰减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨幂律速度相关阻尼系数对排斥性Euler-Poisson方程解的光滑性（smoothness）和全局存在性（global existence）的影响，特别关注不同空间维度下阻尼是否能够抑制爆破。

Method: 考虑一维空间和具有径向对称性（radial symmetry）的多维情形下的排斥性Euler-Poisson方程，引入幂律速度相关阻尼项（power-law velocity-dependent damping coefficient），通过理论分析比较不同维度下解的行为。

Result: 一维情形下，阻尼扩大了全局时间光滑解（globally time-smooth solution）对应的初始数据集合；但在其他维度（四维除外）中，阻尼无法改善解的光滑性质——稳态（steady state）的任意小扰动仍会导致爆破，尽管振荡幅度（amplitude of oscillations）衰减。

Conclusion: 幂律速度相关阻尼对排斥性Euler-Poisson方程解的正则性（regularity）改善效果具有维度依赖性，仅在特殊维度（如一维）有效；高维情形中阻尼无法阻止爆破的发生。

Abstract: We consider repulsive Euler-Poisson equations in both one-dimensional space and in the multidimensional case with radial symmetry, assuming a power-law velocity-dependent damping coefficient. We show that under this assumption, in the one-dimensional case the set of initial data corresponding to a globally time-smooth solution expands, whereas in other dimensions (except for dimension 4) the damping does not influence on improving of smooth properties of the solution. Namely, any arbitrary small perturbation of the steady state blow up, despite of its amplitude of oscillations decays.

</details>

### [201] [On Accretion and Neutrino Investigations of Thermodynamically Reconstructed Black Holes from Three-Parameter Generalized Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16337)
*F. Barzi,W. El Hadri,H. El Moumni,K. Masmar,S. Mazzou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于三参数广义熵（generalized entropy）重构静态黑洞的有效外部几何，通过引入视界响应因子（horizon response factor）$Ξ_h$控制熵变形，系统计算了光子球面（photon sphere）、阴影尺度（shadow scale）、圆轨道、ISCO、Novikov–Thorne盘通量、辐射效率及中微子敏感温度矩等可观测信号，揭示了熵变形对致密轨道和薄盘发射的直接调控规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在建立广义熵与黑洞可观测信号之间的直接联系，避免将熵形变简单映射为径向坐标重定义或类Reissner–Nordström修正，从而基于热力学自洽的方式重构黑洞外部几何并预测光子、吸积盘及中微子信号的响应特征。

Method: 通过广义熵固定视界响应因子$Ξ_h=dS_G/dS|_{S_h}$，要求由表面引力温度（surface-gravity temperature）复现广义热力学温度，从而重构有效外部几何；引入变形参数$λ_G=1/Ξ_h-1$与整数$p\geq2$控制近视界修正的径向局域化，并采用无量纲温度矩（dimensionless temperature moments）保守建模中微子扇区。

Result: 正向$λ_G$使光子球面和ISCO内移、阴影尺度减小、辐射效率升高并将能量释放集中于内盘；负向$λ_G$产生相反趋势。$n=4,6,9$阶温度矩的层级表明，温度指数越高，熵致盘形变越显著。

Conclusion: 可观测的致密轨道变化和薄盘发射特征可直接经由视界响应与广义熵建立关联，熵诱导的盘形变在更高温度矩下愈加明显。

Abstract: We study accretion and neutrino-sensitive thermal signatures of a static black hole reconstructed from a three-parameter generalized entropy. The construction is thermodynamic by design: the entropy deformation is not mapped to a radial-coordinate redefinition or to a prescribed Reissner--Nordström-like correction. Instead, the generalized entropy fixes the horizon response factor $Ξ_h=dS_G/dS|_{S_h}$. The effective exterior geometry is then reconstructed by requiring its surface-gravity temperature to reproduce the generalized thermodynamic temperature. As a result, the metric preserves the horizon area and the Schwarzschild asymptotics, and reduces smoothly to Schwarzschild when $Ξ_h\to1$.
  The deformation is controlled by $λ_G=1/Ξ_h-1$, while the integer $p\geq2$ determines the radial localization of the near-horizon correction. We compute the photon sphere, critical shadow scale, circular geodesics, ISCO, Novikov--Thorne flux, disk temperature, radiative efficiency, energy-at-infinity luminosity, a redshifted spectral proxy, and neutrino-sensitive temperature moments. In particular, positive $λ_G$ moves the photon sphere and ISCO inward, decreases the shadow scale, raises the radiative efficiency, and concentrates the energy release toward the inner disk. By contrast, negative $λ_G$ produces the opposite trend.
  Finally, the neutrino sector is modeled conservatively using dimensionless temperature moments instead of a full neutrino-dominated accretion flow or annihilation-deposition calculation. The hierarchy among the $ n=4$, $n=6$, and $n=9$ moments reveals that entropy-induced disk deformation becomes increasingly apparent with higher temperature exponents. Thus, observable changes in compact orbits and thin-disk emission can be directly linked to generalized entropy via the horizon response.

</details>


### [202] [No late-time role for adiabatic torsion: a no-go result for Hubble-cutoff holographic dark energy in Einstein--Cartan cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16370)
*Fernando Izaurieta,Samuel Lepe,Cristian Quinzacara*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明，在爱因斯坦-嘉当（Einstein-Cartan）挠率（torsion）的弗里德曼宇宙学中，所谓的均匀挠率模式（homogeneous torsion mode）不能作为全息暗能量（holographic dark energy）的哈勃红外截断（Hubble infrared cutoff）来挽救。通过对DESI DR2 BAO数据、高红移星系、CMB和BBN的多重约束，该模式的能量密度参数Ω_Φ被严格限制在5×10^{-24}至8.7×10^{-4}之间，其对暗能量状态方程（equation of state）的修正远不足以解释DESI观测到的phantom穿越（phantom-divide crossing）迹象。在Granda-Oliveros截断下，挠率反而加剧了大撕裂（big-rip）奇点。附录从场方程导出了挠率模式的动力学本质，指出打破该负结果需要放弃a^{-3}标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期有工作声称，爱因斯坦-嘉当理论中的均匀挠率模式可以作为全息暗能量的红外截断（infrared cutoff），产生晚期宇宙加速膨胀（late-time acceleration）和phantom穿越（phantom-divide crossing）现象，从而可能解释DESI巡天观测到的暗能量动力学迹象。本文旨在严格检验这一主张的可行性。

Method: 本文通过解析推导哈勃截断下全息暗能量密度对减速参数（deceleration parameter）的贡献，发现其完全抵消，唯一可能的加速窗口仅存在于挠率反弹（torsion bounce）附近的一个有限红移区间内。作者随后利用五项独立的观测与理论约束——DESI DR2 BAO似然拟合、z=14.32处光谱确认星系的存在、宇宙微波背景辐射（CMB）、大爆炸核合成（BBN）以及暗能量状态方程（dark energy equation of state）的当前值——对参数Ω_Φ≡(Φ_0/H_0)^2施加嵌套上限。此外还分析了Granda-Oliveros截断下的行为。

Result: 在哈勃截断下，全息暗能量密度从减速参数中完全消去，唯一加速窗口是反弹点附近的瞬态区间ā≤a<4^{1/3}ā，将其置于可观测红移会要求哈勃率在近期为零，与实测膨胀史（expansion history）矛盾。五项约束给出Ω_Φ的上界：DESI DR2 BAO：8.7×10^{-4}（95% CL）；z=14.32星系：8.4×10^{-5}；CMB：3.1×10^{-10}；BBN：5×10^{-24}。对当前暗能量状态方程的修正为|1+ω_0|≤2Ω_Φ/Ω_Λ，最低比DESI偏好小两个数量级，最高小二十二个数量级，且落在phantom侧。在Granda-Oliveros截断下，挠率加剧了大撕裂奇点（big-rip singularity）。

Conclusion: 均匀挠率模式无法实现全息暗能量的哈勃截断方案，也不能解释DESI观测到的暗能量动力学信号。对Ω_Φ的观测约束极其严格，使得任何可观测效应均被排除。附录从爱因斯坦-嘉当场方程导出Friedmann方程组，证明a^{-3}标度律来自稀释自旋流体（diluting spin fluid）的运动学；若要绕过本文的负结论，必须破坏这一标度律。

Abstract: In Friedmann cosmology with Einstein--Cartan torsion, the homogeneous torsion mode compatible with a separately conserved matter sector scales as $Φ\propto a^{-3}$ and enters the Friedmann constraint as a stiff component of negative energy density, $-3Φ^{2}\propto a^{-6}$. It has recently been claimed that this mode rescues the Hubble radius as an infrared cutoff for holographic dark energy, producing late-time acceleration and a phantom-divide crossing of possible relevance to DESI. We show that it cannot. With the Hubble cutoff the holographic density drops out of the deceleration parameter, and the only accelerating regime is the transient window $\bar{a}\leq a<4^{1/3}\bar{a}$ around the torsion bounce at $H(\bar{a})=0$; placing that window at observable redshifts would force the Hubble rate to vanish in our recent past, against the measured expansion history. Requiring a viable history yields nested upper bounds on $Ω_Φ\equiv(Φ_{0}/H_{0})^{2}$: fitting the official DESI DR2 BAO likelihood gives $Ω_Φ<8.7\times10^{-4}$ ($95\%$ CL), the existence of a spectroscopically confirmed galaxy at $z=14.32$ gives $8.4\times10^{-5}$, the CMB gives $3.1\times10^{-10}$, and Big Bang nucleosynthesis gives $5\times10^{-24}$. Today's imprint on the dark energy equation of state, $|1+ω_{0}|\leq2Ω_Φ/Ω_Λ$, falls short of the DESI preference by two orders of magnitude at best and twenty-two at worst, and on the phantom side. In the Granda--Oliveros cutoff, torsion deepens rather than prevents the big-rip singularity. An appendix derives the Friedmann pair from the Einstein--Cartan field equations and shows that the $a^{-3}$ scaling is the kinematics of a diluting spin fluid; escaping the no-go requires breaking exactly that.

</details>


### [203] [Probing f(R) AdS Black Hole via Hawking Evaporation, Shadows and Thermal Fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16432)
*Muhammad Israr Aslam,Saira Waheed,Rabia Saleem,Nazek Alessa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在f(R) AdS黑洞（anti-de Sitter black hole）框架下，系统研究了霍金蒸发（Hawking evaporation）、阴影（shadow）和热涨落（thermal fluctuations）。通过数值分析发现黑洞寿命无限，最终成为残余（remnant）；阴影半径随参数ψ₀递减、随λ递增；热力学量分析揭示了参数对稳定性与相变的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在f(R)引力修正理论中，AdS黑洞的热力学与观测特征尚未被充分理解。本文旨在通过数值和解析方法，系统探讨f(R) AdS黑洞的霍金蒸发过程、阴影光学特征以及热力学稳定性，以揭示修正引力参数对黑洞物理行为的影响。

Method: 采用Stefan-Boltzmann定律对霍金蒸发过程进行数值分析；通过观测不同参数值下的黑洞阴影（BH shadow）研究其视觉特性；进一步分析下落吸积物质（infalling accretion matter）在黑洞附近的光学表现；利用多种热力学量（如温度、熵、亥姆霍兹自由能、内能、修正压力、焓、吉布斯自由能、比热）讨论相变与稳定性。

Result: 黑洞寿命（BH lifetime）始终为无限，表明黑洞在晚期成为残余；蒸发速率（evaporation rate）依赖于AdS半径和耦合参数。黑洞阴影半径随ψ₀增大而减小，随λ增大而增大。吸积物质的中心区域受参数影响，但明亮光子环（bright photon ring）的光学外观变化是关键特征。热力学分析表明，参数λ和ψ₀的变化显著影响黑洞的稳定性与相变行为。

Conclusion: f(R) AdS黑洞在晚期表现为残余，其阴影和热力学行为强烈依赖于修正引力参数。这些发现为理解修正引力理论下的黑洞物理提供了数值和理论依据，并揭示了参数调控对黑洞观测特征与热力学相变的重要作用。

Abstract: The process of Hawking evaporation, shadows and thermal fluctuations are investigated within the fabric of f(R) AdS Black Hole (BH). Specifically, the Hawking evaporation process is analyzed numerically using the Stefan-Boltzmann law. The results indicate that the BH lifetime is always infinite, which means the BH becomes a remnant in the late time. Additionally, the evaporation rate depends on the AdS radius and coupling parameters. We further examined the visual properties of BH shadows observed for various values of the two parameters. The results reveal that the BH shadow radius decreases with $ψ_{0}$, while it increases with $λ$. Consequently, we further investigate the infalling accretion matter in the vicinity of BHs. The results depict that while variations in relevant parameters do influence the central region, the important factor is the change in optical appearance of the bright photon ring, which is exhibited at the position of the photon sphere. Next, we discuss many thermodynamical quantities, such as temperature, entropy, Helmholtz free energy, internal energy, corrected pressure, enthalpy, Gibbs free energy and specific heat and interpret how the variations in $λ$ and $ψ_{0}$ impact on the stability and phase transitions of the AdS BHs.

</details>


### [204] [Gravitational Waves as Thermodynamic Shear Excitations in Scalar-Tensor Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16437)
*David S. Pereira*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明，在Jordan-frame标量-张量引力（scalar-tensor gravity）中，类时标量梯度（timelike scalar gradient）定义了一个有效热力学介质。横向无迹（transverse-traceless, TT）扰动会激活局域剪切做功通道，该应力功率进入标量扇区能量平衡，且在二阶下具有规范不变性（gauge invariant）。标量-张量耦合同时控制着非广义相对论（non-GR）的张量阻尼，并为传播的自旋-2模（spin-2 mode）提供了内禀的引力热力学诠释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索标量-张量引力中，标量场梯度所定义的有效热力学介质的动力学性质，特别是引力波（gravitational wave）模与热力学量之间的耦合机制。

Method: 在Jordan-frame标量-张量引力框架下，考虑均匀无剪切背景上的 transverse-traceless 扰动，计算局域剪切做功通道 $\mathcal W_φ=π_{ab}^{(φ)}σ^{ab}$，并分析其领头阶纯TT贡献 $\mathcal P_{\rm TT}^{[1,1]} =\overline{\mathcal K\mathcal T} \dotχ_{ij}^{\rm TT}\dotχ_{\rm TT}^{ij}/4$ 的规范性质与能量平衡。

Result: 局域剪切应力功率由标量扇区提供，进入标量扇区能量平衡，且在二阶微扰论（second-order perturbation theory）下具有规范不变性。相同的标量-张量耦合出现在非GR张量阻尼项中，并在GR归一化的振幅平衡中符号相反。

Conclusion: 标量-张量引力提供了一个可控范例，其中传播的自旋-2模式获得了内禀的引力热力学诠释（intrinsically gravitational thermodynamic interpretation），且该热力学效应依赖于对能量来源的归一化选择。

Abstract: In Jordan-frame scalar--tensor gravity, a timelike scalar gradient defines an effective thermodynamic medium. We show that a transverse--traceless perturbation of a homogeneous shear-free background activates the local shear-work channel $\mathcal W_φ=π_{ab}^{(φ)}σ^{ab}$, with leading pure-TT contribution $\mathcal P_{\rm TT}^{[1,1]} =\overline{\mathcal K\mathcal T} \dotχ_{ij}^{\rm TT}\dotχ_{\rm TT}^{ij}/4$. This stress power follows from local traction mechanics, enters the scalar-sector energy balance, and is gauge invariant at second order. The same scalar--tensor coupling controls non-GR tensor damping and appears with the opposite sign in a GR-normalized amplitude balance, although its interpretation as a separate tensor-energy source is normalization dependent. Scalar--tensor gravity thus provides a controlled example in which a propagating spin-2 mode acquires an intrinsically gravitational thermodynamic interpretation.

</details>


### [205] [Biases in Tests of General Relativity from Microlensed Gravitational-Wave Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16458)
*Anirban Kopty,Apratim Ganguly,N. V. Krishnendu,Anuj Mishra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过模拟被点质量微引力透镜（microlensing）扭曲的GW150914类引力波信号，评估了微透镜效应对标准广义相对论（GR）检验的影响。结果表明，在波动光学（wave-optics）区域内，微透镜引发的波形畸变可在无任何超出GR的新物理的情况下，导致高达~4σ（一维检验）和~4.5σ（二维检验）的假阳性GR偏离信号，揭示波动光学引力透镜是当前和未来GR精密检验的重要天体物理系统误差源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）观测为强场广义相对论（general relativity, GR）检验提供了精确手段，但其可靠性依赖于准确的波形建模。未建模的物理效应可能引入系统偏差，从而模拟出偏离GR的假信号。本研究旨在评估引力波微透镜（GW microlensing）作为一种未建模效应，是否会在标准GR检验中产生虚假的偏离信号。

Method: 作者使用LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA合作组的标准GR检验框架，对GW150914类模拟信号进行贝叶斯参数估计（Bayesian parameter estimation）。信号经过质量范围为10至10⁵倍太阳质量的孤立点质量（point-mass）透镜的微透镜效应处理，且使用未考虑透镜效应的波形模板进行拟合。研究涵盖参数化检验、修正色散关系检验（modified dispersion relation test）、旋进-合并-衰荡一致性检验（inspiral-merger-ringdown consistency test, IMRCT）及其元框架（meta-IMRCT）。为统一比较不同维度的检验结果，作者引入了基于GR分位数（GR quantile）的统一GR偏离显著性统计量。

Result: 波动光学区域内，微透镜引起的波形畸变可产生显著的假性GR偏离，其中一维检验达到约4σ，二维一致性检验达到约4.5σ，尽管注入信号完全符合GR。长波长（long-wavelength）和几何光学（geometric-optics）区域的信号则基本与GR一致。此外，这些表观偏离的显著性（significance）与基于贝叶斯因子（Bayes factors）衡量的微透镜可检测性之间并无强相关性，说明GR检验探测的是全局透镜诊断（global lensing diagnostics）无法捕捉的波形投影。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了波动光学引力透镜（wave-optics gravitational lensing）是当前及未来GR精密检验中不可忽视的重要天体物理系统误差，并强调在下一代引力波分析中必须对传播效应（propagation effects）进行建模，以避免将纯粹的透镜效应误判为对GR的偏离。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave (GW) observations of compact binary mergers enable precision tests of general relativity (GR) in the strong-field regime, but their reliability depends on accurate waveform modeling. Unmodeled physical effects can induce systematic biases that mimic deviations from GR. Here we study the impact of GW microlensing on standard LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA tests of GR using GW150914-like simulated signals lensed by isolated point-mass objects with masses in the range $10-10^{5}M_\odot$. We perform Bayesian parameter estimation with unlensed waveform templates and quantify biases in parameterized tests, modified dispersion relation tests, the inspiral-merger-ringdown consistency test (IMRCT) and the meta-IMRCT framework. To compare these tests with a common discriminator, we introduce a unified GR-deviation significance statistic based on the GR quantile, applicable to both one- and multi-dimensional deviation parameters. We find that microlensing-induced waveform distortions can produce significant false deviations from GR, reaching $\sim4σ$ in one-dimensional tests and $\sim4.5σ$ in two-dimensional consistency tests, despite the injected signals being fully GR-compatible. These false deviations arise mainly in the wave-optics regime, where diffraction induces frequency-dependent amplitude and phase modulations, while signals in the long-wavelength and geometric-optics regimes remain largely consistent with GR. We also find that the significance of these apparent deviations does not correlate strongly with microlensing detectability as measured by Bayes factors, showing that GR tests probe waveform projections not captured by global lensing diagnostics. Our results establish wave-optics gravitational lensing as an important astrophysical systematic for present and future precision tests of GR and highlight the need to model propagation effects in next-generation GW analyses.

</details>


### [206] [Separating the linearized Einstein equations in Kerr](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16581)
*Jianwei Mei*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在克尔（Kerr）时空中直接分离线性化爱因斯坦方程的方法，通过结合无迹条件、Killing-Yano对称性、宇称要求和de Donder规范条件，成功推导出克尔黑洞自旋-2扰动的唯一解耦模式函数组。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克尔黑洞的线性化爱因斯坦方程长期以来难以直接分离，阻碍了对自旋-2扰动（spin-2 perturbation）的精确分析。现有方法通常依赖复杂的数学变换或近似，缺乏系统性的直接分离方案。

Method: 利用无迹条件（traceless condition）、Killing-Yano对称性（Killing-Yano symmetry）、宇称要求（parity requirement）以及de Donder规范条件（de Donder gauge condition）的组合约束，将线性化爱因斯坦方程降阶至可处理水平，进而实现方程的变量分离。

Result: 证明了扰动度规的迹（trace）服从自旋-0扰动方程，因此与自旋-2扰动无关；成功推导出一组唯一的解耦模式函数（decoupled mode functions），用于描述克尔黑洞的自旋-2扰动。

Conclusion: 该工作首次实现了克尔时空中线性化爱因斯坦方程的直接分离，为研究克尔黑洞的自旋-2扰动提供了严格且系统的数学框架。

Abstract: A direct separation of the linearized Einstein equations in Kerr is presented. The trace of the perturbed metric is found to obey the spin-0 perturbation equation and so is irrelevant for the spin-2 perturbations. By combining the traceless condition, the Killing-Yano symmetry, a parity requirement, and the de Donder gauge condition, it has been found possible to reduce the linearized Einstein equations in Kerr to a manageable level, thereby enabling the direct separation of the equations and the derivation of a unique set of decoupled mode functions for the spin-2 perturbation of the Kerr black hole.

</details>


### [207] [Regular Black Hole Formation and Gamma-Ray Burst from Matter Conversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16590)
*Vitalii Vertogradov,Zhanna Kuznetsova,Yu Shi*

TL;DR: 本文研究了重子物质坍缩为Dymnikova-Hayward-Bardeen规则黑洞（regular black holes）的过程，指出为避免中心奇点（central singularity）而形成的新物质会释放大量电磁辐射，这种辐射可作为伽马射线暴（gamma-ray bursts）的可能机制，且与观测兼容要求规则化效应（regularization effects）很小，因而此类规则黑洞与史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）差异微弱。

Method: 研究基于重子物质（baryonic matter）向Dymnikova-Hayward-Bardeen规则黑洞坍缩的物理模型，估算了由阻止奇点形成的物质组分所释放的辐射密度（radiation density）及其对应的热光度（bolometric luminosity）。

Conclusion: 规则黑洞的形成过程可能通过电磁辐射信号被观测到，并与伽马射线暴现象相联系；但观测约束使得规则黑洞在结构上几乎接近于经典的史瓦西黑洞。

Abstract: During the gravitational collapse of a massive star into a regular black hole, a new form of matter must be produced in order to prevent the formation of a central singularity. Since such matter is not present in the initial stellar configuration, it must emerge dynamically during the collapse. This formation process is expected to be accompanied by a strong release of energy in the form of electromagnetic radiation, which may be observable. Here we investigate the gravitational collapse of baryonic matter into Dymnikova-Hayward-Bardeen regular black holes. We estimate the radiation density and the corresponding bolometric luminosity generated by the formation of the matter sector responsible for singularity avoidance. We show that such processes provide a possible mechanism for gamma-ray bursts. Moreover, compatibility with gamma-ray burst requires small regularization effects. In the broader context, our findings reveal the existence of initially expanding closed models that undergo subsequent recollapse towards a future singularity, and open universes exhibiting perpetual expansion into the future. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用变形色散关系（deformed dispersion relation）来表征高阶曲率修正对光子传播的修改，并在克尔旋转背景时空下，解析推导零测地线（null trajectories）的偏转角及传播时间延迟。

Result: 修正后的传播会在偏转角和时延上产生相对于标准克尔预言的显式且可计算的偏差。这些修正对黑洞自旋（spin）具有非平凡依赖关系，且在强场区域（如光子区附近）更为显著。

Conclusion: 本工作建立了一个具体且系统的分析框架，用于量化引力透镜中标准光子传播的偏离。研究指出，相对论性像间距和时间延迟等可观测量，为在强场环境下探测引力紫外修正提供了潜在途径。

Abstract: We investigate gravitational lensing in Kerr spacetime in the presence of a modified photon propagation law arising from higher-curvature effective field theory corrections. Adopting a deformed dispersion relation, we analytically derive the deflection angle and the propagation time delay for null trajectories in a rotating background.
  We show that the modified propagation leads to explicit and calculable deviations from the standard Kerr predictions, affecting both the bending angle and the time delay. These corrections exhibit a nontrivial dependence on the black hole spin and are expected to become more relevant in the strong-field regime. In particular, near the photon region-where the spin-dependent geometry influences photon trajectories-such effects may play a role in shaping observable propagation features.
  Our results establish a concrete and systematic framework to quantify deviations from standard photon propagation in gravitational lensing. They further indicate that observables such as relativistic image separations and time delays provide a potential avenue to probe ultraviolet corrections to gravity in strong-field environments.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大质量引力扰动分析方法在奇异区间可能失效，且对于质量可变大质量引力等修正理论的扰动分析尚不完善，因此需要一种更具普适性的替代方法。

Method: 利用特征分解和矩阵微扰理论构建扰动分析框架，并将其应用于质量可变大质量引力中所有常标量Schwarzschild-(A)dS黑洞解的扰动计算。

Conclusion: 所提出的扰动分析方法在大质量引力及其修正理论中具有普适性和有效性，揭示了 β = α² 条件在张量扇区和标量扇区稳定性中的关键作用，并建立了不同参数解之间的深层几何关系。

Abstract: Based on eigendecomposition and matrix perturbation theory, we propose an alternative method for analyzing perturbations in massive gravity that is applicable to both the base theory and its various modifications. We demonstrate the validity of this approach even in seemingly singular regimes. Applying this framework to mass-varying massive gravity, we compute perturbations for all constant-scalar Schwarzschild-(A)dS black hole solutions. We show that, under the condition $β= α^2$, the tensor sector of these black holes reduces to that of general relativity, while the scalar sector remains free from tachyonic instabilities given appropriate parameter choices. A deeper relationship is also revealed between the solutions with generic parameters and those with $β= α^2$: their solution manifolds intersect at a specific locus where the perturbation vanishes.

Conclusion: 黑洞参数是轨道动力学、振荡特性与热演化的关键调节器，为通过强场天体物理现象探测非线性Kalb-Ramond引力提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: In contrast to conventional linear coupling frameworks, the proposed work investigated the nonlinear effects that become more significant in the strong field regime of a black hole. The logarithmic coupling introduces strong-field modifications to the spacetime geometry, leading to significant departures from the Schwarzschild and Reissner Nordstrom BHs. We analyze the motion of test particles using the effective potential formalism and derive the conserved energy and angular momentum for circular equatorial geodesics. The stability of circular orbits and the location of the innermost stable circular orbit are examined, revealing a strong dependence on the model parameters Q, l, and $β$. The epicyclic frequencies (radial, vertical, and azimuthal) together with the associated periastron precession demonstrate that nonlinear logarithmic corrections can substantially modify quasi periodic oscillation observables. We further investigate the Hawking temperature and energy emission rate, which show that the nonlinear coupling also impacts distinct imprints on the thermodynamic behavior and evaporation characteristics of the black hole. ### [212] [Axial Obstructions to Rotating Bumblebee Vacuum Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17223)

TL;DR: 本文识别了正则旋转常模矢量真空（regular rotating constant-norm vector vacua）存在的两类普遍性障碍：极轴处的非光滑性与曲率奇异性；并以Einstein–bumblebee引力中的Kerr-disformal解为例，证明其矢量真空在极轴上不光滑且存在真正的曲率奇异性，仅非极值分支在非极区定义了正则的局部旋转解。

Method: 从对称性继承条件（symmetry-inheriting condition）和几何分析出发，在非退化分叉面（bifurcation surface）的极点处证明矢量场必须消失，与恒定非零模长相矛盾；进一步分析沿旋转轴的锥度（conicity）变化如何导致随到轴固有距离倒数发散的奇异曲率。将这些一般性结论应用于Einstein–bumblebee引力中的三参数Kerr-disformal族解。

Conclusion: 正则旋转常模矢量真空在极轴处受到两类普遍性障碍的限制，Einstein–bumblebee引力中的Kerr-disformal解证实了这些障碍的物理实现，仅非极值分支在非极区提供正则局部解。

Abstract: We identify two general obstructions to a regular rotating constant-norm vector vacua. Firstly, at the poles of a nondegenerate bifurcation surface, horizon and axial invariance force every smooth symmetry-inheriting one-form to vanish, contradicting a strictly nonzero constant norm. Secondly, we show that a conicity varying along a rotation axis generates a singular curvature that diverges as the inverse proper distance from the axis. We apply these results to a general three parameter family Kerr-disformal solution in Einstein--bumblebee gravity. Consequently, its vector vacuum is not smooth on the axes because of a nonzero constant norm, and the position-dependent conicity leads to genuine curvature singularities on the polar axes. A distinguished nonextremal branch nevertheless admits a regular outer Killing horizon away from the axes and defines an exact local rotating solution in the nonpolar region.

The astrophysical properties of the dark matter halo directly dictate the quantum-like spectrum of scalar field configurations around the central black hole. Remarkably, the conformal coupling constant becomes discretized and is determined solely by the halo's compactness parameter.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Hořava-Lifshitz引力的领头阶宇称偶（leading parity-even）红外部截断下，研究修正的张量色散关系对引力波产生与传播的影响，并利用实际观测数据约束该理论中的自由参数α。

Method: 采用横向无迹（transverse-traceless）规范，构造修正波动方程的推迟格林函数（retarded Green function），并推导至α一阶的辐射区波形。针对准圆轨道双黑洞系统，导出偏振波形、能流、总光度及绝热啁啾演化（adiabatic chirp evolution），并将Hořava-Lifshitz系数映射到LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA的修正色散参数化方案。

Result: 得到引力波振幅、功率和频率演化的相对修正：Δh_A/h_A^GR = -8π²αf²，ΔP/P_GR = Δḟ/ḟ_GR = -16π²αf²；生成相位具有相对第三后牛顿（third post-Newtonian）贡献的频率依赖性。基于GWTC-4.0后验数据，在90%置信度下给出参数约束：-6.2×10² eV⁻² < α < 1.9×10² eV⁻²。

Conclusion: 修正后的引力波仍保留标准“加”和“叉”偏振（plus and cross polarizations），不引入偏振混合、螺旋劈裂（helicity splitting）或引力双折射（gravitational birefringence）。观测数据对α的约束表明该修正可在当前引力波探测精度下被检验。

Abstract: We investigate the generation and propagation of gravitational waves in the leading parity-even infrared truncation of Hořava-Lifshitz gravity, characterized by the modified tensor dispersion relation $ω^{2}=k^{2}+αk^{4}$. Working in the transverse-traceless sector, we show that the higher-spatial-derivative correction preserves the conventional plus and cross polarizations and introduces neither polarization mixing, helicity splitting, nor gravitational birefringence. We construct the retarded Green function of the modified wave operator and derive the radiation-zone waveform to first order in $α$. The resulting signal exhibits a frequency-dependent amplitude renormalization together with a dispersive propagation phase that accumulates over the source-observer distance. We apply the formalism to a binary black hole system in a quasi-circular orbit and obtain the polarization waveforms for an arbitrary observation direction. We further derive the corresponding energy flux, total luminosity, and adiabatic chirp evolution. In terms of the observed gravitational wave frequency $f$, the leading corrections satisfy $Δh_{A}/h_{A}^{\mathrm{GR}}=-8π^{2}αf^{2}$ and $ΔP/P_{\mathrm{GR}} =Δ\dot{f}/\dot{f}_{\mathrm{GR}} =-16π^{2}αf^{2}$, while the accumulated generation phase has the frequency dependence of a relative third post-Newtonian contribution. By mapping the Hořava-Lifshitz coefficient to the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA modified-dispersion parametrization, we obtain $-6.2\times10^{2}\,\mathrm{eV}^{-2} <α< 1.9\times10^{2}\,\mathrm{eV}^{-2}$ at $90\%$ credibility from the GWTC-4.0 posterior.

</details>


### [216] [The impact of physically motivated calibration errors on search pipeline detection parameters for broadband burst Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17439)
*Milan Wils,Brad Ratto,Jeffrey S. Kissel,Tjonnie G. F. Li,Marek J. Szczepańczyk,Gabriele Vedovato,Michele Zanolin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过解析建模与大规模注入实验，系统研究了引力波探测器标定误差对宽带爆发信号（如核塌缩超新星）探测效率的影响。结果表明，尽管标定误差会改变探测统计量，但对探测距离和爆炸能量限的影响均小于1%，在当前探测器灵敏度下影响极小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波探测器标定误差会引入频率依赖的振幅与相位误差，而现有非建模爆发搜寻（unmodelled burst search）仅采用均匀振幅缩放或常时移等近似，无法捕捉标定误差的频率依赖结构。该局限对于核塌缩超新星（core-collapse supernovae）等问题尤为突出，因其信号占据宽频带且具有复杂的时频形态。

Method: 结合解析建模与大规模注入实验（injection campaigns）。首先推导一阶估计（first-order estimates），量化频率依赖的振幅与相位误差对相干网络信噪比（coherent network SNR）和相关系数（correlation coefficient）等探测统计量的影响；随后通过注入实验验证理论预测。

Result: 解析计算预测：相干网络SNR的相对影响随信号强度增大而趋于渐近值；相关系数在探测阈值附近受影响最显著，在高信噪比下被完全压制。注入实验证实标定误差确实改变探测统计量，但主要贡献来自事件所选取时频像素数的间接变化。在所有测试波形下，基于距离的探测效率差异小于1%，爆炸能量限（explosion-energy limits）仍由天体物理不确定性主导。

Conclusion: 在当前探测器灵敏度下，实际标定误差对宽带引力波爆发信号的可探测性影响极小。标定误差对参数估计的影响留待未来研究。

Abstract: Imperfections in the calibration of gravitational wave observatories introduce frequency dependent amplitude and phase errors on the measured GW signal. Previous unmodelled burst searches have approximated these effects using prescriptions such as a uniform amplitude rescaling or a constant time shift, which do not capture the frequency-dependent structure of calibration errors. This limitation is problematic for core-collapse supernovae, whose predicted GW signals occupy a wide frequency band and exhibit complex time-frequency morphology. In this work, we investigate how realistic calibration errors affect burst search pipelines by combining analytical modelling with large-scale injection campaigns. First-order estimates are derived to quantify how frequency-dependent amplitude and phase errors influence detection statistics such as the coherent network SNR and the correlation coefficient. These calculations predict that the relative impact on the coherent network SNR scales with the signal strength until it reaches an asymptotic value. The effect on the correlation coefficient is most pronounced near the detection threshold and is entirely suppressed at high SNR ratio. Injection studies confirm that calibration errors do modify the detection statistics, but show that the dominant contribution arises indirectly through changes in the number of time-frequency pixels selected in an event. Despite these measurable variations, detection efficiencies as a function of distance differ by less than one percent across all tested waveforms, and explosion-energy limits remain dominated by astrophysical uncertainties rather than calibration uncertainty. These results demonstrate that, at current detector sensitivity, realistic calibration errors have minimal impact on the detectability of broadband GW burst signals. The impact of calibration errors on parameter estimation is left for future work.

</details>


### [217] [Shadow of the generalized Vaidya black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17483)
*Vitalii Vertogradov,Ali Övgün*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了由Husain解描述的广义Vaidya黑洞的阴影（shadow）。通过将其转化为共形静态形式并导出零测地线有效势，分析了状态方程参数α对阴影大小的影响；随后针对时变情况推导了准静态慢演化方程，发现阴影的增大或收缩由光子区域（photon region）内的局部有效流入决定，而非由质量变化率Ṁ和电荷变化率Ṉ的单独符号决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义Vaidya黑洞作为更一般的时变黑洞解，其阴影特性尚未被充分理解；特别是状态方程参数α如何影响阴影大小，以及随时间演化时阴影变化的驱动因素仍不清楚。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 首先对Husain解假设正压状态方程（barotropic equation of state），识别出允许齐次收缩 Killing 矢量（homothetic Killing vector）的自相似类（self-similar class），并将几何变换为共形静态形式（conformally static form）。由此导出共形静态代表中的零测地线有效势，确定齐次光子表面（homothetic photon surface），再变换回原始广义Vaidya坐标。对于时变情况，推导了瞬时光子表面（instantaneous photon surface）和临界碰撞参数（critical impact parameter）的准静态慢演化方程。

Result: 在弱能量条件（weak-energy-condition）分支下，参数α控制阴影相对于标准Vaidya情况的缩放：0≤α<1/2分支使光子球（photon-sphere）和阴影半径增大，而1/2<α≤1分支使其减小。对于时变情况，阴影的增大或收缩由光子区域局部的有效流入（local effective influx）主导，而非由Ṁ和Ṉ各自的符号单独决定；对于类电荷分支，给出了吸积增大阴影与电荷快速增长导致阴影收缩的清晰判据。

Conclusion: 广义Vaidya黑洞的阴影大小显著依赖于状态方程参数α；时变演化中，局部有效流入是决定阴影变化的关键物理量。这些结果增进了对时变黑洞阴影动力学的理解，为未来观测上识别此类黑洞提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the shadow of the generalized Vaidya black hole described by the Husain solution. Assuming a barotropic equation of state for the additional matter sector, we first identify the self-similar class admitting a homothetic Killing vector and transform the geometry to a conformally static form. This allows us to derive the effective potential for null geodesics in the conformally static representative, determine the corresponding homothetic photon surface, and then transform the result back to the original generalized Vaidya coordinates. We show that, within the weak-energy-condition branches, the parameter $α$ controlling the equation of state determines whether the shadow is enlarged or reduced relative to the Vaidya case: the branch $0\leqα<1/2$ increases the photon-sphere and shadow radii, whereas the branch $1/2<α\leq 1$ decreases them. We then turn to the genuinely time-dependent Husain metric and derive quasistatic slow-evolution equations for the instantaneous photon surface and critical impact parameter. In particular, we show that the growth or contraction of the shadow is governed by the local effective influx in the photon region rather than by the signs of $\dot M$ and $\dot N$ separately. For the charge-like branch, this yields a transparent criterion for when accretion enlarges the shadow and when rapid charge growth instead causes it to shrink.

TL;DR: 本文研究协变量子黑洞（covariant quantum BH）在不同自旋粒子蒸发下的行为，发现其霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）和质量损失率与史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild BH）不同，且依赖于发射粒子的自旋，表明仅考虑无质量标量场情况可能不足，并为未来检验圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）提供了可能途径。

Method: 本文研究了协变量子黑洞对于不同自旋（spin）粒子的蒸发过程，并将其结果与史瓦西黑洞的情形进行对比分析。

Result: 协变量子黑洞的霍金辐射和质量损失率与史瓦西黑洞存在差异，并且这些量依赖于所发射粒子的自旋。

Conclusion: 仅考虑无质量标量场（massless scalar field）情况下的黑洞蒸发可能是不充分的；上述结果为未来检验圈量子引力理论提供了可能的实验途径。

Abstract: A growing number of phenomena and theoretical problems indicate that quantum gravity theory is necessary. In this paper, we investigate the evaporation of covariant quantum BHs for particles with different spins and compare the results with the Schwarzschild case. Our results show that the Hawking radiation and mass loss rate of covariant quantum BHs differ from those of Schwarzschild BHs and they depend on the spins of the emitted particles. Therefore, these results suggest that it may be insufficient to consider only BH evaporation in the massless scalar field case and may provide a possible way to test loop quantum gravity in the future.

### [219] [Massive Compact Stars Beyond the General Relativity Limit in Finslerian Gravity: A Possible Explanation for the GW190814 Secondary](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17609)

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究在芬斯勒几何引力（Finslerian gravity）框架下，利用Heintzmann IIa引力势构建各向异性致密星模型，发现该模型可将致密星最大质量提升至约2.67倍太阳质量，为GW190814事件中质量处于中子星与黑洞质量间隙（mass gap）内的超质量致密天体提供了一种理论解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论（general relativity）预言致密星存在上限质量，而LIGO-Virgo合作组发现的GW190814事件中，一个质量为2.5–2.67倍太阳质量的致密天体引发了关于中子星最大质量与黑洞最小质量之间是否存在质量间隙（mass gap）的激烈争论。这一观测对传统恒星模型构成挑战，促使研究者探索修改引力理论是否能在不诉诸黑洞形成的前提下容纳此类超质量致密天体。

Method: 在芬斯勒几何引力（Finslerian gravity）框架下，采用Heintzmann IIa引力势，假设线性状态方程（linear equation of state），构建了一类物理上可行的各向异性（anisotropic）致密星模型。通过分析质量-半径关系、转动惯量-质量关系等关键天体物理可观测量，并与广义相对论（GR）对应结果进行详细比较，同时利用稳定性判据对模型的物理可行性进行严格检验。

Result: 该模型能够将致密星最大质量显著提升至约2.67倍太阳质量，为GW190814的次组分这类超质量致密天体提供了一种合理解释。此外，模型预测的转动惯量（moment of inertia）增大，表明更强的转动支持和内部质量分布的重新排列。

Conclusion: 芬斯勒几何引力修正下的各向异性致密星模型可以容纳超出广义相对论预言上限质量的致密天体，为GW190814事件中处于质量间隙内的候选天体提供了可能的理论解释，表明修改引力理论可能是理解超质量致密星物理性质的重要途径。

Abstract: The existence of an upper mass limit for compact stars is one of the fundamental predictions of general relativity (GR), with important implications for the outcome of compact binary mergers and the nature of the proposed neutron star black hole mass gap. The LIGO Virgo collaboration announced the discovery of a compact binary merger, GW190814, containing a compact star with mass 2.5 to 2.67 $M_\odot$ [R. Abbott et al.(2020) ApJ Lett., 896, L44], which provided an exciting new stimulus to the ongoing debate on whether a gap exists between the maximum mass of NS and the minimum mass of black hole. Such GW detection has also challenged conventional stellar models and renewed interest in exploring whether modified theories of gravity can accommodate such ultra-massive compact objects without invoking black hole formation. The present work investigated the structure and physical properties of compact stars within the framework of Finslerian gravity, employing the Heintzmann IIa gravitational potentials and showed that the our model can substantially enhance the maximum mass of compact stars upto $2.67 M_{\odot}$, thereby offering a plausible explanation for massive compact objects such as the secondary component of GW190814. In addition, the moment of inertia is found to increase, indicating stronger rotational support and a redistribution of the internal mass profile. The analysis focuses on key astrophysical observables, including the mass radius and moment of inertia mass relations, and a detailed comparison with the GR counterpart is performed. Assuming a linear equation of state, we construct a class of physically viable anisotropic stellar models and analyze their behavior under the influence of Finslerian corrections. The physical viability of the model is rigorously tested through stability criteria.
