Abstract: This study investigates the dynamical behavior of particle's test around a spinning charged Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton (EMd) quantum corrected black hole (QCBH) by examining the effects of spinning parameter $a$, quantum correction parameter $b$, and charge parameter $Q$. Using EMd spacetime geometry, we analyze the effective potential and effective force to determine the stability and structure of the circular orbits in a strong gravitational field. Furthermore, we calculate the oscillation frequencies radial $(Ω_r)$, vertical $(Ω_θ)$, and angular $(Ω_φ)$, as well as the corresponding Periapsis and Lense-Thirring precession frequencies. The spin parameter primarily determines the spinning properties of spacetime, while the quantum correction and charge particle introduce additional biases to Kerr-Newman geometry, particularly near the event horizon. These corrections alter the position and stability of the circular orbits, and the spectrum effectively associates with particle's motion. ### [221] [Angular momentum flux through post-Newtonian order for noncircular nonspinning black-hole binaries in Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17887)
*Qi Tan,Peng-Cheng Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量（Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton）理论框架下，首次计算了无自旋双黑洞系统在非圆轨道上的瞬时角动量流（instantaneous angular momentum flux），精度达到后牛顿第一阶（first post-Newtonian order）；分别给出了标量、电磁和张量三种通道的贡献，并验证了已知的准圆平衡关系、广义相对论极限以及偶极抑制极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论（全息对偶的重要背景）中研究双黑洞的角动量辐射，是理解该理论下轨道演化（orbital evolution）和波形相位（waveform phasing）的关键步骤。此前能量流（energy flux）已知，但角动量流尚缺，而后者是计算偏心率轨道长期演化的必需耗散信息。

Method: 在爱因斯坦（Einstein）框架下，采用松弛场方程的直接积分方法（direct integration of the relaxed field equations approach）构造波区（wave zone）的标量、电磁和张量引力场；在质心系（center-of-mass frame）中表达所需的源多极矩（source multipole moments）；同时保留波区场中的领先阶 $1/R$ 辐射场和描述有限距离修正的次领先阶 $1/R^2$ 项（不贡献于零无穷远处的通量）。

Result: 分别获得了角动量流中标量、电磁和张量通道的显式表达式。标量和电磁通道以偶极辐射（dipole radiation）为首项，张量通道以四极辐射（quadrupole order）为首项。结果恢复了准圆平衡关系（quasicircular balance relation）、已知的广义相对论极限以及预期的标量和电磁偶极抑制极限（dipole suppression limits）。

Conclusion: 本研究与先前已知的能量流共同构成了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量理论中双黑洞耗散演化的完整信息，为未来研究该理论下的轨道平均偏心率演化（orbit-averaged eccentric evolution）和波形相位提供了必要的理论工具。

Abstract: We compute the instantaneous angular momentum flux from nonspinning black hole binaries in Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton theory for generic noncircular orbits up to relative first post-Newtonian order. Working in the Einstein frame and using the direct integration of the relaxed field equations approach, we construct the scalar, electromagnetic, and tensor gravitational fields in the wave zone and express the required source multipole moments in the center-of-mass frame. In addition to the leading $1/R$ radiative fields, we retain the next-to-leading $1/R^2$ terms in the wave-zone fields, which describe finite-distance corrections and do not contribute to the flux at null infinity. We obtain separately the scalar, electromagnetic, and tensor contributions to the angular momentum flux. The scalar and electromagnetic channels begin with dipole radiation, while the tensor channel begins at quadrupole order. Our results recover the quasicircular balance relation, the known general-relativistic limit, and the expected scalar- and electromagnetic-dipole suppression limits. Together with the previously known energy flux, these results provide the dissipative information required for future studies of orbit-averaged eccentric evolution and waveform phasing in Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton theory.

### [222] [Defocusing dark energy: Raychaudhuri diagnostics beyond $w<-1/3$ and the phantom divide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18008)
*Özgür Akarsu,Antonio De Felice,N. Merve Uzun*

TL;DR: 本文指出在广义相对论中，宇宙加速由总主动引力质量密度为负（ρ+3p<0）导致；对于符号改变的暗能量（如ΛsCDM），传统的状态方程参数w=p/ρ在ρ=0处发散，应改用正则零能条件边界I=ρ+p和Raychaudhuri排斥条件M=ρ+3p作为诊断工具，并证明在密度过零点处w会形成一个具有普适残差的运动学极点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上使用状态方程参数w≡p/ρ来诊断宇宙加速（w<-1/3），但该方法在ρ=0时无法定义，且当ρ<0时不等式方向反转。对于符号改变的暗能量（dark energy），需要一套不依赖于密度符号的正则诊断工具。

Method: 基于广义相对论中的Raychaudhuri方程，重新定义两个分支无关的组合量：I_de=ρ_de+p_de（正则零能条件边界）和M_de=ρ_de+3p_de（主动引力质量密度）。对一个单独守恒且在红移z†处发生有限奇数阶光滑负-正密度交叉的暗能量扇区，解析推导了这些量的符号行为以及w_de的运动学极点结构。

Result: 证明在密度过零点附近，I_de和M_de为负且在过零点非正，而w_de出现运动学极点，其残差为普适值n(1+z†)/3。若M_de在高红移处为正，连续性要求至少存在一个排斥边界z_rep>z†；此时扇区在ρ_de<0时已呈现排斥性。在单脉冲和驻点假设下，减速参数具有一个或三个变号零点。

Conclusion: 建议晚期宇宙学的推断应围绕(ρ,p,I,M)四元组展开，而非仅依赖w。ΛsCDM光滑剖面、指数红外f(T)模型以及最小幻影膜（minimal phantom brane）等实例验证了上述结论。

Abstract: In general relativity, cosmic acceleration is timelike defocusing of the comoving congruence and requires a negative total active gravitational mass density, $\mathcal{M}_{\rm tot}=ρ_{\rm tot}+3p_{\rm tot}<0$. The criterion $w\equiv p/ρ<-1/3$ diagnoses sector repulsion only for $ρ>0$: the inequality reverses for $ρ<0$, and ratio variables are ill-defined at $ρ=0$ even when the stress-energy tensor is finite. For sign-changing effective dark energy (DE), as in $Λ_{\rm s}$CDM-type histories, we instead use the signed density $ρ_{\rm de}$ and two branch-independent combinations. The regular null energy condition (NEC) boundary $\mathcal{I}_{\rm de}=ρ_{\rm de}+p_{\rm de}=0$ replaces the phantom divide $w_{\rm de}=-1$, while $\mathcal{M}_{\rm de}=ρ_{\rm de}+3p_{\rm de}<0$ governs sector-level Raychaudhuri repulsion. For a separately conserved DE sector with a smooth negative-to-positive density crossing of finite odd order $n$ at $z_\dagger$, we prove that $\mathcal{I}_{\rm de}$ and $\mathcal{M}_{\rm de}$ are negative in a punctured neighborhood and non-positive at the crossing, while $w_{\rm de}$ develops a kinematic pole with universal residue $n(1+z_\dagger)/3$. If $\mathcal{M}_{\rm de}>0$ at some sufficiently high redshift, continuity requires at least one repulsion boundary $z_{\rm rep}>z_\dagger$: the sector is already repulsive while $ρ_{\rm de}<0$. We derive the exact range of $ρ_{\rm de}'(z_\dagger)$ for acceleration at the crossing with the total NEC satisfied. Under the stated single-impulse and stationary-point assumptions, the deceleration parameter has one or three sign-changing zeros. A smooth $Λ_{\rm s}$CDM profile, an exponential infrared $f(T)$ model, and the minimal phantom brane illustrate the results. These results motivate organizing late-time inference around $(ρ,p,\mathcal{I},\mathcal{M})$ rather than around $w$ alone.

</details>


### [223] [Post-Newtonian Global Conservation Laws in the Presence of Sensitive Bodies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18145)
*Timothy Clifton,Asta Heinesen,Oliver Pitt*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文扩展了参数化后牛顿（PPN）框架下的半保守与完全保守引力理论概念，使其涵盖受局域环境影响的致密天体（即违背强等效原理的情形），证明了在此类灵敏度存在时全局守恒量仍可存在，并给出了相应的守恒量显式形式以及PPN度规系数的新写法；通过与标量-张量引力理论中已知结果的对比，验证了该方法的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在参数化后牛顿（parameterized post-Newtonian, PPN）框架下，全局守恒定律对动力学计算和参数赋予物理意义至关重要。现有半保守与完全保守引力理论的概念尚未涵盖那些违背强等效原理（strong equivalence principle）、致密天体受局域环境灵敏度影响的场景，因此需要对该理论框架进行扩展。

Method: 通过将半保守与完全保守引力理论的概念扩展至包含对局域环境敏感的致密天体（即灵敏度效应），研究在此类系统中全局守恒量是否存在，并在存在时推导其显式形式；同时识别当引力理论允许存在守恒量且包含灵敏体时，PPN度规系数的新表述方式。

Result: 研究发现，在存在灵敏度效应的条件下，全局守恒量仍然可能存在，并给出了这些守恒量的显式形式；此外，提出了当理论允许守恒量且存在灵敏体时PPN度规系数的新写法。

Conclusion: 通过将所得结果与标量-张量引力理论（scalar-tensor theories of gravity）中的已知结果进行对比，证明了该扩展方法的适用性。

Abstract: The parameterized post-Newtonian (PPN) approach is the state of the art formalism for performing theory independent tests of weak-field gravity, and for constraining possible deviations from Einstein's theory. Within this framework, global conservation laws are useful for the calculation of dynamics and for giving meaning to parameters. In this paper we extend the concept of semi-conservative and fully-conservative theories of gravity to include situations in which compact astrophysical bodies are modeled as masses that are sensitive to their local environment, as relevant for theories that violate the strong equivalence principle. We find that globally conserved quantities can still exist in the presence of such sensitivities, and find their explicit forms when they do. We identify new ways of writing the coefficients that enter into the PPN metric when a theory of gravity admits conserved quantities in the presence of a sensitive body, and demonstrate the applicability of our approach by comparing it to known results in scalar-tensor theories of gravity.

### [224] [Search for continuous gravitational waves from the pulsar J0435+3233](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18219)
*Brian McGloughlin,Jing Ming,Maria Alessandra Papa,Kartikey Sharma,Reinhard Prix,Benjamin Steltner,Heinz-Bernd Eggenstein,Na Wang,Jianping Yuan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用LIGO O4a公开数据对毫秒脉冲星J0435+3233进行连续引力波（continuous gravitational waves）搜索，目标频率为两倍自转频率及其窄带以及r模（r-modes）信号。结果未探测到信号，在95%置信水平上给出的最严格本征引力波振幅上限比自旋下降极限（spin-down limit）低约14倍，并首次将源椭圆度（ellipticity）约束在$10^{-8}$量级的物理感兴趣范围内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: J0435+3233是毫秒脉冲星中具有异常大自旋下降率（spin-down）的特殊天体，其自旋下降率超过了$10^{-12}$ Hz/s，是亚10 ms自旋周期范围内首个达到该量级的脉冲星，因此被认定为连续引力波的潜在强源。此前尚无对该源进行系统引力波搜索的研究。

Method: 使用LIGO O4a公开数据开展搜索，目标信号包括：(1) 精确两倍自转频率；(2) 该频率附近的窄带；(3) 对应r模的信号。分析采用标准连续引力波搜索统计方法，并设定95%置信水平的上限。

Result: 搜索结果为非探测（non-detection）。在95%置信水平上，本征引力波振幅上限比自旋下降极限低约14倍。结合估计源距离1.2 kpc，该上限排除了椭圆度大于$10^{-8}$量级的可能性。

Conclusion: 本文是首个以超过一个数量级的幅度超越自旋下降极限，并将椭圆度约束到$10^{-8}$低量级物理感兴趣范围的研究。这一结果显著提升了对J0435+3233引力波辐射潜力的理解，也为未来连续引力波搜索提供了重要参考。

Abstract: We perform a search for continuous gravitational waves from J0435+3233 using LIGO O4a public data. J0435+3233 is unique among millisecond pulsars as it exhibits an exceptionally large spin-down and marks the first pulsar observed to date with a spin-down larger than $10^{-12}$ Hz/s in the sub $10$ ms spin period range, making it a potentially strong source of continuous gravitational waves. We target signals at exactly twice the rotation frequency, a narrow band around this frequency, and also signals corresponding to r-modes. Our results are consistent with a non-detection. Our most stringent upper limit on the intrinsic gravitational wave amplitude is $h_0=\targetedULninetyfive$, at the 95\% confidence level, which is a factor of $\approx14$ times lower than the spin-down limit. With an estimated source distance of $1.2$ kpc our upper limit on the gravitational wave amplitude excludes source ellipticities greater than $\targetedellipULninetyfive$, making this the first source for which the spin-down upper limit is beaten by over an order of magnitude {\it{and}} the ellipticity is constrained to a physically interesting range, in the low $10^{-8}$ region.

Method: 采用扫描隧道显微镜（STM）对单晶Si(5 5 7)晶圆上制备的三重台阶周期阵列进行实验研究，并对原子级分辨数据做详细结构分析。

Abstract: Scanning tunneling microscopy studies of periodic arrays of triple steps fabricated on single-crystalline Si(5 5 7) wafers demonstrate several possible atomic structures of consecutive steps and Si(1 1 1) terraces maintaining the same periodicity on micrometer-sized surface areas. Detailed analysis of the atomically resolved data reveals the formation of Si(8 8 11) triple-step staircase with a period of 18b=5.99 nm in projection onto the terrace plane, where b=0.333 nm is the distance between atomic rows for the Si(1 1 1)1x1 surface. Schematic models for several possible configurations of either 7x7 or 5x5-reconstructed terraces and triple steps are proposed.

### [226] [Valley polarization, Rashba interaction, and weak altermagnetism in inversion-asymmetric MnPS$_\text{3}|$WS$_\text{2}$ van der Waals heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16454)
*Purba Dutta,Soumajyoti Bid,Nirmal Ganguli*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 基于第一性原理计算，本文研究了MnPS₃/WS₂范德华异质结，发现其兼具交变磁性（altermagnetism）、Rashba自旋劈裂、自旋-谷锁定（spin-valley locking）和谷极化（valley polarization）等多种新兴现象，且能带对齐和电子结构可通过外电场和双轴应变在type-I与type-II之间高效调控，为自旋电子学和谷电子学提供了高度可调的二维平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋电子学和谷电子学领域需要兼具强可调性和丰富物理效应的新型材料平台。近年来，反铁磁体中对称性破缺以及非磁体系中Rashba效应分别诱导出多种有趣现象，但将这些效应集成于同一二维异质结构中并实现协同调控仍待探索。

Method: 采用基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）的第一性原理计算方法，对具有P对称性的MnPS₃单层与WS₂单层构成的范德华异质结进行电子结构和磁性质计算。

Result: 该异质结同时表现出交变磁性、Rashba自旋劈裂、自旋-谷锁定和谷极化；具有约1.65 eV的直接带隙和type-I能带对齐；通过外加电场和面内双轴应变，能带对齐可在type-I与type-II之间可逆调节，并显著调控交变磁性和谷劈裂。

Conclusion: 提出的MnPS₃/WS₂范德华异质结是一个高度可调的多功能平台，在自旋电子学（spintronics）和谷电子学（valleytronics）应用中具有重要潜力。

Abstract: The deliberate breaking of inversion ($\mathcal{P}$) symmetry in antiferromagnets has recently emerged as an effective means to induce various features, such as the emergence of Berry curvature, spin-valley locking, magnetoelectric coupling, and the transition from conventional antiferromagnetism to altermagnetism. Conversely, in non-magnetic systems, inversion symmetry breaking in the presence of strong spin-orbit interaction (SOI) gives rise to momentum-dependent spin splitting via the Rashba effect, enabling tunable spin polarization through external electric fields. Motivated by recent advances in two-dimensional materials, we perform first-principles calculations based on density functional theory to investigate the van der Waals (vdW) heterostructure formed by a $\mathcal{P}$-symmetric MnPS$_3$ monolayer and a WS$_2$ monolayer. We demonstrate that the interface hosts a rich interplay of emergent phenomena, including an altermagnetic phase, Rashba spin splitting, spin-valley locking, and valley polarization. Our results demonstrate that the heterostructure exhibits semiconducting behavior with a direct band gap of approximately 1.65~eV and a type-I band alignment. Remarkably, the electronic structure and band alignment can be effectively tuned between type-I and type-II regimes via an external electric field and in-plane biaxial strain. Furthermore, field-induced modulation enables strong control over the altermagnetic phase and the valley splitting. These findings establish the proposed vdW heterostructure as a highly tunable platform with significant potential for spintronic and valleytronic applications.

### [227] [Bond reconstruction and vacancy clustering in monolayer silicon carbide from first principles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16483)
*Péter Udvarhelyi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过密度泛函理论（density functional theory）研究单层碳化硅中空位及其聚集体的键重构机制，发现键重构对缺陷的稳定性、电子结构和光学性质有决定性影响，并提出一种新型红外色心候选缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解空位相关结构中键重构（bond reconstruction）对形成能、对称性及光电性质的影响机制，这对于二维碳化硅中缺陷的量子特性调控具有重要意义。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory）进行第一性原理计算，并使用多种键描述符（bond descriptors）分析单空位和空位聚集体中的面内重构（in-plane reconstruction）和面外畸变（out-of-plane distortion）。

Result: 孤立单空位同时经历面内重构和面外畸变，共同决定其稳定性和电子结构；键重构是紧凑空位聚集体的关键稳定机制；碳单空位中的重构抑制了光学活性；由三个碳空位围绕一个硅空位组成的高度稳定聚集体具有三重态基态（triplet ground state）和有利的发射声子边带德拜-沃勒因子（Debye-Waller factor），可作为近红外色心候选。

Conclusion: 键重构在定义二维碳化硅中空位缺陷的量子特性中起关键作用，特别是可调控光学活性并产生有前景的量子发射体候选结构。

Abstract: Bond reconstruction in vacancy-related structures affects their formation energies, symmetries, and electronic and optical properties. Using density functional theory, we investigate bond reconstruction mechanisms of monovacancies and vacancy aggregates in monolayer silicon carbide. Multiple bond descriptors reveal that isolated monovacancies undergo both in-plane reconstruction and out-of-plane distortion, which together shape their stability and electronic structure. For compact vacancy aggregates, we show that bond reconstruction acts as a key stabilization mechanism. However, in carbon monovacancy, reconstruction suppresses optical activity. In contrast, a highly stable aggregate composed of three carbon vacancies surrounding a silicon vacancy emerges as a promising infrared color-center candidate, combining a triplet ground state with a favorable Debye-Waller factor of the emission. These results highlight the role of bond reconstruction in defining the quantum properties of vacancy defects in two-dimensional silicon carbide.

### [228] [Instability-Avoiding Active Learning for Cluster Expansions in Complex Multielement Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16486)
*Michael J. Waters,James M. Rondinelli*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将稳定性分类（stability classification）集成到主动学习（active learning）工作流中的方法，用于自动避免对动力学不稳定结构进行昂贵的计算，从而降低团簇展开（cluster expansion）在多主元合金（multi-principal element alloys, MPEAs）中训练的代价。该方法通过基于马氏距离（Mahalanobis distance）的结构选择策略增强训练集多样性，并在Ni-Fe-Cr-Al-Ti-Si合金体系的FCC MPEA上进行了验证。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文将稳定性分类（stability classification）嵌入主动学习（active learning）工作流中，使算法能够自主判断并跳过动力学不稳定的晶体结构，从而避免生成不适用的训练数据。同时，采用基于马氏距离（Mahalanobis distance）的结构选择策略，通过增强训练集的多样性来确保模型鲁棒性（robustness）。

Result: 在Ni-Fe-Cr-Al-Ti-Si合金体系的FCC（面心立方）MPEA上进行了基准测试。该体系中仅Ni和Al在热力学上以FCC结构稳定存在，其他组元可能引入动力学不稳定区域。实验表明，所提出的工作流能够有效规避不稳定结构的计算，同时通过马氏距离（Mahalanobis distance）结构选择提升了模型鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 集成稳定性分类与主动学习的工作流能够在不牺牲模型准确性的前提下，显著减少因动力学不稳定结构导致的无效训练数据，从而降低团簇展开（cluster expansion）在复杂MPEA成分空间中的训练成本。该方法为高效探索广阔且多不稳定的合金成分空间提供了可行方案。

Abstract: The high efficiency of cluster expansions make them appealing for studying chemical disorder in complex composition spaces such as in multi-principal element alloys (MPEAs). Several works have attempted to address the rapidly growing training cost with number of chemical species through active learning, transfer learning, and chemical embedding. However, many composition spaces have large regions where the host lattice becomes dynamical unstable, which are often avoided a priori so as to not generate expensive but inapplicable training data. Here, we demonstrate a procedure for integrating stability classification within an active learning workflow to autonomously avoid calculations for unstable structures. Our workflow augments the stability classification procedure with Mahalanobis distance-based structure selection to ensure model robustness by training set diversification. We benchmark our methods by training a cluster expansion for the complex FCC MPEA spanning the Ni-Fe-Cr-Al-Ti-Si alloy space, in which only Ni and Al are thermodynamically stable as FCC

</details>


### [229] [Phase nucleation and evolution pathways of a nanostructured Inconel 725 alloy during heat treatment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16495)
*Ruqing Cao,Ikponmwosa J. Iyinbor,Andrea M. Hodge,Timothy J. Rupert*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过系统研究溅射Inconel 725薄膜在不同热处理条件下的相选择与偏析行为，揭示了初始纳米孪晶缺陷结构能够主导相变路径：低温直接时效促进δ相在孪晶界析出，抑制γ'/γ"强化相；高温固溶处理消除纳米孪晶后，δ相减少且集中于晶界，实现γ'/γ"相与δ相的空间分离，从而协同提升沉淀强化与晶粒稳定化，硬度接近9 GPa。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理气相沉积（physical vapor deposition）可制备具有独特缺陷结构的纳米超合金，但其相演化路径与传统加工合金存在显著差异。本研究旨在系统探究固溶与时效处理对初始均匀柱状纳米孪晶（nanotwinned）结构的溅射Inconel 725薄膜中相选择与偏析行为的影响。

Method: 对具有均匀柱状纳米孪晶结构的溅射Inconel 725薄膜分别进行低温直接时效处理和高温固溶处理，随后进行时效处理，利用显微组织观察与硬度测试系统表征不同热处理条件下的相析出、元素偏析及微观结构演化。

Result: 低温直接时效促进δ相在孪晶界与富缺陷区大量析出，消耗γ基体中的Nb，抑制γ'/γ"相析出；高温固溶处理通过再结晶（recrystallization）消除纳米孪晶结构，显著减少δ相析出并增加Nb的有效性，使γ'/γ"相在细化γ基体（<1 μm）内以超细球状析出。后续时效驱动γ'/γ"相由球状向透镜状演化，δ析出集中于晶界，实现γ'/γ"相与δ相的空间分离，硬度达约9 GPa。

Conclusion: 初始缺陷结构（如纳米孪晶）可为相选择与析出路径提供模板，通过调控热处理制度实现空间分离的多相协同强化，为纳米超合金的微观组织调控与性能优化提供策略。

Abstract: Physical vapor deposition enables the fabrication of nanostructured superalloys with unique defect architectures, yet their phase evolution pathways can differ significantly from those of conventionally processed alloys. In this study, the effects of solution and aging treatments on phase selection and segregation behavior in sputtered Inconel 725 films with an initially uniform columnar nanotwinned structure were systematically investigated. Direct aging at relatively low temperatures promoted extensive δ-phase precipitation at twin boundaries and defect-rich regions, which depleted Nb from the γ matrix and suppressed γ'/γ" precipitation. In contrast, high-temperature solution treatment induced recrystallization and eliminated the nanotwinned structure, significantly reducing δ-phase precipitation and increasing Nb availability to enable the formation of ultrafine spherical γ'/γ" precipitates within a refined γ matrix (<1 μm). Subsequent aging treatments promoted elemental partitioning and drove the morphological evolution of γ'/γ" precipitates from spherical to lenticular forms, while δ precipitation became increasingly concentrated along grain boundaries. This spatial separation of intragranular γ'/γ" and grain-boundary δ phases enabled simultaneous precipitation strengthening and grain stabilization, resulting in hardness values approaching 9 GPa. As a whole, this study demonstrates that the initial templates provided by defect structures can govern phase selection and precipitation pathways, providing a strategy for tailoring microstructure and achieving synergistic strengthening in nanostructured superalloys.

</details>


### [230] [Signal amplification in simple metal-insulator transition devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16566)

Method: 采用金属-绝缘体转变（metal-insulator transition）材料制成的简单两端器件（two-terminal device），将其工作在相变边缘（verge of the phase transition），利用负微分电阻（negative differential resistance）效应实现信号放大。通过调节直流偏置（DC bias）、交流激发（AC excitation）、串联电阻和温度等实验参数控制放大行为。

Conclusion: 本工作建立了在非线性电子材料中开发和优化类轴突放大功能的框架，为人工神经元与类轴突器件的直接集成开辟了新可能。

Abstract: Signal dissipation in large-scale neural networks can lead to information loss and ultimately to computational failures, necessitating local signal amplification at neuron - synapse connections. In biological nervous systems, axons are responsible for local signal amplification. Translating axon functionality into hardware, i.e., the ability to amplify and transmit signals without loss, is non-trivial because emulating the human brain implies building networks composed of ~10 billion interconnected neurons, each requiring a dedicated compact and scalable amplifier. Here, we demonstrate signal amplification in simple two-terminal devices made of a metal-insulator transition material. By operating the devices on the verge of the phase transition and taking advantage of negative differential resistance, we achieve robust signal amplification up to a factor of ~11.5. We also demonstrate the amplification of spiking sequences generated by a real neuristor, opening new exciting opportunities for the direct integration of artificial neurons and axons. The amplification can be controlled by easily adjustable experimental parameters, including DC bias, AC excitation, series resistance, and temperature. We further propose a model that predicts the gain using readily observable transport characteristics. Our results establish a framework for developing and optimizing axon-like amplification functionalities in nonlinear electronic materials.

Abstract: Organic mixed ionic electronic conductors (OMIECs) are a promising class of polymer materials for applications spanning neuromorphic computation to energy efficient electronics and bioelectronics. Despite being highly tunable, the relationship between structural features and key performance properties such as charge carrier mobility is poorly understood. Scanning nanodiffraction in the transmission electron microscope (TEM) is a powerful probe for elucidating this structure-property relationship, but produces large, noisy datasets that are difficult to interpret because polymer reflections exhibit several distinct morphologies. To address the complexity, we trained a machine learning (ML) model to detect these polymer diffraction peaks and their intensities from synthetic data. Compared to correlative peak detection algorithms, the conventional method for analyzing nanobeam 4D scanning transmission electron microscopy (4DSTEM) data, we show that the ML model is significantly faster and outperforms correlative algorithms in almost all cases, opening up the possibility of near-live visualization of 4DSTEM experiments.

### [232] [Ordinary Disordered Materials Can Carry Hyperuniform Physical Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16579)
*Liyu Zhong,Haina Wang,Yang Jiao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文证明，即使是结构上非超均匀（nonhyperuniform）的无序材料，其物理场（如电荷、束缚电流、涡量、缺陷密度和应力）仍然可以通过局部物理算符（local physical operator）的作用，产生长波涨落被完全抑制的超均匀（hyperuniform）行为。作者建立了一个通用理论框架，将超均匀性从物质的结构属性推广为一种由局部物理约束生成的普适场现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无序物质中的涨落（fluctuations）对材料性质和物理响应有决定性影响。近期研究发现了一类称为结构超均匀材料（structurally hyperuniform materials）的奇特体系，其大尺度密度涨落通过特殊的空间组织被反常抑制。本文旨在探索：即使材料本身不具备结构超均匀性，其物理场是否仍可能表现出超均匀行为。

Method: 作者发展了一个通用理论框架：物理场（导出场）由更原始的母场（parent field）通过局部物理算符生成。在傅里叶空间中，导出场的谱由母场谱与算符傅里叶符号（Fourier symbol）的乘积决定。当算符体现局部规范类约束（local gauge-like constraint）时，其傅里叶符号在小波数处存在零点，从而消除相应的长波涨落。

Result: 无论母场存在多大尺度的无序和非超均匀性，导出场都能完全抑制无穷波长强度涨落（complete suppression of infinite-wavelength intensity fluctuations）。在弹性、静电和静磁学场景中，由算符生成的不相容场（incompatibility）、束缚电荷场（bound charge）和束缚电流场（bound-current field）可以变得超均匀，尽管其母场——本征应变（eigenstrain）、极化强度（polarization）或磁化强度（magnetization）——仍保持常规的无序状态。

Conclusion: 本文的研究拓展了超均匀性（hyperuniformity）的概念：它不再仅仅是物质的一种结构属性，而是由局部物理约束生成的一种普适场现象（universal field phenomenon）。

Abstract: Fluctuations in disordered matter play a central role in determining material properties and physical responses. Recent studies have identified an exotic class of systems known as structurally hyperuniform materials, in which large-scale density fluctuations are anomalously suppressed through special spatial organization of particles, phases, or microstructural features. Here we demonstrate that ordinary, structurally nonhyperuniform disordered materials can nevertheless support hyperuniform physical scalar, vector, and tensor fields such as charge, bound current, vorticity, defect density, and stress. We develop a general theoretical framework in which a physical field is generated from a more primitive parent field through a local physical operator. In Fourier space, the spectrum of the derived field is determined by the product of the parent-field spectrum and the Fourier symbol of the operator. When the operator embodies a local gauge-like constraint, its Fourier symbol possesses zeros at small wavenumber, eliminating the corresponding long-wavelength fluctuations. As a consequence, the derived field exhibits complete suppression of infinite-wavelength intensity fluctuations, irrespective of the large-scale disorder and nonhyperuniformity of the parent field. We demonstrate this mechanism in elastic, electrostatic, and magnetostatic settings, showing that operator-generated incompatibility, bound charge, and bound-current fields can become hyperuniform even when their parent eigenstrain, polarization, or magnetization fields remain conventionally disordered. These findings broaden the notion of hyperuniformity from a structural property of matter to a universal field phenomenon generated by local physical constraints.

</details>


### [233] [Lattice initialisation and finite-size effects of non-equilibrium molecular dynamics simulations for heat transfer across graphene-copper interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16783)
*L. A. van Goor,W. N. Edeling,D. Jafari,H. Lee,E. Luesink,W. W. Wits,A. V. Lyulin,B. J. Geurts*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用非平衡分子动力学（NEMD）研究铜-石墨烯-铜界面热输运，发现晶格初始化和石墨烯褶皱等域结构配置选择对卡皮查热阻（Kapitza resistance）具有强烈敏感性：两种传统晶格初始化策略仅导致晶格参数百分之几的差异，却使Kapitza热阻相差两倍，且该行为与声子谱的应变依赖偏移及界面处阻尼边界层的形成有关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 文献中已有NEMD模拟识别出石墨烯-铜界面Kapitza热阻的趋势，但模拟结果和可靠性可能严重依赖于尚未被充分探索的配置选择（即域长度和域配置，包括晶格初始化和石墨烯褶皱），因此有必要系统研究这些因素对热导率和Kapitza热阻的影响。

Method: 采用非平衡分子动力学（Non-Equilibrium Molecular Dynamics, NEMD）方法模拟铜-石墨烯-铜界面的热输运，通过改变有限域长度和域配置（晶格初始化策略及由此引发的石墨烯褶皱），对比预测的界面热导率和Kapitza热阻，并结合声子谱分析（phonon spectral analysis）和局部结构无序度评估。

Result: 两种传统晶格初始化策略在晶格参数仅相差百分之几的情况下，导致Kapitza热阻相差两倍；该差异伴随石墨烯和铜的声子谱发生应变依赖性偏移，且低应变下声子重叠增大。与常规预期相反，更大的声子模式重叠对应更高的Kapitza热阻，表明仅靠光谱重叠无法捕捉界面热传递动力学。在残余应变较低的晶格中，界面附近形成阻尼边界层，增加了热阻。Kapitza热阻对域长度和边界温度设定不敏感，而铜晶格热导率则表现出明显的域尺寸和温度依赖性。

Conclusion: 界面热输运的NEMD模拟结果对晶格初始化策略高度敏感，差异源于应变相关的声子谱偏移以及界面阻尼边界层的形成；谱重叠（spectral overlap）本身不足以预测界面热传递，需考虑局部结构无序和谱展宽效应；铜晶格热导率受声子平均自由程（mean-free-path）限制，呈现域尺寸和温度依赖性。

Abstract: We study thermal transport across copper-graphene-copper interfaces using Non-Equilibrium Molecular Dynamics (NEMD), focusing on the influence of finite domain length and domain configuration, including lattice initialisation and associated graphene wrinkling, on the predicted thermal conductivity and Kapitza resistance. In the literature, NEMD simulations identified trends in the Kapitza resistance of graphene-copper interfaces. However, the simulation outcomes and reliability may depend heavily on configuration choices that are underexplored in the literature. We identify a strong sensitivity of the Kapitza resistance to domain configuration choices that affect the lattice constants and atomic density. We show that two conventional lattice initialisation strategies yield a factor of two difference in the Kapitza resistance, despite differences of only a few per cent in the lattice parameters. This behaviour is accompanied by strain-dependent shifts in the graphene and copper phonon spectra, and by increased phonon overlap at lower strain. Counter to conventional expectations, greater phonon-mode overlap coincides with higher Kapitza resistance, showing that spectral overlap alone cannot capture the interfacial heat-transfer dynamics. We suggest that in lattices initialised with lower residual strain, a damping boundary layer develops near the interface, and increases thermal resistance, as indicated by increased local structural disorder and local spectral broadening over a wider interfacial region. Beyond strain- and density-related effects associated with the lattice constants, Kapitza resistance shows no significant dependence on domain length or boundary temperature enforcement in this study. By contrast, the copper lattice conductivity exhibits clear domain-size and temperature dependence, consistent with phonon mean-free-path limitations and supported by phonon spectral analysis.

### [234] [Harnessing disorder to decouple extension and shear in kirigami metamaterials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16583)
*Haomin Yu,Hanxun Jin,Mingxuan Bi,Mohammad Jafari,Feng Helen Long,Michael J Greenberg,Farid Alisafaei,Guy Genin*

TL;DR: 本文提出将工程无序（engineered disorder）作为剪纸结构（kirigami）的设计自由度，利用随机切口模式替代传统周期性图案，实现了更广阔且连续的力学响应空间，包括几乎完全消除拉伸-剪切耦合（extension-shear coupling）的可编程各向异性（programmable anisotropy）。研究结合几何感知图神经网络（GNN）与遗传算法（genetic algorithm）进行逆向设计，实验验证了预测的非线性各向异性响应。

Result: 随机剪纸结构实现了比周期性图案更连续、更广阔的力学响应空间，包括可编程各向异性与近乎完全的拉伸-剪切耦合消除。制备的弹性体样品复现了预测的非线性各向异性响应，验证了从设计到物理部件的闭环流程。

Conclusion: 将无序转化为可控变量来调节定向刚度，开发出无寄生剪切拉伸的建筑材料（architected materials），可应用于从软体致动器到与活体组织各向异性匹配的组织接口器件等领域。

Abstract: Kirigami turns stiff sheets into compliant, shape-morphing structures, but its reliance on periodic cut patterns comes at a cost: correlated panel rotations couple extension to shear, so stretching one axis drives a parasitic shear that cannot be suppressed, and also confine anisotropic stiffness to a narrow, discrete set of responses that cannot be tuned independently. Biological tissues overcome an analogous constraint through controlled disorder, such as graded fiber orientations in skin and hierarchical anisotropy in myocardium, achieving direction-dependent mechanics unavailable to regular architectures. Here, we show that engineered disorder is a design degree of freedom for kirigami, with stochastic kirigami accessing a continuous and far broader region of mechanical response than periodic patterns. This includes programmable anisotropy with near-complete elimination of extension-shear coupling. Because disordered patterns lack a simple parameterization, we navigate this design space with a geometry-aware graph neural network (GNN) that maps cut topology to the full nonlinear, bidirectional stress-strain response, coupled to a genetic algorithm that inverse-designs patterns reproducing target responses along two perpendicular axes. The GNN trains an order of magnitude faster and more accurately than image-based models. Fabricated elastomer samples reproduce the predicted nonlinear, anisotropic responses, closing the loop from design to physical component. By turning disorder into a variable to control directional stiffness, this work develops architected materials that stretch without parasitic shear, from soft actuators to tissue-interfacing devices matched to the anisotropy of living tissue.

### [235] [Beyond Janus Atomic Ordering: High-Throughput First-Principles Search for Hidden MoSO Monolayer Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16589)
*Zhijing Huang,Tingting Zeng,Lin Zhang,Zhibin Gao,Longyuzhi Xu,Li Yang,Shuming Zeng,Zonglin Gu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用高通量第一性原理计算（high-throughput first-principles calculations），结合随机采样策略、图论（graph theory）和群论（group theory），从1325种候选结构中筛选稳定结构，并辅以动力学、热力学和力学稳定性分析及从头算分子动力学（AIMD）模拟验证。

Conclusion: 该工作不仅拓展了二维MoSO材料家族，也为通过高通量计算发现稳定功能性二维材料提供了可靠策略。

Abstract: Despite the growing interest in two-dimensional (2D) MoSO systems, existing studies have exclusively focused on conventional Janus structures. In this work, we perform high-throughput first-principles calculations to explore novel stable 2D MoSO monolayers. Combined with random sampling strategy, graph theory and group theory, we successfully screen out three novel non-Janus 2D MoSO monolayers from 1325 candidate structures, namely Reversed 2H-MoSO, Hybrid 2H-MoSO, and Hybrid 1T'-MoSO. Compared with Janus MoSO monolayers, the non-Janus MoSO counterparts possess lower binding energies, varying from -4.38 to -4.51 eV/atom. A systematic combination of dynamic, thermodynamic, and mechanical stability analyses corroborates their excellent structural robustness. Ab initio molecular dynamics (AIMD) simulations confirm their superior thermal resistance, with the structures remaining stable at temperatures beyond 2000 K. Interestingly, unlike the semiconducting Janus MoSO, the Hybrid 1T'-MoSO monolayer exhibits distinct metallic characteristics. Furthermore, we found that strain and curvature can enable controlled phase transitions of MoSO among semiconducting, semimetallic, and metallic phases. More importantly, the Hybrid 1T'-MoSO exhibits favorable HER activity with a Gibbs free energy of -0.002 eV, rendering it a promising candidate for hydrogen evolution catalysis. This work not only expands the family of 2D MoSO materials but also provides a reliable strategy for discovering stable functional 2D materials via high-throughput computation.

### [236] [High-entropy perovskites, architectured by s0/d0/d10 cations, as novel electrolytes for solid oxide fuel cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16616)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固体氧化物燃料电池能高效地将氢气转化为电能，但阴极、阳极和电解质材料的有限可用性仍是一个问题。因此，需要探索新型电解质材料以缓解对特定材料的依赖。

Method: 通过高压扭转加工（high-pressure torsion processing）和煅烧的顺序烧结，合成了三种高熵钙钛矿：(Ba0.50Sr0.50)(Ti0.33Zr0.33Hf0.33)O3（s0/d0阳离子）、(Ba0.50Sr0.50)(Ga0.33In0.33Sn0.33)O3（s0/d10阳离子）和(Ba0.50Sr0.50)(Ti0.33Zr0.33Sn0.33)O3（混合s0/d0/d10阳离子）。随后将其以约6-10微米厚度打印在Ni-SrZr0.5Ce0.4Y0.1O3基板上作为阳极，并涂覆Ba0.5La0.5CoO3作为阴极。采用电化学分析、阻抗谱（impedance spectroscopy）、同步辐射X射线吸收谱（synchrotron X-ray absorption）和光电子能谱（photoelectron spectroscopy）进行表征。

Result: (Ba0.50Sr0.50)(Ti0.33Zr0.33Sn0.33)O3（s0/d0/d10阳离子）表现出最佳性能，具有可忽略的漏电流和最低的欧姆电阻，在973 K下最大功率密度达到0.53 W·cm⁻²。其优异性能与异质电子结构（heterogeneous electronic structure）、调控的空d轨道态（unoccupied d-orbital states）、有利的局域金属-氧键长（local metal-oxygen bond lengths）和外在氧空位（extrinsic oxygen vacancies）相关。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了具有混合s0/d0/d10阳离子的高熵钙钛矿作为新型无稀土金属离子导电电解质（rare-earth metal-free ion-conducting electrolytes）的重要性，特别是在质子型固体氧化物燃料电池（protonic solid oxide fuel cells）中的应用潜力。

Abstract: Solid oxide fuel cells enable efficient conversion of hydrogen into electricity. However, the limited availability of materials for their cathode, anode, and electrolyte remains a concern. This study introduces three high-entropy oxide perovskites as novel electrolyte materials for fuel cells (Ba0.50Sr0.50)(Ti0.33Zr0.33Hf0.33)O3 with s0/d0 cations, (Ba0.50Sr0.50)(Ga0.33In0.33Sn0.33)O3 with s0/d10 cations, and (Ba0.50Sr0.50)(Ti0.33Zr0.33Sn0.33)O3 with mixed s0/d0/d10 cations. Through sequential sintering by high-pressure torsion processing and calcination, these perovskites were synthesized and then printed with a thickness of about 6-10 microns on a Ni-SrZr0.5Ce0.4Y0.1O3 substrate as an anode and then coated with Ba0.5La0.5CoO3 as a cathode. Electrochemical analysis and impedance spectroscopy show that (Ba0.50Sr0.50)(Ti0.33Zr0.33Sn0.33)O3 with s0/d0/d10 cations exhibits the best performance with negligible current leakage and lowest ohmic resistance, while its maximum power density reaches 0.53 W.cm-2 at 973 K. Complementary synchrotron X-ray absorption and photoelectron spectroscopy analyses indicate that the superior performance of (Ba0.50Sr0.50)(Ti0.33Zr0.33Sn0.33)O3 correlates with its heterogeneous electronic structure characterized by tailored unoccupied d-orbital states, and favorable local metal-oxygen bond lengths and extrinsic oxygen vacancies. This investigation demonstrates the significance of high-entropy perovskites with mixed s0/d0/d10 cations as new rare-earth metal-free ion-conducting electrolytes, particularly for protonic solid oxide fuel cells.

</details>


### [237] [Three Million Years Opposite State Data Retention in Partially Switched Wurtzite Ferroelectrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16665)
*Maike Gremmel,Roberto Guido,Victor Witte,Uwe Schröder,Simon Fichtner*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索纤锌矿结构铁电体（wurtzite-structured ferroelectrics）在铁电随机存取存储器（FeRAM）中的应用潜力，尤其是如何克服初始印记变异（initial imprint variation）对器件保持性能和耐久性的限制。

Method: 将标准畴壁运动受限的翻转动力学（domain wall motion limited switching kinetics）与近电极注入模型（near-by-electrode injection model）相结合，对反向态保持（opposite state retention）进行建模；在60 nm–270 nm不同厚度及AlScN和AlScBN不同化合物薄膜上进行实验验证。

Result: 仅切换总极化的一部分（部分极化切换）可显著降低初始印记变异，并在给定时间后产生比完全切换状态更大的切换极化（switching polarization），同时反向态保持性能提升5-7个数量级；在150°C下信息保存时间超过300万年；部分切换还能同时提高抗过早极化损失和击穿的耐久性（endurance）。

Conclusion: 部分极化切换是一种有前景的策略，可用于改善具有大自发极化（spontaneous polarization）的铁电器件（尤其是纤锌矿结构化合物）的工作性能。

Abstract: Ferroelectric memories based on the wurtzite-structured ferroelectrics are projected to store information for more than 3 million years at 150C. These results are extracted by combining standard domain wall motion limited switching kinetics with the near-by-electrode injection model for opposite state retention in ferroelectric random access memory. This impressive performance is greatly aided by switching only a fraction of the total polarization to store data, in order to limit the initial imprint variation of the devices - an effect that is universally observed in films with different thicknesses (60 nm - 270 nm) and different compounds (AlScN and AlScBN). Paradoxically, yet systematically, this reduction in initial imprint consistently results in larger switching polarization after a given time, compared to the fully switching state and 5-7 orders of magnitude improved opposite state retention. Finally, partial switching is able to simultaneously boost endurance against premature polarization loss and breakdown, making it a promising strategy for improved operation of ferroelectric devices with large spontaneous polarization, in particularly wurtzite-structured compounds.

### [238] [Period-dependent suppression of Fourier peaks for topography images: Analysis of periodicity of triple-step arrays on vicinal Si(h h m) surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16699)
*A. Yu. Aladyshkin,A. N. Chaika,V. N. Semenov,A. S. Aladyshkina,A. M. Ionov,S. I. Bozhko*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需预校正即可从原始扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）数据中精确测定高密勒指数邻晶面（high-Miller-index vicinal surfaces）上多原子台阶周期的方法。通过差分高斯（difference-of-Gaussians）方法生成微分图，发现傅里叶峰的强度对有序三台阶阵列的周期高度敏感；第九级傅里叶峰的抑制表明，名义上为Si(5 5 7)取向的硅片可能局部对应Si(8 8 11)取向。该方法可推广至其他含整数个Si(1 1 1)7×7单胞的邻晶面分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高密勒指数邻晶面上多原子台阶周期的可靠测定常受两大因素困扰：一是较窄台阶面（terrace）相对扫描平面倾斜大角度；二是压电扫描器的蠕变（creep）与不校准导致横向畸变。现有方法难以在无需预校正的情况下实现接近原子间距的精度，因此亟需一种更鲁棒的周期测定手段。

Method: 直接从原始STM形貌图出发，采用差分高斯（difference-of-Gaussians, DoG）方法生成微分图（differential maps），然后分析该微分图的傅里叶峰强度对有序三台阶阵列周期的依赖性。

Result: 第九级傅里叶峰的抑制表明，有序三台阶阵列在Si(1 1 1)台阶面投影上的周期为18b=5.99 nm（b=0.333 nm为1×1晶格在[¯1 ¯1 2]方向上的原子行间距）。这意味着名义上(5 5 7)取向的Si晶片可能局部对应Si(8 8 11)取向。

Conclusion: 该方法无需预校正即可从原始STM数据中测定台阶周期，精度接近原子间距；并可推广至其他含窄台阶面与宽台阶面的邻晶面体系，前提是这些台阶面包含整数个Si(1 1 1)7×7单胞。

Abstract: Reliable determination of the periodicity of multiatomic steps on high-Miller-index vicinal surfaces is often complicated by (i) the presence of relatively narrow terraces tilted at large angles relative to the scanning plane, and (ii) unavoidable distortions in the lateral direction resulting from creep and improper calibration of a piezo scanner. We argue that the period of the triple-step arrays on vicinal Si(5\,5\,6) and Si(5 5 7) single-crystal wafers can be determined from raw scanning tunneling microscopy data, without preliminary corrections, with precision approaching the interatomic distance. We demonstrate that the intensity of the Fourier peaks of the differential maps, derived from raw topography images by the difference-of-Gaussians approach, strongly depends on the period of the ordered triple-step arrays. This suppression of the ninth Fourier peak indicates that the regular array of triple steps has a period of $18b=5.99$ nm in projection onto the Si(1 1 1) terrace plane, where $b=0.333$ nm is the distance between atomic rows of the $1\times 1$ lattice in the $[\bar{1}\,\bar{1}\,2]$ direction. This means that the nominally (5\,5\,7)-oriented Si wafers may correspond locally to the Si(8 8 11) orientation. The method can be applied to the precise analysis of other vicinal surfaces with narrow and wide terraces containing an integer number of Si(1 1 1)$7\times 7$ unit cells.

### [239] [Measuring momentum-resolved dissipation of phonon-polaritons in LiNbO$_3$ with terahertz driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16718)

TL;DR: 本文提出太赫兹泵浦-拉曼探测（THz pump-Raman probe, TP-RP）作为一种通用方法，用于映射极性非中心对称材料中的极化激元（polariton）色散，并以LiNbO₃中的声子-极化激元为例，结合多体理论方法高精度提取其频率和阻尼率的动量依赖性，揭示了声子本征阻尼率中非平凡的频率依赖关系及可能的非谐耦合（anharmonic coupling）。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用太赫兹泵浦-拉曼探测（THz pump-Raman probe, TP-RP）技术，利用宽带太赫兹泵浦共振驱动极化激元模式，并通过可调谐近红外（NIR）拉曼脉冲进行探测，从而提取极化激元的动量依赖性频率和阻尼率。实验结果通过多体理论（many-body theoretical approach）进行复现和分析。

Result: TP-RP方法成功应用于LiNbO₃中E(TO₁)声子-极化激元的研究，实现了对极化激元色散的高精度映射。结合理论与实验分析，发现了该声子本征阻尼率（intrinsic damping rate）存在非平凡的频率依赖性，暗示可能存在与其他模式之间的非谐耦合（anharmonic coupling）。

Conclusion: 太赫兹泵浦-拉曼探测（TP-RP）是一种通用的、高精度的极化激元色散映射方法，能够同时获取频率和阻尼率的动量依赖性，为研究极性材料中声子-极化激元及其他极化激元系统的本征耗散和耦合机制提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Mapping the dispersion of polaritons, hybrid quasiparticles arising from light-matter coupling, can provide key insights into the material dielectric response, coupling strength, and energy transfer pathways with other excitations. In this work, we present THz pump-Raman probe (TP-RP) as a versatile method for mapping the polariton dispersion in polar non-centrosymmetric materials, demonstrated here for the case of phonon-polaritons in LiNbO$_3$. By resonantly driving polaritonic modes with a broadband THz pump and probing them with a tunable NIR Raman pulse, TP-RP allows for the extraction of the momentum-dependence of both their frequency and damping rate with high accuracy. The spectral features observed in the pump-probe signal, including the polaritonic response as well as pulse artifacts, are reproduced within a many-body theoretical approach. Applying the technique to study the E(TO$_1$) phonon of LiNbO$_3$ enables the combined analysis of theory and experiments to uncover a nontrivial frequency dependence of the phonon intrinsic damping rate, revealing possible anharmonic couplings to other modes.

Method: 运用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和自旋空间群分析（spin-space-group analysis），并结合有效紧束缚模型（effective tight-binding model）进行理论解释。

Abstract: Altermagnetism is a collinear magnetic state characterized by momentum-dependent spin splitting in fully compensated materials. While widely investigated in systems governed by three- or two-dimensional exchange interactions, its extension to quasi-one-dimensional magnets remains almost unexplored. Focusing on the experimentally established AgCrP$_2$S$_6$ van der Waals magnet, we demonstrate that antiferromagnetic chains embedded in a two-dimensional lattice provide a general route to altermagnetism. Combining first-principles calculations and spin-space-group analysis, we show that out-of-plane symmetry breaking can generate a nonrelativistic d-wave spin splitting. An external out-of-plane electric field validates this mechanism, where the induced splitting increases linearly with field strength and reverses sign with field direction. We rationalize such behaviour by constructing an effective tight-binding model, which links the altermagnetic response to anisotropic third-neighbor interchain hoppings. Additionally, we show that Janus substitution also induces a d-wave spin texture, while ferroelectric interfacing with CuInP$_2$S$_6$ enables polarization-controlled spin-split bands in a fully compensated ferrimagnetic state. ### [241] [Specimen design for material parameter identification using topology optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16865)

Method: 方法核心是将贝叶斯最优实验设计（Bayesian optimal experimental design）与拓扑优化（topology optimization）整合。贝叶斯设计准则（Bayesian design criterion）用于量化预期信息增益（expected information gain），以此驱动试样几何形状（specimen geometry）的拓扑优化。

Result: 该框架能够利用全场测量（full-field measurements）的高维数据，并根据模型当前的不确定性（uncertainty）来指导未来实验的设计。

Conclusion: 本文提出的框架实现了建模与实验的强耦合，使实验配置的识别过程能够最大化本构模型发现的信息量。

Abstract: Constitutive relations close the equations of continuum mechanics, and serve as a surrogate for a material in the design and engineering process. They are often specified in a parameterized form with parameters identified by experiment. In this paper, we propose a framework for identifying experimental configurations that are maximally informative for constitutive model discovery. The framework strongly couples modeling and experimentation: the model leverages high-dimensional data from full-field measurements, while the current uncertainty in the model guides the design of future experiments. We formulate this goal by integrating Bayesian optimal experimental design with topology optimization. The Bayesian design criterion quantifies expected information gain, which drives the topology optimization of the specimen geometry.

### [242] [Operando observation of strain relaxation in fatigued pearlitic steel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16867)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用暗场X射线显微术（Dark-Field X-ray Microscopy, DFXM），对疲劳后的珠光体晶团（pearlitic colony）在退火至550 °C过程中进行原位（operando）晶粒尺度观测，获取取向图和应变图。

Conclusion: 将应变回复归因于片层间受限位错的短程湮灭（short-range annihilation），从而建立了晶粒尺度应变恢复与服役中珠光体铁路钢宏观软化之间的关联。

Abstract: Pearlitic steels are the material of choice for railway wheels and rails, where their lamellar ferrite-cementite structure balances cost, strength, and wear resistance. However, in use, cyclic loading combined with frictional heat softens the steel, promoting fatigue and eventual failure. Here we use Dark-Field X-ray Microscopy (DFXM) to follow, operando, the grain-scale response of a fatigued pearlitic colony during annealing up to 550 °C. Orientation maps reveal negligible lattice rotation and no sub-cell formation, indicating that the cementite lamellae suppress long-range dislocation motion. Strain maps nonetheless show pronounced relaxation: the elastic strain spread narrows by nearly 40%, with recovery starting below 250 °C, within the operating temperatures of railway wheels. We attribute this relaxation to short-range annihilation of dislocations confined between lamellae, linking grain-scale strain recovery to the macroscopic softening of pearlitic railway steels in service.

### [243] [Planar Microcavities can Suppress Exciplex Formation and Increase the Emission Efficiency of Organic Semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16886)
*Tomohiro Ishii,Stéphane Kéna-Cohen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将ZnPc:TPBi共混薄膜嵌入平面法布里-珀罗（Fabry-Pérot）微腔中，采用瞬态光谱（transient spectroscopy）、功率依赖光致发光测量（power-dependent photoluminescence）以及动力学建模（kinetic modelling）进行分析，并结合电磁学计算（electromagnetic calculations）预测福斯特共振能量转移（Förster resonance energy transfer, FRET）的增强因子。

Result: 实验发现，微腔将光致发光量子产率（photoluminescence quantum yield）在连续波激发下提升逾四十倍；瞬态光谱与动力学建模表明，这一增强源于从ZnPc单体到发射性聚集体的长程福斯特能量转移（Förster energy transfer）被增强，从而在与电荷转移至暗激基复合物（dark exciplexes）的竞争中获得优势；电磁学计算预测，在相关距离上FRET增强可达约400倍，与激基复合物介导的损耗被抑制的实验观察一致。

Conclusion: 光学微腔不仅能调控分子如何发光，还能控制分子形成哪些激发态，为提升有机光电器件（organic optoelectronic and photonic devices）的效率并降低效率滚降（roll-off）提供了新途径。

Abstract: Optical microcavities are widely used to control the emission of organic semiconductors, but their ability to reshape the molecular pathways that precede emission remains largely unexplored. Here we show that embedding a ZnPc:TPBi blend in a planar Fabry-Pérot microcavity suppresses the formation of non-radiative exciplexes and removes bimolecular annihilation at high excitation densities, increasing the photoluminescence quantum yield by more than forty-fold under continuous-wave excitation. This enhancement is far larger than expected from the weak Purcell effect. Instead, transient spectroscopy, power-dependent photoluminescence and kinetic modelling point to a cavity-induced rebalancing of excited-state populations: long-range Förster energy transfer from ZnPc monomers to emissive aggregates is enhanced, allowing it to outcompete charge transfer to dark exciplexes. Electromagnetic calculations predict FRET enhancements of up to ~400-fold at relevant distances, consistent with the observed suppression of exciplex-mediated losses. Our results show that optical cavities can control not only how molecules emit, but also which excited states they form, opening a route to improved efficiency and reduced roll-off in organic optoelectronic and photonic devices.

</details>


### [244] [The crystallographic quaternions and their product law](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16899)
*Cyril Cayron*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过引入交叉张量（cross tensor）将四元数（quaternions）推广到晶体基（crystal basis），解决了标准四元数无法直接用于晶体学的问题，并给出了仅依赖于度量张量（metric tensor）的晶体学四元数乘积公式，讨论了其在电子背散射衍射（Electron Back Scatter Diffraction, EBSD）中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准单位四元数基于笛卡尔基（Cartesian basis），无法直接用于晶体学（crystallography）。现有解决方案需要在晶体基与笛卡尔基之间来回进行坐标变换，过程繁琐。本文旨在让四元数在晶体基中直接可用。

Method: 引入一个称为交叉张量（cross tensor）的矩阵，用于在晶体基中计算叉积（cross product），类似于度量张量用于计算标量积（scalar product）。推导出交叉张量与度量张量的逆成正比，进而给出仅依赖于度量张量的晶体学四元数乘积公式。

Result: 成功将四元数推广到晶体基，建立了晶体学四元数乘积公式，该公式仅依赖于度量张量。交叉张量被证明与度量张量的逆成正比。

Conclusion: 晶体学四元数可绕过传统笛卡尔基坐标变换的方式，直接在晶体基中描述旋转，其在电子背散射衍射（EBSD）等晶体学应用中具有潜力。

Abstract: Unit quaternions are widely used in science to encode rotations because the quaternion product is more efficient than matrix product and more stable than Rodrigues product to calculate the composition of two rotations. However, quaternions in their usual form refers to a Cartesian basis; they cannot be used in crystallography as they are. The usual way to solve this issue to apply back-and-forth coordinate changes from the crystal basis to a Cartesian basis attached to the crystal with the help of the structure tensor. Here, we show that actually quaternions can be used directly in the crystal basis by generalizing the quaternion product law. In that aim, we introduced a matrix that we called cross tensor. It allows the calculation of the cross product in the crystal basis, a bit like the metric tensor allows it for the scalar product. We also show the cross tensor is proportional to the inverse of the metric tensor. The formula of crystallographic quaternion product is then given; it depends uniquely on the metric tensor. The application of the crystallographic quaternions to Electron Back Scatter Diffraction is discussed.

Result: 给出了所有十四种三维布拉维晶格的Baldereschi平均点的具体数值（已表格化呈现）。

Abstract: The Baldereschi point of a crystal is a wavevector in the Brillouin zone at which every smooth periodic function of wavevector lies close to its mean value. Although originally introduced in the context of one-electron methods, mean-value points are ideal for explicitly correlated many-electron methods such as quantum Monte Carlo simulations, which can only use a single Bloch wavevector in the Brillouin zone of a simulation supercell. We have therefore evaluated and tabulated the Baldereschi mean-value points of all fourteen three-dimensional Bravais lattices.

Abstract: In electronic materials, flat bands are associated with compact electron localization, with implications for superconductivity, ferromagnetism and strongly correlated systems. Here we report a strategy to achieve elastic flat bands through an inertial retrofitting of classical lattice architectures. The idea is to alter the cell geometry to realize a network of inertial anchors, effectively partitioning the lattice into an array of weakly coupled emergent resonators, whose resonances appear as flat bands in the phonon spectrum. We demonstrate flat-band conditions that combine localized and extended state attributes and induce a giant response that is spatially and temporally persistent. Laser vibrometry experiments reveal three signatures of this mechanism: amplification up to two orders of magnitude compared to pass band and band gap conditions, multi-cell activation that is agnostic to the source location, and a persistent transient response even after several excitation cycles.

### [247] [STEP: Spin Tensor Equivariant Potential for Data-Efficient Learning of Magnetic Potential Energy Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17129)
*Yuanqing Gao,Wen-Hao Luo,Lei Zhang,Kun Cao*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了自旋张量等变势（Spin Tensor Equivariant Potential, STEP），一种将矢量磁矩作为连续几何自由度嵌入等变表示的机器学习原子间势，在单层CrI₃、FeAl、CrN、Fe及Fe₂Mo₃O₈等体系上展示了高数据效率、竞争性精度及对自旋-晶格耦合、磁激子与有限温度磁行为的可靠描述能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确高效地建模磁势能面（magnetic potential energy surfaces）具有挑战性，因为对多样化的非共线自旋-晶格构型（non-collinear spin-lattice configurations）进行自旋极化第一性原理（spin-polarized first-principles）计算的计算代价很高。

Method: STEP将矢量磁矩（vector magnetic moments）视为连续的几何自由度，并将其嵌入等变表示（equivariant representation）中。通过中心-环境张量积（Center-Environment Tensor Product）将中心自旋表示与局域自旋-晶格环境耦合，引入物理先验，同时保持平移不变性（translational invariance）和SO(3)等变性（SO(3) equivariance），并支持特征级别的时间反演对称化（time-reversal symmetrization）。

Result: 在单层CrI₃上的学习曲线分析表明，STEP具有显著的数据效率，高阶张量通道与迭代中心-环境耦合带来了能量、力与磁力误差的陡峭学习曲线。在FeAl、CrN和Fe公开基准上达到竞争性或改进的精度。使用紧凑的CrI₃数据集高保真地再现了声子色散与磁振子谱（magnon spectra），捕捉到微妙的各向异性磁相互作用。在Fe₂Mo₃O₈上定量描述了磁振子-声子杂化（magnon-phonon hybridization）并再现了磁振子极化子（magnon polaron）色散。STEP驱动的自旋动力学模拟给出的单层CrI₃和bcc Fe的居里温度（Curie temperatures）与实验吻合良好。

Conclusion: STEP被确立为一个物理先验引导、数据高效且可扩展的框架，适用于建模自旋-晶格耦合、磁激发（magnetic excitations）及有限温度磁行为（finite-temperature magnetic behavior）。

Abstract: Accurate and efficient modeling of magnetic potential energy surfaces remains challenging because spin-polarized first-principles calculations for diverse non-collinear spin-lattice configurations are computationally demanding. Here we introduce the Spin Tensor Equivariant Potential (STEP), a magnetic machine-learning interatomic potential that treats vector magnetic moments as continuous geometric degrees of freedom and embeds them in an equivariant representation. By coupling the central spin representation to its local spin-lattice environment through a Center-Environment Tensor Product, STEP introduces a physics-informed bias while preserving translational invariance and $\mathrm{SO}(3)$ equivariance and supporting feature-level time-reversal symmetrization. Learning-curve analysis on monolayer CrI$_3$ shows that STEP achieves pronounced data efficiency, with higher-order tensor channels and iterative center-environment couplings leading to steep learning curves for energy, force, and magnetic force errors. On public FeAl, CrN, and Fe benchmarks, STEP achieves competitive or improved accuracy compared with recent magnetic machine-learning potentials. Using a compact but representative CrI$_3$ dataset, STEP reproduces phonon dispersions and magnon spectra with high fidelity, capturing subtle anisotropic magnetic interactions. For Fe$_2$Mo$_3$O$_8$, STEP further provides a quantitative description of magnon--phonon hybridization and reproduces its characteristic magnon polaron dispersion. Finally, spin dynamics simulations driven by STEP yield Curie temperatures for monolayer CrI$_3$ and bcc Fe in good agreement with experiments. These results establish STEP as a physically informed, data-efficient, and scalable framework for modeling spin-lattice coupling, magnetic excitations, and finite-temperature magnetic behavior.

### [248] [XMatcher: An Open-Source Framework for X-Ray Diffraction Phase Identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17162)
*Bin Cao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粉末 X 射线衍射（Powder X-ray diffraction, XRD）广泛用于晶相鉴定，现有机器学习方法虽加速了衍射解读，但在复杂样品中仍缺乏透明且基于证据的验证过程。同时，搜索匹配（search-match）方法虽有效，但多数实现为专有软件，限制可及性和可复现性。

Method: XMatcher 通过以下步骤实现相鉴定：从晶体结构生成理论衍射库；利用化学与衍射约束检索候选相；执行全局角度偏移校正（global angular-shift correction）和一对一峰匹配（one-to-one peak matching）；输出定量一致性指标与峰级证据。其 AutoMix 模块通过评估候选相组合、估计非负衍射贡献并可视化各相峰分布，扩展至多相图谱识别。

Abstract: Powder X-ray diffraction (XRD) is widely used for crystalline phase identification, and recent machine learning approaches have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in accelerating diffraction interpretation. However, reliable phase assignment still requires transparent, evidence-based validation, particularly for complex samples where interpretability and expert assessment remain essential. Search-match methods provide a robust and complementary strategy, yet many implementations are proprietary, limiting accessibility and reproducibility. Here, we introduce XMatcher, an open-source, evidence-driven framework that integrates diffraction databases, matching algorithms, and interactive visualization into a portable workflow. XMatcher generates theoretical diffraction libraries from crystal structures, retrieves candidate phases through chemical and diffraction constraints, applies global angular-shift correction and one-to-one peak matching, and reports quantitative agreement metrics together with peak-level evidence. Its AutoMix module extends identification to multiphase patterns by evaluating candidate phase combinations, estimating non-negative diffraction contributions, and visualizing phase-specific peak distributions. Through a local graphical interface, XMatcher enables ranked candidate inspection, interactive pattern comparison, PDF/CIF-based whole-pattern validation, and reproducible analysis export. By exposing both supporting and conflicting evidence rather than relying on a single similarity score, XMatcher provides an interpretable and reproducible platform for crystalline phase identification.

### [249] [First-principles electron-phonon scattering in real-time TDDFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17265)
*Zhengwei Nie,Subhojit Pal,Marti Lüders,Alexander Buccheri,Hannes Hübener,Shunsuke A. Sato,Umberto De Giovannini*

TL;DR: 该论文开发了一个耗散性实时含时密度泛函理论（dissipative rt-TDDFT）框架，通过在Born-Markov近似下引入基于自能（self-energy）的碰撞积分（collision integrals），将第一性原理电子-声子相互作用（electron-phonon interactions）纳入约化单粒子密度矩阵（reduced one-body density matrix）的演化中，从而在保持量子相干实时传播的同时模拟载流子的弛豫、退相干及时间分辨光谱特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的实时含时密度泛函理论（rt-TDDFT）采用幺正（unitary）描述，无法捕捉不可逆的散射、弛豫和退相干（decoherence）过程，而这些过程是驱动受激载流子向平衡态演化的关键机制。

Method: 在Born-Markov近似下，通过自能推导的碰撞积分将第一性原理的电子-声子相互作用引入约化单粒子密度矩阵的时间演化，从而在保留电子系统量子相干实时传播的前提下引入声子介导的能级和晶格动量重新分布。

Result: 该框架能够纳入描述实际材料中弛豫过程的微观动量转移机制，从而从第一性原理出发模拟载流子的弛豫、退相干以及时间分辨光谱信号。

Conclusion: 该耗散性rt-TDDFT框架提供了一条实用的第一性原理路径，用于模拟真实晶体材料中的弛豫、退相干及时间分辨光谱学特征。

Abstract: Real-time time-dependent density functional theory provides a first-principles description of coherent electron dynamics in laser-driven solids, but its unitary formulation cannot capture the irreversible scattering, relaxation, and decoherence processes that drive excited carriers toward equilibrium. Here, we develop a dissipative rt-TDDFT framework in which first-principles electron-phonon interactions enter the evolution of the reduced one-body density matrix through self-energy-derived collision integrals within the Born-Markov approximation. The approach retains the quantum-coherent real-time propagation of the electronic system while introducing phonon-mediated transitions that redistribute carriers in energy and crystal momentum, thereby incorporating the microscopic momentum-transfer processes responsible for relaxation in real materials. The resulting framework provides a practical first-principles route to simulate relaxation, decoherence, and time-resolved spectroscopic signatures in realistic crystalline materials.

### [250] [Interfacial thermal transport in Si/SiC and SiC/diamond heterostructures: effects of amorphous interlayers and SiC polytypes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17330)
*Pedram Mirchi,Shirin Sabokdast,Ali Rajabpour*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究利用非平衡分子动力学模拟，分析了声子介导的Si/SiC和SiC/diamond界面热传输，重点考察了SiC多型体和非晶中间层的影响。结果表明：4H-SiC比3C-SiC具有更高的界面热导；0.5 nm超薄非晶SiC层在Si/3C-SiC体系中可起到声子桥效应提升热传输；而较厚或富硅的非晶层会显著抑制界面热导；对于SiC/diamond界面，任何非晶层都会严重降低热传输性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解界面热传输机制对于高热导材料（如金刚石）在电子器件热管理中的应用至关重要。本文旨在揭示SiC多型体和非晶中间层对Si/SiC和SiC/diamond界面热导的影响规律，探索通过界面工程优化热传输的潜在途径。

Method: 采用非平衡分子动力学（non-equilibrium molecular dynamics）模拟方法，计算不同界面结构（尖锐界面、含非晶中间层）的界面热导（interfacial thermal conductance, ITC），并结合振动态密度（vibrational density of states, VDOS）分析声子谱匹配与传输通道变化。

Result: 对于尖锐界面，4H-SiC的ITC显著高于3C-SiC，归因于其更宽的活性声子谱和与Si更优的谱匹配。0.5 nm超薄aSiC层使Si/3C-SiC体系的ITC从613提升至716 MW/m^2-K，表现出声子桥效应；而较厚或富硅的非晶层因非弹性声子散射增强而抑制ITC。SiC/diamond界面中，任何非晶层（尤其是aSi）都会严重降低ITC。

Conclusion: 界面热导受声子谱匹配程度和非晶层厚度与组分的强烈调控。超薄非晶SiC层可在特定体系中起到声子桥作用增强热传输，而金刚石侧界面则需保持尖锐无缺陷以充分利用其高热导率。

Abstract: This study examines phonon-mediated heat transfer across Si/SiC and SiC/diamond interfaces using non-equilibrium molecular dynamics simulations, emphasizing the influence of SiC polytypes and amorphous interlayers. For sharp interfaces, 4H-SiC exhibits considerably higher interfacial thermal conductance (ITC) than 3C-SiC, due to its broader active phonon spectrum and superior spectral matching with Si. While amorphous layers generally reduce ITC, a key observation is that an ultrathin 0.5-nm amorphous SiC (aSiC) layer can enhance heat transport in the Si/3C-SiC system: the ITC increases from 613 MW/m^2-K (sharp) to 716 MW/m^2-K, demonstrating a phonon-bridge effect. VDOS (vibrational density of states) analysis confirms that optimized ultrathin aSiC layers improve vibrational overlap and open additional phonon-transport channels. In contrast, thicker or silicon-rich amorphous layers significantly suppress ITC through enhanced inelastic phonon scattering. For SiC/diamond interfaces, any amorphous layer, particularly aSi, causes severe ITC degradation, highlighting the need for sharp, defect-free bonding to exploit diamond's high thermal conductivity.

### [251] [Response-function-optimized phase field modeling of solute trapping and solute drag in rapid alloy solidification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17370)
*Joni Kaipainen,Tatu Pinomaa,Nikolas Provatas*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于优化的校准策略，将目标尖锐界面响应函数嵌入稀合金相场模型，通过优化界面扩散率插值函数来精确描述速度依赖性界面性质（如溶质截留、溶质拖曳、动力学液相线响应），并在Al-Cu体系中验证了该方法在快速凝固微观结构预测中的准确性，揭示了溶质拖曳对凝固形态从枝晶/胞状向带状结构转变的影响，同时扩展至稀多元合金体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 快速凝固微观结构的定量预测需要相场模型准确表征界面性质的速度依赖性，包括溶质分配（solute partitioning）、动力学液相线响应（kinetic liquidus response）、溶质拖曳（solute drag）及动力学过冷（kinetic undercooling）。然而，在为提高数值效率而采用大界面的相场模拟中，这些响应函数难以精确指定。

Method: 引入一种基于优化的校准策略，将稀疏合金相场公式（dilute alloy phase field formulation）中的界面扩散率插值函数（interfacial diffusivity interpolation function）作为响应匹配自由度，通过一维稳态相场解获得优化的扩散率函数，并约束其对预设的连续生长模型目标进行复现，以描述速度依赖的溶质截留（solute trapping）和拖曳修正的液相线动力学。

Result: 在稀Al-Cu体系中，校准后的模型准确再现了预设的响应函数；二维定向凝固模拟表明，增大溶质拖曳系数使凝固形态从枝晶/胞状生长依次转变为混合枝晶-带状结构，最终以带状生长为主。该框架还扩展至稀多元合金，允许为多个溶质物种独立指定平衡分配系数和液相线斜率。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一条将实验、理论或原子尺度信息获得的非平衡界面动力学纳入快速凝固合金定量相场模拟的可行途径。

Abstract: Quantitative prediction of rapid solidification microstructures requires phase field models that represent the velocity dependence of interfacial properties, including solute partitioning, kinetic liquidus response, solute drag, and kinetic undercooling. These response functions control both microsegregation and morphology selection, but are difficult to prescribe accurately in phase field simulations that employ large interfaces for numerical efficiency. We introduce an optimization-based calibration strategy that embeds target sharp-interface response functions into a dilute alloy phase field formulation by treating the interfacial diffusivity interpolation function as a response-matching degree of freedom. The optimized diffusivity functions are obtained from one-dimensional steady-state phase field solutions, constrained to reproduce prescribed continuous-growth-model targets for velocity-dependent solute trapping and drag-modified liquidus kinetics. We demonstrate the calibrated model's accuracy and versatility in dilute Al-Cu by reproducing the prescribed response functions for intermediate solute drag coefficients relevant to rapid solidification. Two-dimensional directional-solidification simulations are conducted to isolate the effect of drag at fixed composition, thermal gradient, and pulling velocity. We show that increasing solute drag shifts the solidification morphology from dendritic/cellular growth to mixed dendritic-banded structures, and finally to predominantly banded growth. We extend the formulation to dilute multicomponent alloys, enabling independent specification of equilibrium partition coefficients and liquidus slopes for multiple solute species. The framework provides a route for incorporating experimentally, theoretically, or atomistically informed nonequilibrium interface kinetics into quantitative phase field simulations of rapidly solidified alloys.

</details>


### [252] [Symmetry-Engineered Nonlinear Hall Response and Optical Response in Strained Monolayer Janus AsTeBr](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17385)
*Dimple Rani,Ritesh Ranjan Badhai,Gayatri Panda,Subrata Jana,Prasanjit Samal*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在具有C₃ᵥ对称性的晶体中，三重旋转对称性迫使Berry曲率偶极矩（BCD）为零，从而抑制了本征非线性霍尔效应（NLHE）。寻找有效手段打破对称性以恢复NLHE是研究的关键动机。

Method: 采用第一性原理密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）结合基于Wannier函数的输运计算方法，研究单层Janus AsTeBr在单轴应变下的电子结构、非线性霍尔效应及光学性质。

Result: 单轴应变将晶体对称性从C₃ᵥ降至C₁，产生有限BCD，导致Berry曲率热点发生各向异性重分布，从而产生显著的非线性霍尔电导率和非线性霍尔电流，最大响应出现在2%拉伸应变下。光学光谱呈现系统性红移和低能带间跃迁增强。

Abstract: The nonlinear Hall effect (NLHE) enables the generation of a transverse charge current in nonmagnetic materials with broken inversion symmetry while preserving time-reversal symmetry through the Berry curvature dipole (BCD). However, in crystals with $C_{3v}$ symmetry, the threefold rotational symmetry forces the BCD to vanish, thereby suppressing the intrinsic NLHE despite the presence of finite local Berry curvature. Here, using first-principles density functional theory combined with Wannier-based transport calculations, we demonstrate that uniaxial strain induces the NLHE in monolayer Janus AsTeBr by lowering the crystal symmetry from $C_{3v}$ to $C_{1}$ and generating a finite BCD. The resulting anisotropic redistribution of Berry-curvature hotspots produces pronounced nonlinear Hall conductivity and nonlinear Hall current, with the maximum response obtained at 2\% tensile strain. To elucidate the accompanying electronic-structure evolution, we further investigate the strain-dependent optical properties through the joint density of states, dielectric function, optical absorption, and reflectance. The optical spectra exhibit a systematic red shift and enhanced low-energy interband transitions, consistent with the strain-induced reconstruction of the electronic structure. Our results establish a microscopic connection between symmetry breaking, Berry-phase geometry, nonlinear Hall transport, and optical response, demonstrating that uniaxial strain provides an effective strategy for tailoring multiple functional properties in Janus two-dimensional materials.

Method: 采用分子模拟（molecular simulations）方法，研究非晶固体在低频机械振荡下缺陷介导的热激活跃迁，并结合退火（annealing）研究以及能量景观中主导弛豫路径（dominant relaxation paths）的分析。

Result: 发现跃迁在空间上具有相关性且存在强相互作用，必须采用一般性的网络描述（general network description）而非传统的独立二能级系统叠加。

Conclusion: 退火处理与能量景观中主导弛豫路径的分析揭示了降低室温机械耗散（room temperature mechanical loss）的新机制。

Abstract: The disordered and defect-rich structure of amorphous solids forms heterogeneous, high-dimensional energy landscapes. Such an energy landscape can be described by a discrete-state network of transitions between stable energy minima. Under low-frequency mechanical oscillations, defect-mediated, thermally activated transitions provide a microscopic mechanism for mechanical dissipation that are the dominant cause of mechanical loss in the mirror coatings of ground based gravitational waves detectors. Using molecular simulations, we find spatially correlated and strongly interacting transitions that require a general network description instead of a superposition of independent two-level systems as traditionally assumed. An annealing study combined with an analysis of dominant relaxation paths in the energy landscape reveals novel mechanisms for reducing room temperature mechanical loss.

Conclusion: 本研究挑战了以d-带为中心的研究范式，将s-带和p-带描述符识别为关键但此前被忽视的贡献因素，重新定义了金属间化合物NRR催化剂的电子描述符空间。该工作为通过DFT-ML方法指导发现用于可持续合成氨的非贵金属材料奠定了基础。

By incorporating intrinsic material properties along with electronic descriptors including s-, p- and d-band centers and fillings, as well as Bader charges of atoms neighboring the adsorbate, predictive ML models were developed with mean absolute errors of 0.26 eV for N2, 0.39 eV for N2H, and 0.17 eV for NH3 adsorption. Beyond their established importance in systems containing p-block elements or nearly filled d-band metals, s- and p-orbitals are also found to contribute significantly to transition-metal alloys activity such as Fe-Co, driven by adsorption-induced sp-d hybridization. By challenging the d-band-centric paradigm and identifying s- and p-band descriptors as critical yet overlooked contributors, this work redefines the electronic descriptor space for intermetallic NRR catalysts and lays the groundwork for DFT-ML-guided discovery of non-noble materials for sustainable ammonia synthesis.

Abstract: The properties of strongly correlated electron materials exhibit a surprising sensitivity to small lattice distortions, providing an opportunity for their tuning by selective distortion driving, usually achieved by optical excitations. Using inelastic electron tunneling in scanning tunneling microscopy, we demonstrate that at the surface of a strongly correlated electron material, we can drive vibrational excitations out of equilibrium, by studying the dynamics of localized modes on the Pd-terminated surface of the delafossite oxide PdCrO2. Result: 发现强化析出相在两种相反的动力学机制下溶解：低温下以弹道溶解（ballistic dissolution）为主，高温下则以溶解-再析出（dissolution and re-precipitation）为主。He气泡和富Kr孔洞在空位可迁移后成核，而长达五个服务年的嬗变反应会不可逆地将合金化学组成引向Ni-Zr金属间化合物。

Conclusion: 上述三种独立机制共同挑战了CuCrZr合金的性能设计基础，表明时效硬化型Cu基热沉合金在聚变堆中的长期性能需要进一步评估。研究提出了一项新的材料学挑战：需要开发能在聚变中子谱引发的热力学与弹道学双重不可逆化学重写作用下维持工程强度的新型Cu基热沉合金。

Abstract: Commercial fusion energy requires materials that survive intense neutron bombardment whilst extracting extreme heat loads for conversion to electricity. The CuCrZr alloy, the leading heat-sink material for fusion reactors, derives its strength from a fine dispersion of nano-precipitates formed during prime-ageing heat-treatment. Whether this precipitation-hardening strategy can withstand fusion-relevant irradiation remains untested. Here we show, combining in situ transmission electron microscopy under heavy-ion irradiation and He implantation with thermodynamic and transmutation modelling, that the hardening precipitates dissolve under two opposing kinetic regimes: ballistic dissolution dominates at low temperatures, whilst dissolution and re-precipitation dominate at high temperatures. Although the accelerated dose rates inherent to ion irradiation shift the balance between ballistic mixing and thermal back-diffusion relative to reactor conditions, precipitate degradation at both kinetic extremes indicates that the prime-aged microstructure is unlikely to remain unaltered under prolonged neutron exposure. He bubbles and Kr-rich voids nucleate once vacancies become mobile, and transmutation over five service years irreversibly redirects the alloy chemistry towards Ni-Zr intermetallics. These three independent mechanisms converge to challenge the strategy on which CuCrZr performance depends, suggesting that the long-term performance of age-hardenable Cu-based heat-sink alloys in fusion reactors warrants further assessment. Our findings reveal a new materials challenge for fusion reactor design and commercialisation: the need for new Cu-based heat-sink alloys able to retain engineered strength whilst their chemistry is irreversibly rewritten - thermodynamically and ballistically - by the fusion neutron spectrum.

### [257] [d-band filling dictates magnetic stability in Mn- and Co-substituted FeRh alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17688)

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算结合相干势近似（coherent potential approximation），系统研究了B2有序Fe基合金中，在Fe亚晶格上替代无序（Mn和Co掺杂）对磁性的影响。研究发现，d带填充（d-band filling）是控制该巡游电子体系（itinerant system）磁稳定性的主要参数：Mn掺杂（空穴掺杂）导致自旋极化塌缩并诱发反铁磁竞争，产生“巡游磁软性”（itinerant magnetic softness）；Co掺杂（电子掺杂）则通过将费米能级钉扎在多数自旋赝能隙中，起到“磁硬化剂”（magnetic hardener）的作用。

Conclusion: 调控费米能级相对于赝能隙（pseudogap）的位置，为控制B2有序巡游磁性材料的磁稳定性提供了一种系统的微观框架，区别于简单的磁-体积模型。

Abstract: The composition-dependent magnetic properties of B2-ordered \zfr~alloys with substitutional disorder on the Fe sublattice are
  investigated using first-principles calculations within the coherent potential approximation. By systematically substituting Mn
  and Co on the Fe sublattice, we establish $d$-band filling as the primary control parameter governing magnetic stability in this
  itinerant system. Mn substitution (hole doping) shifts the Fermi level into the minority-spin bonding states, driving a collapse
  of spin polarization (crossing zero at $x \approx 0.5$) and the emergence of competing antiferromagnetic interactions
  ($η_\mathrm{Mn} < 0$). Even though the ferromagnetic configuration remains energetically well separated from the G-type
  AFM-II configuration across the studied range ($ΔE$ up to $\sim$0.35~eV/atom), this exchange competition drives an
  ``itinerant magnetic softness'' that suppresses the Curie temperature by $\sim$450~K -- a finite-temperature instability set by
  the near-cancellation of competing exchange interactions rather than by AFM--FM energy proximity. In contrast, Co substitution
  (electron doping) acts as a ``magnetic hardener'' by pinning the Fermi level within the majority-spin pseudogap, preserving high
  spin polarization ($|P| \approx 0.75$) and stabilizing ferromagnetic exchange across the full composition range. These results
  show that tuning the Fermi level relative to the pseudogap provides a systematic, microscopic framework for controlling magnetic
  stability in B2-ordered itinerant magnets, distinct from simple magneto-volume models.

### [258] [Efficient Quantum-Mechanical Modeling of Nonradiative Charge Transfer Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17730)
*Alexander Karl,Dominic Waldhoer,Theresia Knobloch,Christoph Wilhelmer,Tibor Grasser*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套基于非辐射多声子（nonradiative multiphonon, NMP）理论的计算框架，通过引入有效交叉保持近似（effective crossing-preserving approximation），推导出解析、数值稳定且计算代价低的电荷捕获与发射速率表达式，适用于大规模半导体器件模拟，并建立了从微观缺陷物理到实际仿真的桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非辐射电荷转移过程在半导体器件可靠性现象（如偏压温度不稳定性、迟滞、随机电报噪声和陷阱辅助隧穿）中至关重要，但全量子力学形式的非辐射多声子（nonradiative multiphonon, NMP）理论计算成本过高，无法直接用于大规模仿真。

Method: 从电子-声子耦合动力学的量子力学基础出发，推导计算高效的电荷捕获与发射速率近似公式，明确其假设与有效性范围；提出一种有效交叉保持近似（effective crossing-preserving approximation），得到全解析、数值稳定且计算廉价的跃迁速率表达式；进一步推导局域缺陷态与扩展电子带之间跃迁的连续介质形式（continuum formulations）。

Result: 所得到的跃迁速率表达式完全解析且数值稳定，计算成本低，适合在宽泛的多维参数空间中反复评估捕获系数；连续介质形式可直接嵌入半导体器件模拟中，实现了微观缺陷物理与大规模电荷转移仿真之间的衔接。

Conclusion: 该框架既可作为实现基于NMP理论物理模型的实际指南，提供系统性的理论推导，又清晰界定了模型的适用极限（validity limits）。

Abstract: Nonradiative charge transfer processes play a central role in a wide range of physical phenomena, including reliability phenomena in semiconductor devices such as bias temperature instability, hysteresis, random telegraph noise, and trap-assisted tunneling. nonradiative multiphonon (NMP) theory provides a physically rigorous framework for describing such charge transitions, but its full quantum-mechanical formulation is computationally too demanding for large-scale simulations. In this work, we present a systematic and implementation-oriented treatment of NMP-based models for practical large-scale simulations. Starting from the quantum-mechanical foundations of coupled electron--phonon dynamics, we derive computationally efficient approximations for charge capture and emission rates and clearly identify the underlying assumptions and validity regimes. In particular, we introduce an effective crossing-preserving approximation that yields fully analytic, numerically stable, and computationally inexpensive transition rates while retaining the essential quantum-mechanical physics. The resulting expressions are therefore well suited for large-scale device simulations, where capture coefficients must be evaluated repeatedly over broad multidimensional parameter spaces. Furthermore, we derive continuum formulations for transitions between localized defect states and extended electronic bands, enabling direct incorporation into semiconductor-device simulations. The resulting framework bridges microscopic defect physics and practical large-scale simulations of charge transfer processes in complex semiconductor devices. At the same time this work serves as a practical guide for implementing physically grounded NMP-based models, providing both a systematic derivation of the underlying theory and a clear guidance on the validity limits.
