### [259] [Physically motivated iso-orbital indicator for meta-GGA exchange functionals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17736)
*Jeet Sharma,Abhishek Bhattacharjee,Bikash Patra,Prasanjit Samal*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文针对meta-GGA泛函中$α$指示符在低密度原子尾区发散的问题，提出用轨道自由DFT中的Pauli动能密度替换分母，消除发散且无需经验正则化参数。在r$^2$SCAN和MS2泛函上测试LKT和PGS两种增强因子后，发现修改后的指示符抑制了半局域交换势的虚假振荡，恢复原子尾区的电子局域化，并将半导体带隙平均绝对误差降低41.1%–48.8%，同时保持结合能精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: meta-广义梯度近似（meta-GGA）泛函中的同轨道指示符$α$在低密度尾区发散，导致非物理的交换势和系统的带隙误差。

Method: 用轨道自由密度泛函理论（orbital-free DFT）中具有物理基础的Pauli动能密度替换$α$的分母，无需经验正则化参数；在r$^2$SCAN和MS2交换泛函中测试LKT与PGS两种增强因子。

Result: 修改后的指示符抑制了半局域交换势的虚假振荡，恢复了原子尾区的正确电子局域化。在十元立方半导体基准测试中，r$^2$SCAN@PGS的带隙平均绝对误差（MAE）降低41.1%，MS2@PGS降低48.8%，结合能精度基本保持。

Conclusion: 两种构造不同的泛函上的一致改进表明该修正具有物理而非泛函特定的来源，为开发满足约束条件的meta-GGA泛函提供了进一步动力。

Abstract: The iso-orbital indicator $α= (τ- τ^\mathrm{vW})/τ^\mathrm{UEG}$ is a key ingredient of meta-generalized gradient approximation (meta-GGA) functionals, but diverges in low-density tails , causing unphysical exchange potentials and systematic band gap errors as noted in [J. Chem. Phys. 150, 161101 (2019)]. We replace the denominator of $α$ with a physically motivated Pauli KED drawn from the orbital-free DFT literature, eliminating the divergence in the low density atomic tail without any empirical regularization parameter. Testing two such enhancement factors: LKT and PGS, within the r$^2$SCAN and MS2 exchange functionals, we find that the modified indicators suppress spurious oscillations in the semilocal exchange potential and restore correct electron localization in atomic tails. For a ten-member cubic semiconductor benchmark, the band gap mean absolute error is reduced by 41.1 % for r$^2$SCAN@PGS and 48.8 % for MS2@PGS, while cohesive energy accuracy is largely preserved. The consistent improvement across two functionals with distinct constructions confirms a physical rather than functional specific origin, and motivates further development of meta-GGA functionals with constraint satisfying iso-orbital indicators.

*Roee Asher,Nadav Moav,Lee A. Burton*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶体可能存在的结构数量远超已知热力学稳定的无机材料数量，这表明实验可及的结构空间可能围绕有限数量的优选结构框架（structural frameworks）组织，因此需要系统性地量化这些框架的重复出现规律。

Method: 对23160种位于热力学凸包（convex hull）上的结构进行分析，识别出6820种不同的结构框架，并将其中在多种化学组成材料中重复出现的2382种框架归类为结构原型。进一步在过滤后的数据集中，分别统计金属体系与离子化合物的结构框架和原型数量。

Result: 在过滤后的数据集中，金属体系表现出尤其强的结构重复性，6270种材料归入535种框架和327种原型；而5557种离子化合物归入1704种框架和696种原型。

Conclusion: 稳定无机材料占据的是一个高度可压缩的结构空间；基于重复出现建立的结构原型目录提供了框架普遍性的经验度量，可用于根据已知化合物中的重复出现情况来估计未来材料中不同结构框架的相对可能性。

Abstract: The number of possible crystal structures vastly exceeds the number realized among thermodynamically stable inorganic materials, suggesting that experimentally accessible structure space is organized around a limited set of preferred structural frameworks. Analysis of 23,160 structures on the thermodynamic convex hull identifies 6,820 distinct structural frameworks, of which 2,382 recur across multiple chemically distinct materials and are therefore classified as structural prototypes. Within a filtered dataset, metallic systems exhibit particularly strong structural recurrence, with 6,270 materials grouped into 535 frameworks and 327 prototypes, while 5,557 ionic compounds occupy 1,704 frameworks and 696 prototypes. These results demonstrate that stable inorganic materials occupy a highly compressible region of structure space and establish a recurrence-based catalog of structural prototypes that provides an empirical measure of framework prevalence, enabling the relative likelihood of structural frameworks in future materials to be estimated from their recurrence among known compounds.

Method: 将前期基于聚合物拓扑描述符的机器学习模型应用于更大范围的聚合物体系，并将加工参数整合到特征集（feature set）中，以评估化学结构和加工条件对Tg预测的影响。

Abstract: Despite the advances in structure-based modeling of polymer properties, accurately predicting glass transition temperature (Tg) is still challenging for polymers whose behavior is strongly influenced by intermolecular interactions and processing conditions. We previously developed a machine-learning model based on polymer topological descriptors to predict Tg. The model performed well and was based solely on the chemistry and structure of the polymer without any inclusion of processing parameters. In this work, we have extended that work by first applying that same model to a larger range of polymers and second by integrating processing parameters into the feature set. The chemistry-based model still demonstrates consistent predictive performance for most polymers, indicating that Tg is indeed primarily chemistry and structure driven and not strongly impacted by processing. However, several polymers exhibited deviations between predicted and experimental Tg values. Detailed analysis reveals that these differences are related to strong intermolecular interactions and processing-dependent factors, particularly for polymers prepared by solution casting and high temperature annealing. These results demonstrate that molecular topology provides a strong foundation for Tg prediction; however, this approach also screens out those classes of polymers for with processing conditions play an important role.

### [264] [Spin-phonon interaction in a symmetry-enforced spin-polarized state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.17980)
*Suman Kalyan Pradhan,Dayal Das,Shubham Patel,Subhajit Mahapatra,Sachin Majee,Dibyendu Majee,Arnab Bera,Achintya Singha,Snehasish Nandy,Samik DuttaGupta,Atindra Nath Pal*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对称性调控磁性材料（symmetry-governed magnetic materials）在无净磁化或杂散场的条件下具有自旋电子学（spintronics）应用潜力，因此理解这些体系中晶格动力学与对称性衍生的自旋极化电子态（spin-polarized electronic states）之间的耦合至关重要。然而，由于自旋极化源于晶体对称性而非传统磁序，自旋-声子耦合的微观机制仍不清楚，这是本工作要解决的核心问题。

Method: 采用温度和偏振分辨的拉曼光谱（temperature- and polarization-resolved Raman spectroscopy）研究g型交错磁体CoNb4Se8，并测量了结构类似的缺Co化合物（Co-deficient compound）作为对照样品，该对照体系缺乏明确的长程磁有序。结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）揭示自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）如何在晶格振动与对称性调控电子态之间建立相互作用通道。

Result: 在CoNb4Se8的磁相变（magnetic transition）附近观测到显著的对称性选择性声子重整化（symmetry-selective phonon renormalization），而缺Co体系中类似的声子反常（phonon anomalies）仍然存在，表明晶格响应不能仅由与相干磁有序（coherent magnetic ordering）相关的传统交换伸缩（exchange-striction）解释。第一性原理计算表明，自旋-轨道耦合建立了晶格振动与对称性调控电子态之间的对称性依赖相互作用通道。

Conclusion: 该研究识别了一种对称性调控磁体中自旋-声子耦合的替代机制，证明即使在没有稳健磁有序的条件下，声子也能灵敏地探测对称性驱动的自旋极化。这项工作为理解和工程化对称性驱动量子材料中的自旋-晶格功能性提供了框架，并给出了将晶格动力学耦合至自旋极化电子态的设计原则。

Abstract: Symmetry-governed magnetic materials have emerged as a promising platform for spintronic functionalities without net magnetization or stray magnetic fields, motivating the exploration of how lattice dynamics couple to symmetry-derived spin-polarized electronic states. Understanding spin-phonon coupling in these systems is therefore essential for uncovering the microscopic origin of spin-lattice interactions and for enabling their control in quantum materials. However, this mechanism remains poorly understood because spin polarization originates from crystal symmetry rather than conventional magnetic order. Here, we address this issue in the g-type altermagnet CoNb4Se8 using temperature- and polarization-resolved Raman spectroscopy, complemented by measurements on a structurally analogous Co-deficient compound lacking well-defined long-range magnetic order. We observe pronounced symmetry-selective phonon renormalization across the magnetic transition in CoNb4Se8, while related phonon anomalies persist in the Co-deficient system, demonstrating that the lattice response cannot be explained solely by conventional exchange-striction associated with coherent magnetic ordering. First-principles calculations reveal that spin-orbit coupling establishes a symmetry-dependent interaction channel between lattice vibrations and symmetry-governed electronic states. Our results identify an alternative mechanism for spin-phonon coupling in symmetry-governed magnetic materials and demonstrate that phonons provide a sensitive probe of symmetry-driven spin polarization even without robust magnetic order. More broadly, this work provides a framework for understanding and engineering spin-lattice functionality in symmetry-driven quantum materials, offering design principles for coupling lattice dynamics to spin-polarized electronic states.

### [266] [DFT+U+V is equivalent to DFT+U with density-dependent hybridized projectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18071)
*Edward Linscott,Alberto Carta,Nicola Marzari*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文证明了在位DFT+U（density-functional theory with on-site Hubbard correction）中的交错+V修正（inter-site +V corrections）在V/U一阶展开下等价于基于密度依赖（density-dependent）且与相邻位杂化的Hubbard投影子（Hubbard projectors）重新定义下的在位DFT+U，揭示了V影响共价性（covalency）的显式机制，并指出了常见近似下等价性的部分失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DFT+U方法在处理局域d或f电子材料时存在过局域化（over-localization）电荷和破坏共价键的问题，交错+V修正虽被广泛使用以缓解此问题，但缺乏严格的形式化证明（formal justification）。

Method: 在V/U的一阶微扰展开（first order in V/U）近似下，从理论上推导交错+V修正与基于密度依赖且与相邻位杂化的Hubbard投影子重新定义后的在位DFT+U之间的等价关系（exact equivalence）。

Result: 交错V修正等价于在位DFT+U在重新定义后的密度依赖Hubbard投影子下的形式；当投影子被冻结（held frozen）时，等价性部分失效。该结果提供了V影响共价性的显式机制。

Conclusion: 该形式化结果不仅重新诠释了现有理论框架，还提出了两个关键问题：V应如何计算，以及Hubbard子空间（Hubbard subspaces）的本质到底是什么。

Abstract: Hubbard-corrected density-functional theory (DFT+$U$) is a popular tool for first-principles modeling of materials with localized $d$ or $f$ electrons, but its on-site corrections tend to over-localize charge and break covalent bonds. Inter-site $+V$ corrections were introduced to counter this and are now widely used, but a formal justification has been lacking. Here we show that -- to first order in $V/U$ -- inter-site corrections are exactly equivalent to on-site DFT+$U$ evaluated on a density-dependent redefinition of the Hubbard projectors, hybridized with those of neighboring sites, providing insight into the explicit mechanism by which $V$ affects covalency. If the projectors are held frozen, as is common practice, the equivalence partially breaks down. Beyond reinterpreting the formalism, these results sharpen the questions of how $V$ should be computed and what the Hubbard subspaces fundamentally are.

</details>


### [267] [First-principles electronic transport properties of Ti and Ti-6Al-4V for modeling ultrashort-pulse laser ablation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18085)
*Korbinian Hobmaier,Guillaume E. Allemand,Alberto Marmodoro,Matthieu J. Verstraete,Ján Minár,Heinz P. Huber,David Redka*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算了六角密堆积钛（hcp Ti）和钛合金Ti-6Al-4V的电子输运性质，发现合金的电子热导率仅为纯钛的约1/6.4，但在双温模型模拟中，合金与纯钛参数集给出的峰值晶格温度差异仅为1.4%，而输运模型的函数形式（如低温Drude限）对预测精度的影响远大于元素与合金的区别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超短脉冲激光烧蚀（ultrashort-pulse laser ablation）的预测建模需要温度依赖的电子结构参数（电子热导率、电子-声子耦合、热容），这些参数在元素金属中已有充分记载，但在合金中严重缺乏。技术重要的钛合金Ti-6Al-4V目前仍使用纯钛参数建模，亟需系统计算并评估这一近似带来的误差。

Method: 采用Korringa–Kohn–Rostoker相干势近似（coherent-potential-approximation, CPA）框架内的Kubo–Greenwood形式论，从第一性原理（first principles）计算hcp Ti和Ti-6Al-4V的电子输运，将化学无序和热无序置于同等地位处理。

Result: 纯钛的电输运率与独立ab initio电子-声子计算及实验一致，并复现了Mott–Ioffe–Regel极限附近的高温饱和行为。在电子-声子非平衡条件下，电子热导率随电子温度升高而饱和并下降：纯钛最大值约2.97 kW/(m·K)，Ti-6Al-4V仅约0.47 kW/(m·K)，相差6.4倍。双温模型（two-temperature model）模拟中，合金与纯钛参数集给出的峰值晶格温度差异仅约1.4%，与实验烧蚀阈值约3%的差异一致。若用低温Drude限替换第一性原理热导率，峰值晶格温度偏差可达19%。

Conclusion: 对于Ti-6Al-4V的激光烧蚀预测，输运模型的函数形式（functional form）比元素与合金参数的区别更为关键。仅使用纯钛参数近似带来的误差在实验不确定度范围内，但使用错误的输运模型（如Drude限）会显著降低预测精度。

Abstract: Predictive modeling of ultrashort-pulse laser ablation requires temperature-dependent material parameters derived from the electronic structure, namely the electronic thermal conductivity, electron--phonon coupling, and heat capacity. These parameters are well documented for elemental metals but remain sparsely documented for alloys, apart from application-relevant exceptions such as stainless steels. The technologically important titanium alloy Ti-6Al-4V is a prominent example, which is still modeled using elemental-titanium values. We compute the electronic transport of hcp Ti and Ti-6Al-4V from first principles, using the Kubo--Greenwood formalism within the Korringa--Kohn--Rostoker coherent-potential-approximation framework, treating chemical and thermal disorder on equal footing. For elemental Ti, the calculated electrical resistivity agrees with independent \textsc{abinit} electron--phonon calculations and experiment, and also reproduces the high-temperature saturation near the Mott--Ioffe--Regel limit. Under electron--phonon nonequilibrium, the electronic thermal conductivity saturates and then decreases with electronic temperature, reaching a maximum of about \SI{2.97}{\kilo\watt\per\metre\per\kelvin} in Ti but only \SI{0.47}{\kilo\watt\per\metre\per\kelvin} in Ti-6Al-4V, a factor of 6.4 lower. In two-temperature-model simulations the alloy and elemental parameter sets yield peak lattice temperatures differing by only about 1.4\%, consistent with reported experimental ablation thresholds that differ by about 3\%, well within their measurement uncertainties. Replacing the first-principles thermal conductivity with the low-temperature Drude limit shifts the peak lattice temperature by up to 19\%, showing that the functional form of the transport model is even more important than the elemental vs alloy distinction for predictive accuracy.

### [268] [Correcting DFT formation energies towards experimental accuracy using foundational MLIPs and latent-feature delta-learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18092)
*Timo Reents,Marnik Bercx,Giovanni Pizzi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

Method: 研究以开源数据库 MC3D 为核心，对比 OQMD 和 Materials Project 两个 DFT 数据库以及实验生成焓。采用基于 r²SCAN 级别的预训练机器学习原子间势（MLIP，特别是 PET-OMATPES）替代 GGA 水平计算，并在此基础上训练经典机器学习模型，利用 MLIP 的潜在特征（latent features）进行 delta-learning 修正。

Conclusion: 研究验证并拓展了将 PBEsol 几何与 meta-GGA 能量相结合的做法至基础模型 MLIP 时代，证明该方法可系统性提升数据库热力学稳定性数据的实验一致性，并为进一步的材料筛选提供更可靠的能学参考。

Abstract: Crystal structure databases curated by high-throughput density functional theory calculations typically serve as the starting point for computational materials discovery efforts. Thermodynamic stability data, such as formation energies and the energy above the convex hull, are important quantities to guide the search for novel materials, enabling filtering for (meta)stable structures. Here, we present the thermodynamic stability of the fully open-source, reproducible, and experimentally focused Materials Cloud three-dimensional crystals database (MC3D). We compare against two other DFT databases, the Open Quantum Materials Database (OQMD) and the Materials Project (MP), as well as against experimental formation enthalpies. We then demonstrate how recent foundational machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) trained at the r$^2$SCAN level (specifically, we test PET-OMATPES here) can be leveraged to improve the agreement of formation energies with experiment, reducing the mean absolute error by more than 40% relative to GGA without requiring any additional DFT calculation. Our results validate and extend the established practice of combining PBEsol geometries with meta-GGA energies to the era of foundational MLIPs. Finally, we train classical machine learning models to further correct the formation energies in a delta-learning framework, where we use the information-rich latent features of the foundational MLIP. These models further reduce the mean absolute error below 50 meV/atom, bringing it down to values comparable with the experimental uncertainty itself. Notably, compared to purely compositional features, the latent features (combined with carefully tuned regularization) simultaneously reduce the prediction error and limit the impact of the learned corrections on the relative phase stability.

### [269] [Optimal transition states for polaron hopping transport without supercells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18096)
*Vasilii Vasilchenko,Matteo Giantomassi,Samuel Poncé,Xavier Gonze*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需超胞（supercell）的从头算（ab initio）极化子跳跃输运框架，基于变分极化子方程（variational polaron equations）和字符串方法（string method），直接在倒空间优化自 trapped 极化子态之间的过渡态，从而评估绝热跳跃速率与迁移率。应用于 LiF 和金红石 TiO₂ 中，揭示了多步和各向异性跳跃机制，其中 TiO₂ 的电子极化子迁移率与实验吻合，而能带型玻尔兹曼输运（Boltzmann transport）则显著高估迁移率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极化子（polaron）形成会局域化载流子并引发从能带型（band-like）到跳跃型（hopping）输运的转变。传统基于 DFT 超胞的方法存在极化子自相互作用（self-interaction）、虚假静电效应（spurious electrostatics）以及对极化子尺寸扩展性差的问题，亟需一种可扩展且无超胞的方案。

Method: 提出一种无超胞框架，核心结合变分极化子方程与字符串方法。通过直接在倒空间（reciprocal space）优化自 trapped 极化子态之间的过渡态（transition states），获取沿反应路径的极化子构型，进而计算绝热跳跃速率（adiabatic hopping rates）和迁移率（mobilities）。

Result: 对 LiF 和金红石 TiO₂ 的测试表明，该方法能够揭示多步跳跃（multi-step hopping）和各向异性跳跃（anisotropic hopping）机制。在金红石 TiO₂ 中，计算所得电子极化子迁移率与实验一致，而能带型玻尔兹曼输运则大幅高估迁移率。

Conclusion: 该方法为电荷运动受自 trapped 机制主导的材料提供了一条可扩展的第一性原理极化子跳跃动力学路径，有效克服了传统超胞方法的局限性。

Abstract: Polaron formation localizes charge carriers and drives a crossover from band-like to hopping transport in materials. Hopping dynamics can be obtained from DFT supercell calculations of transition states, but these suffer from polaron self-interaction, spurious electrostatics, and poor scaling with polaron size. We introduce a supercell-free framework for \textit{ab initio} polaron hopping transport based on variational polaron equations and the string method. The approach optimizes transition states between self-trapped polaron states directly in reciprocal space and provides the polaron configurations along the path, enabling evaluation of adiabatic hopping rates and mobilities. We apply the method to LiF and rutile TiO$_2$, revealing multi-step and anisotropic hopping mechanisms. In rutile TiO$_2$, the computed electron-polaron mobility agrees with experiment, whereas band-like Boltzmann transport substantially overestimates the mobility. Our results establish a scalable route to first-principles polaron-hopping dynamics in materials in which charge motion is governed by self-trapping.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Refractory high-entropy alloys have emerged as promising candidates for high-temperature applications due to their exceptional mechanical properties. Understanding the thermodynamic mechanisms underlying chemical ordering in these complex systems is critical for optimizing their performance. In this work, by utilizing a universal machine learning interatomic potential with hybrid Monte Carlo and molecular dynamics simulations, the temperature-dependent thermodynamics and mechanical properties of (MoCrTi)(100-x)Alx system have been investigated. The heat capacities and short-range order parameters reveal distinct order-disorder transition behaviors. While the Mo25Cr25Ti25Al25 and Mo32Cr32Ti32Al4 alloys exhibit a single transition dominated by the synergistic ordering of B2-type atomic pairs, the Mo28Cr28Ti28Al16 and Mo30Cr30Ti30Al10 alloys display two separate transitions: a low-temperature stage driven by specific pairs (Mo-Al in Mo28Cr28Ti28Al16; Al-Al in Mo30Cr30Ti30Al10) and a high-temperature stage governed by the remaining pairs. Structural analysis indicates that in the low-temperature ordered B2 phase, Mo and Al share one sublattice while Cr and Ti share the other. Furthermore, the relationship between ordering and mechanical stiffness has been identified. Ordering significantly enhances the elastic constants and moduli, and gives rise to a non-monotonic compositional dependence. Unlike random solid solutions, where stiffness increases monotonically with decreasing Al content, ordered configurations exhibit a non-monotonic trend, peaking at the Mo30Cr30Ti30Al10 alloy. This enhancement is attributed to an optimized population of stiff atomic pairs induced by strong short-range order. These findings provide fundamental insights into the interplay between compositions, chemical ordering, and mechanical performance, offering guidance for the design of refractory high-entropy alloys.

### [271] [Defect configuration, not nitrogen content, governs the mechanical integrity of nitrogen-doped graphene: a molecular dynamics study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18129)
*Indranil Rudra,Jahid Emon,A. K. M. Monjur Morshed*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过分子动力学模拟，系统分离了氮掺杂石墨烯中不同氮化学构型（graphitic-N与pyridinic-N）、空位缺陷及缺陷排列方式对力学性能的影响，发现力学损伤主要由空位而非氮本身引起，且缺陷间的相互作用取决于其相对于载荷方向的排列方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氮掺杂石墨烯的力学可靠性常被归因于氮含量，但氮以多种化学构型（chemically distinct configurations）存在，各自对力学的独立作用及其与其他缺陷的相互作用尚不清楚，因此需要系统解耦这些因素。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）对单轴拉伸（uniaxial tension）过程进行研究；设计三种尺寸匹配的缺陷——石墨型氮团簇（graphitic-nitrogen cluster）、空位（void）和吡啶型氮团簇（pyridinic-nitrogen cluster），通过两组对照实验分别隔离边缘化学效应和空位效应。

Result: 石墨型氮团簇对力学性能几乎无影响（强度降低<1%）；空位使极限强度降低约23%；吡啶型氮团簇（兼具空位与边缘氮）损伤最大（约30%），其断裂从氮装饰的边缘突然发生而非像裸空位那样经历韧性损伤过程。缺陷相互作用取决于其相对载荷方向的排列：共线缺陷几乎不相互作用，以较严重者为主导；并排缺陷通过应力场叠加相互耦合，随间距减小而逐渐削弱强度，这种相互作用可延伸至~80 Å的分离距离。

Conclusion: 氮改性石墨烯的力学完整性取决于缺陷的构型（configuration）、氮的键合环境（bonding environment）以及共存缺陷相对于载荷方向的排列方式，而非仅由氮含量或缺陷密度决定，这为容错设计（defect-tolerant design）提供了基础。

Abstract: The mechanical reliability of nitrogen-doped graphene is often attributed to its nitrogen content, yet nitrogen occurs in chemically distinct configurations whose individual mechanical roles, and whose interactions with other defects, remain unresolved. Here, molecular dynamics simulations of uniaxial tension are used to separate the contributions of nitrogen chemistry, missing atoms, and defect arrangement to the strength and fracture of graphene. Three size-matched defects, a graphitic-nitrogen cluster, a void, and a pyridinic-nitrogen cluster, are compared so that two controlled contrasts isolate the effects of edge chemistry and of the vacancy independently. The graphitic cluster leaves the mechanical properties essentially unchanged (a strength reduction of <1 %), whereas the void degrades the ultimate strength by ~23 % and the pyridinic cluster, which combines the same vacancy with edge nitrogen, is the most damaging (~30 %), failing abruptly from its nitrogen-decorated rim rather than through the damage-tolerant process of the bare void. The mechanical impact of a nitrogen cluster is therefore governed by whether it carries vacancies, not by nitrogen itself. When a nitrogen cluster and a void coexist, their interaction is controlled by orientation relative to the load: in-line defects interact negligibly and fail at the more severe member, whereas side-by-side defects couple through overlapping stress fields and weaken the sheet progressively as they approach, an interaction that persists to separations of ~80 Å. These results establish that the mechanical integrity of nitrogen-modified graphene is determined by the configuration of defects, the bonding environment of nitrogen, and the arrangement of coexisting defects relative to the load, rather than by nitrogen content or defect density alone, thereby providing a basis for defect-tolerant design.

In this study, we formulate a 2-D phase-field model to investigate the TiO2 morphology evolution during nanocarving processes. The model incorporates TiO2 reduction reaction, Ti3+ diffusion, and anisotropies in surface energy, diffusivity and reaction rate. Through systematic simulations in both single- and poly-crystals, we elucidate the roles of different anisotropy factors in nanocrystal morphologies at different carving stages, identifying the strong reaction rate anisotropy as the dominant factor for experimentally observed nanowire morphologies. We further explore the effect of grain misorientation angle, generating a nanocarving morphology map to guide grain orientation control.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为MgH₂储氢材料的脱氢动力学提供原子尺度的理解，并建立定量构效关系以指导高性能催化剂的设计。

Method: 采用机器学习势驱动的分子动力学模拟（ML-MD）对原始与掺杂MgH₂进行研究；通过系统考察不同表面取向，识别最活跃的低指数表面；对22种掺杂元素进行综合筛选；利用机器学习分析识别关键描述符。

Result: MgH₂ (100)面被确定为最活跃的低指数表面；发现亚表层H₂生成后扩散至表面脱附的新机制，突破了传统表面路径的认知；Ni被识别为最优掺杂元素；Miedema电子密度（nws）被机器学习确定为关键描述符，且与总释氢量之间存在火山型关系（最优窗口：4.0 < nws < 5.4×10⁻² e/bohr³）。

Conclusion: 本研究从原子层面验证了催化相在MgH₂中发挥的"氢泵"效应，展示了ML-MD在解析复杂催化机制与建立定量构效关系方面的强大能力，为MgH₂及其他储氢材料的高性能催化剂理性设计提供了稳健的框架。

Abstract: Machine learning potential-driven molecular dynamics simulations (ML-MD) were employed to provide atomistic insights into the dehydrogenation kinetics of pristine and doped MgH2. Through systematic investigation of distinct surface orientations, the MgH2 (100) surface was identified as the most active low-index surface for hydrogen release. For pristine MgH2, our simulations revealed a novel H2 formation mechanism characterized by H2 generation in the subsurface region followed by diffusion to the surface for desorption, highlighting the critical role of subsurface processes beyond conventional surface-driven pathways. Comprehensive screening of 22 doping elements identified Ni as the most effective dopant. Among several descriptors, machine learning analysis identified the time-coupled Miedema electron density as the critical descriptor, underscoring the role of electronic properties. Consequently, a volcano-shaped relationship was uncovered between the intrinsic Miedema electron density ( nws ) and total hydrogen release (optimal window: 4.0 < nws < 5.4x10-2 e/bohr3). Dopants within this range serve a dual function: acting as thermodynamic sinks for H attraction while maintaining a balanced interaction strength to facilitate H-H coupling and H2 release. This atomistic-level validation provides strong theoretical support for the experimentally observed "hydrogen pump" effect of catalytic phases. The present study demonstrates the strong capability of ML- MD in navigating through complex catalytic mechanisms and establishing quantitative property-activity relationships, providing a robust framework for rational design of high-performance catalysts for MgH2 and other hydrogen storage materials.

</details>


### [274] [Excitonic effects in the photocarriers dynamics of two-dimensional materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.18183)
*Carlos Betancur,Gianluca Stefanucci,Enrico Perfetto*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过基于激子布洛赫方程（excitonic Bloch equations, XBE）的两粒子框架，揭示了激子关联（excitonic correlations）在半导体光生载流子超快动力学中的关键作用。在非共振光激发WSe₂单层中，XBE预测的载流子弛豫路径与时间分辨角分辨光电子能谱（time-resolved ARPES）实验一致，表明热化载流子的动量分布由激子波函数而非费米-狄拉克统计决定，形成关联非平衡态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统单粒子框架（single-particle frameworks）仅考虑电子-电子和电子-声子散射，忽略在带边（band edges）附近占主导的电子-空穴关联（electron-hole correlations），无法准确描述半导体中光生载流子的超快动力学。

Method: 引入基于激子布洛赫方程（excitonic Bloch equations, XBE）的两粒子框架，该框架同时包含载流子-声子散射并显式考虑激子形成（exciton formation）。

Result: 对非共振光激发WSe₂单层的研究表明：XBE预测出增强的谷间散射（intervalley scattering）以及Q谷载流子布居数（carrier population）超过K谷，这与最先进方法的结果定性不同，但与时间分辨ARPES实验一致；热化载流子的动量分布由激子波函数（exciton wavefunctions）而非费米-狄拉克统计（Fermi-Dirac statistics）决定。

Conclusion: 激子关联（excitonic correlations）是支配激子材料（excitonic materials）中光生载流子动力学的关键机制，所建立的关联非平衡态（correlated nonequilibrium state）信号挑战了传统单粒子热化图像的描述。

Abstract: We investigate the role of excitonic correlations in shaping the ultrafast dynamics of photoexcited carriers in semiconductors. Conventional approaches describe relaxation within single-particle frameworks, where electron-electron and electron-phonon scattering drive thermalization toward Fermi-Dirac distributions, neglecting electron-hole correlations that dominate near band edges. We introduce a two-particle framework based on excitonic Bloch equations (XBE) that captures carrier-phonon scattering and explicitly accounts for exciton formation. Applying this approach to non-resonantly photoexcited WSe$_2$ monolayers, we reveal qualitatively different carrier relaxation pathways: in contrast to state-of-the-art methods, XBE predict enhanced intervalley scattering and dominant carrier population in Q valleys over K valleys, in agreement with time-resolved ARPES experiments. Moreover, the momentum distribution of thermalized carriers is shaped by exciton wavefunctions rather than by Fermi-Dirac statistics, signaling the formation of a correlated nonequilibrium state. These results establish excitonic correlations as a key mechanism governing photocarrier dynamics in excitonic materials.

</details>
